śrīrastubharatamunipraṇītaṃ nāṭyaśāstramatha prathamo dhyāyaḥpraṇamya śirasā devau pitāmahamaheśvarau nāṭyaśāstraṃ pravakṣyāmi brahmaṇā yadudāhṛtam  BhN samāptajapyaṃ vratinaṃ svasutaiḥ parivāritam anadhyāye kadācittu bharataṃ nāṭyakovidam  BhN munayaḥ paryupāsyainamātreyapramukhāḥ purā papracchuste mahātmāno niyatendriyabuddhayaḥ  BhN yo yaṃ bhagavatā samyaggrathito vedasammitaḥ nāṭyavedaṃ kathaṃ brahmannutpannaḥ kasya vā kṛte  BhN katyaṅgaḥ kiṃpramāṇaśca prayogaścāsya kīdṛśaḥ sarvametadyathātattvaṃ bhagavanvaktumarhasi  BhN teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ pratyuvāca tato vākyaṃ nāṭyavedakathāṃ prati  BhN bhavadbhiḥ śucibhirbhūtvā tathāvahitamānasaiḥ śrūyatāṃ nāṭyavedasya sambhavo brahmanirmitaḥ  BhN pūrvaṃ kṛtayuge viprā vṛtte svāyaṃbhuve ntare tretāyuge tha samprāpte manorvaivasvatasya tu  BhN grāmyadharmapravṛtte tu kāmalobhavaśaṃ gate īrṣyākrodhādisaṃmūḍhe loke sukhitaduḥkhite  BhN devadānavagandharvayakṣarakṣomahoragaiḥ jambudvīpe samākrānte lokapālapratiṣṭhite  BhN mahendrapramukhairdevairuktaḥ kila pitāmahaḥ krīḍanīyakamicchāmo dṛṣyaṃ śravyaṃ ca yadbhavet  BhN na vedavyavahāro yaṃ saṃśrāvyaḥ śūdrajātiṣu tasmātsṛjāparaṃ vedaṃ pañcamaṃ sārvavarṇikam  BhN evamastviti tānuktvā devarājaṃ visṛjya ca sasmāra caturo vedānyogamāsthāya tattvavit  BhN neme vedā yataḥ śrāvyāḥ strīśūdrādyāsu jātiṣu vedamanyattataḥ srakṣye sarvaśrāvyaṃ tu pañcamam  BhN dharmyamarthyaṃ yaśasyaṃ ca sopadeśyaṃ sasaṅgraham bhaviṣyataśca lokasya sarvakarmānudarśakam  BhN sarvaśātrārthasampannaṃ sarvaśilpapravartakam nāṭyākhyaṃ pañcamaṃ vedaṃ setihāsaṃ karomyaham  BhN evaṃ saṅkalpya bhagavān sarvavedānanusmaran nāṭyavedaṃ tataścakre caturvedāṅgasambhavam  BhN jagrāha pāṭhyamṛgvedātsāmabhyo gītameva ca yajurvedādabhinayān rasānātharvaṇādapi  BhN vedopavedaiḥ sambaddho nāṭyavedo mahātmanā evaṃ bhagavatā sṛṣṭo brahmaṇā sarvavedinā  BhN utpādya nāṭyavedaṃ tu brahmovāca sureśvaram itihāso mayā sṛṣṭaḥ sa sureṣu niyujyatām  BhN kuśalā ye vidagdhāśca pragalbhāśca jitaśramāḥ teṣvayaṃ nāṭyasaṃjño hi vedaḥ saṃkrāmyatāṃ tvayā  BhN tacchṛtvā vacanaṃ śakro brahmaṇā yadudāhṛtam prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā pratyuvāca pitāmaham  BhN grahaṇe dhāraṇe jñāne prayoge cāsya sattama aśaktā bhagavan devā ayogyā nāṭyakarmaṇi  BhN ya ime vedaguhyajñā ṛṣayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ete sya grahaṇe śaktāḥ prayoge dhāraṇe tathā  BhN śrutvā tu śakravacanaṃ māmāhāmbujasambhavaḥ tvaṃ putraśatasaṃyuktaḥ prayoktāsya bhavānagha  BhN ājñāpito viditvāhaṃ nāṭyavedaṃ pitāmahāt putrānadhyāpayāmāsa prayogaṃ cāpi tattvataḥ  BhN śāṇḍilyaṃ caiva vātsyaṃ ca kohalaṃ dattilaṃ tathā jaṭilambaṣṭakau caiva taṇḍumagniśikhaṃ tathā  BhN saindhavaṃ sapulomānaṃ śāḍvaliṃ vipulaṃ tathā kapiñjaliṃ vādiraṃ ca yamadhūmrāyaṇau tathā  BhN jambudhvajaṃ kākajaṅghaṃ svarṇakaṃ tāpasaṃ tathā kaidāriṃ śālikarṇaṃ ca dīrghagātraṃ ca śālikam  BhN kautsaṃ tāṇḍāyaniṃ caiva piṅgalaṃ citrakaṃ tathā bandhulaṃ bhallakaṃ caiva muṣṭhikaṃ saindhavāyanam  BhN taitilaṃ bhārgavaṃ caiva śuciṃ bahulameva ca abudhaṃ budhasenaṃ ca pāṇḍukarṇaṃ sukeralam  BhN ṛjukaṃ maṇḍakaṃ caiva śambaraṃ vañjulaṃ tathā māgadhaṃ saralaṃ caiva kartāraṃ cogrameva ca  BhN tuṣāraṃ pārṣadaṃ caiva gautamaṃ bādarāyaṇam viśālaṃ śabalaṃ caiva sunāmaṃ meṣameva ca  BhN kāliyaṃ bhramaraṃ caiva tathā pīṭhamukhaṃ munim nakhakuṭṭāśmakuṭṭau ca ṣaṭpadaṃ sottamaṃ tathā  BhN pādukopānahau caiva śrutiṃ cāṣasvaraṃ tathā agnikuṇḍājyakuṇḍau ca vitaṇḍya tāṇḍyameva ca  BhN kartarākṣaṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ kuśalaṃ dussahaṃ tathā lājaṃ bhayānakaṃ caiva bībhatsaṃ savicakṣaṇam  BhN puṇḍrākṣaṃ puṇḍranāsaṃ cāpyasitaṃ sitameva ca vidyujjihvaṃ mahājihvaṃ śālaṅkāyanameva ca  BhN śyāmāyanaṃ māṭharaṃ ca lohitāṅgaṃ tathaiva ca saṃvartakaṃ pañcaśikhaṃ triśikhaṃ śikhameva ca  BhN śaṅkhavarṇamukhaṃ śaṇḍaṃ śaṅkukarṇamathāpi ca śakranemiṃ gabhastiṃ cāpyaṃśumāliṃ śaṭhaṃ tathā  BhN vidyutaṃ śātajaṅghaṃ ca raudraṃ vīramathāpi ca pitāmahājñayāsmābhirlokasya ca guṇepsayā  BhN prayojitaṃ putraśataṃ yathābhūmivibhāgaśaḥ yo yasminkarmaṇi yathā yogyastasmin sa yojitaḥ  BhN bhāratīṃ sātvatīṃ caiva vṛīttimārabhaṭīṃ tathā samāśritaḥ prayogastu prayukto vai mayā dvijāḥ  BhN parigṛhya praṇamyātha brahmā vijñāpito mayā athāha māṃ suraguruḥ kaiśikimapi yojaya  BhN yacca tasyāḥ kṣamaṃ dravyaṃ tad brūhi dvijasattama evaṃ tenāsmyabhihitaḥ pratyuktaśca mayā prabhuḥ  BhN dīyatāṃ bhagavandravyaṃ kaiśikyāḥ samprayojakam nṛttāṅgahārasampannā rasabhāvakriyātmikā  BhN dṛṣṭā mayā bhagavato nīlakaṇṭhasya nṛtyataḥ kaiśikī ṣlakṣṇanaipathyā śṛṅgārarasasambhavā  BhN aśakyā puruṣaiḥ sā tu prayoktuṃ strījanādṛte tato sṛjanmahātejā manasāpsaraso vibhuḥ  BhN nāṭyālaṅkāracaturāḥ prādānmahyaṃ prayogataḥ mañjukeśīṃ sukeśīṃ ca miśrakeśīṃ sulocanām  BhN saudāminīṃ devadattāṃ devasenāṃ manoramām sudatīṃ sundarīṃ caiva vidagdhāṃ vipulāṃ tathā  BhN sumālāṃ santatiṃ caiva sunandāṃ sumukhīṃ tathā māgadhīmarjunīṃ caiva saralāṃ keralāṃ dhṛtim  BhN nandāṃ sapuṣkalāṃ caiva kalamāṃ caiva me dadau svātirbhāṇḍaniyuktastu saha śiṣyaiḥ svayambhuvā  BhN nāradādyāśca gandharvā gānayoge niyojitāḥ evaṃ nāṭyamidaṃ samyagbuddhvā sarvaiḥ sutaiḥ saha  BhN svātināradasaṃyukto vedavedāṅgakāraṇam upasthito haṃ brahmāṇaṃ prayogārthaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ  BhN nāṭyasya grahaṇaṃ prāptaṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇyaham etattu vacanaṃ śrutvā pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥ  BhN mahānayaṃ prayogasya samayaḥ pratyupasthitaḥ ayaṃ dhvajamahaḥ śrīmān mahendrasya pravartate  BhN atredānīmayaṃ vedo nāṭyasaṃjñaḥ prayujyatām tatastasmindhvajamahe nihatāsuradānave  BhN prahṛṣṭāmarasaṃkīrṇe mahendravijayotsave pūrvaṃ kṛtā mayā nāndī hyāśīrvacasaṃyutā  BhN aṣṭāṅgapadasaṃyuktā vicitrā vedanirmitā tadante nukṛtirbaddhā yathā daityāḥ surairjitāḥ  BhN sampheṭavidravakṛtā cchedyabhedyāhavālmikā tato brahmādayo devāḥ prayogaparitoṣitāḥ  BhN pradadurmatsutebhyastu sarvopakaraṇāni vai prītastu prathamaṃ śakro dattavānsvaṃ dhvajaṃ śubham  BhN brahmā kuṭilakaṃ caiva bhṛṅgāraṃ varuṇaḥ śubham sūryaśchatraṃ śivassiddhiṃ vāyurvyajanameva ca  BhN viṣṇuḥ siṃhāsanaṃ caiva kubero mukuṭaṃ tathā śrāvyatvaṃ prekṣaṇīyasya dadau devī sarasvatī  BhN śeṣā ye devagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ tasminsadasyabhipretānnānājātiguṇāśrayān  BhN aṃśāṃśairbhāṣitaṃ bhāvān rasān rūpaṃ balaṃ tathā dattavantaḥ prahṛṣṭāste matsutebhyo divaukasaḥ  BhN evaṃ prayoge prārabdhe daityadānavanāśane abhavankṣubhitāḥ sarve daityā ye tatra saṅgatāḥ  BhN virūpākṣa purogāṃśca vighnānprotsāhya te bruvan na kṣamiṣyāmahe nāṭyametadāgamyatāmiti  BhN tatastairasuraiḥ sārdhaṃ vighnā māyāmupāśritāḥ vācaśceṣṭāṃ smṛtiṃ caiva stambhayanti sma nṛtyatām  BhN tathā vidhvaṃsanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtradhārasya devarāṭ kasmātprayogavaiṣamyamityuktvā dhyānamāviśat  BhN athāpaśyatsado vighnaiḥ samantādparivāritam sahetaraiḥ sūtradhāraṃ naṣṭasaṃjñaṃ jaḍīkṛtam  BhN utthāya tvaritaṃ śakraṃ gṛhītvā dhvajamuttamam sarvaratnojjvalatanuḥ kiñcidudvṛta locanaḥ  BhN raṅgapīṭhagatānvighnānasurāṃścaiva devarāṭ jarjarīkṛtadehāṃstānakarojjarjareṇa saḥ  BhN nihateṣu ca sarveṣua vighneṣu saha dānavaiḥ saṃprahṛṣya tato vākyamāhuḥ sarve divaukasaḥ  BhN aho praharaṇaṃ divyamidamāsāditaṃ tvayā jarjarīkṛtasarvāṅgā yenaite dānavāḥ kṛtāḥ  BhN yasmādanena te vighnāḥ sāsurā jarjarīkṛtāḥ tasmājjarjara eveti nāmato yaṃ bhaviṣyati  BhN śeṣā ye caiva hiṃsārthamupayāsyanti hiṃsakāḥ dṛṣṭvaiva jarjaraṃ te pi gamiṣyantyevameva tu  BhN evamevāstviti tataḥ śakraḥ provāca tānsurān rakṣābhūtaśca sarveṣāṃ bhaviṣyatyeṣa jarjaraḥ  BhN prayoge prastute hyevaṃ sphīte śakramahe punaḥ trāsaṃ sañjanayanti sma vighnāḥ śeṣāstu nṛtyatām  BhN dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ vyavasitaṃ daityānāṃ viprakārajam upasthito haṃ brahmāṇaṃ sutaiḥ sarvaiḥ samanvitaḥ  BhN niścitā bhagavanvighnā nāṭyasyāsya vināśane asya rakṣāvidhiṃ samyagājñāpaya sureśvara  BhN tataśca viśvakarmāṇaṃ brahmovāca prayatnataḥ kuru lakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ nāṭyaveśma mahāmate  BhN tato cireṇa kālena viśvakarmā mahacchubham sarvalakṣaṇasampannaṃ kṛtvā nāṭyagṛhaṃ tu saḥ  BhN proktavāndruhiṇaṃ gatvā sabhāyāntu kṛtāñjalīḥ sajjaṃ nāṭyagṛhaṃ deva tadevekṣitumarhasi  BhN tataḥ saha mahendreṇa suraiḥ sarvaiśca setaraiḥ āgatastvarito dṛṣṭuṃ druhiṇo nāṭyamaṇḍapam  BhN dṛṣṭvā nāṭyagṛhaṃ brahmā prāha sarvānsurāṃstataḥ aṃśabhāgairbhavadbhistu rakṣyo yaṃ nāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ  BhN rakṣaṇe maṇḍapasyātha viniyuktastu candramāḥ lokapālāstathā dikṣu vidikṣvapi ca mārutāḥ  BhN nepathyabhūmau mitrastu nikṣipto varuṇo mbare vedikārakṣaṇe vahnirbhāṇḍe sarvadivaukasaḥ  BhN varṇāścatvāra evātha stambheṣu viniyojitāḥ ādityāścaiva rudrāśca sthitāḥ stambhāntareśvatha  BhN dhāraṇīśvatha bhūtāni śālāsvapsarastathā sarvaveśmasu yakṣiṇyo mahīpṛṣṭhe mahodadhiḥ  BhN dvāraśālāniyuktau tu krutāntaḥ kāla eva ca sthāpitau dvārapatreṣu nāgamukhyau mahābalau  BhN dehalyāṃ yamadaṇḍastu śūlaṃ tasyopari sthitam dvārapālau sthitau caubhau niyatirmṛtyureva ca  BhN pārśve ca raṅgapīṭhasya mahendraḥ sthitavānsvayam sthāpitā mattavāraṇyāṃ vidyuddaityaniṣūdanī  BhN stambheṣu mattavāraṇyāḥ sthāpitā paripālane bhūtayakṣapiśāśca guhyakāśca mahābalāḥ  BhN jarjare tu vinikṣiptaṃ vajraṃ daityanibarhaṇam tatparvasu vinikṣiptāḥ surendrā hyamitaujasaḥ  BhN śiraḥparvasthito brahmā dvitīye śaṅkarastathā tṛtīye ca sthito viṣṇuścaturthe skanda eva ca  BhN pañcame ca mahānāgāḥ śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ evaṃ vighnavināśāya sthāpitā jarjare surāḥ  BhN raṅgapīṭhasya madhye tu svayaṃ brahmā pratiṣṭhitaḥ iṣṭyarthaṃ raṅgamadhye tu kriyate puṣpamokṣaṇam  BhN pātālavāsino ye ca yakṣaguhyakapannagāḥ adhastādraṅgapīṭhasya rakṣaṇe te niyojitāḥ  BhN nāyakaṃ rakṣatīndrastu nāyikāṃ ca sarasvatī vidūṣakamathauṅkāraḥ śeśāstu prakṛtirharaḥ  BhN yānyetāni niyuktāni daivatānīha rakṣaṇe etānyevādhidaivāni bhaviṣyantītyuvāca saḥ  BhN etasminnantare devaiḥ sarvairuktaḥ pitāmahaḥ sāmnā tāvadime vighnāḥ sthāpyantāṃ vacasā tvayā  BhN pūrvaṃ sāmaṃ prayoktavyaṃ dvitīyaṃ dānameva ca tayorupari bhedastu tato daṇḍaḥ prayujyate  BhN devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā vighnānuvāca ha kasmādbhavanto nāṭyasya vināśāya samutthitāḥ  BhN brahmaṇo vacanaṃ śrutvā virūpākṣo bravīdvacaḥ daityairvighnagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ sāmapūrvamidaṃ tataḥ  BhN yo yaṃ bhagavatā sṛṣṭo nāṭyavedaḥ surecchayā pratyādeśo yamasmākaṃ surārthaṃ bhavatā kṛtaḥ  BhN tannaitadevaṃ kartavyaṃ tvayā lokapitāmaha yathā devastathā daityāstvattaḥ sarve vinirgatāḥ  BhN vighnānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā vacanamabravīt alaṃ vo manyunā daityā viṣādaṃ tyajatānaghāḥ  BhN bhavatāṃ devatānāṃ ca śubhāśubhavikalpakaḥ karmabhāvānvayāpekṣī nāṭyavedo mayā kṛtaḥ  BhN naikāntato tra bhavatāṃ devānāṃ cānubhāvanam trailokyāsyāsya sarvasya nāṭyaṃ bhāvānukīrtanam  BhN kvaciddharmaḥ kvacitkrīḍā kvacidarthaḥ kvacicchamaḥ kvaciddhāsyaṃ kvacidyuddhaṃ kvacitkāmaḥ kvacidvadhaḥ  BhN dharmo dharmapravṛttānāṃ kāmaḥ kāmopasevinām nigraho durvinītānāṃ vinītānāṃ damakriyā  BhN klībānāṃ dhārṣṭyajananamutsāhaḥ śūramāninām abudhānāṃ vibodhaśca vaiduṣyaṃ viduṣāmapi  BhN īśvarāṇāṃ vilāsaśca sthairyaṃ duḥkhārditasya ca arthopajīvināmartho dhṛtirudvegacetasām  BhN nānābhāvopasampannaṃ nānāvasthāntarātmakam lokavṛttānukaraṇaṃ nāṭyametanmayā kṛtam  BhN uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ narāṇāṃ karmasaṃśrayam hitopadeśajananaṃ dhṛtikrīḍāsukhādikṛt  BhN etadraseṣu bhāveṣu sarvakarmakriyāsvatha sarvopadeśajananaṃ nāṭyaṃ loke bhaviṣyati  BhN duḥkhārtānāṃ śramārtānāṃ śokārtānāṃ tapasvinām viśrāntijananaṃ kāle nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati  BhN dharmyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ hitaṃ buddhivivardhanam lokopadeśajananaṃ nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati  BhN na tajjñānaṃ na tacchilpaṃ na sā vidyā na sā kalā nāsau yogo na tatkarma nāṭye smin yanna dṛśyate  BhN tannātra manyuḥ kartavyo bhavadbhiramarānprati saptadvīpānukaraṇaṃ nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati  BhN yenānukaraṇaṃ nāṭyametattadyanmayā kṛtam  BhN devānāmasurāṇāṃ ca rājñāmatha kuṭumbinām brahmarṣīṇāṃ ca vijñeyaṃ nāṭyaṃ vṛttāntadarśakam  BhN yo yaṃ svabhāvo lokasya sukhaduḥkhasamanvitaḥ so ṅgādyabhinayopeto nāṭyamityabhidhīyate  BhN vedavidyetihāsānāmākhyānaparikalpanam vinodakaraṇaṃ loke nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati  BhN śrutismṛtisadācārapariśeṣārthakalpanam vinodajananaṃ loke nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati  BhN etasminnantare devān sarvānāha pitāmahaḥ kriyatāmadya vidhivadyajanaṃ nāṭyamaṇḍape  BhN balipradānairhomaiśca mantrauṣadhisamanvitaiḥ bhojyairbhakṣaiśca pānaiśca baliḥ samupakalpatām  BhN martyalokagatāḥ sarve śubhāṃ pūjāmavāpsyatha apūjayitvā raṅgaṃ tu naiva prekṣāṃ pravartayet  BhN apūjayitvā raṅgaṃ tu yaḥ prekṣāṃ kalpayiṣyati niṣphalaṃ tasya tat jñānaṃ tiryagyoniṃ ca yāsyati  BhN yajñena saṃmitaṃ hyedadraṅgadaivatapūjanam tasmātsarvaprayatnena kartavyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN nartako rthapatirvāpi yaḥ pūjāṃ na kariṣyati na kārayiṣyantyanyairvā prāpnotyapacayaṃ tu saḥ  BhN yathāvidhiṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yastu pūjāṃ kariṣyati sa lapsyate śubhānarthān svargalokaṃ ca yāsyati  BhN evamuktvā tu bhagavāndruhiṇaḥ sahadevataiḥ raṅgapūjāṃ kuruśveti māmevaṃ samacodayat  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre nāṭyotpattirnāma prathamo dhyāyaḥatha bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre dvitīyo dhyāyaḥbharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā papracchurmunayastataḥ bhagavan śrotumicchāmo yajanaṃ raṅgasaṃśrayam  BhN atha vā yā kriyāstatra lakṣaṇaṃ yacca pūjanam bhaviṣyadbhirnaraiḥ kāryaṃ kathaṃ tannāṭyaveśmani  BhN ihādirnāṭyayogasya nāṭyamaṇḍapa eva hi tasmāttasyaiva tāvattvaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vaktumarhasi  BhN teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato bravīt lakṣaṇaṃ pūjanaṃ caiva śrūyatāṃ nāṭyaveśmanaḥ  BhN divyānāṃ mānasī sṛṣṭirgṛheṣūpavaneṣu ca yathā bhāvābhinirvartyāḥ sarve bhāvāstu mānuṣāḥ narāṇāṃ yatnataḥ kāryā lakṣaṇābhihitā kriyā  BhN śrūyatāṃ tadyathā yatra kartavyo nāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ tasya vāstu ca pūjā ca yathā yojyā prayatnataḥ  BhN iha prekṣyāgṛhaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhīmatā viśvakarmaṇā trividhaḥ sanniveśaśca śāstrataḥ parikalpitaḥ  BhN vikṛṣṭaścaturaśraśca tryaśraścaiva tu maṇḍapaḥ teṣāṃ trīṇi pramāṇāni jyeṣṭhaṃ madhyaṃ tathāvaram  BhN pramāṇameṣāṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ hastadaṇḍasamāśrayam śataṃ cāṣṭau catuḥṣaṣṭirhastā dvātriṃśadeva ca  BhN aṣṭādhikaṃ śataṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭistu madhyamam kanīyastu tathā veśma hastā dvātriṃśadiṣyate  BhN devānāṃ tu bhavejjyeṣṭhaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ madhyamaṃ bhavet śeṣāṇāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ tu kanīyaḥ saṃvidhīyate  BhN prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ praśastaṃ madhyamaṃ smṛtam tatra pāṭhyaṃ ca geyaṃ ca sukhaśrāvyataraṃ bhavet  BhN prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ triprakāro vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ vikṛṣṭaścaturasraśca tryasraścaiva prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN kanīyastu smṛtaṃ tryasraṃ caturasraṃ tu madhyamam jyeṣṭhaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāṭyavedaprayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN pramāṇaṃ yacca nirdiṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ viśvakarmaṇā prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ taccaiva hi nibodhata  BhN aṇū rajaśca vālaśca likṣā yūkā yavastathā aṅgulaṃ ca tathā hasto daṇḍaścaiva prakīrtitaḥ  BhN aṇavo ṣṭau rajaḥ proktaṃ tānyaṣṭau vāla ucyate vālāstvaṣṭau bhavellikṣā yūkā likṣāṣṭakaṃ bhavet  BhN yūkāstvaṣṭau yavo jñeyo yavāstvaṣṭau tathāṅgulam aṅgulāni tathā hastaścaturviṃśatirucyate  BhN caturhasto bhaveddaṇḍo nirdiṣṭastu pramāṇataḥ anenaiva pramāṇena vakṣyāmyeṣāṃ vinirṇayam  BhN catuḥṣaṣṭikarānkuryāddīrghatvena tu maṇḍapam dvātriṃśataṃ ca vistāranmartyānāṃ yo bhavediha  BhN ata ūrdhvaṃ na kartavyaḥ kartṛbhirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ yasmādavyaktabhāvaṃ hi tatra nāṭyaṃ vrajediti  BhN maṇḍape viprakṛṣṭe tu pāṭhyamuccāritasvaram anissaraṇadharmatvādvisvaratvaṃ bhṛśaṃ vrajet  BhN yaścāpyāsyagato bhāvo nānādṛṣṭisamanvitaḥsa veśmanaḥ prakṛṣṭatvād vrajedavyaktatāṃ parām  BhN prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ tasmānmadhyamamiṣyate yāvatpāṭhyaṃ ca geyaṃ ca tatra śravyataraṃ bhavet  BhN prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ triprakāro vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ vikṛṣṭaścaturasraśca tryasraścaiva prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN kanīyastu smṛtaṃ tryasraṃ caturasraṃ tu madhyamam jyeṣṭhaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāṭyavedaprayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN devānāṃ mānasī sṛṣṭirgṛheṣūpavaneṣu ca yatnabhāvābhiniṣpannāḥ sarve bhāvā hi mānuṣā  BhN tasmāddevakṛtairbhāvairna vispardheta mānuṣaḥ mānuṣasya tu gehasya sampravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN bhūmervibhāgaṃ pūrvaṃ tu parīkṣeta prayojaka tato vāstu pramāṇena prārabheta śubhecchayā  BhN samā sthirā tu kaṭhinā kṛṣṇā gaurī ca yā bhavet bhūmistatraiva kartavyaḥ kartṛbhirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ  BhN prathamaṃ śodhanaṃ kṛtvā lāṅgalena samutkṛṣet asthikīlakapālāni tṛṇagulmāṃśca śodhayet  BhN śodhayitvā vasumatīṃ pramāṇaṃ nirdiśettataḥ trīṇyuttarāṇi saumyaṃ ca viśākhāpi ca revatī hastitiṣyānurādhāśca praśastā nāṭyakarmaṇi puṣyanakṣatrayogena śuklaṃ sūtraṃ prasārayet  BhN kārpāsaṃ bālbajaṃ vāpi mauñjaṃ vālkalameva ca sūtraṃ budhaistu kartavyaṃ yasya cchedo na vidyate  BhN ardhacchinne bhavetsūtre svāmino maraṇaṃ dhruvam tribhāgacchinnayā rajvā rāṣṭrakopo vidhīyate  BhN chinnāyāṃ tu caturbhāge prayokturnāśa ucyate hastātprabhraṣṭayā vāpi kaścitvapacayo bhavet  BhN tasmānnityaṃ prayatnena rajjugrahaṇamiṣyate kāryaṃ caiva prayatnena mānaṃ nāṭyagṛhasya tu  BhN muhūrtenānukūlena tithyā sukaraṇena ca brāhmaṇāṃstarpayitvā tu puṇyāhaṃ vācayettataḥ  BhN śāntitoyaṃ tato dattvā tataḥ sūtraṃ prasārayet catuṣṣaṣṭikarānkṛtvā dvidhā kuryātpunaśca tān  BhN pṛṣṭhato yo bhavedbhāgo dvidhābhūtasya tasya tu samamardhavibhāgena raṅgaśīrṣaṃ prakalpayet  BhN paścime ca vibhāge tha nepathyagṛhamādiśet vibhajya bhāgānvidhivadyayathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN śubhe nakṣatrayoge ca maṇḍapasya niveśanam śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣairmṛdaṅgapaṇavādibhiḥ  BhN sarvātodyaiḥ praṇuditaiḥ sthāpanaṃ kāryameva tu utsāryāṇi tvaniṣṭāni pāṣaṇḍyāśramiṇastathā  BhN kāṣāyavasanāścaiva vikalāścaiava ye narāḥ niśāyāṃ ca baliḥ kāryā nānābhojanasaṃyutaḥ  BhN gandhapuṣpaphalopetā diśo daśa samāśritaḥ pūrveṇa śuklānnayuto nīlānno dakṣiṇena ca  BhN paścimena baliḥ pīto raktaścaivottareṇa tu yādṛśaṃ diśi yasyāṃ tu daivataṃ parikalpitam  BhN tādṛśastatra dātavyo balirmantrapuraskṛtaḥ sthāpane brāhmaṇebhyaśca dātavyaṃ ghṛtapāyasam  BhN madhuparkastathā rājñe kartṛbhyaśca guḍaudanam nakṣatreṇa tu kartavyaṃ mūlena sthāpanaṃ budhaiḥ  BhN muhūrtenānukūlena tithyā sukaraṇena ca evaṃ tu sthāpanaṃ kṛtvā bhittikarma prayojayet  BhN bhittikarmaṇi nirvṛtte stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ tataḥ tithinakṣatrayogena śubhena karaṇena ca  BhN stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ rohiṇyā śravaṇena vā ācāryeṇa suyuktena trirātropoṣitena ca  BhN stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ prāpte sūryodaye śubhe prathame brāhmaṇastambhe sarpissarṣapasaṃskṛtaḥ  BhN sarvaśuklo vidhiḥ kāryo dadyātpāyasameva ca tataśca kṣatriyastambhe vastramālyānulepanam  BhN sarva raktaṃ pradātavyaṃ dvijebhyaśca guḍaudanam vaiśyastambhe vidhiḥ kāryo digbhāge paścimottare  BhN sarvaṃ prītaṃ pradātavyaṃ dvijebhyaśca ghṛtaudanam śūdrastambhe vidhiḥ kāryaḥ samyakpūrvottarāśraye  BhN nīlaprāyaṃ prayatnena kūsaraṃ ca dvijāśanam pūrvoktabrāhmaṇastambhe śuklamālyānulepane  BhN nikṣipetkanakaṃ mūle karṇābharaṇasaṃśrayam tāmraṃ cādhaḥ pradātavyaṃ stambhe kṣatriyasaṃjñake  BhN vaiśyastambhasya mūle tu rajataṃ sampradāpayet śūdrastambhasya mūle tu dadyādāyasameva ca  BhN sarveṣveva tu nikṣepyaṃ stambhamūleṣu kāñcanam svastipuṇyāhaghoṣeṇa jayaśabdena caiva hi  BhN stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ puṣpamālāpuraskṛtam ratnadānaiḥ sagodānairvastradānairanalpakaiḥ  BhN brāhmaṇāṃstarpayitvā tu stambhānutthāpayettataḥ acalaṃ cāpyakampañca tathaivāvalitaṃ punaḥ  BhN stambhasyotthāpane samyagdoṣā hyete prakīrtitāḥ avṛṣṭiruktā calane valane mṛtyuto bhayam  BhN kampane paracakrāttu bhayaṃ bhavati dāruṇam doṣairetairvihīnaṃ tu stambhamutthāpayecchivam  BhN pavitre brāhmaṇastambhe dātavyā dakṣiṇā ca gauḥ śeṣāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ kāryaṃ sthāpane kartṛsaṃśrayam  BhN mantrapūtaṃ ca taddeyaṃ nāṭyācāryeṇa dhīmatā purohitaṃ nṛpaṃ caiva bhojayenmadhupāyasaiḥ  BhN kartṝnāpi tathā sarvānkṛsarāṃ lavaṇottarām sarvamevaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā sarvātodyaiḥ pravāditaiḥ  BhN abhimantrya yathānyāyaṃ stambhānutthāpayecchuciḥ yathācalo girirmerurhimavāṃśca mahābalaḥ  BhN jayāvaho narendrasya tathā tvamacalo bhava stambhadvāraṃ ca bhittiṃ ca nepathyagṛhameva ca  BhN evamutthāpayetajjño vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā raṅgapīṭhasya pārśve tu kartavyā mattavāraṇī  BhN catustambhasamāyuktā raṅgapīṭhapramāṇataḥ adhyardhahastotsedhena kartavyā mattavāraṇī  BhN utsedhena tayostulyaṃ kartavyaṃ raṅgamaṇḍapam tasyāṃ mālyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca gandhaṃ vastraṃ tathaiva ca  BhN nānāvarṇāni deyāni tathā bhūtapriyo baliḥ āyasaṃ tatra dātavyaṃ stambhānāṃ kuśailairadhaḥ  BhN bhojane kṛsarāścaiva dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇāśanam evaṃ vidhipuraskāraiḥ kartavyā mattavāraṇī  BhN raṅgapīṭhaṃ tataḥ kāryaṃ vidhidṛṣṭeṇa karmaṇā raṅgaśīrṣastu kartavyaṃ ṣaḍdārukasamanvitam  BhN kāryaṃ dvāradvayaṃ cātra nepathyagṛhakasya tu pūraṇe mṛttikā cātra kṛṣṇā deyā prayatnataḥ  BhN lāṅgalena samutkṛṣya nirloṣṭatṛṇaśarkaram lāṅgale śuddhavarṇo tu dhuryo yojyau prayatnataḥ  BhN kartāraḥ puruṣaścātra ye ṅgadoṣavivirjitāḥ ahīnāṅgaiśca voḍhavyā mṛttikā piṭakairnavaiḥ  BhN evaṃvidhaiḥ prakartavyaṃ raṅgaśīrṣaṃ prayatnataḥ kūrmapṛṣṭhaṃ na kartavyaṃ matsyapṛṣṭhaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN śuddhādarśatalākāraṃ raṅgaśīrṣaṃ praśasyate ratnāni cātra deyāni pūrve vajraṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ  BhN vaiḍūryaṃ dakṣiṇe pārśve sphaṭikaṃ paścime tathā pravālamuttare caiva madhye tu kanakaṃ bhavet  BhN evaṃ raṅgaśiraḥ kṛtvā dārukarma prayojayet ūhapratyūhasaṃyuktaḥ nānāśilpaprayojitam  BhN nānāsañjavanopetaṃ bahuvyālopaśobhitam sasālabhañjikābhiśca samantātsamalaṅkṛtam  BhN nirvyūhakuharopetaṃ nānāgrathitavedikam nānāvinyāsasaṃyuktaṃ citrajālagavākṣakam  BhN supīṭhadhāriṇīyuktaṃ kapotālīsamākulam nānākuṭṭimavinyastaiḥ stambhaiścāpyupaśobhitam  BhN evaṃ kāṣṭhavidhiṃ kṛtvā bhittikarma prayojayet stambhaṃ vā nāgadantaṃ vā vātāyanamathāpi vā  BhN koṇaṃ vā sapratidvāraṃ dvāraviddhaṃ na kārayet kāryaḥ śailaguhākāro dvibhūmirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ  BhN mandavātāyanopeto nirvāto dhīraśabdavān tasmānnivātaḥ kartavyaḥ kartṛbhirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ  BhN gambhīrasvaratā yena kutapasya bhaviṣyati bhittikarmavidhiṃ kṛtvā bhittilepaṃ pradāpayet  BhN sudhākarma bahistasya vidhātavyaṃ prayatnataḥ bhittiṣvatha viliptāsu parimṛṣṭāsu sarvataḥ  BhN samāsu jātaśobhāsu citrakarma prayojayet citrakarmaṇi cālekhyāḥ puruṣāḥ srījanāstathā  BhN latābandhāśca kartavyāścaritaṃ cātmbhogajam evaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭyaveśma prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN punareva hi vakṣyāmi caturaśrasya lakṣaṇam samantataśca kartavyā hastā dvātriṃśadeva tu  BhN śubhabhūmivibhāgastho nāṭyajñairnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ yo vidhiḥ pūrvamuktastu lakṣaṇaṃ maṅgalāni ca  BhN vikṛṣṭe tānyaśeṣāṇi caturaśre pi kārayet caturaśraṃ samaṃ kṛtvā sūtreṇa pravibhajya ca  BhN bāhyataḥ sarvataḥ kāryā bhittiḥ śliṣṭeṣṭakā dṛḍhā tatrābhyantarataḥ kāryā raṅgapīṭhopari sthitāḥ  BhN daśa prayoktṛbhiḥ stambhāḥ śaktā maṇḍapadhāraṇe stambhānāṃ bāhyataścāpi sopānākṛti pīṭhakam  BhN iṣṭakādārubhiḥ kāryaṃ prekṣakāṇāṃ niveśanam hastapramāṇairutsedhairbhūmibhāgasamutthitaiḥ  BhN raṅgapīṭhāvalokyaṃ tu kuryādāsanajaṃ vidhim ṣaḍanyānantare caiva punaḥ stambhānyathādiśam  BhN vidhinā sthāpayetajño dṛḍhānmaṇḍapadhāraṇe aṣṭau stambhānpunaścaiva teṣāmupari kalpayet  BhN sthāpyaṃ caiva tataḥ pīṭhamaṣṭahastapramāṇataḥ viddhāsyamaṣṭahastaṃ ca pīṭhaṃ teṣu tato nyaset  BhN tatra stambhāḥ pradātavyāstajñairmaṇḍapadhāraṇe dhāraṇīdhāraṇāste ca śālastrībhiralaṅkṛtāḥ  BhN nepathyagṛhakaṃ caiva tataḥ kāryaṃ prayatnataḥ dvāraṃ caikaṃ bhavettatra raṅgapīṭhapraveśanam  BhN janapraveśanaṃ cānyadābhimukhyena kārayet raṅgasyābhimukhaṃ kāryaṃ dvitīyaṃ dvārameva tu  BhN aṣṭahastaṃ tu kartavyaṃ raṅgapīṭhaṃ pramāṇataḥ caturaśraṃ samatalaṃ vedikāsamalaṅkṛtam  BhN pūrvapramāṇanirdiṣṭā kartavyā mattavāraṇī catuḥstambhasamāyuktā vedikāyāstu pārśvataḥ  BhN samunnataṃ samaṃ caiva raṅgaśīrṣaṃ tu kārayet vikṛṣṭe tūnnataṃ kāryaṃ caturaśre samaṃ tathā  BhN evametena vidhinā caturaśraṃ gṛhaṃ bhavet ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi tryaśragehasya lakṣaṇam  BhN tryaśraṃ trikoṇaṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭyaveśmaprayoktṛbhiḥ madhye trikoṇamevāsya raṅgapīṭhaṃ tu kārayet  BhN dvāraṃ tainaiva koṇena kartavyaṃ tasya veśmanaḥ dvitīyaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ raṅgapīṭhasya pṛṣṭhataḥ  BhN vidhiryaścaturaśrasya bhittistambhasamāśrayaḥ sa tu sarvaḥ prayoktavyastryaśrasyāpi prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN evametena vidhinā kāryā nāṭyagṛhā budhaiḥ punareṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi pūjāmevaṃ yathāvidhiḥ  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre maṇḍapavidhāno nāma dvitīyo dhyāyaḥatha tṛtīyodhyāyaḥsarvalakṣaṇasaṃpanne kṛte nāṭyagṛhe śubhe gāvo vaseyuḥ saptāhaṃ saha japyaparairdvijaiḥ  BhN tato dhivāsayedveśma raṅgapīṭhaṃ tathaiva ca mantrapūtena toyena prokṣitāṅgo niśāgame  BhN yathāsthānāntaragato dīkṣitaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ trirātropoṣito bhūtvā nāṭyācāryo hatāmbaraḥ  BhN namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ sarvalokodbhavaṃ bhavam jagatpitāmahaṃ caiva viṣṇumindraṃ guhaṃ tathā  BhN sarasvatīṃ ca lakṣmīṃ ca siddhiṃ medhāṃ dhṛtiṃ smṛtim somaṃ sūryaṃ ca maruto lokapālāṃstathāśvinau  BhN mitramagniṃ surānvarṇān rudrānkālaṃ kaliṃ tathā mṛtyuṃ ca niyatiṃ caiva kāladaṇḍaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN viṣṇupraharaṇaṃ caiva nāgarājaṃ ca vāsukim vajraṃ vidyutsamudrāṃśca gandharvāpsaraso munīn  BhN bhūtān piśācān yakṣāṃśca guhyakāṃśca maheśvarān asurānnāṭyavighnāṃśca tathānyāndaityarākṣasān  BhN tathā nāṭyakumārīśca mahāgrāmaṇyameva ca yakṣāṃśca guhyakāṃścaiva bhūtasaṅghāstathaiva ca  BhN etāṃścānyāṃśca devarṣīnpraṇamya racitāñjaliḥ yathāsthānāntaragatānsamāvāhya tato vadet  BhN bhavadbhirno niśāyāṃ tu kartavyaḥ samparigrahaḥ sāhāyyaṃ caiva dātavyamasminnāṭye sahānugaiḥ  BhN sampūjya sarvānekatra kutapaṃ samprayujya ca jarjarāya prayuñjīta pūjāṃ nāṭyaprasiddhaye  BhN tvaṃ mahendrapraharaṇaṃ sarvadānavasūdanam nirmitassarvadevaiśca sarvavighnanibarhaṇa  BhN nṛpasya vijayaṃ śaṃsa ripūṇāṃ ca parājayam gobrāhmaṇaśivaṃ caiva nāṭyasya ca vivardhanam  BhN evaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyamupāsyaṃ nāṭyamaṇḍape niśāyāṃ tu prabhātāyāṃ pūjanaṃ prakramediha  BhN ārdrāyāṃ vā maghāyāṃ vā yāmye pūrveṣu vā triṣu āśleṣāmūlayorvāpi kartavyaṃ raṅgapūjanam  BhN ācāryeṇa tu yuktena śucinā dīkṣitena ca raṅgasyodyotanaṃ kāryaṃ devatānāṃ ca pūjanam  BhN dinānte dāruṇe ghore muhūrte yamadaivate ācamya tu yathānyāyaṃ devatā vai niveśayat  BhN raktāḥ pratisarāḥ sūtraṃ raktagandhāśca pūjitāḥ raktāḥ sumanasaścaiva yacca raktaṃ phalaṃ bhavet  BhN yavaissiddhārthakairlājairakṣataiḥ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ nāgapuṣpasya cūrṇena vituṣābhiḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ  BhN etairdravyairyutaṃ kuryāddevatānāṃ niveśanam ālikhenmaṇḍalaṃ pūrvaṃ yathāsthānaṃ yathāvidhiḥ  BhN samantastaśca kartavyaṃ hastā ṣoḍaśa maṇḍalam dvārāṇi cātra kurvīta vidhānena caturdiśam  BhN madhye caivātra kartavye dve rekhe tiryagūrdhvage tayoḥ kakṣyāvibhāgena daivatāni niveśayat  BhN padmopaviṣṭaṃ brahmāṇaṃ tasya madhye niveśayet ādau niveśyo bhagavānsārdhaṃ bhūtagaṇaiḥ śivaḥ  BhN nārāyaṇo mahendraśca skandaḥ sūryo śvinau śaśī sarasvatī ca lakṣmīśca śraddhā medhā ca pūrvataḥ  BhN pūrvadakṣiṇato vahnirniveśyaḥ svāhayā saha viśvedevāḥ sagandharvā rudrāḥ sarpagaṇāstathā  BhN dakṣiṇena niveśyastu yamo mitraśca sānugaḥ pitṝnpiśācānuragān guhyakāṃśca niveśayat  BhN naiṝtyāṃ rākṣasāṃścaiva bhūtāni ca niveśayat paścimāyāṃ samudrāṃśca varuṇaṃ yādasāṃ patim  BhN vāyavyāyāṃ diśi tathā sapta vāyūnniveśayet tatraiva viniveśyastu garuḍaḥ pakṣibhiḥ saha  BhN uttarasyāṃ diśi tathā dhanadaṃ saṃnivieśayet nāṭyasya mātṝśca tathā yakṣānatha saguhyakān  BhN tathaivottarapūrvāyāṃ nandyādyāṃśca gaṇeśvarān brahmarṣibhūtasaṃghāṃśca yathābhāgaṃ niveśayat  BhN stambhe sanatkumāraṃ tu dakṣiṇe dakṣameva ca grāmaṇyamuttare stambhe pūjārthaṃ saṃniviśayet  BhN anenaiava vidhānena yathāsthānaṃ yathāvidhi suprasādāni sarvāṇi daivatāni niveśayat  BhN sthāne sthāne yathānyāyaṃ viniveśya tu devatāḥ tāsāṃ prakurvīta tataḥ pūjanaṃ tu yathārhataḥ  BhN devatābhyastu dātavyaṃ sitamālyānulepanam gandharvavahnisūryobhyo raktamālyānulepanam  BhN gandhaṃ mālyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ datvā tataḥ prakurvīta baliṃ pūjāṃ yathāvidhiḥ  BhN brahmāṇaṃ madukarpeṇa pāyasena sarasvatīm śivaviṣṇumahendrādyāḥ sampūjyā modakairatha  BhN ghṛtaudanena hutabhukṣomarkau tu guḍaudanaiḥ viśvedevāḥ sagandharvā munayo madhupāyasaiḥ  BhN yamamitrau ca sampūjyāvapūpairmodakaistathā pitṝnpiśācānuragān sarpiḥkṣīreṇa tarpayet  BhN pakvānena tu māṃsena surāsīthuphalāsavaiḥ arcayedbhūtasaṃghāṃśca caṇakaiḥ palalāplutaiḥ  BhN anenaiva vidhānena sampūjyā mattavāraṇī pakvāmena tu māṃsena sampūjyā rakṣasāṃ gaṇāḥ  BhN surāmāṃsapradāneana dānavānpratipūjayet śeṣāndevagaṇāṃstajjñaḥ sāpūpotkārikaudanaiḥ  BhN matsyaiśca piṣṭabhakṣyaiśca sāgarānsaritastathā sampūjya varuṇaṃ cāpi dātavyaṃ ghṛtapāyasam  BhN nānāphūlaphalaścāpi munīnsampratipūjayet vāyūṃśca pakṣiṇaścaiva vicitrairbhakṣyabhojanaiḥ  BhN mātṝrnāṭyasya sarvāstā dhanadaṃ ca sahānugaiḥ apūpairlājikāmiśrairbhakṣyabhojyaiśca pūjayet  BhN evameṣāṃ baliḥ kāryo nānābhojanasaṃśrayaḥ punarmantravidhānena balikarma ca vakṣyate  BhN devadeva mahābhāga sarvalokapitāmaha mantrapūtamimaṃ sarvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva me balim  BhN devadeva mahābhāga gaṇeśa tripurāntaka pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayodyataḥ  BhN nārāyaṇāmitagate padmanābha surottama pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayārpitaḥ  BhN purandarāmarapate vajrapāṇe śatakrato pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva vidhimantrapuraskṛtaḥ  BhN devasenāpate skanda bhagavan śaṅkarapriya baliḥ prītena manasā ṣaṇmukha pratigṛhyatām  BhN mahādeva mahāyogindevadeva surottama saṃpragṛhya baliṃ deva rakṣa vighnātsadotthitāt  BhN devi devamahābhāge sarasvati haripriye pragṛhyatāṃ balirmātarmayā bhaktyā samarpitaḥ  BhN nānānimittasambhūtāḥ paulastyāḥ sarva eva turākṣasendrā mahāsatvāḥ pratigṛhṇīta me balim  BhN lakṣmīḥ siddhirmatirmedhā sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ mantrapūtamimaṃ devyaḥ pratigṛhṇantu me balim  BhN sarvabhūtānubhāvajña lokajīvana māruta pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayodyataḥ  BhN devavaktra suraśreṣṭha dhūmaketo hutāśana bhaktyā samudyato deva baliḥ samprati gṛhyatām  BhN sarvagrahāṇāṃ pravara tejorāśe divākara bhaktyā mayodyato deva baliḥ samprati gṛhyatām  BhN sarvagrahapate soma dvijarāja jagatpriya pragṛhyatāmeṣa balirmantrapūto mayodyataḥ  BhN mahāgaṇeśvarāḥ sarve nandīśvarapurogamāḥ pragṛtāṃ balirbhaktyā mayā samprati coditaḥ  BhN namaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pratigṛhṇantvimaṃ balim bhūtebhyaśca namo nityaṃ yeṣāmeṣa baliḥ priyaḥ kāmapāla namo nityaṃ yasyāyaṃ te vidhiḥ kṛtaḥ  BhN nāradastumbaruścaiva viśvāvasupurogamāḥ parigṛhṇantu me sarve gandharvā balimudyatam  BhN yamo mitraśca bhagavānīśvarau lokapūjitau imaṃ me pratigṛhṇītāṃ baliḥ mantrapuraskṛtam  BhN rasātalagatebhyaśca pannagebhyo namo namaḥ diśantu siddhiṃ nāṭyasya pūjitāḥ pāpanāśanāḥ  BhN sarvāmbhasāṃ patirdevo varuṇo haṃsavāhanaḥ pūjitaḥ prītamānastu sasamudranadīnadaḥ  BhN vainateya mahāsatva sarvapakṣipate vibho pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayodyataḥ  BhN dhanādhyakṣo yakṣapatirlokapālo dhaneśvaraḥ saguhyakassayakṣaśca pratigṛhṇātu me balim  BhN namo stu nāṭyamātṛbhyo brāhmyādyābhyo namonamaḥ sumukhībhiḥ prasannābhirbaliradya pragṛhyatām  BhN rudrapraharaṇaṃ sarvaṃ pratigṛhṇātu me balim viṣṇupraharaṇaṃ caiva viṣṇubhaktyā mayodyatam  BhN tathā kṛtāntaḥ kālaśca sarvaprāṇivadheśvarau mṛtyuśca niyatiścaiva pratigṛhṇātu me balim  BhN yāścāsyāṃ mattavāraṇyāṃ saṃśritā vastudevatāḥ mantrapūtamimaṃ samyakpratigṛhṇantu me balim  BhN anye ye devagandharvā diśo daśa samāśritāḥ divyāntarikṣābhaumāśca tebhyaścāyaṃ baliḥ kṛtaḥ  BhN kumbhaṃ salilasampūrṇaṃ puṣpamālāpuraskṛtam sthāpayedraṅgamadhye tu suvarṇaṃ cātra dāpayet  BhN ātodyāni tu sarvāṇi kṛtvā vastrottarāṇi tu gandhairmālyaiśca dhūpaiśca bhakṣyairbhojyaiśca pūjayet  BhN pūjayitvā tu sarvāṇi daivatāni yathākramam jarjarastvabhisampūjyaḥ syāttato vighnajarjaraḥ  BhN śvetaṃ śirasi vastraṃ syānnīlaṃ raudre ca parvaṇi viṣṇuparvaṇi vai pītaṃ raktaṃ skandasya parvaṇi  BhN mṛḍaparvaṇi citraṃ tu deyaṃ vastraṃ hitārthinā sadṛśaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ dhūpamālyānulepanam  BhN ātodyāni tu sarvāṇi vāsobhiravaguṇṭhayet gandhairmālyaiśca dhūpaiśca bhakṣyabhojaiśca pūjayet  BhN sarvamevaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā gandhamālyānulepanaiḥ vighnajarjaraṇārthaṃ tu jarjaraṃ tvabhimantrayet  BhN atra vighnavināśārthaṃ pitāmahamukhaissuraiḥ nirmitastvaṃ mahāvīryo vajrasāro mahātanuḥ  BhN śiraste rakṣatu bramhā sarvairdevaguṇaiaḥ taha dvitīyaṃ ca haraḥ parva tṛtīyaṃ ca janārdanaḥ  BhN caturthaṃ ca kumāraste pañcamaṃ pannagottamaḥ nityaṃ sarve pi pāntu tvāṃ surārthe ca śivo bhava  BhN nakṣatre bhijiti tvaṃ hi prasūto hitasūdana jayaṃ cābhyudayaṃ caiva pārthivasya samāvaha  BhN jarjaraṃ pūjayitvaiavaṃ baliṃ sarvaṃ nividya ca agnau homaṃ tataḥ kuryānmantrāhuitipuraskṛtam  BhN hutāśa eva dīptābhirulkābhiḥ parimārjanam nṛpaternartakīnāṃ ca kuryāddīptyabhivardhanam  BhN abhidyotya sahātodyairnṛpatiṃ nartakīstathā mantrapūtena toyena punarabhyukṣya tānvadet  BhN mahākule prasūtāḥ stha guṇaughaiścāpyalaṅkṛtāḥ yadvo janmaguṇopetaṃ tadvo bhavatu nityaśaḥ  BhN evamuktvā tato vākyaṃ nṛpatairbhūtaye budhaḥ nāṭyayogaprasiddhyarthamāśiṣassamprayojayet  BhN sarasvatī dhṛtirmedhā hrīḥ śrīrlakṣmīssmṛtirmatiḥ pāntu vo mātaraḥ saumyāssiddhidāśca bhavantu vaḥ  BhN homaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ havirmantrapuraskṛtam bhindyātkumbhaṃ tataścaiva nāṭyācāryaḥ prayatnataḥ  BhN abhinne tu bhavetkumbhe svāminaḥ śatruto bhayam bhinne caiva tu vijñeyaḥ svāminaḥ śatrusaṃkṣayaḥ  BhN bhinne kumbhe tataścaiva nāṭyacāryaḥ prayatnataḥ pragṛhya dīpikāṃ dīptāṃ sarvaṃ raṅgaṃ pradīpayet  BhN kṣveḍitaiḥ sphoṭitaiścaiva valgitaiśca pradhāvitaiḥ raṅgamadhye tu tāṃ dīptāṃ saśabdāṃ samprayojayet  BhN śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣairmṛdaṅgapaṇavaistathā sarvātodyaiḥ praṇaditai raṅge yuddhāni kārayet  BhN tatra cchinnaṃ va bhinnaṃ ca dāritaṃ ca saśoṇitam kṣataṃ pradīptamāyastaṃ nimittaṃ siddhilakṣaṇam  BhN samyagiṣṭastu raṅgo vai svāminaḥ śubhamāvahet purasyābālavṛddhasya tathā jānapadasya ca  BhN duriṣṭastu tathā raṅgo daivatairduradhiṣṭhitaḥ nāṭyavidhvasanaṃ kuryānnṛpasya ca tathāśubham  BhN ya evaṃ vidhimutsṛjya yatheṣṭaṃ samprayojayet prāpnotyapacayaṃ śīghraṃ tiryagyoniṃ ca gacchati  BhN yajñena sammitaṃ hyetadraṅgadaivatapūjanam apūjayitvā raṅgaṃ tu naiva prekṣāṃ prayojayet  BhN pūjitāḥ pūjayantyete mānitā mānayanti ca tasmātsarvaprayatnena kartavyaṃ raṅgapūjanam  BhN na tathā pradahatyagniḥ prabhañjanasamīritaḥ yathā hyapaprayogastu prayukto dahati kṣaṇāt  BhN śāstrajñena vinītena śucinā dīkṣitena ca nāṭyācāryeṇa śāntena kartavyaṃ raṅgapūjanam  BhN sthānabhraṣṭaṃ tu yo dadyādbalimudvignamānasaḥ mantrahīno yathā hotā prāyaścittī bhavettu saḥ  BhN ityayaṃ yo vidhirdṛṣṭo raṅgadaivatapūjane nave nāṭyagṛhe kāryaḥ prekṣāyāṃ ca prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre raṅgadaivatapūjanaṃ nāma tṛtīyo dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥatha caturtho dhyāyaḥevaṃ tu pūjanaṃ kṛtvā mayā proktaḥ pitāmahaḥ ājñāpaya prabho kṣipraṃ kaḥ prayogaḥ prayujyatām  BhN tato smyukto bhagavatā yojayāmṛtamanthanam etadutsāhajananaṃ suraprītikaraṃ tathā  BhN yo yaṃ samavakārastu dharmakāmārthasādhakaḥ mayā prāggrathito vidvansa prayogaḥ prayujyatām  BhN tasminsamavakāre tu prayukte devadānavāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ samabhavansarve karmabhāvānudarśanāt  BhN kasyacitvatha kālasya māmāhāmbujasambhavaḥnāṭyaṃ sandarśayāmo dya trinetrāya mahātmane  BhN tataḥ sārdhaṃ surairgatvā vṛṣabhāṅkaniveśanam samabhyarcya śivaṃ paścāduvācedaṃ pitāmahaḥ  BhN mayā samavākarastu yo yaṃ sṛṣṭaḥ surottama śravaṇe darśane cāsya prasādaṃ kartumarhasi  BhN paśyāma iti deveśo druhiṇaṃ vākyamabravīt tato māmāha bhagavān sajjo bhava mahāmate  BhN tato himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe nānānāgasamākule bahubhūtagaṇākīrṇe ramyakandaranirzhare  BhN pūrvaraṅgaḥ kṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ tatrāyaṃ dvijasattamāḥ tathā tripuradāhaśca ḍimasaṃjñaḥ prayojitaḥ  BhN tato bhūtagaṇā hṛṣṭāḥ karnabhāvānukīrtanāt mahādevaśca suprītaḥ pitāmahamathābravīt  BhN aho nāṭyamidaṃ samyak tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ mahāmate yaśasyaṃ ca śubhārthaṃ ca puṇyaṃ buddhivivardhanam  BhN mayāpīdaṃ smṛtaṃ nṛtyaṃ sandhyākāleṣu nṛtyatā nānākaraṇasaṃyuktairaṅgahārairvibhūṣitam  BhN pūrvaraṅgavidhāvasmiṃstvayā samyakprayojyatām vardhamānakayogeṣu gīteṣvāsāriteṣu ca  BhN mahāgīteṣu caivārthānsamyagevābhineṣyasi yaścāyaṃ pūrvaraṅgastu tvayā śuddhaḥ prayojitaḥ  BhN ebhirvimiśritaścāyaṃ citro nāma bhaviṣyati śrutvā maheśvaravacaḥ pratyuktastu svayaṃbhuvā  BhN prayogamaṅgahārāṇāmācakṣva surasattama tatastaṇḍuṃ samāhūya proktavān bhuvaneśvaraḥ  BhN prayogamaṅgahārāṇāmācakṣva bharatāya vai tato ye taṇḍunā proktāstvaṅgahārā mahātmanā  BhN tānvaḥ karaṇasaṃyuktānvyākhyāsyāmi sarecakān sthirahasto ṅgahārastu tathā paryastakaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN sūcividdhastathā caiva hyapaviddhastathaiva ca ākṣiptako tha vijñeyastathā coddhaṭṭitaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN viṣkambhaścaiva samproktastathā caivāparājitaḥ viṣkambhāpasṛtaścaiava mattākrīḍastathaiva ca  BhN svastiko recitaścaiva pārśvasvastika eva ca vṛścikāpasṛtaḥ prokto bhramaraśca tathāparaḥ  BhN mattaskhalitakaścaiva madādvilasitastathā gatimaṇḍalako jñeyaḥ paricchinnastathaiva ca  BhN parivṛttacito tha syāttathā vaiśākharecitaḥ parāvṛtto tha vijñeyastathā caivāpyalātakaḥ  BhN pārśvacchedo tha samprokto vidyudbhrāntastathaiva ca ūrūdvṛttastathā caiva syādālīḍhastathaiva ca  BhN recitaścāpi vijñeyastathaivācchuritaḥ smṛtaḥ ākṣiptarecitaścaiva sambhrāntaśca tathāparaḥ  BhN apasarpastu vijñeyastathā cārdhanikuṭṭakaḥ dvātriṃśadete samproktā aṅgahārāstu nāmataḥ  BhN eteṣāṃ tu pravakṣyāmi prayogaṃ karaṇāśrayam hastapādapracāraśca yathā yojyaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN aṅgahāreṣu vakṣyāmi karaṇeṣu ca vai dvijāḥ sarveṣāmaṅgahārāṇāṃ niṣpattiḥ karaṇairyataḥ  BhN tānyataḥ sampravakṣyāmi nāmataḥ karmatastathā hastapādasamāyogo nṛtyasya karaṇaṃ bhavet  BhN dve nṛttakaraṇe caiva bhavato nṛttamātṛkā dvābhyāṃ tribhiścaturbhirvāpyaṅgahārastu mātṛbhiḥ  BhN tribhiḥ kalāpakaṃ caiva caturbhiḥ ṣaṇḍakaṃ bhavet pañcaiva karaṇāni syuḥ saṅghātaka iti smṛtaḥ  BhN ṣaḍbhirvā saptabhirvāpi aṣṭabhirnavabhistathā karaṇairiha saṃyuktā aṅgahārāḥ prakīrtāḥ  BhN eteṣāmeva vakṣyāmi hastapādavikalpanam talapuṣpapuṭaṃ pūrvaṃ vartitaṃ valitoru ca  BhN apaviddhaṃ samanakhaṃ līnaṃ svastikarecitam maṇḍalasvastikaṃ caiva nikuṭṭakamathāpi ca  BhN tathaivārdhanikuṭṭaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ardharecitakaṃ caiva vakṣaḥsvastikameva ca  BhN unmattaṃ svastikaṃ caiva pṛṣṭhasvastikameva ca dikṣvastikamalātaṃ ca tathaiva ca kaṭīsamam  BhN ākṣiptarecitaṃ caiva vikṣiptākṣiptakaṃ tathā ardhasvastikamuddiṣṭamañcitaṃ ca tathāparam  BhN bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ proktamūrdhvajānu tathaiva ca nikuñcitaṃ ca mattalli tvardhamattalli caiva hi  BhN syādrecakanikkuṭṭaṃ ca tathā pādāpaviddhakam valitaṃ ghūrṇitaṃ caiva lalitaṃ ca tathāparam  BhN daṇḍapakṣaṃ tathā caiva bhujaṅgatrastarecitam nūpuraṃ caiva samproktaṃ tathā vaiśākharecitam  BhN bhramaraṃ caturaṃ caiva bhujaṅgāñcitameva ca daṇḍarecitakaṃ caiva tathā vṛścikakuṭṭitam  BhN kaṭibhrāntaṃ tathā caiva latāvṛścikameva ca chinnaṃ ca karaṇaṃ proktaṃ tathā vṛścikarecitam  BhN vṛścikaṃ vyaṃsitaṃ caiva tathā pārśvanikuṭṭakam lalāṭatilakaṃ krāntaṃ kuñcitaṃ cakramaṇḍalam  BhN uromaṇḍalamākṣiptaṃ tathā talavilāsitam argalaṃ cātha vikṣiptamāvṛttaṃ dolapādakam  BhN vivṛttaṃ vinivṛttaṃ ca pārśvakrāntaṃ niśumbhitam vidyutbhrāntamatikrāntaṃ vivartitakameva ca  BhN gajakrīḍitakaṃ caiva talasaṃsphoṭitaṃ tathā garuḍaplutakaṃ caiva gaṇḍasūci tathāparam  BhN parivṛttaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ pārśvajānu tathaiva ca gṛdhrāvalīnakaṃ caiva sannataṃ sūcyathāpi ca  BhN ardhasūcīti karaṇaṃ sūcividdhaṃ tathaiva ca apakrāntaṃ ca samproktaṃ mayūralalitaṃ tathā  BhN sarpitaṃ daṇḍapādaṃ ca hariṇaplutameva ca preṅkholitaṃ nitambaṃ ca skhalitaṃ karihastakam  BhN prasarpitakamuddiṣṭaṃ siṃhavikrīḍataṃ tathā siṃhākarṣitamudvṛttaṃ tathopasṛtameva ca  BhN talasaṃghaṭṭitaṃ caiva janitaṃ cāvahitthakam niveśamelakākrīḍamūrūdvṛttaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN madaskhalitakaṃ caiva viṣṇukrāntamathāpi ca sambhrāntamatha viṣkambhamudghaṭṭitamathāpi ca  BhN vṛṣabhakrīḍitaṃ caiva lolitaṃ ca tathāparam nāgāpasarpitaṃ caiva śakaṭāsyaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN gaṅgāvataraṇaṃ caivetyuktamaṣṭādhikaṃ śatam aṣṭottaraśataṃ hyetatkaraṇānāṃ mayoditam  BhN nṛtye yuddhe niyuddhe ca tatha gatiparikrame gatipracāre vakṣyāmi
