tūddhaṭṭite sadā paryāyodveṣṭitau hastau pādau caiva nikuṭṭitau  BhN kuñcitāvañcitaua caiva hyūrūdvṛttaṃ tathaiva ca caturaśraṃ karaṃ kṛtvā pādena ca nikuṭṭakam  BhN bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ caiva karaṃ codviṣṭitaṃ punaḥ paricchinnaṃ ca kartavyaṃ trikaṃ bhramarakeṇa tu  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ viṣkambhe parikīrtitam daṇḍapādaṃ karaṃ caiva vikṣipyākṣipya caiva hi  BhN vyaṃsitaṃ vāmahastaṃ ca saha pādena sarpayet nikuṭṭakadvayaṃ kāryamākṣiptaṃ maṇḍalorasi  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kartavyamaparājite kuṭṭitaṃ karaṇaṃ kṛtvā bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā  BhN recitena tu hastena patākaṃ hastamādiśet ākṣiptakaṃ prayuñjīta hyuromaṇḍalakaṃ tathā  BhN latākhyaṃ sakaṭakacchinnaṃ viṣkambhāpasṛte bhavet trikaṃ suvalitaṃ kṛtvā nūpuraṃ karaṇaṃ tathā  BhN bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ savyaṃ tathā vaiśākharecitam ākṣiptakaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā paricchinnaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN bāhyabhramarakaṃ kuryāduromaṇḍalameva ca nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN mattākrīḍo bhavedeṣa hyaṅgahāro harapriyaḥ recitaṃ hastapādaṃ ca kṛtvā vṛścikameva ca  BhN punastenaiva yogena vṛścikaṃ samprayojayet nikuṭṭakaṃ tathā caiva savyāsavyakṛtaṃ kramāt  BhN latākhyaḥ sakaṭicchedo bhavetsvastikarecite pārśve tu svastikaṃ baddhvā kāryaṃ tvatha nikuṭṭakam  BhN dvitīyasya ca pārśvasya vidhiḥ syādyameva hi tataśca karamāvartya hyūrūpṛṣṭhe nipātayet  BhN ūrūdvṛttaṃ tataḥ kuryādākṣiptaṃ punareva hi nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN pārśvasvastika ityeṣa hyaṅgahāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ vṛścikaṃ karaṇaṃ kṛtvā latākhyaṃ hastameva ca  BhN tameva ca karaṃ bhūyo nāsāgre sannikuñcayet tamevodveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā nitambaṃ parivartayet  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ vṛścikāpasṛte bhavet kṛtvā nūpurapādaṃ tu tathākṣiptakameva ca  BhN paricchinnaṃ ca kartavyaṃ sūcīpādaṃ tathaiva ca nitambaṃ karihastaṃ cāpyuromaṇḍalakaṃ tathā  BhN kaṭīcchinnaṃ tataścaiva bhramaraḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ matallikaraṇaṃ kṛtvā karamāvartya dakṣiṇam  BhN kapolasya pradeśe tu kāryaṃ samyaṅnikuñcitamapaviddhaṃ drutaṃ caiva talasaṃsphoṭasaṃyutam  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ mattaskhalitake bhavet dolaiḥ karaiḥ pracalitaiḥ svastikāpasṛtaiḥ padaiḥ  BhN añcitairvalitairhastaistalasaṅghaṭṭitaistathā nikuṭṭitaṃ ca kartavyamūrūdvṛtaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ madādvilasite bhavet maṇḍalaṃ sthānakaṃ kṛtvā tathā hastau ca recitau  BhN udghaṭṭitena pādena mattallikaraṇaṃ bhavet ākṣiptaṃ karaṇaṃ caiva hyuromaṇḍalameva ca  BhN kaṭicchinnaṃ tathā caiva bhavettu gatimaṇḍale samapādaṃ prayujyātha paricchinnaṃ tvanantaram  BhN āviddhena tu pādena bāhyabhramarakaṃ tathā vāmasūcyā tvatikrāntaṃ bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ paricchinne vidhīyate śirasastūpari sthāpyau svastiakau vicyutau karau  BhN tataḥ savyaṃ karaṃ cāpi gātramānamya recayet punarutthāpayettatra gātramunnamya recitam  BhN latākhyau ca karau kṛtvā vṛścikaṃ samprayojayet recitaṃ karihastaṃ ca bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā  BhN ākṣiptakaṃ prayuñjīta svastikaṃ pādameva ca parāṅgmukhavidhirbhūya evameva bhavediha  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ parivṛttakarecitee recitau saha gātreṇa hyapaviddhau karau yadā  BhN punastenaiva deśena gātramunnamya recayet kuryānnūpurapādaṃ ca bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā  BhN recitaṃ maṇḍalaṃ caiva bāhuśīrṣe nikuñcayet ūrūdvṛttaṃ tathākṣiptamuromaṇḍalameva ca  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kuryādvaiśākharecite ādyaṃ tu janitaṃ kṛtvā pādamekaṃ prasārayet  BhN tathaivālātakaṃ kuryāt trikaṃ tu parivartayet añcitaṃ vāmahastaṃ ca gaṇḍadeśe nikuṭṭayet  BhN kaṭicchinnaṃ tathā caiva parāvṛtte prayojayet svastikaṃ karaṇaṃ kṛtvā vyaṃsitau ca karau punaḥ  BhN alātakaṃ prayuñjīta hyūrdhvajānu nikuñcitam ardhasūcī ca vikṣiptamudvṛttākṣiptake tathā  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnamaṅgahāre hyalātake nikuṭya vakṣasi karāvūrdhvajānu prayojayet  BhN ākṣiptasvastikaṃ kṛtvā trikaṃ tu parivartayet uromaṇḍalakau hastau nitambaṃ karihastakam  BhN kaṭicchinnaṃ tathā caiva pārśvacchede vidhīyate sūcīvāmapadaṃ dadhyādvidyudbhrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam  BhN dakṣiṇena punaḥ sūcī vidyudbhrāntaṃ ca vāmataḥ paricchinnaṃ tathā caiva hyatikrāntaṃ ca vāmakam  BhN latākhyaṃ sakaṭicchinnaṃ vidyudbhrāntaśca sa smṛtaḥ kṛtvā nūpurapādaṃ tu savyavāmau pralambitau  BhN karau pārśve tatastābhyāṃ vikṣiptaṃ samprayojayet tābhyāṃ sūcī tathā caiva trikaṃ tu parivartayet  BhN latākhyaṃ sakaṭicchinnaṃ kurtādudvṛttake sadā ālīḍhavyaṃsitau hastau bāhuśīrṣe nikuṭṭayet  BhN nūpuraścaraṇo vāmastathālātaśca dakṣiṇaḥ tenaivākṣiptakaṃ kuryāduromaṇḍalakau karau  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnamālīḍhe samprayojayet hastaṃ tu recitaṃ kṛtvā pārśvamānasya recayet  BhN punastenaiva yogena gātramānasya recayet recitaṃ karaṇaṃ kāryamuromaṇḍalameva ca  BhN kaṭicchinnaṃ tu kartavyamaṅgahāre tu recite nūpuraṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā trikaṃ tu parivartayet  BhN vyaṃsitena tu hastena trikameva vivartayet vāmaṃ cālātakaṃ kṛtvā sūcīmatraiva yojayet  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kuryādācchurite sadā recitau svastikau pādau recitau svastikau karau  BhN kṛtvā viśleṣamevaṃ tu tenaiva vidhinā punaḥ punarutkṣepaṇaṃ caiva recitaireva kārayet  BhN udvṛttākṣiptake caiva hyuromaṇḍalameva ca nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN ākṣiptarecito hyeṣa karaṇānāṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ vikṣipta karaṇaṃ kṛtvā hastapādaṃ mukhāgamam  BhN vāmasūcisahakṛtaṃ vikṣipedvāmakaṃ karam vakṣaḥsthāne bhavetsavyo valitaṃ trikameva ca  BhN nūpurākṣiptake caiva hyardhasvastikameva ca nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca hyuromaṇḍalakaṃ tathā  BhN kaṭicchinnaṃ ca kartavyaṃ sambhrānte nṛttayoktṛbhiḥ apakrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā vyaṃsitaṃ hastameva ca  BhN kuryādudveṣṭitaṃ caiva hyardhasūcīṃ tathaiva ca vikṣiptaṃ sakaṭicchinnamudvṛttākṣiptake tathā  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kartavyamapasarpite kṛtvā nūpurapādaṃ ca drutamākṣipya ca kramam  BhN pādasya cānugau hastau trikaṃ ca parivartayet nikuṭya karapādaṃ cāpyuromaṇḍalakaṃ punaḥ  BhN karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kāryamardhanikuṭṭake dvātriṃśadete samproktā hyaṅgahārā dvijottamāḥ  BhN caturo recakāṃścāpi gadato me nibodhata pādarecaka ekaḥ syāt dvitīyaḥ kaṭirecakaḥ  BhN kararecakastṛtīyastu caturthaḥ kaṇṭharecakaḥ recitākhyaḥ pṛthagbhāve valane cābhidhīyate udvāhanātpṛthagbhāvāccalanāccāpi recakaḥ  BhNab pārśvātpārśve tu gamanaṃ skhalitaiścalitaiḥ padaiḥ vividhaiścaiva pādasya pādarecaka ucyate  BhNab trikasyodvartanaṃ caiva chaṭīvalanameva ca tathāpasarpaṇaṃ caiva kaṭirecaka ucyate  BhNab udvartanaṃ parikṣepo vikṣepaḥ parivartanam visarpaṇaṃ ca hastasya hastarecaka ucyate  BhNab udvāhanaṃ sannamanaṃ tathā pārśvasya sannatiḥ bhramaṇaṃ cāpi vijñeyo grīvāyā recako budhaiḥ  BhNab recakairaṅgahāraiśca nṛtyantaṃ vīkṣya śaṅkaram  BhN sukumāraprayogeṇa nṛtyantīṃ caiva pārvatīm mṛdañgabherīpaṭahairbhāṇḍaḍiṇḍimagomukhaiḥ  BhN paṇavairdaduraiścaiva sarvātodyaiḥ pravāditaiḥ dakṣayajñe vinihate sandhyākāle maheśvaraḥ  BhN nānāṅgahāraiḥ prānṛtyallayatālavaśānugaiaḥ piṇḍibandhāṃstato dṛṣṭvā nandibhadramukhā gaṇāḥ  BhN cakruste nāma piṇḍīnāṃ bandhamāsāṃ salakṣaṇam īśvarasyeśvarī pinḍī nandinaścāpi paṭṭasī  BhN caṇḍikāyā bhavetpiṇḍī tathā vai siṃhavāhinī tārkṣyapiṇḍī bhavedviṣṇoḥ padmapiṇḍī svayaṃbhuvaḥ  BhN śakrasyairāvatī piṇḍī jhaṣapiṇḍī tu mānmathī śikhipiṇḍī kumārasya rūpapiṇḍī bhavecchriyaḥ  BhN dhārāpiṇḍī ca jāhnavyāḥ pāśapiṇḍī yamasya ca vāruṇī ca nadīpiṇḍī yākṣī syāddhanadasya tu  BhN halapiṇḍī balasyāpi sarpapiṇḍī tu bhoginām gāṇeśvarī mahāpiṇḍī dakṣayajñavimardinī  BhN triśūlākṛtisaṃsthānā raudrī syādandhakadviṣaḥ evamanyāsvapi tathā devatāsu yathākramam  BhN dhvajabhūtāḥ prayoktavyāḥ piṇḍībandhāḥ sucihnitāḥ recakā aṅgahārāśca piṇḍībandhātasthaiva ca  BhN sṛṣṭvā bhagavatā dattāstaṇḍave munaye tadā tenāpi hi tataḥ samyaggānabhāṇḍasamanvitaḥ  BhN nṛttaprayogaḥ sṛṣṭo yaḥ sa tāṇḍava iti smṛtaḥ ṛṣaya ūcuḥ yadā prāptyarthamarthānāṃ tajjñairabhinayaḥ kṛtaḥ  BhN kasmānṛttaṃ kṛtaṃ hyetatkaṃ svabhāvamapekṣate na gītakārthasambaddhaṃ na cāpyarthasya bhāvakam  BhN kasmānnṛttaṃ kṛtaṃ hyetadgīteṣvāsāriteṣu ca bharataḥ atrocyate na khalvarthaṃ kañcinnṛttamapekṣate  BhN kiṃ tu śobhāṃ prajanayediti nṛttaṃ pravartitam prāyeṇa sarvalokasya nṛttamiṣṭaṃ svabhāvataḥ  BhN maṅgalamiti kṛtvā ca nṛttametatprakīrtitam vivāhaprasavāvāhapramodābhyuadayādiṣu  BhN vinodakāraṇaṃ ceti nṛttametatpravartitam ataścaiva pratikṣepādbhūtasaṅghaiḥ pravartitāḥ  BhN ye gītakādau yujyante samyaṅnṛttavibhāgakāḥ devena cāpi samproktastaṇḍustāṇḍavapūrvakam  BhN gītaprayogamāśritya nṛttametatpravartyatām prāyeṇa tāṇḍavavidhirdevastutyāśrayo bhavet  BhN sukumāraprayogaśca śṛṅgārarasasambhavaḥ tasya taṇḍuprayuktasya tāṇḍavasya vidhikriyām  BhN vardhamānakamāsādya sampravakṣyami lakṣaṇam kalānāṃ vṛddhimāsādya hyakṣarāṇāṃ ca vardhanāt  BhN layasya vardhanāccāpi vardhamānakamucyate kṛttvā kutapavinyāsaṃ yathāvaddvijasattamāḥ  BhN āsāritaprayogastu tataḥ kāryaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ tatra tūpohanaṃ kṛttvā tantrīgānasamanvitam  BhN kāryaḥ praveśo nartakyā bhāṇḍavādyasamanvitaḥ viśuddhakaraṇāyāṃ tu jātyāṃ vādyaṃ prayojayet  BhN gatyā vādyānusāriṇyā tasyāścārīṃ prayojayet vaiśākhasthānakeneha sarvarecakacāriṇī  BhN puṣpāñjalidharā bhūtvā praviśedraṅgamaṇḍapam puṣpāñjaliṃ visṛjyātha raṅgapīṭhaṃ parītya ca  BhN praṇamya devatābhyaśca tato bhinayamācaret yatrābhineyaṃ gītaṃ syāttatra vādyaṃ na yojayet  BhN aṅgahāraprayoge tu bhāṇḍavādyaṃ vidhīyate samaṃ raktaṃ vibhaktaṃ ca sphuṭaṃ śuddhaprahārajam  BhN nṛttāṅgagrāhi vādyajñairvādyaṃ yojyaṃ tu tāṇḍave prayujya gītavādye tu niṣkrāmennartakī tataḥ  BhN anenaiva vidhānena praviśantyaparāḥ pṛthak anyāścānukrameṇātha piṇḍīṃ badhnanti yāḥ striyaḥ  BhN tāvatparyastakaḥ kāryo yāvatpiṇḍī na badhyate piṇḍīṃ baddhvā tataḥ sarvā niṣkrāmeyuḥ striyastu tāḥ  BhN piṇḍībandheṣu vādyaṃ tu kartavyamiha vādakaiaḥ paryastakapramāṇena citraughakaraṇānvitam  BhN tatropavāhanaṃ bhūyaḥ kāryaṃ pūrvavadeva hi tataścāsāritaṃ bhūyo gāyanaṃ tu prayojayet  BhN pūrveṇaiva vidhānena praviśeccāpi nartakī gītakārthaṃ tvabhinayed dvitīyāsāritasya tu  BhN tadeva ca punarvastu nṛttenāpi pradarśayet āsārite samāpte tu niṣkrāmennartakī tataḥ  BhN pūrvavatpraviśantyanyāḥ prayogaḥ syātsa eva hi evaṃ pade pade kāryo vidhirāsāritasya tu  BhN bhāṇḍavādyakṛte caiva tathā gānakṛte pi ca ekā tu prathamaṃ yojyā dve dvitīyaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN tisro vastu tṛtīyaṃ tu catasrastu caturthakam piṇḍīnāṃ vidhayaścaiva catvāraḥ samprakīrtitāḥ  BhN piṇḍī śṛṅkhalikā caiva latābandho tha bhedyakaḥ piṇḍībandhastu piṇḍatvādgulmaḥ śṛṅkhalikā bhavet  BhN jālopanaddhā ca latā sanṛtto bhedyakaḥ smṛtaḥ piṇḍībandhaḥ kaniṣṭhe tu śṛṅkhalā tu layāntare  BhN madhyame ca latābandho jyeṣṭhe caivātha bhedyakaḥ piṇḍīnāṃ vividhā yoniryantraṃ bhadrāsanaṃ tathā  BhN śikṣāyogastathā caiva prayoktavyaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ evaṃ prayogaḥ kartavyo vardhamāne tapodhanāḥ  BhN gītānāṃ chandakānāṃ ca bhūyo vakṣyāmyahaṃ vidhim yāni vastunibaddhāni yāni cāṅgikṛtāni tu  BhN gītāni teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi prayogaṃ nṛttavādyayoḥ tatrāvataraṇaṃ kāryaṃ nartakyāḥ sārvabhāṇḍikam  BhN kṣepapratikṣepakṛtaṃ bhāṇḍopohanasaṃskṛtam prathamaṃ tvabhineyaṃ syadgītake sarvavastukam  BhN tadeva ca punarvastu nṛtteenāpi pradarśeyat yo vidhiḥ pūrvamuktastu nṛttābhinayavādite  BhN āsāritavidhau sa syādgītānāṃ vastukeṣvapi evaṃ vastunibandhānāṃ gītakānāṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN śṛṇutāṅganibaddhānāṃ gītānāmapi lakṣaṇam ya eva vastukavidhirnṛttābhinayavādite  BhN tamevāṅganibaddheṣu cchandakeṣvapi yojayet vādyaṃ gurvakṣarakṛtaṃ tathālpākṣarameva ca  BhN mukhe sopohane kuryādvarṇānāṃ viprakarṣataḥ yadā gītivaśādaṅgaṃ bhūyo bhūyo nivartate  BhN tatrādyamabhineyaṃ syāccheṣaṃ nṛttena yojayet yadā gītivaśādaṅgaṃ bhūyo bhūyo nivartate  BhN tripāṇilayasaṃyuktaṃ tatra vādyaṃ prayojayet yathā layastathā vādyaṃ kartavyamiha vādakaiḥ  BhN tataṃ cānugataṃ cāpi oghaṃ ca karaṇānvitam sthire tattvaṃ prayoktavyaṃ madhye cānugataṃ bhavet  BhN bhūyaścaughaḥ prayoktavyastveṣa vādyagato vidhiḥ chandogītakamāsādya tvaṅgāni parivartayet  BhN eṣa kāryo vidhirnityaṃ nṛttābhinayavādite yāni vastunibaddhāni teṣāmante graho bhavet aṅgānāṃ tu parāvṛttāvādāveva graho mataḥ  BhN evameṣa vidhiḥ kāryo gīteṣvāsāriteṣvapi devastutyāśrayaṃ hyetatsukumāraṃ nibodhata  BhN strīpuṃsayostu saṃlāpo yastu kāmasamudbhavaḥ tajjñeyaṃ sukumāraṃ hi śṛṅgārarasasambhavam  BhN yasyāṃ yasyāmavasthāyāṃ nṛttaṃ yojyaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ tatsarvaṃṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tacca me śṛṇuta dvijāḥ  BhN aṅgavastunivṛttau tu tathā varṇanivṛttiṣu tathā cābhudayasthāne nṛttaṃ tajjñaḥ prayojayet  BhN yattu saṃdṛśyate kiñciddampatyormadanāśrayam nṛttaṃ tatra prayoktavyaṃ praharṣārthaguṇodbhavam  BhN yatra sannihite kānte ṛtukālādidarśanam gītakārthābhisaṃbaddhaṃ nṛttaṃ tatrāpi ceṣyate  BhN khaṇḍiatā vipralabdhā vā kalahāntaritāpi vā yasminnaṅge tu yuvatirna nṛttaṃ tatra na yojayet  BhN sakhīpravṛtte saṃlāpe tathāsannihite priye na hi nṛttaṃ prayoktavyaṃ yasyā na proṣitaḥ priyaḥ  BhN dūtyāśrayaṃ yadā tu syādṛtukālādi darśanam autsukyacintāsaṃbaddhaṃ na nṛttaṃ tatra yojayet  BhN yasminnaṅge prasādaṃ tu gṛhnīyānnāyikā kramāt tataḥprabhṛti nṛttaṃ tu śeṣeṣvaṅgeṣu yojayet  BhN devastutyāśrayakṛtaṃ yadaṅgaṃ tu bhavedatha māheśvarairaṅgahārairuddhataistatprayojayet  BhN yattu śṛṅgārasaṃbaddhaṃ gānaṃ strīpuruṣāśrayam devīkṛtairaṅgahārairlalitaistatprayojayet  BhN catuṣpadā narkuṭake khañjake parigītake vidhānaṃ sampravakṣyāmi bhāṇḍavādyavidhiṃ prati  BhN khañjanarkuṭasaṃyuktā bhasvedyā tu catuṣpadā pādānte sannipāte tu tasyā bhāṇḍagraho bhavet  BhN yā dhruvā chandasā yaktā samapādā samākṣarā tasyāḥ pādāvasāne tu pradeśinyā graho bhavet  BhN kṛtvaikaṃ parivartaṃ tu gānasyābhinayasya ca punaḥ pādanivṛttiṃ tu bhāṇḍavādyena yojayet  BhN aṅgavastunivṛtau tu varṇāntaranivṛttiṣu tathopasthāpane caiva bhāṇḍavādyaṃ prayojayet  BhN ye pi cāntaramārgāssyuḥ tantrivākkaraṇaiḥ kṛtāḥ teṣu sūcī prayoktavyā bhāṇḍena saha tāṇḍave  BhN maheśvarasya caritaṃ ya idaṃ samprayojayetsarvapāpaviśuddhātmā śivalokaṃ sa gacchati  BhN evameṣa vidhiḥ sṛrdṛṣṭastāṇḍavasya prayogataḥ bhūyaḥ kiṃ kathyatāmanyannāṭyavedavidhiṃ prati  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre tāṇḍavalakṣaṇaṃ nāma caturtho dhyāyaḥatha pūrvaraṅgavidhāno nāma pañcamo dhyāyaḥbharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā nāṭyasantānakāraṇam punarevābruvanvākyamṛṣayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ  BhN yathā nāṭyasya janmedaṃ jarjarasya ca sambhavaḥ vighnānāṃ śamanaṃ caiva daivatānāṃ ca pūjanam  BhN tadasmābhiḥ śrutaṃ sarvaṃ gṛhītvā cāvadhāritam nikhilena yathātattvamicchāmo vedituṃ punaḥ  BhN pūrvaraṅgaṃ mahātejaḥ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam yathā buddhyāmahe brahmaṃstathā vyākhyātumarhasi  BhN teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ pratyuvāca punarvākyaṃ pūrvaraṅgavidhiṃ prati  BhN pūrvaraṅgaṃ mahābhāgā gadato me nibodhata pādabhāgāḥ kalāścaiva parivartāstathaiva ca  BhN yasmādraṅge prayogo yaṃ pūrvameva prayujyate tasmādayaṃ pūrvaraṅgo vijñeyo dvijasattamāḥ  BhN asyāṅgāni tu kāryāṇi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ tantrībhāṇḍasamāyoagaiḥ pāṭhyayogakṛtaistathā  BhN pratyāhāro vataraṇaṃ tathā hyārambha eva ca āśrāvaṇā vaktrapāṇistathā ca parighaṭṭanā  BhN saṅghoṭanā tataḥ kāryā mārgāsāritameva ca jyeṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni tathaivāsāratāni ca  BhN etāni tu bahirgītānyantaryavanikāgataiḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ prayojyāni tantrībhāṇḍakṛtāni ca  BhN tataḥ sarvaistu kutapaiḥ saṃyuktānīha kārayet vighaṭya vai yavanikāṃ nṛttapāṭhyakṛtāni tu  BhN gītānāṃ madrakādīnāṃ yojyamekaṃ tu gītakam vardhamānamathāpīha tāṇḍavaṃ yatra yujyate  BhN tataścotthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ parivartanameva ca nāndī śuṣkāvakṛṣṭā ca raṅgadvāraṃ tathaiva ca  BhN cāri caiva tataḥ kāryā mahācārī tathaiva ca trikaṃ prarocanāṃ cāpi pūrvaraṅge bhavanti hi  BhN etānyaṅgāni kāryāṇi pūrvaraṅgavidhau dvijāḥ eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇamahaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN kutapasya tu vinyāsaḥ pratyāhāra iti smṛtaḥ tathāvataraṇaṃ proktaṃ gāyikānāṃ niveśanam  BhN parigītakriyārambha ārambha iti kīrtitaḥ ātodyarañjanārthaṃ tu bhavedāśrāvaṇāvidhiḥ  BhN vādyavṛttivibhāgārthaṃ vaktrapāṇirvidhīyate tantryojaḥkaraṇārthaṃ tu bhavecca parighaṭṭanā  BhN tathā pāṇivibhāgārthaṃ bhavetsaṃghoṭanāvidhiḥ tantrībhāṇḍasamāyogānmārgāsāritamiṣyate  BhN kalāpātavibhāgārthaṃ bhavedāsāritakriyā kīrtanāddevatānāṃ ca jñeyo gītavidhistathā  BhN ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyami hyutthāpanavidhikriyām  BhN yasmādutthāpayantyatra prayogaṃ nāndipāṭhakāḥ pūrvameva tu raṅge smiṃstasmādutthāpanaṃ smṛtam  BhN yasmācca lokapālānāṃ parivṛtya caturdiśam vandanāni prakurvanti tasmācca parivartanam  BhN āśīrvacanasaṃyuktā nityaṃ yasmātprayujyate devadvijanṛpādīnāṃ tasmānnāndīti saṃjñitā  BhN atra śuṣkākṣaraireva hyavakṛṣṭā dhruvā yataḥ tasmācchuṣkāvakṛṣṭeyaṃ jarjaraślokadarśitā  BhN yasmādabhinayastvatra prathamaṃ hyavatāryate raṅgadvāramato jñeyaṃ vāgaṅgābhinayātmakam  BhN śṛṅgārasya pracaraṇāccārī samparikīrtitā raudrapracaraṇāccāpi mahācārīti kīrtitā  BhN vidūṣakaḥ sūtradhārastathā vai pāripārśvakaḥ yatra kurvanti sañjalpaṃ taccāpi trigataṃ matam  BhN upakṣepeṇa kāvyasya hetuyuktisamāśrayā siddhenāmantraṇā yā tu vijñeyā sa prarocanā  BhN ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi hyāśrāvaṇavidhikriyām bahirgītavidhau samyagutpattiṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā  BhN citradakṣiṇavṛtau tu saptarūpe pravartite sopohane sanirgīte devastutyabhinandite  BhN nāradādyaistu gandharvaiḥ sabhāyāṃ devadānavāḥ nirgītaṃ śrāvitāḥ samyaglayatālasamanvitam  BhN tacchrutvā tu sukhaṃ gānaṃ devastutyabhinanditamabhavankṣubhitāḥ sarve mātsaryāddaityarākṣasāḥ  BhN sampradhārya ca te nyonyamityavocannavasthitāḥ nirgītaṃ tu savāditramidaṃ gṛhṇīmahe vayam  BhN saptarūpeṇa santuṣṭā devāḥ karmānukīrtanāt vayaṃ gṛhṇīma nirgītaṃ tuṣyāmo traiva sarvadā  BhN te tatra tuṣṭā daityāstu sādhayanti punaḥ punaḥ ruṣṭāścāpi tato devāḥ pratyabhāṣanta nāradam  BhN ete tuṣyanti nirgīte dānavā saha rākṣasaiḥ praṇaśyatu prayogo yaṃ kathaṃ vā manyate bhavān  BhN devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā nārado vākyamabravīt dhātuvādyāśrayakṛtaṃ nirgītaṃ mā praṇaśyatu  BhN kintūpohanasaṃyuktaṃ dhātuvādyavibhūṣitam bhaviṣyatīdaṃ nirgītaṃ saptarūpavidhānataḥ  BhN nirgītenāvabaddhāśca daityadānavarākṣasāḥ na kṣobhaṃ na vighātaṃ ca kariṣyantīha toṣitāḥ  BhN evaṃ nirgītametattu daityānāṃ spardhayā dvijāḥ devānāṃ bahumānena bahirgītamiti smṛtam  BhN dhātubhiścitravīṇāyāṃ gurulaghvakṣarānvitam varṇālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ prayoktavyaṃ budhairatha  BhN nirgītaṃ geyate yasmādapadaṃ varṇayojanāt asūyayā ca devānāṃ bahirgītamidaṃ smṛtam  BhN nirgītaṃ yanmayā proktaṃ saptarūpasamanvitam utthāpanādikaṃ yacca tasya kāraṇamucyate  BhN āśrāvaṇāyāṃ yuktāyāṃ daityāstuṣyanti nityaśaḥ vaktrapāṇau kṛte caiva nityaṃ tuṣyanti dānavāḥ  BhN parighaṭṭanayā tuṣṭā yuktāyāṃ rākṣasāṃ gaṇāḥ saṅghoṭanakriyāyāṃ ca tuṣyantyapi ca guhyakāḥ  BhN mārgāsāritamāsādya tuṣṭā yakṣā bhavanti hi gītakeṣu prayukteṣu devāstuṣyanti nityaśaḥ  BhN vardhamāne prayukte tu rudrastuṣyati sānugaḥ tathā cotthāpane yukte brahmā tuṣṭo bhavediha  BhN tuṣyanti lokapālāśca prayukte parivartane nāndīprayoge tha kṛte prīto bhavati candramāḥ  BhN yuktāyāmavakṛṣṭāyāṃ prītā nāgā bhavanti hi tathā śuṣkāvakṛṣṭāyāṃ prītaḥ pitṛgaṇo bhavet  BhN raṅgadvāre prayukte tu viṣṇuḥ prīto bhavediha jarjarasya prayoge tu tuṣṭā vighnavināyakāḥ  BhN tathā cāryā prayuktāyāmumā tuṣṭā bhavediha mahācāryā prayuktāyāṃ tuṣṭo bhūtagaṇo bhavet  BhN āśrāvaṇādicāryantametaddaivatapūjanam pūrvaraṅge mayā khyātaṃ tathā cāṅgavikalpanam  BhN devastuṣyanti yo yena yasya yanmanasaḥ priyam tattathā pūrvaraṅge tu mayā prokaṃ dvijottamāḥ  BhN sarvadaivatapūjārhaṃ sarvadaivatapūjanam dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ pūrvaraṅgapravartanam  BhN daityadānavatuṣṭyarthaṃ sarveṣāṃ ca divaukasām nirgītāni sagītāni pūrvaraṅgakṛtāni tu  BhN yā vidyā yāni śilpāni yā gatiryaśca ceṣṭitam lokālokasya jagatastadasminnāṭakāśraye  BhN nirgītānāṃ sagītānāṃ vardhamānasya caiva hi dhruvāvidhāne vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ karma caiva hi  BhN prayujya gītakavidhiṃ vardhamānamathāpi ca gītakānte tataścāpi kāryā hyutthāpanī dhruvā  BhN adau dve ca caturthaṃ cāpyaṣṭamaikādaśe tathā gurvakṣarāṇi jānīyatpāde hyekādaśe tathā  BhN catuṣpadā bhavetsā tu caturaśrā tathaiva ca caturbhissannipātaiśca trilayā triyatistathā  BhN parivartāśca catvāraḥ pāṇayastraya eva ca jātyā caiva hi viślokā tāṃ ca tālena yojayet  BhN śamyā tu dvikalā kāryā talo dvikala eva ca punaścaikakalā śamyā sannipātaḥ kalātrayam  BhN evamaṣṭakalaḥ kāryaḥ sannipāto viacakṣaṇaiḥ catvāraḥ sannipātāśca parivartaḥ sa ucyate  BhN pūrvaṃ sthitalayaḥ kāryaḥ parivarto vicakṣaṇaiḥ tṛtīye sannipāte tu tasyā bhāṇḍagraho bhavet  BhN ekasminparivarte tu gate prāpte dvitīyake kāryaṃ madhyalaye tajjñaiḥ sūtradhārapraveśanam  BhN puṣpāñjaliṃ samādāya rakṣāmaṅgalasaṃskṛtāḥ śuddhavastrāḥ sumanasastathā cādbhutadṛṣṭayaḥ  BhN sthānantu vaiṣṇavaṃ kṛtvā sauṣṭhavāṅgapuraskṛtam dīkṣitāḥ śucayaścaiva praviśeyuḥ samaṃ trayaḥ  BhN bhṛṅgārajarjaradharau bhavetāṃ pāripārśvikau madhye tu sūtrabhṛttābhyāṃ vṛttaḥ pañcapadīṃ vrajet  BhN padāni pañca gaccheyurbrahmaṇo yajanecchayā padānāñcāpi vikṣepaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN tritālāntaraviṣkambhamutkṣipeccaraṇaṃ śanaiḥpārśvotthānotthitaṃ caiva tanmadhye pātayetpunaḥ  BhN evaṃ pañcapadīṃ gatvā sūtradhāraḥ sahetaraḥ sūcīṃ vāmapade dadyādvikṣepaṃ dakṣiṇena ca  BhN puṣpāñjalyapavargaśca kāryo brāhme tha maṇḍale raṅgapīṭhasya madhye tu svayaṃ brahmā pratiṣṭhitaḥ  BhN tataḥ salalitairhastairabhivandya pitāmaham abhivādāni kāryāṇi trīṇi hastena bhūtale  BhN kālaprakarṣahetośca pādānāṃ pravibhāgataḥ sūtradhārapraveśādyo vandanābhinayāntakaḥ  BhN dvitīyaḥ parivartastu kāryo madhyalayāśritaḥ tataḥ paraṃ tṛtīye tu maṇḍalasya pradakṣiṇam  BhN bhavedācamanaṃ caiva jarjaragrahaṇaṃ tathā utthāya maṇḍalāttūrṇaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pādamuddharet  BhN vedhaṃ tenaiva kurvīta vikṣepaṃ vāmakena ca punaśca dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ pārśvasaṃsthaṃ samuddharet  BhN tataśca vāmavedhastu vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca ityanena vidhānena samyakkṛtvā pradikṣaṇam  BhN bhṛṅgārabhṛtamāhūya śaucaṃ cāpi samācaret yathānyāyaṃ tu kartavyā tena hyācamanakriyā  BhN ātmaprokṣaṇamevādbhiḥ kartavyaṃ tu yathākramam prayatnakṛtaśaucena sūtradhāreṇa yatnataḥ  BhN sannipātasamaṃ grāhyo jarjaro vighnajarjaraḥ pradakṣiṇādyo vijñeyo jarjaragrahaṇāntakaḥ  BhN tṛtīyaḥ parivartastu vijñeyo vai drute laye gṛhītvā jarjaraṃ tvaṣṭau kalā japyaṃ prayojayet  BhN vāmavedhaṃ tataḥ kuryādvikṣepaṃ dakṣiṇasya ca tataḥ pañcapadīṃ caiva gacchettu kutaponmukhaḥ  BhN vāmavedhastu tatrāpi vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya tu jarjaragrahaṇādyo yaṃ kutapābhimukhāntakaḥ  BhN caturthaḥ parivartastu kāryo drutalaye punaḥ karapādanipātāstu bhavntyatra tu ṣoḍaśa  BhN tryaśre dvādaśa pātāstu bhavanti karapādayoḥ vandanānyatha kāryāṇi trīṇi hastena bhūtale  BhN ātmaprokṣaṇamadbhiśca tryaśre naiva vidhīyate evamutthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ tatastu parivartanam  BhN caturaśraṃ laye madhye sannipātairathāṣṭabhiḥ yasyā laghūni sarvāṇi kevalaṃ naidhanaṃ guru  BhN bhavedatijagatyāntu sā dhruvā parivartanī vārtikena tu mārgeṇa vādyenānugatena ca  BhN lalitaiḥ pādavinyāsairvandyā devā yathādiśam dvikalaṃ pādapatanaṃ pādacāryā gataṃ bhavet  BhN vāmapādena vedhastu kartavyo nṛttayoktṛbhiḥ dvitālāntaraviṣkambho vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca  BhN tataḥ pañcapadīṃ gacchedatikrāntaiḥ padaratha tato bhivādanaṃ kuryāddevatānāṃ yathādiśam  BhN vandeta prathamaṃ pūrvāṃ diśaṃ śakrādhidaivatām dvitīyāṃ dakṣiṇāmāśāṃ vandeta yamadevatām  BhN vandeta paścimāmāśāṃ tato varuṇadaivatām caturthīmuttarāmāśāṃ vandeta dhanadāśrayām  BhN diśāṃ tu vandanaṃ kṛtvā vāmavedhaṃ prayojayet dakṣiṇena ca kartavyaṃ vikṣepaparivartanam  BhN prāṅgmukhastu tataḥ kuryātpuruṣastrīnapuṃsakaiḥ tripadyā sūtrabhṛdrudrabrahmopendrābhivādanam  BhN dakṣiṇaṃ tu padaṃ puṃso vāmaṃ strīṇāṃ prakīrtitam punardakṣiṇameva syānnātyutkṣiptaṃ napuṃsakam  BhN vandeta pauruṣeṇeśaṃ strīpadena janārdanam napuṃsakpadenāpi tathaivāmbujasambhavam  BhN parivartanamevaṃ syāttasyānte praviśettataḥ caturthakāraḥ puṣpāṇi pragṛhya vidhipūrvakam  BhN yathāvattena kartavyaṃ pūjanaṃ jarjarasya tu kutapasya ca sarvasya sūtradhārasya caiva hi  BhN tasya bhāṇḍasamaḥ kāryastajjñairgatiparikramaḥ na tatra gānaṃ kartavyaṃ tatra stobhakriyā bhavet  BhN caturthakāraḥ pūjāṃ tu sa kṛtvāntarhito bhavet tato geyāvakṛṣṭā tu caturaśrā sthitā dhruvā  BhN guruprāyā tu sā kāryā tathā caivāvapāṇikā sthāyivarṇāśrayopetā kalāṣṭakavinirmitā  BhN caturthaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva saptamaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ tathā laghūni pāde paṅktyāntu sāvakṛṣṭā dhruvā smṛtā  BhN sūtradhāraḥ paṭhettatra madhyamaṃ svaramāśritaḥ nāndīṃ padairdvādaśabhiraṣṭabhirvāpyalaṅkṛtām  BhN namo stu sarvadevebhyo dvijātibhyaḥ śubhaṃ tathā jitaṃ somena vai rājñā śivaṃ gobrāhmaṇāya ca  BhN brahmottaraṃ tathaivāstu hatā brahmadviṣastathā praśāstvimāṃ mahārājaḥ pṛthivīṃ ca sasāgarām  BhN rāṣṭraṃ pravardhatāṃ caiva raṅgasyāśā samṛddhyatu prekṣākarturmahāndharmo bhavatu brahmabhāṣitaḥ  BhN kāvyakarturyaśaścāstu dharmaścāpi pravardhatām ijyayā cānayā nityaṃ prīyantāṃ devatā iti  BhN nāndīpadāntareṣveṣu hyevamāryeti nityaśaḥ vadetāṃ samyaguktābhirvāgbhistau pāripārśvikau  BhN evaṃ nāndī vidhātavyā yathāvallakṣaṇānvitā tataśśuṣkāvakṛṣṭā syājjarjaraślokadarśikā  BhN navaṃ gurvākṣarāṇyādau ṣaḍlaghūni gurutrayam śuṣkāvakṛṣṭā tu bhavetkalā hyaṣṭau pramāṇataḥ  BhN yathādigle digle digle digle jambukapalitakate tecām kṛtvā śuṣkāvakṛṣṭāṃ tu yathāvaddvijasattamāḥ  BhN tataḥ ślokaṃ paṭhedekaṃ gambhīrasvarasaṃyutam devastotraṃ puraskṛtya yasya pūjā pravartate  BhN rājño vā yatra bhaktiḥ syādatha vā brahmaṇasstavam gaditvā jarjaraślokaṃ raṅgadvāre ca yatsmṛtam  BhN paṭhedanyaṃ punaḥ ślokaṃ jarjarasya vināśanam jarjaraṃ namayitvā tu tataścārīṃ prayojayet  BhN pāripārśvikayośca syātpaścimenāpasarpaṇam aṅkitā cātra kartavyā dhruvā madhyalayānvitā  BhN caturbhiḥ sannipātaiśca caturaśrā pramāṇataḥ ādyamantyaṃ caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ca tathā guru  BhN yasyāṃ hrasvāni śeṣāṇi sā jñeyā tvaṅkitā budhaiḥ asyāḥ prayogaṃ vakṣyāmi yathā pūrvaṃ maheśvaraḥ  BhN sahomayā krīḍitavānnānābhāvaviceṣṭataiḥ kṛtvāvahitthaṃ sthānaṃ tu vāmaṃ cādhomukhaṃ bhujam  BhN caturaśramuraḥ kāryamañcitaścāpi mastakaḥ nābhipradeśe vinyasya jarjaraṃ ca tulādhṛtam  BhN vāmapallavahastena pādaistālāntarotthitaiḥ gacchetpañcapadīṃ caiva savilāsāṅgaceṣṭitaiḥ  BhN vāmavedhastu kartavyo vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca śṛṅgārarasasaṃyuktāṃ paṭhedāryāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ  BhN cārīślokaṃ gaditvā tu kṛtvā ca parivartanam taireva ca padaḥ kāryaṃ paścimenāpasarpaṇam  BhN pāripārśvikahaste tu nyasya jarjaramuttamam mahācārīṃ tataścaiva prayuñjīta yathāvidhi  BhN caturaśrā dhruvā tatra tathā drutalayānvitā caturbhissannipātaiśca kalā hyaṣṭau pramāṇataḥ  BhN ādyaṃ caturthamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ daśamaṃ guru laghu śeṣaṃ dhruvāpāde caturviṃśatike bhavet  BhN yathāpādatalāhatipātitaśailaṃ kṣobhitabhūtasamagrasamudram tāṇḍavanṛtyamidaṃ pralayānte pātu jagatsukhadāyi harasya  BhN bhāṇḍonmukhena kartavyaṃ pādavikṣepaṇaṃ tataḥ sūcīṃ kṛtvā punaḥ kuryādvikṣepaparivartanam  BhN atikrāntaiḥ salalitaiḥ pādairdrutalayānvitaiḥ tritālāntaramutkṣepairgacchetpañcapadīṃ tataḥ  BhN tatrāpi vāmavedhastu vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca taireva ca padaiḥ kāryaṃ prāṅmukhenāpasarpaṇam  BhN punaḥ padāni trīṇyeva gacchetprāṅmukha eva tu tataśca vāmavedhaḥ syādvikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca  BhN tato raudrarasaṃ ślokaṃ pādasaṃharaṇaṃ paṭhet tasyānte tu tripadyātha vyāharetpāripārśvikau  BhN tayorāgamane kāryaṃ gānaṃ narkuṭakaṃ budhaiḥ tathā ca bhāratībhede trigataṃ samprayojayet  BhN vidūṣakastvekapadāṃ sutradhārasmitāvahām asambaddhakathāprāyāṃ kuryātkathanikā tataḥ  BhN vitaṇḍāṃ gaṇḍasaṃyuktāṃ tālikāñca prayojayet kastiṣṭhati jitaṃ kenetyādikāvyaprarūpiṇīm  BhN pāripārśvakasañjalpo vidūṣakavirūpitaḥ sthāpitaḥ sūtradhāreṇa trigataṃ samprayujyate  BhN prarocanā ca kartavyā siddhenopanimatraṇam raṅgasiddhau punaḥ kāryaṃ kāvyavastunirūpaṇam  BhN sarvameva vidhiṃ kṛtvā sūcīvedhakṛtairatha pādairanāviddhagatairniṣkrāmeyuḥ samaṃ trayaḥ  BhN evameṣa prayoktavyaḥ pūrvaraṅgo yathāvidhi caturaśro dvijaśreṣṭhāstryaśraṃ cāpi nibodhata  BhN ayameva prayogaḥ syādaṅgānyetāni caiva hi tālapramāṇaṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ kevalaṃ tu viśeṣakṛt  BhN śamyā tu dvikalā kāryā tālo hyekakalastathā punaścaikakalā śamyā sannipātaḥ kalādvayam  BhN anena hi pramāṇena kalātālalayānvitaḥ kartavyaḥ pūrvaraṅgastu tryaśro pyutthāpanādikaḥ  BhN ādyaṃ caturthaṃ daśamamaṣṭamaṃ naidhanaṃ guru yasyāstu jāgate pāde sā tryaśrotthāpinī dhruvā  BhN vādyaṃ gatipracāraśca dhruvā tālastathaiva ca saṃkṣiptānyeva kāryāṇi tryaśre nṛttapravedibhiḥ  BhN vādyagītapramāṇena kuryādaṅgaviceṣṭitam vistīrṇamatha saṃkṣiptaṃ dvipramāṇavinirmitam  BhN hastapādapracārastu dvikalaḥ parikīrtitaḥ caturaśre parikrānte pātāḥ syuḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu  BhN tryaśre dvādaśa pātāstu bhavanti karapādayoḥ etatpramāṇaṃ vijñeyamubhayoḥ pūrvaraṅgayoḥ  BhN kevalaṃ parivarte tu gamane tripadī bhavet digvandane pañcapadī caturaśre vidhīyate  BhN ācāryabuddhyā kartavyastryaśrastālapramāṇataḥ tasmānna lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ punaruktaṃ bhavedyataḥ  BhN evameṣa prayoktavyaḥ pūrvaraṅgo dvijottamāḥ tryaśraśca caturaśraśca śuddho bhāratyupāśrayaḥ  BhN evaṃ tāvadayaṃ śuddhaḥ pūrvaraṅgo mayoditaḥ citratvamasya vakṣyāmi yathākāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN vṛtte hyutthāpane viprāḥ kṛte ca parivartane caturthakāradattābhiḥ sumanobhiralaṅkṛte  BhN udāttairgānairgandharvaiḥ parigīte pramāṇataḥ devadundubhayaścaiva ninadaiyurbhṛśaṃ yataḥ  BhN siddhāḥ kusumamālābhirvikireyuḥ samantataḥ aṅgahāraiśca devyastā upanṛtyeyuragrataḥ  BhN yastāṇḍavavidhiḥ prokto nṛte piṇḍīsamanvitaḥ recakairaṅgahāraiśca nyāsopanyāsasaṃyutaḥ  BhN nāndīpadānāṃ madhye tu ekaikasminpṛthakpṛthak prayoktavyo budhaiḥ samyakcitrabhāvamabhīpsubhiḥ  BhN evaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ śuddhaṃ citraṃ prayatnataḥ tataḥparaṃ prayuñjīta nāṭakaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam  BhN tatastvantarhitāḥ sarvā bhaveyurdivyayoṣitaḥ niṣkrāntāsu ca sarvāsu nartakīṣu tataḥ param  BhN pūrvaraṅge prayoktavyamaṅgajātamataḥparam evaṃ śuddho bhaveccitraḥ pūrvaraṅgo vidhānataḥ  BhN kāryo nātiprasaṅgo tra nṛtāgītavidhiṃ prati gīte vādye ca nṛtte ca pravṛtte tiprasaṅgataḥ  BhN khedo bhavetprayoktṝṇāṃ prekṣakāṇāṃ tathaiva ca khinnānāṃ rasabhāveṣu spaṣṭatā nopajāyate  BhN tataḥ śeṣaprayogastu na rāgajanako bhavet lakṣanena vinā bāhyalakṣaṇādvistṛtaṃ bhavet lokaśāstrānusāreṇa tasmānnāṭyaṃ pravartate  BhNab tryaśraṃ vā caturaśraṃ vā śuddhaṃ citramathāpi vā  BhN prayujya raṅgānniṣkrāmetsūtradhārḥ sahānugaḥ devapārthivaraṅgānāmāśīrvacanasaṃyutām  BhN kavernāmaguṇopetāṃ vastūpakṣeparūpikām laghuvarṇapadopetāṃ vṛttaiścitrairalaṅkṛtām  BhN antaryavanikāsaṃsthaḥ kuryādāśrāvaṇāṃ tataḥ āśrāvanāvasāne ca nāndīṃ kṛtvā sa sūtradhṛt punaḥ praviśya raṅgaṃ tu kuryātprastāvanāṃ tataḥ  BhN prayujya vidhinaivaṃ tu pūrvaragaṃ prayogataḥ  BhN sthāpakaḥ praviśettatra sūtradhāraguṇākṛtiḥ sthānaṃ tu vaiṣṇavaṃ kṛtvā sauṣṭhavāñgapuraskṛtam  BhN praviśya raṅgaṃ taireva sūtradhārapadairvrajet śthāpakṣya praveśe tu kartavyarthānugā dhruvā  BhN tryaśrā vā caturaśrā vā tajjñairmadhyalayānvitā kuryādanantaraṃ cārīṃ devarahmaṇaśaṃsinīm  BhN suvākyamadhuraiḥ ślokernānābhasavarasānvitaiḥ prasādya raṅgaṃ vidhivatkavernāma ca kīrtayet  BhN prastavā tataḥ kuryātkāvyaprakhyāpanāśrayām uddhātyakādi kartavyaṃ kāvyopakṣepaṇāśryam  BhN divye divyāśrayo bhūtvā mānuṣe mānuṣāśrayaḥ divyamānuṣasaṃyoge divyo vā mānuṣo pi vā  BhN mukhabījānusadṝśaṃ nānāmārgasamāśrayam āāvidhairupakṣepaiḥ kāvyopakṣepaṇaṃ bhavet  BhN prastāvyaivaṃ tu niṣkrāmetkāvyaprastāvakastataḥ evameṣa prayoktavyaḥ pūrvaraṅgo yathāvidhi  BhN ya imaṃ pūrvaraṅgaṃ tu vidhinaiva prayojayet nāśubhaṃ prāpnuyātkiñcitsvargalokaṃ ca gacchati  BhN yaścāpi vidhimutsṛjya yatheṣṭaṃ samprayojayet prāpnotyapacayaṃ ghoraṃ tiryaggyoniṃ ca gacchati  BhN na tathāgniḥ pradahati prabhañjanasamīrataḥ yathā hyaprayogastu prayukto dahati kṣaṇāt  BhN ityevāvantipāñcāladākṣiṇātyauḍhramāgadhaiḥ kartavya pūrvaraṅgastu dvipramāṇavinirmitaḥ  BhN eṣa vaḥ kathito viprāḥ pūrvaraṅgāśrito vidhiḥ bhūyaḥ kiṃ kathyatāṃ samyaṅnāṭyavedavidhiṃ prati  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre pūrvaraṅgaprayogo nāma pañcamo dhyāyaḥatha ṣaṣṭho dhyāyaḥpūrvaraṅgavidhiṃ śrutvāpunarāhurmahattamāḥ bharataṃ munayaḥ sarve praśnānpañcābhidhatsva naḥ  BhN ye rasā iti paṭhyante nāṭye nāṭyavicakṣaṇaiḥ rasatvaṃ kena vai teṣāmetadākhyātumarhasi  BhN bhāvāścaiva kathaṃ proktāḥ kiṃ vā te bhāvayantyapi saṃgrahaṃ kārikāṃ caiva niruktaṃ caiva tatvataḥ  BhN teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ pratyuvāca punarvākyaṃ rasabhāvavikalpanam  BhN ahaṃ vaḥ kathayiṣyāmi nikhilena tapodhanāḥ saṃgrahaṃ kārikāṃ caiva niruktaṃ ca yathākramam  BhN na śakyamasya nāṭyasya gantumantaṃ kathañcana kasmādbahutvājjñānānāṃ śilpānāṃ vāpyanantataḥ  BhN ekasyāpi na vai śakyastvanto jñānārṇavasya hi gantuṃ kiṃ punaranyeṣāṃ jñānānāmarthatattvataḥ  BhN kintvalpasūtragranthārthamanumānaprasādhakam nāṭyasyāsya pravakṣyāmi rasabhāvādisaṅgraham  BhN vistareṇopadiṣṭānāmarthānāṃ sūtrabhāṣyayoḥ nibandho yo samāsena saṅgrahaṃ taṃ vidurbudhāḥ  BhN rasā bhāvā hyabhinayāḥ dharmī vṛttipravṛttayaḥ siddhiḥ svarāstathātodyaṃ gānaṃ raṅgaśca saṅgrahaḥ  BhN alpābhidhānenārtho yaḥ samāsenocyate budhaiḥ sūtrataḥ sānumatavyā kārikārthapradarśinī  BhN nānānāmāśrayotpannaṃ nighaṇṭunigamānvitam dhātvarthahetusaṃyuktaṃ nānāsiddhāntasādhitam  BhN sthāpito rtho bhavedyatra samāsenārthāsūcakaḥ dhātvarthavacaneneha niruktaṃ tatpracakṣate  BhN saṅgraho yo mayā proktaḥ samāsena dvijottamāḥ vistaraṃ tasya vakṣyāmi saniruktaṃ sakārikam  BhN śṛṅgārahāsyakaruṇā raudravīrabhayānakāḥ bībhatsādbhutasaṃjñau cetyaṣṭau nāṭye rasāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN ete hyaṣṭau rasāḥ proktā druhinena mahātmanā punaśca bhāvānvakṣyāmi sthāyisañcārisattvajān  BhN ratihāsaśca śokaśca krodhotsāhau bhayaṃ tathā jugupsā vismayaśceti sthāyibhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BhN nirvedaglāniśaṅkākhyāstathāsūyā madaḥ śramaḥ ālasyaṃ caiva dainyaṃ ca cintāmohaḥ smṛtirdhṛtiḥ  BhN vrīḍā capalatā harṣa āvego jaḍatā tathā garvo viṣāda autsukyaṃ nidrāpasmāra eva ca  BhN suptaṃ vibodho marṣaścāpyavahitthamathogratā matirvyādhistathonmādastathā maraṇameva ca  BhN trāsaścaiva vitarkaśca vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ trayastriṃśadamī bhāvāḥ samākhyātāstu nāmataḥ  BhN stambhaḥ svedo tha romāñcaḥ svarabhedo tha vepathuḥ vaivarṇyamaśru pralaya ityaṣṭau sātvikāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN āṅgikau vācikaścaiva hyāhāryaḥ sātvikastathā catvāro bhinayā hyete vijñeyā nāṭyasaṃśrayāḥ  BhN lokadharmī nāṭyadharmī dharmīti dvividhaḥ smṛtaḥ bhāratī sātvatī caiva kaiśikyārabhaṭī tathā  BhN catasro vṛttayo hyetā yāsu nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam āvantī dākṣiṇātyā ca tathā caivoḍhramāgadhī  BhN pāñcālamadhyamā ceti vijñeyāstu pravṛttayaḥ daivikī mānuṣī caiva siddhiḥ syāddvividhaiva tu  BhN śārīrāścaiva vaiṇāśca sapta ṣaḍjādayaḥ svarāḥ niṣādarṣabhagāndhāramadhyapañcamadhaivatāḥ  BhNab tataṃ caivāvanaddhaṃ ca ghanaṃ suṣirameva ca  BhN caturvidhaṃ ca vijñeyamātodyaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam tataṃ tantrīgataṃ jñeyamavanaddhaṃ tu pauṣkaram  BhN ghanastu tālo vijñeyaḥ suṣiro vaṃśa eva ca praveśākṣepaniṣkrāmaprāsādikamathāntaram  BhN gānaṃ pañcavidhaṃ jñeyaṃ dhruvāyogasamanvitam caturasro vikṛṣṭaśca raṅgastryaśraśca kīrtitaḥ  BhN evameṣo lpasūtrārtho nirdiṣṭo nāṭyasaṃgrahaḥ ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sūtragranthavikalpanam  BhN tatra rasāneva tāvadādāvabhivyākhyāsyāmaḥ na hi rasādṛte kaścidarthaḥ pravartate tatra vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyogādrasaniṣpattiḥ ko dṛṣṭāntaḥ atrāha yathā hi nānāvyañjanauṣadhidravyasaṃyogādrasaniṣpattiḥ tathā nānābhāvopagamādrasaniṣpattiḥ  yathā hi guḍādibhirdravyairvyañjanairauṣadhibhiśca ṣāḍavādayo rasā nirvartyante tathā nānābhāvopagatā api sthāyino bhāvā rasatvamāpnuvantīti atrāha rasa iti kaḥ padārthaḥ ucyateāsvādyatvāt kathamāsvādyate rasaḥ yathā hi nānāvyañjanasaṃskṛtamannaṃ bhuñjāna rasānāsvādayanti sumanasaḥ puruṣa harṣādīṃścādhigacchantitathā nānābhāvābhinayavyañjitān vāgaṅgasattopetān sthāyibhāvānāsvādayanti sumanasaḥ prekṣakāḥharṣādīṃścādhigacchanti tasmānnāṭyarasā ityabhivyākhyātāḥ atrānuvaṃśyau ślokau bhavataḥyathā bahudravyayutairvyañjanairbahubhiryutam āsvādayanti bhuñjānā bhaktaṃ bhaktavido janāḥ  BhN bhāvābhinayasaṃbaddhānsthāyibhāvāṃstathā budhāḥ āsvādayanti manasā tasmānnāṭyarasāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN atrāhakiṃ rasebhyo bhāvānāmabhinirvṛttirutāho bhāvebhyo rasānāmiti keṣāñcinmataṃ parasparasambandhādeṣāmabhinirvṛttiriti tanna kasmāt dṛśyate hi bhāvebhyo rasānāmabhinirvṛttirna tu rasebhyo bhāvānāmabhinirvṛttiriti bhavanti cātra ślokāḥnānābhinayasambaddhānbhāvayanti rasanimān yasmāttasmādamī bhāvā vijñeyā nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN nānādravyaibahuvidhairvyañjanaṃ bhāvyate yathā evaṃ bhāvā bhāvayanti rasānabhinayaiḥ saha  BhN na bhāvahīno sti raso na bhāvo rasavarjitaḥ parasparakṛtā siddhistayorabhinaye bhavet  BhN vyañjanauṣadhisaṃyogo yathānnaṃ svādutāṃ nayet evaṃ bhāvā rasāścaiva bhāvayanti parasparam  BhN yathā bījādbhavedvṛkṣo vṛkṣātpuṣpaṃ phalaṃ yathā tathā mūlaṃ rasāḥ sarve tebhyo bhāvā vyavasthitāḥ  BhN tadeṣaṃ rasānāmutpattivarṇadaivatanidarśanānyabhivyākhyāsyāmaḥ teṣāmutpattihetavaścatvāro rasāḥ tadyathā śṛṅgāro raudrau vīro bībhatsa iti  atraśṛṅgārāddhi bhaveddhāsyo raudrācca karuṇo rasaḥ vīrāccaivādbhutotpattirbībhatsācca bhayānakaḥ  BhN śṛṅgārānukṛtiryā tu sa hāsyastu prakīrtitaḥ raudrasyaiva ca yatkarma sa jñeyaḥ karuṇo rasaḥ  BhN vīrasyāpi ca yatkarma so dbhutaḥ parikīrtitaḥ bībhatsadarśanaṃ yacca jñeyaḥ sa tu bhayānakaḥ  BhN atha varṇāḥśyāmo bhavati śṛṅgāraḥ sito hāsyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ kapotaḥ karuṇaścaiva rakto raudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN gauro vīrastu vijñeyaḥ kṛṣṇaścaiva bhayānakaḥ nīlavarṇastu bībhatsaḥ pītaścaivādbhutaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN atha daivatāniśṛṅgāro viṣṇudevatyo hāsyaḥ pramathadaivataḥ raudro rudrādhidaivatyaḥ karuṇo yamadaivataḥ  BhN bībhatsasya mahākālaḥ kāladevo bhayānakaḥ vīro mahendradevaḥ syādadbhuto brahmadaivataḥ  BhN etameteṣāṃ rasānāmutpattivarṇadaivatānyabhivyākhyātāni idānīmanubhāvavibhāvavyabhicārisaṃyuktānāṃ lakṣaṇanidarśanānyabhivyākhyāsyāmaḥ sthāyibhāvāṃśca rasatvamupaneṣyāmaḥ tatra śṛṅgāro nāma ratisthāyibhāvaprabhavaḥ ujjvalaveṣātmakaḥ yatkiñcilloke śuci medhyamujjvalaṃ darśanīyaṃ vā tacchṛṅgāreṇopamīyate yastāvadujjvalaveṣaḥ sa śṛṅgāravānityucyate  yathā ca gotrakulācārotpannānyāptopadeśasiddhāni puṃsāṃ nāmāni bhavanti tathaiveṣāṃ rasānāṃ bhāvānāṃ ca nāṭyāśritānāṃ cārthānāmācārotpannānyoptopadeśasiddhāni  nāmāni  evameṣa ācārasiddho hṛdyojjvalaveṣātmakatvācchṛṅgāro rasaḥ sa ca strīpuruṣahetuka uttamayuvaprakṛtiḥ tasya dve adhiṣṭhāne sambhogo vipralambhaśca tatra sambhogastāvatṛtumālyānulepanālaṅkāreṣṭajanaviṣayavarabhavanopabhogopavanagamanānubhavanaśravaṇadarśanakrīḍālīlādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tasya nayanacāturyabhrūkṣepakaṭākṣasañcāralalitamadhurāṅgahāravākyādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ vyabhicāriṇaścāsyālasyaugryajugupsāvarjyāḥ vipralambhakṛtastu nirvedaglāniśaṅkāsūyāśramacintautsukyanidrāsvapnavibodhavyādhyunmādamadāpasmārajāḍyamaraṇādibhiranubhāvairabhinetavyaḥ atrāhayadyayaṃ ratiprabhavaḥ śṛṅgāraḥ kathamasya karuṇāśrayiṇo bhāvā bhavanti atrocyatepūrvamevābhihitaṃ sambhogavipralambhakṛtaḥ śṛṅgāra iti vaiśikaśāstrakāraiśca daśāvastho bhihitaḥ tāśca sāmānyābhinaye vakṣyāmaḥ karuṇastu śāpakleśavinipatiteṣṭajanavibhavanāśavadhabandhasamuttho nirapekṣabhāvaḥ autsukyacintāsamutthaḥ sāpekṣabhāvo vipralambhakṛtaḥ evamanyaḥ karuṇo nyaśca vipralambha iti evameṣa sarvabhāvasaṃyuktaḥ śṛṅgāro bhavati api casukhaprāyeṣu sampannaḥ ṛtumālyadisevakaḥ puruṣaḥ pramadāyuktaḥ śṛṅgāra iti saṃjñitaḥ  BhN api cātra sūtrārthānuviddhe ārye bhavataḥṛtumālyālaṅkāraiḥ priyajanagāndharvakāvyasevābhiḥ upavanagamanavihāraiḥ śṛṅgārarasaḥ samudbhavati  BhN nayanavadanaprasādaiḥ smitamadhuravacodhṛtipramodaiśca madhuraiścāṅgavihāraistasyābhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ  BhN atha hāsyo nāma hāsasthāyibhāvātmakaḥ sa ca vikṛtaparaveṣālaṅkāradhārṣṭyalaulyakuhakāsatpralāpavyaṅgadarśanadoṣodāharaṇādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tasyoṣṭhanāsākapolaspandanadṛṣṭivyākośākuñcanasvedāsyarāgapārśvagrahaṇādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ vyabhicāriṇaścāsyāvahitthālasyatandrānidrāsvapnaprabodhādayaḥ dvividhaścāyamātmasthaḥ parasthaśca yadā svayaṃ hasati tadātmasthaḥ yadā tu paraṃ hāsayati tadā parasthaḥ atrānuvaṃśye ārye bhavataḥ viparitālaṅkārairvikṛtācarābhidhānaveṣaiśca vikṛtairarthaviśeṣairhasatīti rasaḥ smṛto hāsyaḥ  BhN vikṛtācārairvākyairaṅgavikāraiśca vikṛtaveṣaiśca hāsayati janaṃ yasmāttasmajjjñeyo raso hāsyaḥ  BhN strīnīcaprakṛtāveṣa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dṛśyate rasaḥ ṣaḍbhedāścāsya vijñeyāstāṃśca vakṣyāmyahaṃ punaḥ  BhN smitamatha hasitaṃ vihasitamupahasitaṃ cāpahasitamatihasitam dvau dvau bhedau syātāmuttamamadhyādhamaprakṛtau  BhN tatrasmitahasite jyeṣṭhānāṃ madhyānāṃ vihasitopahasite ca adhamānāmapahasitaṃ hyatihasitaṃ cāpi vijñeyam  BhN atra ślokāḥīṣadvikasitairgaṇḍaiḥ kaṭākṣaiḥ sauṣṭhavānvitaiḥ alakṣitadvijaṃ dhīramuttamānāṃ smitaṃ bhavet  BhN utphullānananetraṃ tu gaṇḍairvikasitairatha kiñcillakṣitadantaṃ ca hasitaṃ tadvidhīyate  BhN atha madhyamānāmākuñcitākṣigaṇḍaṃ yatsasvanaṃ madhuraṃ tathā kālāgataṃ sāsyarāgaṃ tadvai vihasitaṃ bhavet  BhN utphullanāsikaṃ yattu jihmadṛṣṭinirīkṣitam nikuñcitāṅgakaśirastaccopahasitaṃ bhavet  BhN athādhamānāmasthānahasitaṃ yattu sāśrunetraṃ tathaiva ca utkampitāṃsakaśirastaccāpahasiataṃ bhavet  BhN saṃrabdhasāśrunetraṃ ca vikṛṣṭasvaramuddhatam karopagūḍhapārśvaṃ ca taccātihasitaṃ bhavet  BhN hāsyasthānāni yāni syuḥ kāryotpannāni nāṭake uttamādhamamadhyānāmevaṃ tāni prayojayet  BhN ityeṣa svasamutthastathā parasamutthaśca vijñeyaḥ dvividhastriprakṛtigatastryavasthabhāvo raso hāsyaḥ  BhN atha karuṇo nāma śokasthāyibhāvaprabhavaḥ sa ca śāpakleśavinipatiteṣṭajanaviprayogavibhavanāśavadhabandhavidravopaghātavyasanasaṃyogādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samupajāyate tasyāśrupātaparidevanamukhaśoṣaṇavaivarṇyasrastagātratāniśśvāsasmṛtilopādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ  vyabhicāriṇaścāsya nirvedaglānicintautsukyāvegabhramamohaśramabhayaviṣādadainyavyādhijaḍatonmādāpasmāratrāsālasyamaraṇastambhavepathuvaivarṇyāśrusvarabhedādayaḥ atrārye bhavataḥiṣṭavadhadarśanādvā vipriyavacanasya saṃśravādvāpi ebhirbhāvaviśeṣaiḥ karuṇo nāma saṃbhavati  BhN sasvanaruditairmohāgamaiśca paridaivatairvilapitaiśca abhineyaḥ karuṇaraso dehāyāsābhighātaiśca  BhN atha raudro nāma krodhasthāyibhāvātmakorakṣodānavoddhatamanuṣyaprakṛtiḥsaṃgrāmahetukaḥ sa ca krodhādharṣaṇādhikṣepānṛtavacanopaghātavākpāruṣyābhidrohamātsaryādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tasya ca tāḍanapāṭanapīḍācchedanapraharaṇāharaṇaśastrasaṃpātasaṃprahārarudhirākarṣaṇādyāni karmāṇi punaśca raktanayanabhrukuṭikaraṇadantoṣṭhapīḍanagaṇḍasphuraṇahastāgraniṣpeṣādiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ bhāvāścāsyāsammohotsāhāvegāmarṣacapalataugryagarvasvedavepathuromāñcagadgadādayaḥ atrāhayadabhihitaṃ rakṣodānavādīnāṃ raudro rasaḥ kimanyeṣāṃ nāsti ucyateastyanyeṣāmapi raudro rasaḥ kintvadhikāro tra gṛhyate te hi svabhāvata eva raudraḥ kasmāt bahubāhavo bahumukhāḥ proddhūtavikīrṇapiṅgalaśirojāḥ raktodvṛttavilocanā bhīmāsitarūpiṇaścaiva yacca kiñcitsamārambhate svabhāvaceṣṭitaṃ vāgaṅgādikaṃ tatsarvaṃ raudramevaiṣām śṛṅgāraśca taiḥ prāyaśaḥ prasabhyaṃ sevyate teṣāṃ cānukāriṇo ye puruṣasteṣāmapi saṅgrāmasamprahārakṛto raudro raso numantavyaḥ atrānuvaṃśye ārye bhavataḥyuddhaprahāraghātanavikṛtacchedanavidāraṇaiścaiva saṃṅgrāmasambhramādyairebhiḥ sañjāyate raudraḥ  BhN nānāpraharaṇamokṣaiḥ śiraḥkabandhabhujakartanaiścaiva ebhiścārthaviśeṣairasyābhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ  BhN iti raudraraso dṛṣṭo raudravāgaṅgaceṣṭitaḥ śastraprahārabhūyiṣṭha ugrakarmakriyātmakaḥ  BhN atha vīro nāmottamaprakṛtirutsāhātmakaḥ sa cāsaṃmohādhyavasāyanavinayabalaparākramaśaktipratāpaprabhāvādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tasya sthairyadhairyaśauryatyāgavaiśāradyādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ bhāvāścāsya dhṛtimatigarvāvegaugryāmarṣasmṛtiromāñcādayaḥ atrārye rasavicāramukheutsāhādhyavasāyādaviṣāditvādavismayāmohāt vividhādarthaviśeṣādvīraraso nāma sambhavati  BhN sthitidhairyavīryagarvairutsāhaparākramaprabhāvaiśca vākyaiścākṣepakṛtairvīrarasaḥ samyagabhineyaḥ  BhN atha bhayānako nāma bhayasthāyibhāvātmakaḥ sa ca vikṛtaravasattvadarśanaśivolūkatrāsodvegaśūnyāgārāraṇyagamanasvajanavadhabandhadarśanaśrutikathādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tasya pravepitakaracaraṇanayanacapalapulakamukhavaivarṇyasvarabhedādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ bhāvāścāsya stambhasvedagadgadaromāñcavepathusvarabhedavaivarṇyaśaṅkāmohadainyāvegacāpalajaḍatātrāsāpasmāramaraṇādayaḥ atrāryāḥvikṛtaravasattvadarśanasaṃgrāmāraṇyaśūnyagṛhagamanāt gurunṛpayoraparādhātkṛtakaśca bhayānako jñeyaḥ  BhN gātramukhadṛṣṭibhedairūrustambhābhivīkṣaṇodvegaiḥ sannamukhaśoṣahṛdayaspandanaromodgamaiśca bhayam  BhN etatsvabhāvajaṃ syātsattvasamutthaṃ tathaiva kartavyam punarebhireva bhāvaiḥ kṛtakaṃ mṛduceṣṭitaiḥ kāryam  BhN karacaraṇavepathustambhagātrahṛdayaprakampena śuṣkoṣṭhatālukaṇṭhairbhayānako nityamabhineyaḥ  BhN atha bībhatso nāma jugupsāsthāyibhāvātmakaḥ sa cāhṛdyāpriyācoṣyāniṣṭaśravaṇadarśanakīrtanādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tasya sarvāṅgasaṃhāramukhavikūṇanollekhananiṣṭhīvanodvejanādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ bhāvāścāsyāpasmārodvegāvegamohavyādhimaraṇādayaḥ atrānuvaṃśye ārye bhavataḥanabhimatadarśanena ca gandharasasparśaśabdadoṣaiśca udvejanaiśca bahubhirbībhatsarasaḥ samudbhavati  BhN mukhanetravikūṇanayā nāsāpracchādanāvanamitāsyaiḥ avyaktapādapatanairbībhatsaḥ samyagabhineyaḥ  BhN athādbhuto nāma vismayasthāyibhāvātmakaḥ sa ca divyajanadarśanepsitamanorathāvāptyupavanadevakulādigamanasabhāvimānamāyendrajālasambhāvanādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate  tasya nayanavistārānimeṣaprekṣaṇaromāñcāśrusvedaharṣasādhuvādadānaprabandhahāhākārabāhuvadanacelāṅgulibhramaṇādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ bhāvāścāsya stambhāśrusvedagadgadaromāñcāvegasambhramajaḍatāpralayādayaḥ atrānuvaṃśye ārye bhavataḥyattvātiśayārthayuktaṃ vākyaṃ śilpaṃ ca karmarūpaṃ vā tatsarvamadbhutarase vibhāvarūpaṃ hi vijñeyam  BhN sparśagrahollukasanairhāhākāraiśca sādhuvādaiśca vepathugadgadavacanaiḥ svedādyairabhinayastasya  BhN śṛṅgāraṃ trividhaṃ vidyātdvāṅnaipathyakriyātmakam aṅganaipathyavākyaiśca hāsyaraudrau tridhā smṛtau  BhN dharmopaghātajaścaiva tathārthāpacayodbhavaḥ tathā śokakṛtaścaiva karuṇastrividhaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN dānavīraṃ dharmavīraṃ yuddhavīraṃ tathaiva ca rasaṃ vīramapi prāha brahmā trividhameva hi  BhN vyājāccaivāparādhācca vitrāsitakameva ca punarbhayānakañcaiva vidyāt trividhameva hi  BhN bībhatsaḥ kṣobhajaḥ śuddha udvegī syāt dvitīyakaḥ viṣṭhākṛmibhirudvegī kṣobhajo rudhirādiajaḥ  BhN divyaścānandajaścaiva dvidhā khyāto dbhuto rasaḥ divyadarśanajo divyo harṣādānadajaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN atha śānto nāma śamasthāyibhāvātmako mokṣapravartakaḥ sa tu tattvajñānavairāgyāśayaśuddhyādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tasya yamaniyamādhyātmadhyānadhāraṇopāsanasarvabhūtadayāliṅgagrahaṇādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ vyabhicāṇaścāsya nirvedasmṛtidhṛtisarvāśramaśaucastambharomāñcādayaḥ atrāryāḥ ślokāśca bhavantimokṣādhyātmasamutthastattvajñānārthahetusaṃyuktaḥ naiḥśreyasopadiṣṭaḥ śāntaraso nāma sambhavati  BhN buddhīndriyakarmendriyasaṃrodhādhyātmasaṃsthitopetaḥ sarvaprāṇisukhahitaḥ śāntaraso nāma vijñeyaḥ  BhN na yatra duḥkhaṃ na sukhaṃ na dveṣo nāpi matsaraḥ samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu sa śāntaḥ prathito rasaḥ  BhN bhāvā vikārā ratyādyāḥ śāntastu prakṛtirmataḥ vikāraḥ prakṛtairjātaḥ punastatraiva līyate svaṃ svaṃ nimittamāsādya śāntādbhāvaḥ pravartate  BhN punarnimittāpāye ca śānta evopalīyate evaṃ navarasā dṛṣṭā nāṭyajñairlakṣaṇānviatāḥ  BhN  evamete rasā jñeyāstvaṣṭau lakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhāvānāmapi lakṣaṇam  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre rasādhyāyaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥatha saptamo dhyāyaḥbhāvānidānīṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ atrāhabhāvā iti kasmāt kiṃ bhavantīti bhāvāḥ kiṃ vā bhāvayantīti bhāvāḥ ucyatevāgaṅgasattvopetānānkāvyārthānbhāvayantīti bhāvā iti bhū iti karaṇe dhātustathā ca bhāvitaṃ vāsitaṃ kṛtamityanarthāntaram loke pi ca prasiddham aho hyanena gandhena rasena vā sarvameva bhāvitamiti tacca vyāptyartham ślokāścātravibhāvenāhṛto yo rtho hyanubhāvaistu gamyate vāgaṅgasattvābhinayaiḥ sa bhāva iti saṃjñitaḥ  BhN vāgaṅgamukharāgeṇa sattvenābhinayena ca kaverantargataṃ bhāvaṃ bhāvayanbhāva ucyate  BhN nānābhinayasambaddhānbhāvayanti rasānimān yasmātasmādamī bhāvā vijñeyā nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN atha vibhāva iti kasmāt ucyatevibhavo vijñānārthaḥ vibhāvaḥ kāraṇaṃ nimittaṃ heturiti paryāyāḥ vibhāvyate nena vāgaṅgasattvābhinayā ityato vibhāvaḥ yathā vibhāvitaṃ vijñātamityanarthāntaram atra ślokaḥbahavo rthā vibhāvyante vāgaṅgābhinayāśrayāḥ anena yasmāttenāyaṃ vibhāva iti saṃjñitaḥ  BhN athānubhāva iti kasmāt ucyateanubhāvyate nena vāgaṅgasattvakṛto bhinaya iti atra ślokaḥvāgaṅgābhinayeneha yatastvartho nubhāvyate śākhāṅgopāṅgasaṃyuktastvanubhāvastataḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN evaṃ te vibhāvānubhāvasaṃyuktā bhāvā iti vyākhyātāḥ ato hyeṣāṃ bhāvānāṃ siddhirbhavati tasmādeṣāṃ bhāvānāṃ vibhāvānubhāvasaṃyuktānāṃ lakṣaṇanidarśanānyabhivyākhyāsyāmaḥ tatra vibhāvānubhāvau lokaprasiddhau lokasvabhāvānugatatvācca tayorlakṣaṇaṃ nocyate tiprasaṅganivṛtyartham bhavati cātra ślokaḥlokasvabhāvasaṃsiddhā lokayātrānugāminaḥ anubhāvā vibhāvāśca jñeyāstvabhinaye budhaiḥ  BhN tatrāṣṭau bhāvāḥ sthāyinaḥ trayastriṃśadvyabhicāriṇaḥ aṣṭau sātvikā iti bhedāḥ evamete kāvyarasābhivyaktihetava ekonapañcāśadbhāvāḥ pratyavagantavyāḥ ebhyaśca sāmānyaguṇayogena rasā niṣpadyante atra ślokaḥyo rtho hṛdayasaṃvādī tasya bhāvo rasodbhavaḥ śarīraṃ vyāpyate tena śuṣkaṃ kāṣṭhamivāgninā  BhN atrāha yadi kāvyārthasaṃśritairvibhāvānubhāvavyañjitairekonapañcāśadbhāvaiḥ sāmānyaguṇayogenābhiniṣpadyante rasāstatkathaṃ sthāyina eva bhāvā rasatvamāpnuavanti ucyateyathā hi samānalakṣaṇāstulyapāṇipādodaraśarīrāḥ samānāṅgapratyaṅgā api puruṣāḥ kulaśīlavidyākarmaśilpavicakṣaṇatvādrājatvamāpnuvantitatraiva cānye lpabuddhayasteṣāmevānucarā bhavantitathāvibhāvānubhāvavyabhicāriṇaḥ sthāyibhāvānupāśritā bhavanti bahvāśrayatvāsvāmibhūtāḥ sthāyino bhāvāḥ tadvatsthānīyapuruṣaguṇabhūtā anye bhāvāstānguṇatayā śrayante sthāyibhāvā rasatvamāpnuvanti parijanabhūtā vyabhicāriṇo bhāvāḥ atrāhako dṛṣṭānta iti  yathā narendro bahujanaparivāro pi sa eva nāma labhate nānyaḥ sumahānapi puruṣaḥ tathā vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicāriparivṛtaḥ sthāyī bhāvo rasanāma  labhate  bhavati cātra ślokaḥyathā narāṇāṃ nṛpatiḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ ca yathā guruḥ evaṃ hi sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāvaḥ sthāyi mahāniha  BhN lakṣaṇaṃ khalu pūrvamabhihitameṣāṃ rasasaṃjñakānām idānīṃ bhāvasāmānyalakṣaṇamabhidhāsyāmaḥ tatra sthāyibhāvānvakṣyāmaḥratirnāma pramodātmikā ṛtumālyānulepanābharaṇabhojanavarabhavanānubhavanāprātikūlyādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tāmabhinayetsmitavadanamadhurakathanabhrūkṣepakaṭākṣādibhiranubhāvaiḥ atra ślokaḥiṣṭārthaviṣayaprāptyā ratirityupajāyate saumyatvādabhineyā sā vāṅmādhuryāṅgaceṣṭitaiḥ  BhN hāso nāma paraceṣṭānukaraṇakuhakāsambaddhapralāpapaurobhāgyamaurkhyādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tamabhinayetpūrvoktairhasitādibhiranubhāvaiḥ bhavati cātra ślokaḥparaceṣṭānukaraṇāddhāsaḥ samupajāyate smitahāsātihasitairabhineyaḥ sa paṇḍitaiḥ  BhN śoko nāma iṣṭajanaviyogavibhavanāśavadhabandhaduḥkhānubhanavanādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate  tasyāsrapātaparidevitavilapitavaivarṇyasvarabhedasrastagātratābhūmipatanasasvanaruditākranditadīrghaniḥśvasitajaḍatonmādamohamaraṇādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ  prayoktavyaḥ  ruditamatra trividham ānandajamārtijamīrṣyāsamudbhavaṃ ceti bhavanti cātrāryāḥānande pyārtikṛtaṃ trividhaṃ ruditaṃ sadā budhairjñeyam tasya tvabhinayayogānvibhāvagatitaḥ pravakṣyāmi  BhN harṣotphullakapolaṃ sānusmaraṇādapāṅgavisṛtāsram romāñcagātramanibhṛtamānandasamudbhavaṃ bhavati  BhN paryāptavimuktāsraṃ sasvanamasvasthagātragaticeṣṭam bhūminipātanivartitavilapitamityārtijaṃ bhavati  BhN prasphuritauṣṭhakapolaṃ saśiraḥkampaṃ tathā saniḥśvāsam bhrukuṭīkaṭākṣakuṭilaṃ strīṇāmīrṣyākṛtaṃ bhavati  BhN strīnīcaprakṛtiṣveṣa śoko vyasanasambhavaḥ dhairyeṇottamamadhyānāṃ nīcānāṃ ruditena ca  BhN krodho nāma ādharṣaṇākruṣṭakalahavivādapratikūlādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate asya vikṛṣṭanāsāpuṭodvṛttanayanasaṃdaṣṭhoṣṭhapuṭagaṇḍasphuraṇādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ ripujo gurujaścaiva praṇayiprabhavastathā bhṛtyajaḥ kṛtakaśceti krodhaḥ pañcavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN atrāryā bhavantibhṛkuṭīkuṭilotkaṭamukhaḥ sandaṣṭhoṣṭhaḥ spṛśankareṇa karam kruddhaḥ svabhujāprekṣī śatrau niryantraṇaṃ ruṣyet  BhN kiñcidavāṅgmukhadṛṣṭiḥ sāsrasvedāpamārjanaparaśca avyaktolbaṇaceṣṭo gurau vinayayantrito ruṣyet  BhN alpaprataravicāro vikirannaśrūṇyapāṅgavikṣepaiḥ sabhrukuṭisphuritoṣṭhaḥ praṇayopagatāṃ priyā ruṣyet  BhN atha parijane tu roṣastarjananirbhartsanākṣivistāraiḥ viprekṣaṇaiśca vividhairabhineyaḥ krūratārahitaḥ  BhN kāraṇamavekṣamāṇaḥ prāyeṇāyāsaliṅgasaṃyuktaḥ vīrarasāntaracārī kāryaḥ kṛtako bhavati kopaḥ  BhN utsāho nāma uttamaprakṛtiḥ sa cāviṣādaśaktidhairyaśauryādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tasya dhairyatyāgavaiśāradyādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ atra ślokaḥasammohādibhirvyakto vyavasāyanayātmakaḥ utsāhastvabhineyaḥ syādapramādotthitādibhiḥ  BhN bhayaṃ nāma strīnīcaprakṛtikam  gururājāparādhaśvāpadaśūnyāgārāṭavīparvatagahanagajāhidarśananirbhartsanakāntāradurdinaniśāndhakarolūkanaktañcarārāvaśravaṇādibhirvibhāvaiḥ  samutpadyate   tasya prakampitakaracaraṇahṛdayakampanastambhamukhaśoṣajihvāparilehanasvedavepathutrāsasaparitrāṇānveṣaṇadhāvanotkṛṣṭādibhiranubhavairabhinayaḥ  prayoktavyaḥ  atra ślokāḥgururājāparādhena raudrāṇāṃ cāpi darśanāt śravaṇādapi ghorāṇāṃ bhayaṃ mohena jāyate  BhN gātrakampanavitrāsairvaktraśoṣaṇasambhramaiḥvisphāritaikṣaṇaiḥ kāryamabhineyakriyāguṇaiḥ  BhN sattvavitrāsanodbhūtaṃ bhayamutpadyate nṛṇām ślokaḥnāsāpracchādaneneha gātrasaṅkocanena ca udvejanaiḥ sahṛllekhairjugupsāmabhinirdiśet  BhN vismayo nāma māyendrajālamānuṣakarmātiśayacitrapustaśilpavidyātiśayādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tasya praharṣapulakādibhiḥ  BhN evamete sthāyino bhāvā rasasaṃjñāḥ pratyavagantavyāḥ vyabhicāriṇa idānīṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ atrāhavyabhicāriṇa iti kasmāt ucyatevi abhi ityetāvupasargau cara iti gatyartho dhātuḥ vividhamābhimukhyena raseṣu carantīti vyabhicāriṇaḥ vāgaṅgasattvopetāḥ prayoge rasānnayantīti vyabhicāriṇaḥ atrāhakathaṃ nayantīti ucyatelokasiddhānta eṣaḥyathā sūrya idaṃ dinaṃ nakṣatraṃ vā nayatīti na ca tena bāhubhyāṃ skandhena vā nīyate kiṃ tu lokaprasiddhametat yathedaṃ sūryo nakṣatraṃ dina vā nayatīti evamete vyabhicāriṇa ityavagantavyāḥ tāniha saṅgrahābhihitāṃstrayastriṃśadvyabhicāriṇo bhāvān varṇayiṣyāmaḥ  tatra nirvedo nāma dāridryavyādhyavamānādhikṣepākruṣṭakrodhatāḍaneṣṭajanaviyogatattvajñānādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate strīnīcakusattvānām ruditaniḥśvasitocchvasitasampradhāraṇādibhiranubhāvaistamabhinayet atra ślokaḥdāridryeṣṭaviyogādyaiḥ nirvedo nāma jāyate sampradhāraṇaniḥśvāsaistasya tvabhinayo bhavet  BhN atrānuvaṃśye ārye bhavataḥiṣṭajanaviprayogāddāridryādvyādhitastathā duḥkhāt ṛddhiṃ parasya dṛṣṭvā nirvedo nāma sambhavati  BhN bāṣpapariplutanayanaḥ punaśca niḥśvāsanadīnamukhanetraḥ yogīva dhyānaparo bhavati hi nirvedavānpuruṣaḥ  BhN  glānirnāma vāntaviriktavyādhitaponiyamopavāsamanastāpātiśayamadanasevanātivyāyāmādhvagamanakṣutpipāsānidrācchedādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tasyāḥ sābhineyā mandabhramaṇena kampena  BhN gaditaiḥ kṣāmakṣāmairnetravikāraiśca dīnasañcāraiḥ ślathabhāvenāṅgānāṃ muhurmuhurnirdiśed glānim  BhN śaṅkā nāma sandehātmikā strīnīcaprabhavā pañcavidhaṃ syāttasyābhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ  BhN kaścinmatto gāyati roditi kaścittathā hasati kaścit paruṣavacanābhidhāyī kaścitkaścittathā svapiti  BhN uttamasattvaḥ śete hasati ca gāyati ca kāryā madavṛddhirnāṭyayogamāsādya kāryo madakṣayo vai yaḥ khalu pītvā praviṣṭaḥ syāt  BhN santrāsācchokādvā bhayātpraharṣācca kāraṇopagatāt utkramyāpi hi kāryo madapraṇāśaḥ kramāttajjñaiḥ  BhN ebhirbhāvaviśeṣairmado drutaṃ sampraṇāśamupayāti abhyudayasukhairvākyairyathaiva śokaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti  BhN śramo nāma adhvavyāyāmasevanādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tasya socchvāsairniḥśvasitaiḥ santāpaiścaiva hṛdayaśūnyatayā abhinetavyā cintā mṛjāvihīnairadhṛtyā ca  BhN moho nāma daivopaghātavyasanābhighātavyādhibhayāvegapūrvavairānusmaraṇādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tasya niścaitanyabhramaṇapatanāghūrṇanādarśanādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ atra ślokastāvadāryā caasthāne taskarāndṛṣṭvā trāsanairvividhairapi tatpratīkāraśūnyasya mohaḥ samupajāyate  BhN vyasanābhighātabhayapūrvavairasaṃsmaraṇarogajo mohaḥ sarvendriyasammohāttasyābhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ  BhN smṛtirnāma sukhaduḥkhakṛtānāṃ bhāvānāmanusmaraṇam sā ca dhūmākulanetratāṅgasaṅkocanavidhūnanātikrāntāpakrāntādibhiḥ kuñjarodbhramaṇakṛtaṃ nāma tvaritāpasarpaṇacañcalagamanabhayastambhavepathupaścādavalokanavismayādibhiḥ priyaśravaṇakṛtaṃ BhN jaḍatānāma sarvakāryāpratipattiḥ iṣṭāniṣṭaśravaṇadarśanavyādhyādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tāmabhinayedakathanāvibhāṣaṇatūṣṇīmbhāvāpratibhānimeṣanirīkṣaṇaparavaśatvādibhiranubhāvaiḥ atrāryā yojayet  BhN autsukyaṃ nāma iṣṭajanaviyogānusmaraṇodyānadarśanādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tasya dīrghaniḥśvasitādhomukhavicintananidrātandrīśayanābhilāṣādibhiranubhavairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ svapnaiśca yuñjīta  BhN vibodho nāma āhārapariṇāmanidrācchedasvapnāntatīvraśabdaśravaṇādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tamabhinayejjṛmbhaṇākṣiparimardanaśayanamokṣaṇādibhiranubhāvaiḥ atrāryā bhavatiāhāravipariṇāmācchabdasparśādibhiśca sambhūtaḥ pratibodhastvabhineyo jṛmbhaṇavadanākṣiparimardaiḥ  BhN amarṣo nāma vidyaiśvaryaśauryabalādhikairadhikṣiptasyāvamānitasya vā samutpadyate tamabhinayecchiraḥkampanaprasvedanādhomukhacintanadhyānādhyavasāyopāyasahāyānveṣaṇādibhiranubhāvaiḥ atra ślokauākṣiptānāṃ sabhāmadhye vidyāśauryabalādhikaiḥ nṝṇāmutsāhasaṃyogādamarṣo nāma jāyate  BhN utsāhādhyavasāyābhyāmadhomukhavicintanaiḥ śiraḥprakampasvedādyaistaṃ prayuñjīta paṇḍitaḥ  BhN avahitthaṃ nāma ākārapracchādanātmakam tacca lajābhayāpajayagauravajaihmayādibhirvibhāviḥ samutpadyate tasyānyathākathanāvalokitakathābhaṅgakṛtakadhairyādibhiranubhāvairabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ atra śloko bhavatidhārṣṭyajaihmyādisambhītamavahitthaṃ bhayatmakam taccāgaṇanayā kāryaṃ nātīvottarabhāṣaṇāt  BhN ugratā āma cauryābhigrahāṇanṛpāparādhāsatpralāpādibhirvibhāvaiḥ samutpadyate tāṃ ca vadhabandhanatāḍananirbhatsanādibhiranubhāvairabhinayet atrāryā bhavaticauryābhigrahanavaśānnṛpāparādhādathogratā bhavti vadhabandhatāḍanādibhiranubhāvairabhinayastasyāḥ  BhN bhavati cātra ślokaḥnānāśātrārthabodhena matiḥ saṃjāyate nṛṇām śiṣyopadeśārthakṛtastasyāstvabhinayo bhavet  BhN vyādhirnāma vātapittakaphasannipātaprabhavaḥ tasya jvarādayo viśeṣāḥ jvarastu dvividhaḥ saśītaḥ sadāhaśca  tatra saśīto nāma pravepitasarvāṅgopkampananikuñcanāgnyabhilāṣaromāñcahanuvalananāsāvikūnanamukhaśoṣaṇaparidevitādibhiranubhāvairabhineyaḥ sadāho nāma vikṣiptāṅgakaracaraṇabhūmyabhilāṣānulepanaśītābhilāṣaparidevanamukhaśoṣotkruṣṭādibhiranubhāvaiḥ ye cānye vyādhayaste pi khalu mukhavikūṇanagātrastambhasrastākṣiniḥśvasanastanitotkruṣṭavepanādibhiranubhāvairabhineyāḥ atra śloko bhavatisamāsatastu vyādhīnāṃ kartavyo bhinayo budhaiḥ srastāṅgagātravikṣepaistathā mukhavikūṇanaiḥ  BhN unmādo nāma iṣṭajanaviyogavibhavanāśābhighātavātapittaśleṣmaprakopādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate  tamanimittahasitaruditotkruṣṭāsambaddhapralāpaśayitopaviṣṭotthitapradhāvitanṛttagītapaṭhitabhasmapāṃsvavadhūlanatṛṇanirmālyakucelacīraghaṭakakapālaśarāvābharaṇadhāraṇopabhogairanekaiścānavasthitaiśceṣṭānukaraṇādibhiranubhāvairabhinayet atrārye bhavataḥiṣṭajanavibhavanāśādabhighātādvātapittakaphakopāt vividhāccittavikārādunmādo nāma sambhavati  BhN animittaruditahasitopaviṣṭagītapradhāvitotkruṣṭaiḥ anyaiśca vikārairakṛtairunmādaṃ samprayuñjīta  BhN maraṇaṃ nāma vyādhijamabhighātajañca tatra yadāntrayakṛcchūladoṣavaiṣamyagaṇḍapiṭakajvaraviṣūcikādibhirutpadyate tadvyādhiprabhavam abhighātajaṃ tu śastrāhidaṃśaviṣapānaśvāpadagajaturagarathapaśuyānapātavināśaprabhavam etayorabhinayaviśeṣānvakṣyāmaḥtatra vyādhijaṃ viṣaṇṇagātrāvyāyatāṅgaviceṣṭitanimīlitanayanahikkāśvāsopetānavekṣitaparijanāvyaktākṣarakathanādibhiranubhāvairabhinayet atra śloko bhavativyādhīnāmekabhāvo hi maraṇābhinayaḥ smṛtaḥ viṣaṇṇagātrairniśceṣṭairindriayaiśca vivarjitaḥ  BhN abhighātaje tu nānāprakārābhinayaviśeṣāḥ śastrakṣatāhidaṣṭaviṣapītagajādipatitaśvāpadahatāḥ yathā tatra śastrakṣate tāvatsahasā bhūmipatanavepanasphuraṇādibhirabhinayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ ahidaṣṭaviṣapītayorviṣayogo yathā kārśyavepathuvidāhahikkāphenaskandhabhaṅgajaḍatāmaraṇānītyaṣṭau viṣavegāḥ atra ślokau bhavataḥkārśyaṃ tu prathame vege dvitīye vepathurbhavet dāhaṃ tṛtīye hikkāṃ ca caturthe samprayojayet  BhN phenañca pañcame kuryātṣaṣṭhe skandhasya bhañjanam jaḍatāṃ saptame kuryādaṣṭame maraṇaṃ bhavet  BhN atrāryā bhavatiśvāpadagajaturagarathodbhavaṃ tu paśuyānapatanajaṃ vāpi śāstrakṣatavatkuryādanavekṣitagātrasañcāram  BhN ityeva maraṇaṃ jñeyaṃ nānāvasthāntarātmakam prayoktavyaṃ budhaiḥ samyagyathā bhavāṅgaceṣṭitaiḥ  BhN trāso nāma vidyudulkāśanipātanirghātāmbudharamahāsattvapaśuravādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tamabhinayetsaṃkṣiptāṅgotkampanavepathustambharomāñcagadgadapralāpādibhiranubhāvaiḥ atra śloko bhavatimahābhairavanādadyaistrāsaḥ samupajāyate srastāṅgākṣinimeṣaiśca tasya tvabhinayo bhavet  BhN vitarko nāma sandehavimarśavipratipattyādibhirvibhāvairutpadyate tamabhinayedvividhavicāritapraśnasampradhāraṇamantrasaṅgūhanādibhiranubhāvaiḥ atra śloko bhavativicāraṇādisambhūtaḥ sandehātiśayātmakaḥ vitarkaḥ so bhineyastu śirobhrūkṣepakampanaiḥ  BhN  evamete trayastriṃśadvyabhicāriṇo bhāvā deśakālāvasthānurūpyeṇāmagataparagatamadhyasthā uttamamadhyamādhamaiḥ strīpuṃsaiḥ svaprayogavaśādupapādyā  iti  trayastriṃśadime bhāvā vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ sāttvikāṃstu punarbhāvānpravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN atrāhakimanye bhāvāḥ sattvena vinābhinīyante yasmāducyateete sāttvikā iti atrocyateiha hi sattvaṃ nāma manaḥprabhavam tacca samāhitamanastvāducyate manasaḥ samādhau sattvaniṣpattirbhavati tasya ca yo sau svabhāvo romāñcāśruvaivarṇyādilakṣaṇo yathābhāvopagataḥ sa na śakyo nyamanasā kartumiti lokasvabhāvānukaraṇatvācca nāṭyasya sattvamīpsitam ko dṛṣṭāntaḥiha hi nāṭyādharmipravṛttāḥ sukhaduḥkhakṛtā bhāvāstathā sattvaviśuddhāḥ kāryā yathā sarūpā bhavanti tatra duḥkhaṃ nāma rodanātmakaṃ tatkathamaduḥkhitena sukhaṃ ca praharṣātmakamasukhitena vābhineyam etadevāsya sattvaṃ yat duḥkhitena sukhitena vāśruromāñcau darśiyitavyau iti kṛtvā sāttvikā bhāvā ityabhivyākhyātāḥ ta imestambhaḥ svedo tha romāñcaḥ svarabhedo tha vepathuḥ vaivarṇyamaśrupralaya ityaṣṭau sāttvikā matāḥ  BhN atrāryāḥtatrakrodhabhayaharṣalajāduḥkhaśramarogatāpaghātebhyaḥ vyāyāmaklamadharmaiḥ svedaḥ sampīḍanāccaiva  BhN harṣabhayaśokavismayaviṣādaroṣādisambhavaḥ stambhaḥ śītabhayaharṣaroṣasparśajarārogajaḥ kampaḥ  BhN ānandāmarṣābhyāṃ dhūmāñjanajṛmbhaṇādbhayācchokāt animeṣaprekṣaṇataḥ śītādrogādbhavedaśru  BhN śītakrodhabhayaśramarogaklamatāpajaṃ ca vaivarṇyam sparśabhayaśītaharṣāt krodhādrogācca romāñcaḥ  BhN svarabhedo bhayaharṣakrodhajarāraukṣyarogamadajanitaḥ śramamūrchamadanidrābhighātamohādibhiḥ pralayaḥ  BhN evamete budhairjñeyā bhāvā hyaṣṭau tu sāttvikāḥ karma caiṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabhāvānubhāvakam  BhN niḥsaṃjño niṣprakampaśca sthitaḥ śūnyajaḍākṛtiḥ skannagātratayā caiva stambhaṃ tvabhinayedbudhaḥ  BhN vyajanagrahaṇāccāpi svedāpanayanena ca svedasyābhinayo yojyastathā vātābhilāṣataḥ  BhN muhuḥ kaṇṭikitatvena tathollukasanena ca pulakena ca romāñcaṃ gātrasparśena darśayet  BhN svarabhedo bhinetavyo bhinnagadgadanisvanaiḥ vepanātsphuraṇātkampādvepathuṃ sampradarśayet  BhN mukhavarṇaparāvṛttyā nāḍīpīḍanayogataḥ vaivarṇyamabhinetavyaṃ prayatnāttaddhi duṣkaram  BhN bāṣpāmbuplutanetratvānnetrasaṃmārjanena ca muhuraśrukaṇāpātairasraṃ tvabhinayedbudhaḥ  BhN niśceṣṭo niṣprakampatvādavyaktaśvasitādapi mahīnipatanāccāpi pralayābhinayo bhavet  BhN ekonapañcāśadime yathāvadbhāvāstryavasthā gaditā mayeha bhūyaśca ye yatra rase niyojyāstān śrotumarhanti ca vipramukhyāḥ  BhN atra ślokāḥśaṅkāvyādhistathāglāniścintāsūyā bhayaṃ tathā vismayaśca vitarkaśca stambhaścapalatā tathā  BhN romāñcaharṣau nidrā ca tathonmādamadāvapi svedaścaivāvahitthaṃ ca pralayo vepathustathā  BhN viṣādaśramanirvedā garvāvegau dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ matirmoho vibodhaśca suptamautsukyavarjite  BhN krodhāmarṣau ca hāsaśca śoko pasmāra eva ca dainyaṃ ca maraṇaṃ caiva ratirutsāhasaṃyutā  BhN trāsavaivarṇyaruditaiḥ svarabhedaḥ śamo pi ca jaḍatā ca tathā ṣaṭ ca catvāriṃśatprakīrtitāḥ  BhN ālasyaugryajugupsākhyairevaṃ bhāvaistu varjitāḥ udbhāvayanti śṛṅgāraṃ sarve bhāvāḥ svasaṃjñayā  BhN yathāvasaramete hi sthāyisañcārisattvajāḥ uddīpayanti śṛṅgāraṃ rasamāsādya saṃjñitam  BhN glāniḥ śaṅkā hyasūyā ca śramaścapalatā tathā suptaṃ nidrāvahitthaṃ ca hāsye bhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BhN nirvedaścaiva cintā ca dainyaṃ glānyāsrameva cajaḍatā maraṇaṃ caiva vyādhiśca karuṇe smṛtāḥ  BhN garvo sūyā madotsāhāvāvego marṣa eva ca krodhaścapalataugryaṃ ca vijñeyā raudrasambhavāḥ  BhN asammohastathotsāha āvego harṣa eva ca matiścaiva tathogratvamamarṣo mada eva ca  BhN romāñcaḥ svarabhedaśca krodho sūyā dhṛtistathā garvaścaiva vitarkaśca vīre bhāvā bhavanti hi  BhN svedaśca vepathuścaiva romāñco gadgadastathā trāsaśca maraṇaścaiava vaivarṇyaṃ ca bhayānake  BhN apasmārastathonmādo viṣādo mada eva ca mṛtyurvyādhirbhayaṃ caiva bhāvā bībhatsasaṃśrayāḥ  BhN stambhaḥ svedaśca mohaśca romāñco vismayastathā āvego jaḍatā harṣo mūrchā caivādbhutāśrayāḥ  BhN ye tvete sāttvikā bhāvā nānābhinayasaṃśritāḥ raseṣveteṣu sarve te jñeyā nāṭyaprayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN na hyekarasajaṃ kāvyaṃ kiñcidasti prayogataḥ bhāvo vāpi raso vāpi pravṛttirvṛttireva ca  BhN  bahūnāṃ samavetānāṃ rūpaṃ yasya bhavedbahu sa mantavyo rasaḥ sthāyī śeṣāḥ sañcāriṇo matāḥ  BhN dīpayantaḥ pravartante ye punaḥ sthāyinaṃ rasam te tu sañcāriṇo jñeyāste hi sthāyitvamāgatāḥ  BhN vibhāvānubhāvayuto hyaṅgavastusamāśrayaḥ saṃcāribhistu saṃyuktaḥ sthāyyeva tu raso bhavet  BhN sthāyī sattvātirekeṇa prayoktavyaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ sañcāryākāramātreṇa sthāyī yasmādavasthitaḥ  BhN ye tvete sāttvikā bhāvā nānābhinayayojitāḥ raseṣveteṣu sarveṣu te jñeyā nāṭyakovidaiḥ  BhN na hyekarasajaṃ kāvyaṃ naikabhāvaikavṛttikam vimarde rāgamāyāti prayuktaṃ hi prayatnataḥ  BhN bhāvā vāpi rasā vāpi pravṛttirvṛttireva vā bībhatsādbhutaśāntānāṃ traividhyaṃ nātra kathyate  BhN ṣaṇṇāṃ rasānāṃ traividhyaṃ nānābhāvārasānvitam sattvaprayojito hyarthaḥ prayogo tra virājate viditvā hi virājante loke citraṃ hi durlabham  BhN nānābhāvārthasaṃpannāḥ sthāyisattvābhicāriṇaḥ puṣpāvakīrṇāḥ kartavyāḥ kāvyeṣu hi rasā budhaiḥ  BhN evaṃ rasāśca bhāvāśca vyavasthā nāṭake smṛtāḥ ya evametāñjānāti sa gacchetsiddhimuttamām  BhN iti śrībhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre bhāvavyañjako nāma saptamo dhyāyaḥaṣṭamo dhyāyaḥṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥbhāvānāṃ ca rasānāṃ ca samutthānaṃ yathākramam tvatprasādācchrutaṃ sarvamicchāmo vedituṃ punaḥ  BhN nāṭye katividhaḥ kāryaḥ tajjñairabhinayakramaḥ kataṃ vābhinayo hyeṣa katibhedastu kīrtitaḥ  BhN sarvametadyathātattvaṃ kathayasva mahāmune yo yathābhinayo yasmin yoktavyaḥ siddhimicchatā  BhN teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ pratyuvāca punarvākyaṃ caturo bhinayān prati  BhN ahaṃ vaḥ kathayiṣyāmi nikhilena tapodhanāḥ yasmādabhinayo hyeṣa vidhivat samudāhṛtam  BhN yaduktaṃ catvāro bhinaya iti tān varṇayiṣyāmaḥ atrāhaabhinaya iti kasmāt atrocyateabhītyupasargaḥ ṇīñ iti prāpaṇārthako dhātuḥ asyābhinītyevaṃ vyavasthitasya erajityacpratyatyayāntasyābhinaya ityevaṃ rūpaṃ siddham etacca dhātvarthānuvacanenāvadhāryaṃ bhavati atra ślokauabhipūrvastu ṇīñ dhāturābhimukhyārthanirṇaye yasmātpadārthānnayati tasmādabhinayaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN vibhāvayati yasmācca nānārthān hi prayogataḥ śākhāṅgopāṅgasaṃyuktastasmādabhinayaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN caturvidhaścaiva bhavennāṭyasyābhinayo dvijāḥ anekabhedavāhūyaṃ nāṭyaṃ hyasmin pratiṣṭhitam  BhN āṅgiko vācikaścaiva hyāhāryaḥ sāttvikastathā jñeyastvabhinayo viprāḥ caturdhā parikalpitaḥ  BhN sāttvikaḥ pūrvamuktastu bhāvaiśca sahito mayā aṅgābhinayamevādau gadato me nibodhata  BhN trividhastvāṅgiko dyneyaḥ śārīro mukhajastathā tathā ceṣṭākṛtaścaiva śākhāṅgopāṅgasaṃyutaḥ  BhN śirohastakaṭīdakṣaḥ pārśvapādasamanvitaḥ aṅgapratyaṅgasaṃyuktaḥ ṣaḍaṅgo nāṭyasaṃgrahaḥ  BhN tasya śirohastoraḥpārśvakaṭīpādataḥ ṣaḍaṅgāni netrabhrūnāsādharakapolacibukānyupāṅgāni  BhN asya śākhā ca nṛttaṃ ca tathaivāṅkura eva ca vastūnyabhinayasyeha vijñeyāni prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN āṅgikastu bhavecchākhā hyaṅkuraḥ sūcanā bhavet aṅgahāraviniṣpannaṃ nṛttaṃ tu karaṇāśrayam  BhN mukhaje bhinaye viprā nānābhāvarasāśraye śirasaḥ prathamaṃ karma gadato me nibodhata  BhN ākampitaṃ kampitaṃ ca dhūtaṃ vidhutameva ca parivāhitamādhūtamavadhūtaṃ tathāñcitam  BhN nihañcitaṃ parāvṛttamutkṣiptaṃ cāpyadhogatam lolitaṃ caiva vijñeyaṃ trayodaśavidhaṃ śiraḥ  BhN śanairākampanādūrdhvamadhaścākampitaṃ bhavet drutaṃ tadeva bahuśaḥ kampitaṃ kampitaṃ śiraḥ  BhN ṛjusthitasya cordhvādhaḥ kṣepādākampitaṃ bhavet bahuśaścalitaṃ yacca tatkampitamihocyate  BhN saṃjñopadeśapṛcchāsu svabhāvābhāṣaṇe tathā nirdeśāvāhane caiva bhavedākampitaṃ śiraḥ  BhN roṣe vitarke vijñāne pratijñāne tha tarjane praśnātiśayavākyeṣu śiraḥ kampitamiṣyate  BhN śiraso recanaṃ yattu śanaistad dhutamiṣyate drutamārecanādetadvidhutaṃ tu bhavecchiraḥ  BhN anīpsite viṣāde ca vismaye pratyayaṃ tathā pārśvāvalokane śūnye pratiṣedhe dhutaṃ śiraḥ  BhN śītagraste bhayārte ca trāsite jvarite tathā pītamātre tathā madye vidhutaṃ tu bhavecchiraḥ  BhN paryāyaśaḥ pārśvagataṃ śiraḥ syāt parivāhitam ādhūtamucyate tiryak sakṛdudvāhitaṃ tu yat  BhN sādhane vismaye harṣe smite cāmarṣite tathā vicāre vihṛte caiva līlāyāṃ parivāhitam  BhN garvecchādarśane caiva pārśvasthordhvanirīkṣaṇeādhutaṃ tu śiro jñeyamātmasambhāvanādiṣu  BhN yadadhaḥ sakṛdākṣiptamavadhūtaṃ tu tacchiraḥ sandeśāvāhanālāpasaṃjñādiṣu nadiṣyate  BhN kiñcit pārśvanatagrīvaṃ śiro vijñeyamañcitam vyādhite mūrchite matte cintāyāṃ hanudhāraṇam  BhN utkṣipāṃsāvasaktaṃ yatkuñcitabhrūlataṃ śiraḥ nihañcitaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ strīṇāmetat prayojayet  BhN garve māne vilāse ca bivvoke kilakiñcite moṭṭāyite kuṭṭamite stambhamāne nihañcitam  BhN parāvṛttānukaraṇāt parāvṛttamihocyate tat syānmukhāpaharaṇe pṛṣṭhataḥ prekṣaṇādiṣu  BhN utkṣiptaṃ cāpi vijñeyamunmukhāvasthitaṃ śiraḥ prāṃśudivyāstrayogeṣu syādutkṣiptaṃ prayogataḥ  BhN adhomukhaṃ sthitaṃ cāpi budhāḥ prāhuradhogatam lajjāyāṃ ca praṇāme ca duḥkhe cādhogataṃ śiraḥ  BhN sarvato bhramaṇāccaiva śiraḥ syāt parilolitam mūrcchāvyādhimadāveśagrahanidrādiṣu smṛtam  BhN ṛjusvabhāvasaṃsthānaṃ prākṛtaṃ tu svabhāvajam maṃgalyādhyayanadhyānasvabhāvajayakarmasu  BhN ebhyo nye bahavo bhedā lokābhinayasaṃśritāḥ te ca lokasvabhāvena prayoktavyā prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN trayodaśavidhaṃ hyetacchiraḥkarma mayoditam ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dṛṣṭīnāmiha lakṣaṇam  BhN kāntā bhayānakā hāsyā karuṇā cādbhutā tathā raudro vīrā ca bībhatsā vijñeyā rasadṛṣṭayaḥ  BhN snigdhā hṛṣṭā ca dīnā ca kruddhā dṛptā bhayānvitā jugupsitā vismitā ca sthāyibhāveṣu dṛṣṭayaḥ  BhN śūnyā ca malinā caiva śrāntā lajjānvitā tathā glānā ca śaṅkitā caiva viṣaṇṇā mukulā tathā  BhN kuñcitā cābhitaptā ca jihmā salalitā tathā vitarkitārdhamukulā vibhrāntā viluptā tathā  BhN ākekarā vikośā ca trastā ca madirā tathā ṣaṭtriṃśad dṛṣṭayo hyetā tāsu nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  BhN asya dṛṣṭividhānasya nānābhāvarasāśrayam lakṣaṇaṃ sampravakṣyami yathākarma prayogataḥ  BhN harṣaprasādajanitā kāntātyarthaṃ samanyathā sabhrūkṣepakaṭākṣā ca śṛṅgāre dṛṣṭirikṣyate  BhN prodvṛttaniṣṭabdhapuṭā sphuradudvṛttatārakā dṛṣṭirbhayānākātyarthaṃ bhītā jñeyā bhayānake  BhN kramādākuñcitapuṭā vibhrāntākulatārakā hāsyā dṛṣṭistu kartavyā kuhakābhinayaṃ prati  BhN patitordhvapuṭā sāsrā manyumantharatārakā nāsāgrānugatā dṛṣṭiḥ karuṇā karuṇe rase  BhN yā tvākuñcitapakṣmāgrā sāścaryoddhattatārakā saumyā vikasitāntā ca sādbhutā dṛṣṭiradbhute  BhNkr ūrā rūkṣāruṇodvṛtaniṣṭabdhapuṭatārakā bhrukuṭīkuṭilā dṛṣṭiḥ raudre raudrī rasā smṛtā  BhN dīptā vikasitā kṣubdhā gambhīrā samatārakā utphullamadhyā dṛṣṭistu vīrā vīrarasāśrayā  BhN nikuñcitapuṭāpāṅgā ghūrṇopaplutatārakā saṃśliṣṭasthirapakṣmā ca bībhatsā dṛṣṭiriṣyate  BhN nāsāgrasaktā nimiṣā tathādhobhāgacāriṇī ākekarapuṭā śānte śāntā dṛṣṭirbhavedasau  BhN rasajā dṛṣṭayo hyetā vijñeyā lakṣaṇānvitā ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sthāyibhāvasamāśrayāḥ  BhN vyākośamadhyā madhurā sthitatārābhilāṣiṇī sānandāśruplutā dṛṣṭiḥ snigdheyaṃ ratibhāvajā  BhN calā hasitagarbhā ca viśattārānimeṣiṇī kiñcidākuñcitā dṛṣṭiḥ hṛṣṭā hāse prakīrtitā  BhN avasrastottarapuṭā kiñcitsaraṃbdhatārakā mandasañcāriṇī dīnā sā śoke dṛṣṭiriṣyate  BhN rūkṣā sthiroddhatapuṭā niṣṭabdhoddhṛttatārakā kuṭilā bhrukuṭirdṛṣṭiḥ kruddhā krodhe vidhīyate  BhN saṃsthite tārke yasyāḥ sthitā vikasitā tathā sattvamudgiratī dṛptā dṛṣṭirutsāhasaṃbhavā  BhN visphāritobhayapuṭā bhayakampitatārakā niṣkrāntamadhyā dṛṣṭistu bhayabhāve bhayānvitā  BhN saṃkocitapuṭādhyāmā dṛṣṭirmīlitatārakā pakṣmoddeśāt samudvignā jugupsāyāṃ jugupsitā  BhN bhṛśamudvṛttatārā ca naṣṭobhayapuṭānvitā samā vikasitā dṛṣṭirvismitā vismaye smṛtā  BhN sthāyibhāvāśrayā hyetā vijñeyāḥ dṛṣṭayo budhaiḥ saṃcāriṇīnāṃ dṛṣṭīnāṃ sampravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN samatārā samapuṭā niṣkampā śūnyadarśanā bāhyārthāgrāhiṇī dhyāmā śūnyā dṛṣṭiḥ prakīrtitā  BhN praspandamānapakṣmāgrā nātyarthamukulaiḥ puṭaiḥ malināntā ca malinā dṛṣṭirvismitatārakā  BhN śramapramlāpitapuṭā kṣāmā kuñcitalocanā sannā patitatārā ca śrāntā dṛṣṭiḥ prakīrtitā  BhN kiñcidañcitapakṣmāgrā patitordhvapuṭā hriyā trapādhogatatārā ca dṛṣṭirlajjānvitā tu sā  BhN mlānabhrupuṭapakṣmā yā śithilā mandacāriṇī kramapravṛṣṭatārā ca glānā dṛṣṭistu sā smṛtā  BhN kiñciccalā sthirā kiñcidudgatā tiryagāyatā gūḍhā cakitatārā ca śaṅkitā dṛṣṭiriṣyate  BhN viṣādavistīrṇapuṭā paryastāntā nimeṣiṇī kiñcinniṣṭabdhatārā ca kāryā dṛṣṭīrviṣādinī  BhN sphuradāśliṣṭapakṣmāgrā mukulordhvapuṭāñcitā sukhonmīlitatārā ca mukulā dṛṣṭiriṣyate  BhN ānikuñcitapakṣmāgrā puṭairākuñcitaistathā saṃnikuñcitatārā ca kuñcitā dṛṣṭiriṣyate  BhN mandāyamānatārā yā puṭaiḥ pracalitaistathā santāpopaplutā dṛṣṭirabhitaptā tu savyathā  BhN lambitākuñcitapuṭā śanaistiryaṅ nirīkṣiṇī nigūḍhā gūḍhatārā ca jihmā dṛṣṭirudāhṛtā  BhN madhurākuñcitāntā ca sabhrūkṣepā ca sasmitā samamanyavikārā ca dṛṣṭiḥ sā lalitā smṛtā  BhN vitarkodvartitapuṭā tathaivotphullatārakā adhogatavicārā ca dṛṣṭireṣā vitarkitā  BhN ardhavyākośapakṣmā ca hlādārdhamukulaiḥ puṭaiḥ smitārśamukulā dṛṣṭiḥ kiñcillulitatārakā  BhN anavasthitatārā ca vibhrāntākuladarśanā vistīrṇotphullamadhyā ca vibhrāntā dṛṣṭirucyate  BhN puṭau prasphuritau yasya niṣṭabdhau patitau punaḥ viluptodvṛttatārā ca dṛṣṭireṣā tu viplutā  BhN ākuñcitapuṭāpāṅgā saṅgatārdhanimeṣiṇī muhurvyāvṛttatārā ca dṛṣṭirākekarā smṛtā  BhN vikośitobhayapuṭā protphullā cānimeṣiṇī anavasthitasañcārā vikośā dṛṣṭirucyate  BhN trāsodvṛttapuṭā yā tu tathotkampitatārakā santrāsotphullamadhyā ca trastā dṛṣṭirudāhṛtā  BhN āghurṇamānamadhyā yā kṣāmāntāñcitalocanā dṛṣṭirvikasitāpāṅgā madirā taruṇe made  BhN kiñcidākucitapuṭā hyanavasthitatārakā tathā calitapakṣmā ca dṛṣṭirmadhyamade bhavet  BhN sanimeṣānimeṣā ca kiñcid darśitatārakā adhobhāgacarī dṛṣṭiradhame tu made smṛtā  BhN ityevaṃ lakṣitā hyetā ṣaṭatriṃśad dṛṣṭayo mayā rasajā sahajāścāsāṃ viniyogaṃ nibodhata  BhN rasajāsstu raseṣveva sthāyiṣu sthāyidṛṣṭayaḥ śṛṇuta vyabhicāriṇyaḥ sañcāriṣu yathāsthitāḥ  BhN śūnyā dṛṣṭistu cintāyāṃ stambhe cāpi prakīrtitā nirvede cāpi malinā vaivarṇye ca vidhīyate  BhN śrāntā śramārte svede ca lajāyāṃ lalitā tathā apasmāre tathā vyādhau glānyāṃ glānā vidhīyate  BhN śaṅkāyāṃ śaṅkitā jñeyā viṣādārthe viṣādinī nidrāsvapnasukhārtheṣu mukulā dṛṣṭiriṣyate  BhN kuñcitāsūyitāniṣṭaduṣprekṣākṣivyathāṣu ca abhitaptā ca nirvede hyabhighātābhitāpayoḥ  BhN jihmā dṛṣṭirasūyāyāṃ jaḍatālasyayostathā dhṛtau harṣe salalitā smṛtau tarke ca tarkitā  BhN ālhādiṣvardhamukulā gandhasparśasukhādiṣu vibhrāntā dṛṣṭirāvege sambhrame vibhrame tathā  BhN viluptā capalonmādaduḥkhārtimaraṇādiṣu ākekarā durāloke vicchedapreakṣiteṣu ca  BhN vibodhagarvāmarśaugryamatiṣu syādvikośitā trastā trāse bhaved dṛṣṭirmadirā ca madeṣviti  BhN ṣaṭatriṃśad dṛṣṭayo hyetā yathāvat samudāhṛtāḥ rasajānāṃ tu dṛṣṭīnāṃ bhāvajānāṃ tathaiava ca  BhN tārāpuṭabhruvāṃ karma gadato me nibodhata bhramaṇaṃ valanaṃ pātaścalanaṃ sampraveśanam  BhN vivartanaṃ samudvṛttaṃ niṣkrāmaḥ prākṛtaṃ tathā puṭāntarmaṇḍalāvṛttistārayorbhramaṇaṃ smṛtam  BhN valanaṃ gamanaṃ tryasraṃ pātanaṃ srastatā tathā calanaṃ kampanaṃ jñeyaṃ praveśo ntaḥpraveśanam  BhN vivartanaṃ kaṭākṣastu samudvṛttaṃ samunnatiḥ niṣkrāmo nirgamaḥ proktaḥ prākṛtaṃ tu svabhāvajam  BhN athaiṣāṃ rasabhāveṣu viniyogaṃ nibodhata bhramaṇaṃ calanodvṛtte niṣkrāmo vīraraudrayoḥ  BhN niṣkrāmaṇaṃ saṃvalanaṃ kartavyaṃ tu bhayānake hāsyabībhatsayoścāpi praveśanamiheṣyate  BhN pātanaṃ karuṇe kāryaṃ niṣkrāmaṇamathādbhute prākṛtaṃ śeṣabhāveṣu śṛṅgāre ca vivartitam  BhN svabhāvasiddhamevaitat karmaṃ lokakriyāśrayam evaṃ raseṣu bhāveṣu tārākarmāṇi yojayet  BhN athātraiva pravakṣyāmi prakāran darśanasya tu samaṃ sācaynuvṛtte ca hyālokitavilokite  BhN pralokitollokite cāpyavalokitameva ca samatāraṃ ca saumyaṃ ca yaddṛṣṭaṃ tat samaṃ smṛtam  BhN pakṣmāntaragatatāraṃ ca tryasraṃ sācīkṛtaṃ tu tat rūpanirvarṇanā yuktamanuvṛttamiti smṛtam  BhN sahasā darśanaṃ yat syāttadālokitamucyate vilokitaṃ pṛṣṭatastu pārśvābhyāṃ tu pralokitam  BhN ūrdhvamullokitaṃ jñeyamavalokitamapyadhaḥ ityeṣu darśanavidhiḥ sarvabhāvarasāśrayaḥ  BhN tārākṛto syānugataṃ puṭakarma nibodhata unmeṣaśca nimeṣaśca prasṛtaṃ kuñcitaṃ samam  BhN vivartitaṃ sa sphuritaṃ pihitaṃ savitāḍitam viśleṣaḥ puṭayoryastu sa tūnmeṣaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN samāgamo nimeṣaḥ syādāyāmaḥ prasṛtaṃ bhavet ākucitaṃ kuñcitaṃ syāt samaṃ svābhāvikaṃ smṛtam  BhN vivartitaṃ samudvṛttaṃ sphuritaṃ spanditaṃ tathā sthagitaṃ pihitaṃ proktamāhataṃ tu vitāḍitam  BhN athaiṣaṃ rasabhāveṣu viniyogaṃ nibodhata krodhe vivartitaṃ kāryo nimeṣonmeṣaṇaiḥ saha  BhN vismayārtheṣu harṣe ca vīre ca prasṛtaṃ smṛtam aniṣṭadarśane gandhe rase sparśe ca kuñcitam  BhN śṛṅgāre ca samaṃ kāryamīrṣyāsu sphuritaṃ tathā suptamūrcchitavātoṣṇadhūmavarṣāñjanārtiṣu  BhN netraroge ca pihitamabhighāte vitāḍitam ityevaṃ rasabhāveṣu tārakāpuṭayorvidhiḥ  BhN kāryānugatamasyaiva bhruvoḥ karma nibodhata utkṣepaḥ pātanaścaiva bhrukuṭī caturaṃ bhruvoḥ  BhN kuñcitaṃ recitaṃ caiva sahajaṃ ceti saptadhā bhruvorunnatirutkṣepaḥ samamekaikaśo pi vā  BhN anenaiva krameṇaiva pātanaṃ syādadhomukham bhruvormūlasamutkṣepāt bhrukuṭī parikīrtitā  BhN caturaṃ kiciducchvāsānmadhurāyatayā bhruvoḥ ekasyā ubhayorvāpi mṛdubhaṅgastu kuñcitam  BhN ekasyā eva lalitādutkṣepādrecitaṃ bhruvaḥ sahajātaṃ tu sahajaṃ karma svābhāvikaṃ smṛtam  BhN athaiṣāṃ sampravakṣyāmi rasabhāvaprayojanam kope vitarke helāyāṃ līlādau sahaje tathā  BhN śravaṇe darśane caiva bhruvamekāṃ samutkṣipet utkṣepo vismaye harṣe roṣe caiava dvayorapi  BhN āsūyitajugupsāyāṃ hāsye ghrāṇe ca pātanam krodhasthāneṣu dīpteṣu yojayet bhrukuṭiṃ budhaḥ  BhN śṛṅgāre lalite saumye sukhe sparśe prabodhane evaṃ vidheṣu bhāveṣu caturaṃ tu prayojayet  BhN strīpuruṣayośca saṃlāpe nānāvasthāntarātmake moṭṭāyite kuṭṭamite vilāse kilakiñcite  BhN nikuñcitaṃ tu kartavyaṃ nṛtte yojyaṃ tu recitam anāviddheṣu bhāveṣu vidyāt svābhāvikaṃ budhaḥ  BhN ityevaṃ tu bhruvaḥ proktaṃ nāsākarma nibodhata natā mandā vikṛṣṭā ca socchvāsā ca vikūṇitā  BhN svābhāvikā ceti budhaiḥ ṣaḍvidhā nāsikā smṛtā natā muhuḥśliṣṭapuṭā mandā tu nibhṛtā smṛtā  BhN vikṛṣṭotphullitapuṭā socchvāsā kṛṣṭamārutā vikūṇitā saṃkucitā samā svābhāvikā smṛtā  BhN nāsikālakṣaṇaṃ hyetat viniyogaṃ nibodhata madotkampasamāyukte nārīṇāmanurodhane  BhN niḥśvāse ca natā kāryā nāsikā nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ vicchinnamandarudite socchvāse ca natā smṛtā  BhN nirvegautsukyacintāsu mandā śoke ca yojayet tīvragandhe vikṛṣṭāṃ tau raudre vīre tathaiva ca  BhN iṣṭaghrāṇe tathocchvāse dīrghocchvāsāṃ prayojayet vikūṇitā ca kartavyā jugupsāyāmasūyādiṣu  BhN kāryā śeṣu bhāveṣu tajñaiḥ svābhāvikā tathā kṣāmaṃ phullaṃ ca ghūrṇaṃ ca kampitaṃ kuñcitaṃ samam  BhN ṣaḍvidhaṃ gaṇḍamuddiṣṭaṃ tasya lakṣaṇamucyate kṣāmaṃ cāvanataṃ jñeyaṃ phullaṃ vikasitaṃ bhavet  BhN vitataṃ ghūrṇamatroktaṃ kampitaṃ sphuritaṃ bhavet syāt kuñcitaṃ saṃkuñcitaṃ samaṃ prākṛtamucyate  BhN gaṇḍayorlakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ viniyogaṃ nibodhata kṣāmaṃ duḥkheṣu kartavyaṃ praharṣe phullameva ca  BhN pūrṇamutsāhagarveṣu romaharṣeṣu kampitam kuñcitaṃ ca saromāñcaṃ sparśe śīte bhaye jvare  BhN prākṛtaṃ śeṣabhāveṣu gaṇḍakarma bhavediti vivartanaṃ kampanaṃ ca visargo vinigūhanam  BhN sandaṣṭakaṃ samudgaṃ ca ṣaṭ karmāṇyadharasya tu vikūṇitaṃ vivartastu vepanaṃ kampanaṃ smṛtam  BhN viniṣkrāmo visargastu praveśo vinigūhanam sandaṣṭakaṃ dvijaiardaṣṭaṃ samudgaḥ sahajonnati  BhN ityoṣṭhalakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ viniyogaṃ nibodhata asūyāvedanāvajñābhayādiṣu vivartanam  BhN kampanaṃ vepanaṃ śītabhayaroṣajavādiṣu strīaṇāṃ vilāse vivvoke visargo rañjane tathā  BhN vinigūhanamāyāse sandaṣṭaṃ krodhakarmasu samudgastvanukampāyāṃ cumbane cābhinandane  BhN ityoṣṭhakarmāṇyuktāni cibukasya nibodhata kuṭṭanaṃ khaṇḍanaṃ chinnaṃ cukkitaṃ lehanaṃ samam  BhN daṣṭaṃ ca dantakriyayā cibukaṃ tviha lakṣyate kuṭṭanaṃ dantasaṃgharṣaḥ saṃsphoṭaḥ khaṇḍanaṃ muhuḥ  BhN chinnaṃ tu gāḍhasaṃśleṣaścukkitaṃ dūravicyutiḥ lehanaṃ jihvayā lehaḥ kiñcit śleṣaḥ samaṃ bhavet  BhN dantairdaṣṭe dhare daṣṭamityeṣāṃ viniyojanam bhayaśītajvarakrodhagrastānāṃ kuṭṭanaṃ bhavet  BhN japādhyayanasaṃlāpabhakṣyayoge ca khaṇḍanam chinnaṃ vyādhau bhaye śīte vyāyāme rudite mṛte  BhN jṛmbhaṇe cukkitaṃ kāryaṃ tathā lehye ca lehanam samaṃ svabhāvabhāveṣu sandaṣṭaṃ krodhakarmasu  BhN iti dantoṣṭhajihvānāṃ karaṇāccibukakriyā vidhutaṃ vinivṛttaṃ ca nirbhugnaṃ bhugnameva ca  BhN vivṛtaṃ ca tathodvāhi karmāṇyatrāsyajāni tu vyāvṛttaṃ vinivṛttaṃ syādvidhutaṃ tiryagāyatam  BhN avāṅmukhatvaṃ nirbhugnaṃ vyābhugnaṃ kiñcidāyatam viśliṣṭoṣṭhaṃ ca vivṛtamudvāhyutkṣiptameva ca  BhN vinivṛttamasūyāyāmīrṣyākrodhakṛtena ca avajñāvivṛtādau ca strīṇā kāryā prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN vidhutaṃ vāraṇe caiva naivamityevamādiṣu nirbhugnaṃ cāpi vijñeyaṃ gambhīrālokanādiṣu  BhN bhugnaṃ lajānvite yojyaṃ yatīnāṃ tu svabhāvajam nirvedautsukyacintāsu naye ca vinimantraṇe  BhN vivṛttaṃ cāpi vijñeyaṃ hāsyaśokabhayādiṣu strīṇāmudvāhi līlāyāṃ garve gacchatyanādare  BhN eva nāmeti kāryaṃ ca kopavākye vicakṣaṇaiḥ samaṃ sācyanuvṛttādi yacca dṛṣṭivikalpitam  BhN tajjñaistenānusāreṇa kāryaṃ tadanugaṃ
