nāsikodbhavā jñeyāḥ ūṣmāṇaśca śaṣasahāḥ yaralavavarṇāstathaiva cāntaḥsthāḥ  BhN jihvāmūlīyaḥ kaḥ pa upadhmānīyasaṃjñayā jñeyaḥ kacaṭatapā svaritāḥ syuḥ khachaṭhathaphā syuḥ sadā kramyāḥ  BhN kaṇṭhyorasyān vidyāt ghajhaḍhadhabhān pāṭhyasaṃprayoge tu vedyo visarjanīyo jihvāsthāne sthito varṇaḥ  BhN ete vyañjanavarṇāḥ samāsataḥ saṃjñayā mayā kathitāḥ śabdaviṣayaprayoge svarāṇstu bhūyaḥ pravakṣyāmi  BhN yasmin sthāne sa samo vijñeyo yaḥ savarṇasaṃjño sau ya ime svarāścaturdaśa nirdiṣṭāstatra vai daśa samānāḥ pūrvo hrasvaḥ teṣāṃ paraśca dīrgho vagantavyaḥ  BhN itthaṃ vyañjanayogaiḥ svaraiśca sākhyātanāmapadavihitaiḥ kāvyanibandhāśca syurdhātunipātopasargāstu  BhN ebhirvyañjanavargairnāmākhyātopasarganipātaiḥ taddhitasandhivibhaktibhiradhiṣṭhitaḥ śabda ityuktaḥ  BhN pūrvācāryairuktaṃ śabdānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ samāsayogena vistaraśaḥ punareva prakaraṇavaśāt saṃpravakṣyāmi  BhN arthapradhānaṃ nāma syādākhyātaṃ tu kriyākṛtam dyotayantyupasargāstu viśeṣaṃ bhāvasaṃśrayam  BhN tatprāhuḥ saptavidhaṃ ṣaṭkārakasaṃyutaṃ prathitasādhyam nirdeśasaṃpradānāpadānaprabhṛtisaṃjñābhiḥ  BhN nāmākhyātārthaviṣayaṃ viśeṣaṃ dyotayanti te pṛthaktatropasargebhyo nipātā niyame cyute  BhN saṃpratyatītakālakriyādisaṃyojitaṃ prathitasādhyam vacanaṃ nāgatayuktaṃ susadṛśasaṃyojanavibhaktam  BhN pañcaśatadhātuyuktaṃ pañcaguṇaṃ pañcavidhamidaṃ vāpi svādyadhikāraguṇairarthaviśeṣairvibhūṣitanyāsam prātipadikārthaliṅgairyuktaṃ pañcavidhamidaṃ jñeyam  BhN ākhyātaṃ pāṭhyakṛtaṃ jñeyaṃ nānārthāśrayaviśeṣam vacanaṃ nāmasametaṃ puruṣavibhaktaṃ tadākhyātam  BhN prātipadikārthayuktāndhātvarthānupasṛjanti ye svārthaiḥ upasargā hyupadiṣṭāstasmāt saṃskāraśāstre smin  BhN prātipadikārthayogāddhātucchandoniruktayuktyā ca yasmānnipatanti pade tasmātproktā nipātāstu  BhN pratyayavibhāgajanitāḥ prakarṣasaṃyogasatvavacanaiśca yasmātpūrayate rthān pratyaya uktastatastasmāt  BhN loke prakṛtipratyayavibhāgasaṃyogasatvavacanaiśca tāṃstān pūrayate rthāṃsteṣu yastaddhitastasmāt  BhN ekasya bahūnāṃ vā dhātorliṅgasya vā padānāṃ vā vibhajantyarthaṃ yasmāt vibhaktayastena tāḥ proktāḥ  BhN viśiṣṭāstu svarā yatra vyañjanaṃ vāpi yogataḥ sandhīyate pade yasmāttasmāt sandhiḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN varṇapadakramasiddhaḥ padaikayogācca varṇayogācca sandhīyate ca yasmāttasmāt sandhiḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ  BhN luptavibhaktirnāmnāmekārthaṃ saṃharatsamāso pi tatpuruṣādikasaṃjñairnirdiṣṭaḥ ṣaḍvidho viprāḥ  BhN ebhiḥ śabdavidhānairvistāravyañjanārthasaṃyuktaiḥ padabandhāḥ kartavyā nibaddhabandhāstu cūrṇā vā  BhN vibhaktyantaṃ padaṃ jñeyaṃ nibaddhaṃ cūrṇameva ca tatra cūrṇapadasyeha sannibodhata lakṣaṇam  BhN anibaddhapadaṃ chandovidhānāniyatākṣaram arthāpekṣyakṣarasyūtaṃ jñeyaṃ cūrṇapadaṃ budhaiḥ  BhN nibaddhākṣarasaṃyuktaṃ yaticchedasamanvitam nibaddhaṃ tu padaṃ jñeyaṃ pramāṇaniyatātmakam  BhN evaṃ nānārthasaṃyuktaiḥ pādairvarṇavibhūṣitaiḥ caturbhistu bhavedyuktaṃ chando vṛttābhidhānavat  BhN ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ smṛtānyebhiḥ pādaiśchandasi saṃkhyayā samañcārdhasamañcaiva tathā viṣamameva ca  BhN chandoyuktaṃ samāsena trividhaṃ vṛttamiṣyate nānāvṛttiviniṣpannā śabdasyaiṣā tanūssmṛtā  BhN chandohīno na śabdo sti na cchandaśśabdavarjitam tasmāttūbhyasaṃyogo nāṭyasyodyotakaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN ekākṣaraṃ bhaveduktamatyuktaṃ dvyakṣaraṃ bhavet madhyaṃ tryakṣaramityāhuḥ pratiṣṭhā caturakṣarā  BhN supratiṣṭhā bhavet pañca gāyatrī ṣaḍ bhavediha saptākṣarā bhaveduṣṇigaṣṭākṣarānuṣṭubucyate  BhN navākṣarā tu bṛhatī paṅktiścaiva daśākṣarā ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub jagatī dvādaśākṣarā  BhN trayodaśātijagatī śakvarī tu caturdaśā atiśakvarī pañcadaśā ṣoḍaśāṣṭiḥ prakīrtitā  BhN atyaṣṭiḥ syātsaptadaśā dhṛtiraṣṭādaśākṣarā ekonaviṃśatirdhṛtiḥ kṛtirviṃśatireva ca  BhN prakṛtiścaikaviṃśatyā dvāviṃśatyākṛtistathā vikṛtiḥ syāt trayoviṃśā caturviṃśā ca saṃkṛtiḥ  BhN pañcaviṃśatyatikṛtiḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyutkṛtirbhavet ato dhikākṣaraṃ chando mālāvṛttaṃ tadiṣyate  BhN chandasāṃ tu tathā hyete bhedāḥ prastārayogataḥ asaṃkhyeyapramāṇāni vṛttānyāhurato budhāḥ  BhN gāyatrīprabhṛtittveṣāṃ pramāṇaṃ saṃvidhīyate prayogajāni sarvāṇi prāyaśo na bhavanti hi  BhN vṛttāni ca catuṣṣaṣṭirgāyatryāṃ kīrtitāni tu śataṃ viṃśatiraṣṭau ca vṛttānyuṣṇihyathocyate  BhN ṣaṭpañcāśacchate dve ca vṛttānāmapyanuṣṭubhi śatāni pañca vṛtānāṃ bṛhatyāṃ dvādaśaiva ca  BhN paṅktyāṃ sahasraṃ vṛttānāṃ caturviṃśatireva ca traiṣṭubhe dve sahasre ca catvāriṃśattathāṣṭa ca  BhN sahasrāṇyapi catvāri navatiśca ṣaḍuttarā jagatyāṃ samavarṇānāṃ vṛttānāmiha sarvaśaḥ  BhN aṣṭau sahasrāṇi śataṃ dvyadhikā navatiḥ punaḥ jagatyāmatipūrvāyāṃ vṛttānāṃ parimāṇataḥ  BhN śatāni trīṇyaśītiśca sahasrāṇyapi ṣoḍaśa vṛttāni caiva catvāri śakvaryāḥ parisaṃkhyayā  BhN dvātriṃśacca sahasrāṇi sapta caiva śatāni ca aṣṭau ṣaṣṭiśca vṛttāni hyāśrayantyatiśakvarīm  BhN pañcaṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi sahasrārdhañca saṃkhyayā ṣaṭtriṃśaccaiva vṛttāni hyaṣṭyāṃ nigaditāni ca  BhN ekatriṃśatsahasrāṇi vṛttānāñca dvisaptatiḥ tathā śatasahasrañca chandāṃsyatyaṣṭisaṃjñite  BhN dhṛtyāmapi hi piṇḍena vṛttānyākalpitāni tu tajjñaiḥ śatasahasre dve śatamekaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN dviṣaṣṭiśca sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśacca yogataḥ catvāri caiva vṛttāni samasaṃkhyāśrayāṇi tu  BhN atidhṛtyāṃ sahasrāṇi caturviṃśatireva ca tathā śatasahasrāṇi pañca vṛttaśatadvayam  BhN aṣṭāśītiśca vṛttāni vṛttajñaiḥ kathitāni ca kṛtau śatasahasrāṇi daśa proktāni saṃkhyayā  BhN catvāriṃśattathā cāṣṭau sahasrāṇi śatāni ca pañcaṣaṭsaptatiścaiva vṛttānāṃ parimāṇataḥ  BhN tathā śatasahasrāṇāṃ prakṛtau viṃśatirbhavet sapta vai gaditāstvatra navatiścaiva saṃkhyayā  BhN sahasrāṇi śataṃ caikaṃ dvipañcāśattathaiva ca vṛttāni parimāṇena vṛttajñairgaditāni tu  BhN catvāriṃśattathaikañca lakṣāṇāmatha saṃkhyayā tathā ceha sahasrāṇi navatiścaturuttarā  BhN śatatrayaṃ samākhyātaṃ hyākṛtyāṃ caturuttaram jñeyā śatasahasrāṇāmaśītistryadhikā budhaiḥ  BhN aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi vṛttānāṃ ṣaṭ śatāni ca aṣṭau caiva tu vṛttāni vikṛtyāṃ gaditāni tu  BhN tathā śatasahasrāṇi saptaṣaṣṭiśca saptatiḥ sapta caiva sahasrāṇi ṣoḍaśe dve śate tathā  BhN koṭiścaiveha vṛttāni saṃkṛtau kathitāni vai koṭitrayañcābhikṛtyāṃ pañcatriṃśadbhiranvitam  BhN pañcāśadbhiḥ sahasraiśca caturbhiradhikaistathā catuṣṭayaṃ śatānām ca dvātriṃśadbhiḥ samanvitam  BhN ṣaṭ koṭayastathotkṛtyāṃ lakṣāṇāmekasaptatiḥ catuṣṣaṣṭiśatānyaṣṭau sahasrāṇyaṣṭa caiva hi  BhN uktādutkṛtiparyantavṛttasaṃkhyāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ etena ca vikalpena vṛtteṣveteṣu nirdiśet  BhN sarveṣāṃ chandasāmevaṃ vṛttāni kathitāni vai tisraḥ koṭayo daśa tathā sahasrāṇāṃ śatāni tu  BhN catvāriṃśattathā dve ca sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu saptabhiḥ sahitānyeva sapta caiva śatāni ca  BhN ṣaḍviṃśatirihānyāni vyākhyātāni samāsataḥ samāni gaṇanāyuktimāśritya kathitāni vai  BhN sarveṣāṃ chandasāmevaṃ trikairvṛttaṃ prayojayet jñeyāścāṣṭau trikāstatra saṃjñābhiḥ sthānamaccharam  BhN trīṇyakṣarāṇi vijñeyastriko ṃśaḥ parikalpitaḥ gurulaghvakṣarakṛtaḥ sarvavṛtteṣu nityaśaḥ  BhN gurupūrvo bhakāraḥ syānmakāre tu gurutrayam jakāro gurumadhyasthaḥ sakāro ntyagurustathā  BhN laghumadhyasthito rephastakāro ntyalaghuḥ paraḥ laghupūrvo yakārastu nakāre tu laghutrayam  BhN ete hyaṣṭau trikāḥ prājñairvijñeyā brahmasambhavāḥ lāghavārthaṃ punaramī chandojñānamavekṣya ca  BhN ebhirvinirgatāścānyā jātayo tha samādayaḥ asvarāḥ sasvarāścaiva procyante vṛttalakṣaṇaiḥ  BhN gurvekaṃ giti vijñeyaṃ tathā laghu liti smṛtam niyataḥ padavicchedo yatirityabhidhīyate  BhN guru dīrghaṃ plutañcaiva saṃyogaparameva ca sānusvāravisargaṃ ca tathāntyañca laghu kvacit  BhN gāyatryāṃ dvau trikau jñeyau uṣṇik caikādhikākṣarā anuṣṭup dvyadhikā caiva bṛhatyāṃ ca trikāstrayaḥ  BhN ekākṣarādhikā paṅktistriṣṭup ca dvyadhikākṣarā catustrikā tu jagatī saikātijagatī punaḥ  BhN śakvarī dvyadhikā pañcatrikā jñeyātiśakvarī ekādhikākṣarāṣṭiśca dvyadhikātyaṣṭirucyate  BhN ṣaṭtrikāstu dhṛtiḥ proktā saikā cātidhṛtistathā kṛtiśca dvyadhikā proktā prakṛtyāṃ sapta vai trikāḥ  BhN ākṛtistvadhikaikena dvyadhikā vikṛtistathā aṣṭatrikāḥ saṃkṛtau syāt saikā cābhikṛtiḥ punaḥ  BhN utkṛtirdvyadhikā caiva vijñeyā gaṇamānataḥ gurvekaṃ ga iti proktaṃ guruṇī gāviti smṛtau laghvekaṃ la iti jñeyaṃ laghunī lāviti smṛtau  BhN saṃpadvirāmapādāśca daivatasthānamakṣaram varṇaḥ svaro vidhirvṛttamiti chandogato vidhiḥ  BhN naivātiriktaṃ hīnaṃ vā yatra saṃpadyate kramaḥ vidhāne cchandasāmeṣa saṃpadityabhisaṃjñitaḥ  BhN yatrārthasya samāptiḥ syāt sa virāma iti smṛtaḥ pādaśca padyaterdhātoścaturbhāga iti smṛtaḥ  BhN agnyādidaivataṃ proktaṃ sthānaṃ dvividhamucyate śarīrāśrayasaṃbhūtaṃ digāśrayamathāpi ca  BhN śārīraṃ mantrasaṃbhūtaṃ chando gāyatrasaṃjñitam kruṣṭe madhyaṃ dinaṃ proktaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ parikīrtyate  BhN tṛtīyasavanañcāpi śīrṣaṇyaṃ jāgataṃ hi yat hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutañcaiva trividhañcākṣaraṃ smṛtam  BhN śvetādayastathā varṇā vijñeyāśchandasāmiha tāraścaiva hi mandraśca madhyamastrividhaḥ svaraḥ  BhN dhruvāvidhāne caivāsya saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam vidhirgaṇakṛtaścaiva tathaivārthakṛto bhavet  BhN chandato yasya pāde syāddhīnaṃ vādhikameva vā akṣaraṃ nicṛditi proktaṃ bhūrik ceti dvijottamāḥ  BhN akṣarābhyāṃ sadā dvābhyāmadhikaṃ hīnameva vā tacchando nāmato jñeyaṃ svarāḍiti virāḍapi  BhN sarveṣāmeva vṛttānāṃ tajjñairjñeyā gaṇāstrayaḥ divyo divyetaraścaiva divyamānuṣa eva ca  BhN gāyatryuṣṇiganuṣṭup ca bṛhatī paṅktireva ca triṣṭup ca jagatī caiva divyo yaṃ prathamo gaṇaḥ  BhN tathātijagatī caiva śakvarī cātiśakvarī aṣṭiratyaṣṭirapi ca dhṛtiścātidhṛtirgaṇaḥ  BhN kṛtiśca prakṛtiścaiva hyākṛtirvikṛtistathā saṃkṛtyabhikṛtī caiva utkṛtirdivyamānuṣā  BhN eteṣāṃ chandasāṃ bhūyaḥ prastāravidhisaṃśrayam lakṣaṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi naṣṭamuddiṣṭameva ca  BhN prastāro kṣaranirdiṣṭo mātroktaśca tathaiva hi dvikau glāviti varṇoktau miśrau cetyapi mātrikau  BhN guroradhastādādyasya prastāre laghu vinyaset agratastu samādeyā guravaḥ pṛṣṭhatastathā  BhN prathamaṃ gurubhirvarṇairlaghubhistvavasānajam vṛttantu sarvachandassu prastāravidhireva tu  BhN gurvadhastāllaghuṃ nyasya tathā dvidvi yathoditam nyasyet prastāramārgo yamakṣaroktastu nityaśaḥ  BhN mātrāsaṃkhyāvinirdiṣṭo gaṇo mātrāvikalpitaḥ miśrau glāviti vijñeyau pṛthak lakṣyavibhāgataḥ  BhN mātrāgaṇo guruścaiva laghunī caiva lakṣite āryāṇāṃ tu caturmātrāprastāraḥ parikalpitaḥ  BhN gītakaprabhṛtīnāntu pañcamātro gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ vaitālīyaṃ puraskṛtya ṣaṇmātrādyāstathaiva ca  BhN tryakṣarāstu trikā jñeyā laghugurvakṣarānvitāḥ mātrāgaṇavibhāgastu gurulaghvakṣarāśrayaḥ  BhN antyād dviguṇitādrūpād dvidvirekaṃ gurorbhavet dviguṇāñca laghoḥ kṛtvā saṃkhyāṃ piṇḍena yojayet  BhN ādyaṃ sarvaguru jñeyaṃ vṛttantu samasaṃjñitam kośaṃ tu sarvalaghvantyaṃ miśrarūpāṇi sarvataḥ  BhN vṛttānāṃ tu samānānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ saṃyojya tāvatīm rāśyūnāmardhaviṣamāṃ samāsādabhinirdiśet  BhN ekādikāṃ tathā saṃkhyāṃ chandaso viniveśya tu yāvat pūrṇantu pūrveṇa pūrayeduttaraṃ gaṇam  BhN samānāṃ viṣamāṇāṃ ca saṃguṇayya tathā sphuṭam rāśyūnāmabhijānīyādviṣamāṇāṃ samāsataḥ  BhN evaṃ kṛtvā tu sarveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ pūrvapūraṇam kramānnaidhanamekaikaṃ pratilomaṃ visarjayet  BhN sarveṣāṃ chandasāmevaṃ laghvakṣaraviniścayam jānīta samavṛttānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ saṃkṣepatastathā  BhN vṛttasya parimāṇantu chitvārdhena yathākramam nyasellaghu yathā saikamakṣaraṃ guru cāpyatha  BhN evaṃ vinyasya vṛttānāṃ naṣṭoddiṣṭavibhāgataḥ gurulaghvakṣarāṇīha sarvachandassu darśayet  BhN iti chandāṃsi yānīha mayoktāni dvijottamāḥ vṛttānyeteṣu nāṭye smin prayojyāni nibodhata  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre vācikābhinaye chandovidhānaṃ nāma caturdaśo dhyāyaḥatha pañcadaśo dhyāyaḥchandāṃsyevaṃ hi yānīha mayoktāni dvijottamāḥ vṛttāni teṣu nāṭye smin prayojyāni nibodhata  BhN ādye punarantye dve dve guruṇī cet sā syāttanumadhyā gāyatrasamutthā  BhN yathāsaṃtyaktavibhūṣā bhraṣṭāñjananetrā hastārpitagaṇḍā kiṃ tvaṃ tanumadhyā  BhN laghugaṇa ādau bhavati catuṣkaḥ guruyugamantye makarakaśīrṣā  BhN yathāsvayamupayāntaṃ bhajasi na kāntam bhayakari kiṃ tvaṃ makarakaśīrṣā  BhN ekamātraṃ ṣaṭke syād dvitīyaṃ pāde khyātarūpā vṛtte sā mālinī nāmnā  BhN ṣaḍakṣarakṛte pāde laghu yatra dvitīyakam śeṣāṇi tu gurūṇi syurmālinī sā matā yathā  BhN snānagandhādhikyairvastrabhūṣāyogaiḥ vyaktamevāsau tvaṃ mālinī prakhyātā  BhN dvitīyaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva laghu yatra pratiṣṭhitam śeṣāṇi ca gurūṇi syurmālatī nāma sā yathā  BhN śobhate baddhayā ṣaṭpadāviddhayā mālatīmālayā māninī līlayā  BhN dvitīyaṃ ca caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ca yadā laghu yasyāḥ saptākṣare pāde jñeyā sā tūddhatā yathā  BhN sau trikau yadi pāde hyantimaśca gakāraḥ uṣṇigutthitapādā uddhatā khalu nāmnā  BhN dantakṛntakṛtāstraṃ vyākulālakaśobham śaṃsatīva tavāsyaṃ nirdayaṃ ratayuddham  BhN ādau dve nidhane caiva guruṇī yatra vai sadā pāde saptākṣare jñeyā nāmnā bhramaramālikā  BhN pāde pāde niviṣṭau samyagviracitau tsau antye yadi gakāraḥ sā tu bhramaramālā  BhN yathānānākusumacitre prāpte surabhimāse eṣā bhramati mattā kānte bhramaramālā  BhN ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca pañcamaṃ saptamaṃ tathā gurūṇyaṣṭākṣare pāde siṃhalekheti sā yathā  BhN jātu yasya gau na pāde saṃsthitaḥ samasvarūpe tāmanuṣṭubāśrayasthāṃ vāvadanti siṃhalekhām  BhN yattvayā hyanekabhāvaiśceṣṭitaṃ rahaḥ sugātri tanmano mama praviṣṭaṃ vṛttamadya siṃhalekham  BhN caturthaṃ ca dvitīyaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhamaṣṭamameva ca gurūṇyaṣṭākṣare pāde yatra tanmattaceṣṭitam  BhN yadā tu jātparau ralau gakāra eva ca sthitaḥ anuṣṭubudbhavaṃ tadā vadanti mattaceṣṭitam  BhN yathācarāvaghūrṇitekṣaṇaṃ vilambitākulālakam asaṃsthitaiḥ padaiḥ priyā karoti mattaceṣṭitam  BhN aṣṭākṣarakṛte pāde sarvāṇyeva bhavanti hi gurūṇi yasminsā nāmnā vidyunmāleti kīrtitā  BhN mau gau cāntyau yasyāḥ pāde pādasyānte vicchedaśca sā cānuṣṭupchandasyuktā nityaṃ sadbhirvidyunmālā  BhN sāmbhobhārairānānadbhiḥ śyāmāmbhodairvyāpte vyomni ādityāṃśuspardhinyeṣā dikṣu bhrāntā vidyunmālā  BhN pañcamaṃ saptamaṃ cāntyaṃ guru pāde ṣṭake tathā chandojñairjñeyametattu vṛttaṃ cittavilāsitam  BhN smitavaśaviprakāśairdaśanapadairamībhiḥ varatanu pūrṇacandraṃ tava mukhamāvṛṇoti  BhN navākṣarakṛte pāde trīṇi syurnaidhanāni ca gurūṇi yasyāḥ sā nāmnā jñeyā madhukarī yathā  BhN ṣaḍiha yadi laghūni syurnidhanagatamakāraścet budhajanabṛhatīsaṃsthā bhavati madhukarī nāmnā  BhN kusumitamabhipaśyantī vividhatarugaṇaiśchannam vanamatiśayagandhāḍhyaṃ bhramati madhukarī hṛṣṭā  BhN daśākṣarakṛte pāde trīṇyādau trīṇi naidhane yasyā gurūṇi sā jñeyā paṅktirutpalamālikā  BhN trīṇyādau yadi hi gurūṇi syuścatvāro yadi laghavo madhye paṅktāvantagatamakāraḥ syādvijñeyā kuvalayamālākhyā  BhN yathāasmiṃste śirasi tadā kānte vaiḍūryasphaṭikasuvarṇāḍhye śobhāṃ svāṃ na vahati tāṃ baddhā suśliṣṭā kuvalayamāleyam  BhN dvitīyaṃ ca caturthaṃ ca ṣaṣṭamaṣṭamameva ca hrasvaṃ daśākṣare pāde yatra sā śikhisāriṇī  BhN jau trikau hi pādagau tu yasya gau ca saṃśritau tathā samau stau paṅktiyogasupratiṣṭhitāṅgī sā mayūrasāriṇīti nāmnā  BhN yathānaiva te sti saṃgamo manuṣyairnāpi kāmabhogacihnamanyat garbhiṇīva dṛśyase hyanārye kiṃ mayūrasāriṇī tvamevam  BhN ādyaṃ caturthamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ daśamaṃ tathā gurūṇi traiṣṭubhe pāde yatra syurdodhakaṃ tu tat  BhN bhau tu bhagāviti yasya gaṇāḥ syuḥ syācca yatistricaturbhirathāsmin traiṣṭubhameva hi tatkhalu nāmnā dodhakavṛttamiti pravadanti  BhN yathāpraskhalitāprapadapravicāyaṃ mattavighūrṇitagātravilāsam paśya vilāsini kuñjarametaṃ dodhakavṛttamayaṃ prakaroti  BhN ādau dvau pañcamaṃ caivāpyaṣṭamaṃ naidhanaṃ tathā guruṇyekādaśe pāde yatra tanmoṭakaṃ yathā  BhN eṣo mbudatulyanisvanaravaḥ kṣīvaḥ skhalamānavilambagatiḥ śrutvā ghanagarjitamadritaṭe vṛkṣān pratimoṭayati dviradaḥ  BhN navamaṃ saptamaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ tṛtīyaṃ ca bhavellaghu sarvāsvavasthāsu ca kāmatantre yogyāsi kiṃ vā bahunendravajrā  BhN ebhireva tu saṃyuktā laghubhistraiṣṭubhī yadā upendravajrā vijñeyā laghvādāviha kevalam  BhN priye śriyā varṇaviśeṣaṇena smitena kāntyā sukumārabhāvaiḥ amī guṇā rūpaguṇānurūpā bhavanti te kiṃ tvamupendravajrā  BhN ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ navamaṃ tathā gurūṇyekādaśe pāde yatra sā tu rathoddhatā  BhN kiṃ tvayā subhaṭa dūravarjitaṃ nātmano na suhṛdāṃ priyaṃ kṛtam yatpalāyanaparāyaṇasya te yāti dhūliradhunā rathoddhatā  BhN yathākiṃ tvayā kumatisaṅgayā sadā nājñayeva suhṛdāṃ priyaṃ kṛtam yad gṛhādvacanaroṣakampitā yāti tūrṇamabalā rathoddhatā  BhN ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ daśamaṃ guru yasyāstu traiṣṭubhe pāde vijñeyā svāgatā hi sā  BhN yathāadya me saphalamāyatanetre jīvitaṃ madanasaṃśrayabhāvam āgatāsi bhavanaṃ mama yasmātsvāgataṃ tava varoru niṣīda  BhN ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca navamaṃ caiva laghunī traiṣṭubhe yadi gurūṇyanyāni pāde tu sā jñeyā śālinī yathā  BhN duḥśīlaṃ vā nirguṇaṃ vāparaṃ vā loke dhairyādapriyaṃ na bravīṣi tasmācchīlaṃ sādhuhetoḥ suvṛttaṃ mādhuryātsyātsarvathā śālinī tvam  BhN tṛtīyaṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca navamaṃ dvādaśaṃ tathā gurūṇi jāgate pāde yatra tattoṭakaṃ bhavet  BhN yadi so tra bhavettu samudrasamastriṣu cāpi tathā niyamena yatiḥ satataṃ jagatīvihitaṃ hi tataṃ gaditaṃ khalu toṭakavṛttamidam  BhN yathākimidaṃ kapaṭāśrayadurviṣahaṃ bahuśāṭhyamatholbaṇarūkṣakatham svajanapriyasajjanabhedakaraṃ nanu toṭakavṛttamidaṃ kuruṣe  BhN ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭhameva ca tathopāntyaṃ jagatyāṃ ca guru cetkumudaprabhā  BhN yau trikau tathā nyau yadi khalu pāde ṣaḍbhireva varṇairyadi ca yatiḥ syāt nityasaṃniviṣṭā jagatividhāne nāmataḥ prasiddhā kumudanibhā sā  BhN yathāmanmathena viddhā salalitabhāvā nṛttagītayogā pravikasitākṣī nindyamadya kiṃ tvaṃ vigalitaśobhā candrapādayuktā kumudavatī ca  BhN matāntareyadi khalu pāde nyau trikau yathā yau yatirapi varṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhireva cetsyāt jagatividhāne nityasaṃniviṣṭā kumudanibhā sā nāmataḥ prasiddhā  BhN yathākumudanibhā tvaṃ kāmabāṇaviddhā kimasi natabhrūḥ śītavātadagdhā mṛdunalinīvāpāṇḍuvaktraśobhā kathamapi jātā hyagrataḥ sakhīnām  BhN dvādaśākṣarake pāde saptamaṃ daśamaṃ laghu ādau pañcākṣaracchedaścandralekhā tu sā yathā  BhN vaktraṃ saumyaṃ te padmapatrāyatākṣaṃ kāmasyāvāsaṃ sunāsoccaprahāsam kāmasyāpīdaṃ kāmamāhartukāmaṃ kānte kāntyā tvaṃ candralekheva bhāsi  BhN tṛtīyamantyaṃ navamaṃ pañcamaṃ ca yadā guru dvādaśākṣarake pāde yatra sā pramitākṣarā  BhN yathāsmitabhāṣiṇī hyacapalāparuṣā nibhṛtāpavādavimukhī satatam api kasyacidyuvatirasti sukhā pramitākṣarā sa hi pumāñjayati  BhN dvitīyamantyaṃ daśamaṃ caturthaṃ pañcamāṣṭame gurūṇi dvādaśe pāde vaṃśasthā jagatī tu sā  BhN yadi trikau jtau bhavatastu pādatastathaiva ca jrāvavasānasaṃsthitau tadā hi vṛttaṃ jagatīpratiṣṭhitaṃ vadanti vaṃśasthamitīha nāmataḥ  BhN na me priyā tvaṃ bahumānavarjitāṃ priyaṃ priyā te paruṣābhibhāṣiṇī tathā ca paśyāmyahamadya vigrahaṃ dhruvaṃ hi vaṃśasthagatiṃ kariṣyati  BhN caturthamantyaṃ daśamaṃ saptamaṃ ca yadā guru bhaveddhi jāgate pāde tadā syāddhariṇaplutā  BhN paruṣavākyakaśābhihitā tvayā bhayavilokanapārśvanirīkṣaṇā varatanuḥ pratataplutasarpaṇairanukaroti gatairhariṇaplutam  BhN saptamaṃ navamaṃ cāntyamupāntyaṃ ca yadā guru dvādaśākṣarake pāde kāmadatteti sā yathā  BhN karajapadavibhūṣitā yathā tvaṃ sudati daśanavikṣatādharā ca gatirapi caraṇāvalagnamandā tvamasi mṛganibhākṣi kāmadattā  BhN ādyaṃ caturthaṃ daśamaṃ saptamaṃ ca yadā laghu pāde tu jāgate yasyā aprameyā tu sā yathā  BhN na te kācidanyā samā dṛśyate strī nṛloke viśiṣṭā guṇairadvitīyaiḥ trilokyāṃ guṇajjñān samāhṛtya sarvān jagatyaprameyāsi sṛṣṭā vidhātrā  BhN dvitīyaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva hyaṣṭamekādaśe yathā pāde yatra laghūni syuḥ padminī nāma sā yathā  BhN rāstrikāḥ sāgarākhyā niviṣṭā yadā syāt trike ca trike yuktarūpā yatiḥ sanniviṣṭā jagatyāstatassā budhair nāmataścāpi saṃkīrtyate padminī  BhN dehatoyāśayā vaktrapadmojjvalā netrabhṛṅgākulā dantahaṃsasmitā keśapāśacchadā cakravākastanī padminīva priye bhāsi me sarvadā  BhN phullapadmānanā tvaṃ dvirephekṣaṇā keśapatracchadā cakravākastanī pītatoyāvalī baddhakāñcīguṇā padminīva priye bhāsi nīre sthitā  BhN ādau ṣaṭ daśamaṃ caiva pāde yatra laghūnyatha śeṣāṇi tu gurūṇi syurjāgate puṭasaṃjñitā  BhN yadi caraṇaniviṣṭau nau tathā myau yatividhirapi yuktyāṣṭābhiriṣṭaḥ bhavati ca jagatīsthaḥ sarvadāsau ya iha hi puṭavṛttaṃ nāmatastu  BhN upavanasalilānāṃ bālapadmairbhramaraparabhṛtānāṃ kaṇṭhanādaiḥ madanamadavilāsaiḥ kāminīnāṃ kathayati puṭavṛttaṃ puṣpamāsaḥ  BhN dvitīyāntye caturthaṃ ca navamaikādaśe guru vicchedo tijagatyāṃ tu caturbhiḥ sā prabhāvatī  BhN kathaṃ nvidaṃ kamalaviśālalocane gṛhaṃ dhanaiḥ pihitakare divākare acintayantyabhinavavarṣavidyutastvamāgatā sutanu yathā prabhāvatī  BhN trīṇyādāvaṣṭamaṃ caiva daśamaṃ naidhanadvayam gurūṇyatijagatyāṃ tu tribhiśchedaiḥ praharṣiṇī  BhN bhāvasthairmadhurakathaiḥ subhāṣitaistvaṃ sāṭopaskhalitavilambitairgataiśca śobhāḍhyairharasi manāṃsi kāmukānāṃ suvyaktaṃ hyatijagatī praharṣiṇī ca  BhN ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ caiva daśamaikādaśe laghu trayodaśākṣare pāde jñeyaṃ mattamayūrakam  BhN vidyunnaddhāḥ sendradhanurañjitadehā vātoddhūtāḥ śvetavalākākṛtaśobhāḥ ete meghā garjitanādojjvalacihnāḥ prāvṛṭkālaṃ mattamayūrāḥ kathayanti  BhN ādau dve caturthaṃ caiva cāṣṭamaikādaśe guru antyopāntye ca śakvaryā vasantatilakā yathā  BhN citrairvasantakusumaiḥ kṛtakeśahastā sragdāmamālyaracanā suvibhūṣitāṅgī nānāvasantakavibhūṣitakarṇapāśā sākṣādvasantatilakeva vibhāti nārī  BhN pañcādau śakvarī pāde gurūṇi trīṇi naidhane pañcākṣarādau ca yatirasaṃbādhā tu sā yathā  BhN yathāmānālokajñaḥ sutabalakulaśīlāḍhyo yasminsammānaṃ na sadṛśamanu paśyeddhi gacchettaṃ tyaktvā drutagatiraparaṃ deśaṃ kīrṇā nānārthairavaniriyamasaṃbādhā  BhN catvāryādau gurūṇi syurdaśamaikādaśe tathā antyopāntye ca śakvaryāḥ pāde tu śarabhā yathā  BhN eṣā kāntā vrajati lalitā vepamānā gulmaiścchannaṃ vanamabhinavaiḥ saṃpraviddham hā hā kaṣṭaṃ kimidamiti no vedmi mūḍho vyaktaṃ kānte śarabhalalitāntvaṃ karoṣi  BhN adau ṣaṭ daśamaṃ caiva laghu caiva trayodaśam yatrātiśakvare pāde jñeyā nāndīmukhī tu sā  BhN yathāna khalu tava kadācitkrodhatāmrāyatākṣaṃ bhrukuṭivalitabhaṅgaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ mayāsyam kimiha bahubhiruktairyā mamecchā hṛdisthā tvamasi madhuravākyā devi nāndīmukhīva  BhN ādyaṃ caturthaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca naidhanaṃ ca yadā guru ṣoḍaśākṣarake pāde yatrebhalalitaṃ tu tat  BhN bhrau yadi nāśca nityamiha viracitacaraṇaḥ gaśca tathā vai bhavati nidhanamupagataḥ syādapi cāṣṭimeva yadi satatamanugataṃ tatkhalu vṛttamagravṛṣabhagajavilasitam  BhN kālatoyadharaiḥ sudhīradhanapaṭupaṭaharavaiḥ sarjakadambanīpakuṭajakusumasurabhiḥ kandalasendragopakaracitamavanitalaṃ vīkṣya karotyasau vṛṣabhagajavilasitam  BhN ādyātparāṇi vai pañca dvādaśaṃ satrayodaśaḥ antyopāntye ca dīrghāṇi lalitapravaraṃ hi tat  BhN yadā ymau pādasthau bhavata iha cetstau tathā gau tathā ṣaḍbhiścānyairyatirapi ca varṇairyathā syāt tadapyaṣṭau nityaṃ samanugatamevoktamanyaiḥ prayogajñairvṛttaṃ pravaralalitaṃ nāmatastu  BhN yathānakhālīḍhaṃ gātraṃ daśanakhacitaṃ coṣṭhagaṇḍaṃ śiraḥ puṣponmiśraṃ pravilulitakeśālakāntam gatiḥ khinnā ceyaṃ vadanamapi saṃbhrāntanetram aho ślāghyaṃ vṛttaṃ pravaralalitaṃ kāmaceṣṭam  BhN ādyātparāṇi pañcātha dvādaśaṃ satrayodaśam antyaṃ saptadaśe pāde śikhariṇyāṃ gurūṇi ca  BhN caturbhistasyaiva pravaralalitasya trikagaṇair yadā lau gaścānte bhavati caraṇe tyaṣṭigadite yadā ṣaḍbhiścchedo bhavati yadi mārgeṇa vihitas tadā vṛtteṣveṣā khalu śikhariṇī nāma gaditā  BhN yathāmahānadyā bhogaṃ pulinamiva bhāti te jaghanaṃ tathāsyaṃ netrāḍhyaṃ bhramarasahitaṃ paṅkajamiva gatirmandā ceyaṃ sutanu tava ceṣṭā sulalitā stanābhyāṃ tābhyāṃ tvaṃ śikhariṇi supīnāsi vanite  BhN yatra pañca laghūnyādau trayodaśacaturdaśe ṣoḍaśaikādaśe caiva tatsyādvṛṣabhaceṣṭitam  BhN yadi hi caraṇe nsau slau gaḥ kramādviniveśitār yadi khalu yatiḥ ṣaḍbhirvarṇairstathā daśabhiḥ punaḥ yadi vihitaṃ syādatyaṣṭiḥ prayogasukhāśrayaṃ vṛṣabhalalitaṃ vṛttaṃ jñeyaṃ tathā hariṇīti vā  BhN yathājaladhararavaṃ śrutvā śrutvā madocchrayadarpito vilikhitamahīśṛṅgākṣepairvṛṣaiḥ pratinardya ca svayuvativṛto goṣṭhādgoṣṭhaṃ prayāti ca nirbhayo vṛṣabhalalitaṃ citraṃ vṛttaṃ karoti ca śādvale  BhN catvāryādau ca daśamaṃ guru yatra trayodaśaṃ caturdaśaṃ tathāntye dve caikādaśamathāpi ca  BhN yadā saptadaśe pāde śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha bhavanti yasminsā jñeyā śrīdharī nāmato yathā  BhN mo bhnau ca syuścaraṇaracitāstau gurū ca praviṣṭāśchedaḥ śiṣṭo yadi ca daśabhiḥ syāttathānyaiścaturbhiḥ atyaṣṭau ca pratiniyamitā varṇataḥ spaṣṭarūpā sā vijñeyā dvijamunigaṇaiḥ śrīdharī nāmatastu  BhN snānaiścūrṇaiḥ sukhasurabhibhirgandhavāsaiśca dhūpaiḥ puṣpaiścānyaiḥ śirasi racitairvastrayogaiśca taistaiḥ nānāratnaiḥ kanakakhacitairaṅgasaṃbhogasaṃsthairvyaktaṃ kānte kamalanilayā śrīdharīvātibhāsi  BhN ādyaṃ caturthaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca daśamaṃ naidhanaṃ guru tadvaṃśapatrapatitaṃ daśabhiḥ saptabhiryatiḥ  BhN yathā eṣa gajo drimastakataṭe kalabhaparivṛtaḥ krīḍati vṛkṣagulmagahane kusumabhiranate megharavaṃ niśamya muditaḥ pavanajavasamaḥ sundari vaṃśapatrapatitaṃ punarapi kurute  BhN dvitīyamantyaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāpyaṣṭamaṃ dvādaśaṃ tathā caturdaśaṃ pañcadaśaṃ pāde saptadaśākṣare  BhN bhavanti yatra dīrghāṇi śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha vilambitagatiḥ sā tu vijñeyā nāmato yathā  BhN yadā dviruditau hi pādamabhisaṃśritau jsau trikau tathaiva ca punastayornidhanamāśritau yau lagau tadaṣṭiratipūrvikā yatirapi svabhāvādyathā vilambitagatistadā nigaditā dvijairnāmataḥ  BhN yathāvighūrṇitavilocanā pṛthuvikīrṇahārā punaḥ pralambaraśanā calatskhalitapādamandaklamā na me priyamidaṃ janasya bahumānarāgeṇa yanmadena vivaśā vilambitagatiḥ kṛtā tvaṃ priye  BhN pañcādau pañcadaśakaṃ dvādaśaikādaśe guru caturdaśaṃ tathāntye dve citralekhā dhṛtau smṛtā  BhN yathā nānāratnāḍhyairbahubhiradhikaṃ bhūṣaṇairaṅgasaṃsthairnānā gandhāḍhyairmadanajanakairaṅgarāgairvicitraiḥ keśaiḥ snānāḍhyaiḥ kusumabharitairvastrarāgaiśca taistaiḥ kānte saṃkṣepāt kimiha bahunā citralekheva bhāsi  BhN antyaṃ saptadaśaṃ caiva ṣoḍaśaṃ sacaturdaśam trayodaśaṃ dvādaśaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhamaṣṭamameva ca  BhN trīṇyādau ca gurūṇi syuryasmiṃstvekonaviṃśake pāde laghūni śeṣāṇi śārdūlakrīḍitaṃ tu tat  BhN msau jsau tau guru ca prayoganiyatā yasminniviṣṭāstrikā ādyā cāntyayatiścatustrikayutā jñeyā parā saptabhiḥ nityaṃ yatpadamāśritā hyatidhṛtirnityaṃ kavīnāṃ priyaṃ tajjñeyaṃ khalu vṛttajātinipuṇaiḥ śārdūlavikrīḍitam  BhN yathānānāśastraśataghnitomarahatāḥ prabhraṣṭasarvāyudhāḥ nirbhinnodarapādabāhuvadanā nirṇāśitāḥ śatravaḥ dhairyotsāhaparākramaprabhṛtibhistaistairvicitrairguṇair vṛttaṃ te ripughāti bhāti samare śārdūlavikrīḍitam  BhN tāvattvaṃ vijitendriyaḥ śubhamate sarvātmanā pratyahaṃ dāne śīlavidhau ca yojaya manaḥ svargāpavargāpaham yāvad vyādhijarāpracaṇḍanakharo vyāyatsaṭābhirbhṛśaṃ mṛtyuste na karoti jīvitamṛgaiḥ śārdūlavikrīḍitam  BhN catvāryādau ca ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ sacaturdaśam tathā pañcadaśaṃ caiva ṣiḍaśaṃ naidhanaṃ tathā  BhN etāni ca gurūṇi syuḥ śeṣāṇi tu laghūnyatha pāde yatra kṛtau jñeyā nāmnā suvadanā tu sā  BhN mrau mnau ybhau lgau ca samyagyadi ca viracitāḥ pāde kramavaśād vicchedaḥ saptabhiḥ syātpunarapi ca yatiḥ saptākṣarakṛtā yadyeṣā saṃśritā syātkṛtimapi ca punaḥ śliṣṭākṣarapadā vidvadbhirvṛttajātau tata iha gaditā nāmnā suvadanā  BhN yathānetre līlālasānte kamaladalanibhe bhrūcāpavinate raktoṣṭhaṃ pīnamadhyaṃ samasahitaghanāḥ snigdhāśca daśanāḥ karṇāvaṃsapralambau cibukamapi nataṃ ghoṇā surucirā vyaktaṃ tvaṃ martyaloke varatanu vihitāsyekā suvadanā  BhN catvāryādau tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ saptamaṃ ca caturdaśam aṣṭādaśaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā pañcadaśaṃ punaḥ  BhN antyopāntye gurūṇyatra laghūnyanyāni sarvadā ekaviṃśatike pāde sragdharā nāma sā yathā  BhN mrau mnau yau yaśca samyagyadi hi viracitāḥ syustrikāḥ pādayoge varṇaiḥ pūrvopadiṣṭairyatirapi ca punaḥ saptabhiḥ saptabhiḥ syāt vṛttaṃ samyagyadi syātprakṛtimanugataṃ tatvavidbhiḥ pradiṣṭaṃ vijñeyaṃ vṛttajātau kavijanadayitā sragdharā nāmatastu  BhN yathācūtāśokāravindaiḥ kuravakatilakaiḥ karṇikāraiḥ śirīṣaiḥ punnāgaiḥ pārijātairvakulakuvalayaiḥ kiṃśukaiḥ sātimuktaiḥ etairnānāprakāraiḥ bahulasurabhibhirviprakīrṇaiśca taistair vāsantaiḥ puṣpavṛndairnaravara vasudhā sragdharevādya bhāti  BhN caturthamādyaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca daśamaṃ dvādaśaṃ tathā ṣoḍaśāṣṭādaśe caiva naidhanaṃ ca gurūṇyatha  BhN dvāviṃśatyakṣare pāde śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha bhavanti yatra tajjñeyaṃ bhadrakaṃ nāmato yathā  BhN bhrau caraṇe yadā viniyatau trikau kramavaśādathātikṛtividhau nrau ca tataḥ paraṃ ca rucirāvanantarakṛtau nagāvapi punaḥ tacca daśāṣṭavarṇaracitā caturṣvapi tathā yatiśca satataṃ bhadrakavṛttameva khalu nāṭyayogakuśalairbudhairnigaditam  BhN utplutamekahastacaraṇaṃ dvitīyakararecitaṃ vaṃśamṛdaṅgavādyamadhuraṃ vicitrakaraṇānugaṃ bahuvidham bhadrakametadadya subhage vidagdhagaticeṣṭitaiḥ sulalitair nṛtyasi vibhramākulapadaṃ viviktarasabhāvitaṃ śaśimukhi  BhN antyamekonaviṃśaṃ ca saptamaṃ satrayodaśam ekādaśaṃ saptadaśaṃ pañcamaṃ ca gurūṇyatha  BhN śeṣāṇi ca laghūni syurvikṛtyāścaraṇe budhaiḥ vṛttaṃ tadaśvalalitaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāmato yathā  BhN yadi ca nakāra ādiracitaḥ pade viracito nta eva lagau yadi ca nabhau tridhā ca nihitau krameṇa khalu madhyāvapi tathā yadi ca samāśritaṃ hi vikṛtiṃ yatiśca daśabhistathaikasahitais tata iha kīrtitaṃ munigaṇairviśuddhacaritaistadaśvalalitam  BhN vividhaturaṅganāgarathayodhasaṅkulamalaṃ balaṃ samuditaṃ śaraśataśaktikuntaparidhāsiyaṣṭivitataṃ bahupraharaṇam ripuśatamuktaśastraravabhītaśaṅkitabhaṭaṃ bhayākuladiśaṃ kṛtamabhivīkṣya saṃyugamukhe samarpitaguṇaṃ tvayāśvalalitam  BhN ṣaḍādāvaṣṭamaṃ caiva hyekādaśacaturdaśe viṃśaṃ saptadaśaṃ caiva trayoviṃśaṃ tathaiva ca  BhN etāni ca laghūni syuḥ śeṣāṇyatha gurūṇi ca caturviṃśatike pāde meghamāleti sā yathā  BhN yadi khalu caraṇasthitau nau trikau kṛtikāravyāstathā rāḥ syuḥ kramāt bhavati yadi yatistathā saptabhiḥ saptabhistriṣvato nyā yatiḥ pañca vidyāttathā  BhN pavanabalasamāhṛtā tīvragambhīranādā balākāvalīmekhalā kṣitidharasadṛśoccarūpā mahānīladhūmāñjanābhāmbugarbhodbhavā surapatidhanurujjvalābaddhakakṣyā taḍiddyotasannāhapaṭṭījvalā gaganatalavisāriṇī prāvṛṣaṇyā dṛḍhaṃ meghamālādhikaṃ śobhate  BhN ādyaṃ caiva caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭhameva ca navamaṃ daśamaṃ caiva naidhanaṃ ca bhavedguru  BhN laghūnyanyāni śeṣāṇi pāde syuḥ pañcaviṃśake vṛttajjñaiḥ sā tu vijñeyā krauñcapādīti nāmataḥ  BhN bhmau yadi pāde sbhāvapi ceṣṭāvabhikṛtirapi ca hi yadi khalu vihitā nāśca samudrāḥ syurviniviṣṭā yadi ca khalu guru bhavati nidhanagatam pañcabhirādau chedamupetā punarapi yatiriha yadi khalu daśabhiḥ krauñcapadeyaṃ vṛttavidhāne suragaṇapitṛgaṇamunigaṇavihitā  BhN yaḥ kila dākṣaṃ vidrutasomaṃ kratuvaramacamasamapagatakalaśaṃ pātitayūpaṃ kṣiptacaṣālaṃ vicayanamasamidhamapaśukacarukam kārmukamuktenāśu cakāra vyapagatasuragaṇapitṛgaṇamiṣuṇā nityamasau te daityagaṇāriḥ pradahatu makhamiva ripugaṇamakhilam  BhN yā kapilākṣī piṅgalakeśī kaliruciranudinamanunayakaṭhinā dīrghatarābhiḥ sthūlasirābhiḥ parivṛtavapuratiśayakuṭilagatiḥ āyatajaṅghā nimnakapolā laghutarakucayugaparigatahṛdayā sā parihāryā krauñcapadā strī dhruvamiha niravadhisukhamabhilaṣatā  BhN aṣṭāvādau gurūṇi syustathā caikonaviṃśakam ekaviṃśaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ caturviṃśaṃ sanaidhanam  BhN etāni guru saṃkhyāni śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha ṣaḍviṃśatyakṣare pāde tadbhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam  BhN yasyāṃ mau to nāḥ strau nityaṃ praticaraṇamathagaditakāstrikā hyanupūrvaśaḥṣaḍviṃśatyāmekonāyāṃ ca yadi hikhalu yatirabhidhā caturbhirathāṣṭābhiḥ paścādantyau lgau saṃyojyau yadi bhavatimanujadayitāṃ samāśritamutkṛtiṃnāmnā vṛttaṃ loke khyātaṃ kavivadanavikasanaparaṃ bhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam  BhN yathārūpopetāṃ devaiḥ sṛṣṭāṃ samadagajavilasitagatiṃ nirīkṣya tilottamāṃprādakṣiṇyātprāptāṃ draṣṭuṃ bahuvadanamacalanayanaṃ śiraḥ kṛtavān hariḥ dīrghaṃ niśvasyāntargūḍhaṃ stanavadanajaghanarucirāṃ nirīkṣya tathā punaḥpṛṣṭhe nyastaṃ devendreṇa pravaramaṇikanakavalayaṃ bhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam  BhN daṇḍakaṃ nāma vijñeyamutkṛteradhikataram meghamālādikaṃ tatsyānnau cādau kāguhā trikāḥ  BhN yathāmuditajanapadākulā sphītasasyākarā bhūtadhātrī bhavantaṃ samabhyarcatidviradakaraviluptahintālatālīvanāstvāṃ namasyanti vindhyādayaḥ parvatāḥ sphuṭitakalaśāśuktinigīrṇamuktā phalairūrmihastairnamasyanti vaḥ sāgarāḥmuditajalacarākulāḥ saṃprakīrṇamalāḥ kīrtayantīva kīrtiṃ mahānimnagāḥ  BhN etāni samavṛttāni mayoktāni dvijottamāḥ viṣamārdhasamānāṃ tu punarvakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN yatra pādāstu viṣamā nānāvṛttasamudbhavāḥ grathitāḥ pādayogena tad vṛttaṃ viṣamaṃ smṛtam  BhN dvau samaṃ dvau ca viṣamau vṛtte rdhaviṣame tathā sarvapādaiśca viṣamairvṛttaṃ viṣamamucyate  BhN hrasvādyamatha dīrghādyaṃ dīrghaṃ hrasvamathāpi vā yugmojaviṣamaiḥ pādaiḥ vṛttamardhasamaṃ bhavet  BhN pāde siddhe samaṃ siddhaṃ viṣamaṃ sārvapādikam dvayorardhasamaṃ vidyādeṣa chedastu pādataḥ  BhN chedāstu ye mayā proktā samavṛttavikalpitaḥ trikairviṣamavṛttānāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN naidhane nyatarasyāṃ vai prathame pāda iṣyate dvitīye caraṇe ca syādityanuṣṭup samāsataḥ  BhN sau gau tu prathame pāde srau lgau cāpi dvitīyake yugme rdhaviṣame pāde jñeyā pathyā tu sā trikaiḥ  BhN priyadaivatamitrāsi priyasaṃbandhibāndhavā priyadānaratā pathyā dayite tvaṃ priyāsi me  BhN mrau gau tu prathame pāde ysau lgau ca dvitīyake pāde bhau lgau tṛtīye ca caturthe tu tasau lagau  BhN naivācāro na te mitraṃ na saṃbandhiguṇapriyā sarvathā sarvaviṣamā pathyā na bhavasi priye  BhN ayujorlakṣaṇaṃ hyetadviparītaṃ tu yatra ca pathyā hi viparītā sā vijñeyā nāmato yathā  BhN kṛtena ramaṇasya kiṃ sakhi roṣeṇa te pyartham viparītā na pathyāsi tvaṃ jaḍe kena mohitā  BhN caturthādakṣarādyatra trilaghu syādayuktataḥ anuṣṭupcapalā sā tu vijñeyā nāmato yathā  BhN na khalvasyāḥ priyatamaḥ śrotavyaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ sakhyā nāradasya pratikṛtiḥ kathyate capalā hīyam  BhN vipulā tu yuji jñeyā laghutvātsaptamasya tu sarvatra saptamasyaiva keṣāṃcidvipulā yathā  BhN saṃkṣiptā vajramadhye hi hemakumbhanibhastanī vipulāsi priye śroṇyāṃ pūrṇacandranibhānane  BhN gaṅgeva meghopagame āplāvitavasundharā kūlavṛkṣānārujantī sravantī vipulā balāt  BhN āgatā meghasamaye bhīru bhīrukulodgate ekarātrau paragṛhaṃ corī bandhanamarhasi  BhN evaṃ vividhayogāstu pathyāpādā bhavanti hi yugmojaviṣamaiḥ pādaiḥ śeṣairanyaistrikairyathā  BhN gurvantakaḥ sarvalaghustriko nityaṃ hi neṣyate prathamādakṣarādyatra caturthātprāglaghuḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN pathyāpādaṃ samāsthāpya trīṇyante tu gurūṇyatha bhavanti pāde satataṃ budhaistadvakramiṣyate  BhN dantakṣatādharaṃ subhru jāgaraglānanetraṃ ca ratisaṃbhogakhinnaṃ te darśanīyataraṃ vaktram  BhN ityeṣā sarvaviṣamā nāmato nuṣṭubucyate tadvidāṃ matavaiṣamyaṃ trikādakṣaratastathā  BhN pāde ṣoḍaśamātrāstu gāthāṃśakavikalpitāḥ caturbhiraṃśakairjñeyā vṛttajñairvānavāsikā  BhN asaṃsthitapadā suvihvalāṅgī madaskhalitaceṣṭitairmanojñā kva yāsyasi varoru suratakāle viṣamā kiṃ vānavāsikā tvam  BhN sjau sgau ca prathame pāde tathā caiva tṛtīyake ketumatyāṃ gaṇāḥ proktāḥ bhrau ngau gaśca sadā budhaiḥ  BhN sphuritādharaṃ cakitanetraṃ raktakapolamambujadalākṣam kimidaṃ ruṣāpahṛtaśobhaṃ ketumatīsamaṃ vada mukhaṃ te  BhN vaktrasyāparapūrvasya cādau nau ro lagau trikāḥ najau rajau dvitīye ca śeṣāgraṃ punareva tu  BhN prathame ca tṛtīye nau ralau gaśca prakīrtitaḥ gaṇāścāparavaktre tu najau jrau dvicaturthayoḥ  BhN sutanu jalaparītalocanaṃ jaladaniruddhamivendumaṇḍalam kimidamaparavaktrameva te śaśivadane dya mukhaṃ parāṅmukham  BhN nau yau tu prathame pāde njau jrau gaśca tathāpare yatra tatpuṣpitāgrā syādyadi śeṣaṃ tu pūrvavat  BhN pavanabalavidhūtacāruśākhaṃ pramuditakokilakaṇṭhanādaramyam madhukaraparigīyamānaśabdaṃ varatanu paśya vanaṃ supuṣpitāgram  BhN sjau slau cādau yathā nsau jgau bhnau jlau gaśca tathā punaḥ sjau sjau gaśca trikā hyete udgatāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BhN tava romarājiratibhāti sutanu madanasya mañjarī nābhikamalavivarotpatitā bhramarāvalīva kusumātsamudgatā  BhN sjau slau ca tato nsau jgau nau sau ceti tṛtīyake sjau sjau gaśca caturthe tu lalitāyā gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN lalitākulabhramitacāru vasanakaracārupallavā pravikasitakamalakāntimukhī pravibhāsi devī surataśramāturā  BhN evametāni vṛttāni samāni viṣamāṇi ca nāṭakādyeṣu kāvyeṣu prayoktavyāni sūribhiḥ  BhN santyanyānyapi vṛttāni yānyuktānīha piṇḍaśaḥ na ca tāni prayojyāni na śobhāṃ janayanti hi  BhN yānyataḥ pratiṣiddhāni gītake tāni yojayet dhruvāyoge tu vakṣyāmi teṣāṃ caiva vikalpanam  BhN vṛttalakṣaṇamevaṃ tu samāsena mayoditam ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi hyāryāṇāmapi lakṣaṇam  BhN pathyā ca vipulā caiva caṣalā mukhato parā jaghane capalā caiva āryāḥ pañca prakīrtitāḥ  BhN āsāṃ tu saṃpravakṣyāmi yatimātrāvikalpanam lakṣaṇaṃ niyamaṃ caiva vikalpaguṇasaṃśrayam  BhN yatiśchedastu vijñeyaścaturmātro gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ dvitīyāntyau yujau pādāvayujau tvaparau smṛtau  BhN gurumadhyavihīnastu caturgaṇasamanvitaḥ ayuggaṇo vidhātavyo yuggaṇastu yathepsitaḥ  BhN ṣaṣṭho vai dvivikalpastu naidhano hyekasaṃsthitaḥ paścādardhe tu ṣaṣṭhaḥ syādekamātrastu kevalaḥ  BhN dvivikalpastu ṣaṣṭho yo gurumadhyo bhavettu saḥ tathā sarvalaghuścaiva yatisaṃjñāsamāśritā  BhN dvitīyādilaghurjñeyaḥ saptame pañcame yatiḥ prathamādirathāntye ca pañcame vā vidhīyate  BhN gaṇeṣu triṣu pādasya yasyāḥ pathyā tu sā bhavet ataśca vipulānyā tu vijñeyā yatilakṣaṇā  BhN ayujaḥ sarvaguravo gurumadhyā gaṇā yujaḥ yasyāḥ syuḥ pādayoge tu vijñeyā capalā hi sā  BhN triṃśadādye tu vijñeyāḥ saptaviṃśatiścāpare ubhayorardhayorjñeyo mātrāpiṇḍo vibhāgaśaḥ  BhN triṃśattasyāśca yadi syuretāni dviguṇāni tu trīṇyakṣarāṇi cānyāni nyasya saṃkhyāvibhāgaśaḥ  BhN etāni laghusaṃjñāni nirdiṣṭāni samāsataḥ sarveṣāṃ caivamāryāṇāmakṣarāṇāṃ yathākramam  BhN ardhāṣṭamagaṇārdhā ca savavāryā prakīrtitā ṣaṣṭhaśca dvivikalpastu naidhane hyekasaṃsthitaḥ  BhN paścādvā yo gaṇaḥ ṣaṣṭha ekamātraḥ sa ucyate dvivikalpastu yaḥ ṣaṣṭho gurumadhyo bhavettu saḥ  BhN yathā sarvalaghuścaiva yatiḥ saṃkhyāsamāśritā sā dvitīyā dvilaghukā saptame prathame yatiḥ  BhN gurumadhyavihīnastu caturgaṇasamanvitaḥ ayuggaṇo vidhātavyaḥ yuggaṇastu sa eva ca  BhN prathamatṛtīyau pādau dvādaśamātrau bhavettu sā pathyā vipulānyā khalu gaditā pūrvoditalakṣaṇopetā  BhN pathyā yathāraktamṛdupadmanetrā sitadīrghabahulamṛdukeśī kasya tu pṛthumṛdujaghanā tanubāhvaṃ sodarī pathyā  BhN vipulā yathāvipulajaghanavadanastananayanaistāmrādharoṣṭhakaracaraṇaiḥ āyatanāsāgaṇḍairlalāṭakarṇaiḥ śubhā kanyā  BhN dvitīyaśca caturthaśca gurumadhyagato bhavet ubhayorardhayoryatra vijñeyā capalā yathā  BhN udbhaṭagāminī paruṣabhāṣiṇī kāmacihnakṛtaveṣā jānāti māṃsayuktā surāpriyā sarvataścapalā  BhN pūrvārdhe lakṣaṇaṃ hyetadasyāḥ sa ca mukhena tu paścimārdhe tu capalā yasyāḥ sā jaghanena tu  BhN mukhacapalā yathāāryāmukhe tu capalā tathāpi cāryā na me yataḥ sā kim dakṣā gṛhakṛtyeṣu tathā duḥkhe bhavati duḥkhārtā  BhN jaghanacapalā yathāvaramṛganayane capalāsi varoru śaśāṅkadarpaṇanibhāsye kāmasya sārabhūte na pūrvamadacārujaghanena  BhN ubhayorardhayoretallakṣaṇaṃ dṛśyate yadi vṛttajñaiḥ sā tu vijñeyā sarvataścapalā sakhi  BhN kāryau dvādaśamātrau ca pādāvādyau tṛtīyakau aṣṭādaśa dvitīyaṃ ca tathā pañcadaśottamā  BhN catuḥpañcaprakārāṇāṃ catuṣkāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ prastārayogamāsādya bāhulyaṃ saṃpradarśayet  BhN pañcapañcāśadādyā tu triṃśadādyā tathaiva ca āryā tvakṣarapiṇḍena vijñeyātra prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN triṃśatastvatha varṇebhyo laghuvarṇatrayaṃ bhavet śeṣāṇi gurusaṃkhyāni hyevaṃ sarvatra nirdiśet  BhN sarveṣāmeva cāryāṇāmakṣarāṇāṃ yathākramam sarveṣāṃ jātivṛttānāṃ pūrvamuttarasaṃkhyayā  BhN vikalpagaṇanāṃ kṛtvā saṃkhyāpiṇḍena nirdiśet āryāgītirathāryaiva kevalaṃ tvaṣṭabhirgaṇaiḥ  BhN itarārthe jaḥ ṣaṣṭhastu nalaghugaṇa iṣyate vṛttairevaṃ tu vividhairnānāchandassamudbhavaiḥ kāvyabandhāstu kartavyāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇānvitāḥ  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre chandovicitirnāma pañcadaśo dhyāyaḥatha ṣoḍaśo dhyāyaḥvibhūṣaṇaṃ cākṣarasaṃhatiśca śobhābhimānau guṇakīrtanaṃ ca protsāhanodāharaṇe niruktaṃ guṇānuvādo tiśayaśca hetuḥ  BhN sārūpyamithyādhyavasāyasiddhi padoccayākrandamanorathāśca ākhyānayāñcāpratiṣedhapṛcchā dṛṣṭāntanirbhāsanasaṃśayāśca  BhN āśīḥ priyoktiḥ kapaṭaḥ kṣamā ca prāptiśca paścāttapanaṃ tathaiva arthānuvṛttirhyupapattiyuktī kāryo nunītiḥ paridevanaṃ ca  BhN ṣaṭtriṃśadetāni hi lakṣaṇāni proktāni vai bhūṣaṇasaṃmitāni kāvyeṣu bhāvārthagatāni tajjñaiḥ samyag prayojyāni yathārasaṃ tu  BhN alaṅkārairguṇaiścaiva bahubhiḥ samalaṅkṛtam bhūṣaṇairiva vinyastaistad bhūṣaṇamiti smṛtam  BhN yatrālpairakṣaraiḥ śliṣṭairvicitramupavarṇyate tamapyakṣarasaṅghātaṃ vidyāllakṣaṇasaṃjñitam  BhN siddhairarthaissamaṃ kṛtvā hyasiddho rthaḥ prasādhyate yatra ślakṣṇavicitrārthā sā śobhetyabhidhīyate  BhN dhāryamāṇastu bahubhirvacanaiḥ kāryayuktibhiḥ na yaḥ paryavatiṣṭheta so bhimānastu saṃjñitaḥ  BhN kīrtyamānairguṇairyatra vividhārthasamudbhavaiḥ doṣā na parikathyante tajjñeyaṃ guṇakīrtanam  BhN loke guṇātiriktānāṃ bahūnāṃ yatra nāmabhiḥ eko bhiśabdyate yastu vijñeyaṃ guṇakīrtanam  BhN utsāhajananaiḥ spaṣṭairarthairopamyasaṃśrayaiḥ prasiddhairupagūḍhaṃ ca jñeyaṃ protsāhanaṃ budhaiḥ  BhN yatraikasyāpi śabdasya darśanātsubahūnyapi yānti siddhimanuktāni tadudāharaṇaṃ smṛtam  BhN niruktaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ tathyaṃ cātathyameva vā siddhiprasādhitaṃ tathyamatathyaṃ cāprasādhitam  BhN guṇānuvādo hīnānāmuttamairupamākṛtaḥ uttamārthaviśeṣo yaḥ sa cāpyatiśayaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN bahūnāṃ bhāṣamāṇānāmekasyārthavinirṇayāt siddhopamānavacanaṃ heturityabhisaṃjñitaḥ  BhN apadeśastu parokṣo yasmādutpadyate nukaraṇena lakṣaṇasamānakaraṇāt sārūpyaṃ tattu nirdeśyam  BhN abhūtapūrvairyatrārthaistulyasyārthasya nirṇayaḥ sa mithyādhyavasāyastu procyate kāvyalakṣaṇe  BhN bahūnāṃ tu pradhānānāṃ madhye yannāma kīrtyate ekārthasādhanakṛtaṃ sā siddhiriti kīrtyate  BhN guṇairbahubhirekārthaiḥ padairyaḥ saṃpraśasyate padoccayaṃ tu tadvidyānnānārthagrathanātmakam  BhN ātmabhāvamupanyasya parasādṛśyayuktibhiḥ tīvrārthabhāṣaṇaṃ yatsyādākrandaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ  BhN hṛdayasthasya bhāvasya suspaṣṭārthapradarśanam anyāpadeśakathanairmanoratha iti smṛtaḥ  BhN apṛṣṭairathavā pṛṣṭairnirṇayaḥ kriyate tu yaḥ ākhyānamiti tajjñeyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam  BhN ādau yatkrodhajananamante harṣapravardhanam yattu priyaṃ punarvākyaṃ sā yāñcā parikīrtitā  BhN kāryeṣu viparīteṣu yadi kiñcit pravartate nivāryate ca kāryajjñaiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN yatrākārodbhavairvākyairātmānamathavā param pṛcchannivābhidhatte rthaṃ sā pṛcchetyabhisaṃjñitā  BhN vidvān pūrvopalabdhau yatsamatvamupapādayet nidarśanakṛtastajjñaiḥ sa dṛṣṭānta iti smṛtaḥ  BhN anekayuktimadvākyamanekārthaprasādhakam anekavākyasaṃyuktaṃ tannirbhāsanamucyate  BhN aparijñātatattvārthaṃ yatra vākyaṃ samāpyate so nekatvādvicārāṇāṃ saṃśayaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  BhN yatra śāstrārthasampannāṃ manorathasamudbhavām aprārthanīyāmanyāṃ vā vidustāmāśiṣaṃ budhāḥ  BhN ādau yat krodhajananamante harṣapravardhanam tat priyaṃ vacanaṃ jñeyamāśīrvādasamanvitam  BhN chalayuktyā tvanyeṣāmabhisandhānābhibhāvakaṃkapaṭam dvitriprayogayukto vijñeyaḥ kapaṭasaṅghātaḥ  BhN durjanodāhṛtai rūkṣaiḥ sabhāmadhye titāḍitaḥ akrodhaḥ krodhajananairvākyairyaḥ sā kṣamā bhavet  BhN dṛṣṭvaivāvayavaṃ kañcidbhāvo yatrānumīyate prāptiṃ tāmabhijānīyāllakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam  BhN akāryaṃ sahasā kṛtvākṛtvā kāryamathāpi vā santāpo manaso yastu paścāttāpaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN praśrayeṇārthasaṃyuktaṃ yatparasyānuvartanam snehāddākṣiṇyayogādvā sānuvṛttistu saṃjñitā  BhN prāptānāṃ yatra doṣāṇāṃ kriyate śamanaṃ punaḥ sā jñeyā hyupapattistu lakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam  BhN sādhyate yo rthasambandho mahadbhiḥ samavāyataḥ parasparānukūlyena sā yuktiḥ parikīrtitā  BhN yatrāpasārayan doṣaṃ guṇamarthena yojayet guṇābhivādaṃ doṣān vā kāryaṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ viduḥ  BhN apūrvakrodhajanitamaparādhaṃ pramṛjya yat sevārthaṃ madhuraṃ vākyamanunītiḥ prakīrtitā  BhN doṣairyadanyanāmoktaiḥ prasiddhārthaiḥ prayojayet anyatrārthena sambaddhaṃ jñeyaṃ tat paridevanam  BhN upamā rūpakaṃ caiva dīpakaṃ yamakaṃ tathā alaṅkārāstu vijñeyā catvāro nāṭakāśrayāḥ  BhN yatkiñcit kāvyabandheṣu sādṛśyenopamīyate upamā nāma sā jñeyā guṇākṛtisamāśrayā  BhN ekasyaikena sā kāryā hyanekenāthavā punaḥ anekasya tathaikena bahūnāṃ bahubhistathā  BhN tulyaṃ te śaśinā vaktramityekenaikasaṃśrayā śaśāṅkavat prakāśante jyotīṃṣīti bhavettu yā  BhN ekasyānekaviṣayā sopamā parikīrtitā śyenabarhiṇabhāsānāṃ tulyārthamiti yā bhavet  BhN ekasya bahubhiḥ sāmyādupamā nāṭakāśrayā bahūnāṃ bahubhirjñeyā ghanā iva gajā iti  BhN praśaṃsā caiva nindā ca kalpitā sadṛśī tathā yā kiñcitsadṛśī jñeyā sopamā pañcadhā budhaiḥ  BhN praśaṃsā yathādṛṣṭvā tu tāṃ viśālākṣīṃ tutoṣa manujādhipaḥ munibhiḥ sādhitāṃ kṛcchrāt siddhiṃ mūrtimatīmiva  BhN nindā yathāsā taṃ sarvaguṇairhīnaṃ sasvaje karkaśacchavim vane kaṇṭakinaṃ vallī dāvadagdhamiva drumam  BhN kalpitā yathākṣaranto dānasalilaṃ lālāmantharagāminaḥ mataṅgajā virājante jaṅgamā iva parvatāḥ  BhN sadṛśī yathāyattvayādya kṛtaṃ karma paricittānurodhinā sadṛśaṃ tattavaiva syādatimānuṣakarmaṇaḥ  BhN kiñcitsadṛśī yathāsampūrṇacandravadanā nīlotpaladalekṣaṇā mattamātaṅgagamanā samprāpteyaṃ sakhī mama  BhN upamāyā budhairete bhedā jñeyāḥ samāsataḥ śeṣā ye lakṣaṇairnoktāste grāhyāḥ kāvyalokataḥ  BhN nānādhikaraṇārthānāṃ śabdānāṃ saṃpradīpakam ekavākyena saṃyuktaṃ taddīpakamucyate  BhN prasṛtaṃ madhuraṃ cāpi guṇaiḥ sarvairalaṅkṛtam kāvye yannāṭake viprāstaddīpakamiti smṛtam  BhN yathāsarāṃsi haṃsaiḥ kusumaiśca vṛkṣā mattairdvirephaiśca saroruhāṇi goṣṭhībhirudyānavanāni caiva tasminnaśūnyāni sadā kriyante  BhN svavikalpena racitaṃ tulyāvayavalakṣaṇam kiñcitsādṛśyasampannaṃ yadrūpaṃ rūpakaṃ tu tat  BhN nānādravyānurāgādyairyadaupamyaguṇāśrayam rūpanirvarṇanāyuktaṃ tadrūpakamiti smṛtam  BhN yathāpadmānanāstāḥ kumudaprahāsā vikāsinīlotpalacārunetrāḥ vāpīstriyo haṃsakulairnaḥ svanadbhirvirejuranyonyamivāhvayantyaḥ  BhN śabdābhyāsastu yamakaṃ padādiṣu vikalpitam viśeṣadarśanañcāsya gadato me nibodhata  BhN pādāntayamakaṃ caiva kāñcīyamakameva ca samudgayamakaṃ caiva vikrāntayamakaṃ tathā  BhN yamakaṃ cakravālaṃ ca sandaṣṭayamakaṃ tathā padādiyamakañcaiva hyāmreḍitamathāpi ca  BhN caturvyavasitañcaiva mālāyamakameva ca etādṛśavidhaṃ jñeyaṃ yamakaṃ nāṭakāśrayam  BhN caturṇāṃ yatra pādānāmante syātsamamakṣaram tadvai pādāntayamakaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāmato yathā  BhN dinakṣayāt saṃhṛtaraśmimaṇḍalaṃdivīva lagnaṃ tapanīyamaṇḍalam vibhāti tāmraṃ divi sūryamaṇḍalaṃyathā taruṇyāḥ stanabhāramaṇḍalam  BhN lokānāṃ prabhaviṣṇurdaityendragadānipātanasahiṣṇuḥ jayati suradaityajiṣṇurbhagavānasuravaramathanakārī viṣṇuḥ  BhN pādasyānte tathā cādau syātāṃ yatra same pade tatkāñcīyamakaṃ caiva vijñeyaṃ sūribhiryathā  BhN yāmaṃ yāmaṃ candravatīnāṃ dravatīnāṃvyaktāvyaktā sārajanīnāṃ rajanīnām phulle phulle sambhramare vābhramare vārāmā rāmā vismayate ca smayate ca  BhN ardhenaikena yadvṛttaṃ sarvameva samāpyate samudgayamakaṃ nāma tajjñeyaṃ paṇḍitairyathā  BhN ketakīkusumapāṇḍuradantaḥśobhate pravarakānanahastī ketakīkusumapāṇḍuradantaḥśobhate pravarakānanahastī  BhN ekaikaṃ pādamutkramya dvau pādau sadṛśau yadi vikrāntayamakaṃ nāma tadvijñeyamidaṃ yathā  BhN sa pūrvaṃ vāraṇo bhūtvā dviśṛṅga iva parvataḥ abhavaddantavaikalyādviśṛṅga iva parvataḥ  BhN pūrvasyāntena pādasya parasyādiryadā samaḥ cakravaccakravālaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ nāmato yathā  BhN tulyātpādadvayādantyādekenādiryadā samaḥ sarvatra cakravālantu tadvijñeyaṃ budhairyathā  BhN śailā yathā śatrubhirāhatā hatā hatāśca bhūyastvanupuṅkhapuṅkhagaiḥ khagaiśca sarvairyudhi sañcitāścitāścitādhirūḍhā nihitāstalaistalaiḥ  BhN ādau dvau yatra pādau tu bhavetāmakṣare samau sandaṣṭayamakaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ tadbudhairyathā  BhN paśya paśya ramaṇasya me guṇān yena yena vaśagāṃ karoti mām yena yena hi sameti darśanaṃ tena tena vaśagāṃ karoti mām  BhN ādau pādasya tu yatra syāt samāveśaḥ samākṣaraḥ pādādiyamakaṃ nāma tadvijñeyaṃ budhairyathā  BhN viṣṇuḥ sṛjati bhūtāni viṣṇuḥ saṃharate prajāḥ viṣṇuḥ prasūte trailokyaṃ viṣṇurlokādhidaivatam  BhN pādasyāntaṃ padaṃ yatra dvirdvirekamihocyate jñeyamāmreḍitaṃ nāma yamakaṃ tatra sūribhiḥ  BhN vijṛmbhitaṃ niḥśvasitaṃ muhurmuhuḥ kathaṃ vidheyaṃ smaraṇaṃ pade pade yathā ca te dhyānamidaṃ punaḥ punardhuvaṃgatā te rajanī vinā vinā  BhN sarve pādāḥ samā yatra bhavanti niyatākṣarāḥ caturvyavasitaṃ nāma tadvijñeyaṃ budhairyathā  BhN vāraṇānāmayameva kālo vāraṇānāmayameva kālaḥ vāraṇānāmayameva kālo vāraṇānāmayameva kālaḥ  BhN nānārūpaiḥ svarairyuktaṃ yatraikaṃ vyañjanaṃ bhavet tanmālāyamakaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ paṇḍitairyathā  BhN lalī balī halī mālī khelī mālī salī jalī khalo balo balo mālī musalī tvābhirakṣatu  BhN asau hi rāmā rativigrahapriyā rahaḥpragalbhā ramaṇaṃ manogatam ratena rātriṃ ramayet pareṇa vā na cedudeṣyattaruṇaḥ paro ripuḥ  BhN na puṣkarākṣaḥ kṣatajokṣitākṣaḥ kṣaratkṣatevyaḥ kṣatajaṃdurīkṣaḥ kṣatairgavākṣairiva saṃvṛtājñaḥ sākṣāt sahasrākṣa ivāvabhāti  BhN ebhirarthakriyāpekṣaiḥ kāryaṃ kāvyaṃ tu lakṣaṇaiḥ ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kāvye doṣān guṇāṃstathā  BhN gūḍhārthamarthāntaramarthahīnaṃ bhinnārthamekārthamabhiplutārtham nyāyāvapetaṃ viṣamaṃ visandhi śabdacyutaṃ vai daśa kāvyadoṣāḥ  BhN paryāyaśabdābhihataṃ gūḍhārthamabhisaṃjñitam avarṇyaṃ varṇyate yatra tadarthāntaramiṣyate  BhN arthahīnaṃ tvasambaddhaṃ sāvaśeṣārthameva ca bhinnārthamabhivijñeyamasabhyaṃ grāmyameva ca  BhN vivakṣito nya evārtho yatrānyārthena bhidyate bhinnārthaṃ tadapi prāhuḥ kāvyaṃ kāvyavicakṣaṇāḥ  BhN aviśeṣābhidhānaṃ yat tadekārthamiti smṛtam abhiplutārthaṃ vijñeyaṃ yat padena samasyate  BhN nyāyādapetaṃ vijñeyaṃ pramāṇaparivarjitam vṛttabhedo bhavedyatra viṣamaṃ nāma tadbhavet  BhN anupaśiṣṭaśabdaṃ yat tadvisandhīti kīrtitam śabdacyutañca vijñeyamaśabdasvarayojanāt  BhN ete doṣāstu vijñeyāḥ sūribhirnāṭakāśrayāḥ guṇā viparyayādeṣāṃ mādhuryaudāryalakṣaṇāḥ  BhN śleṣaḥ prasādaḥ samatāsamādhirmādhuryamojaḥ padasaukumāryam arthasya ca vyaktirudāratā ca kāntiśca kāvyasya guṇā daśaite  BhN īpsitenārthajātena sambaddhānāṃ parasparam śliṣṭatā yā padānāṃ hi śleṣa ityabhidhīyate  BhN vicāragahanaṃ yatsyāt sphuṭañcaiva svabhāvataḥ svataḥ supratibaddhañca śliṣṭaṃ tat parikīrtyate  BhN apyanukto budhairyatra śabdo rtho vā pratīyate sukhaśabdārthasaṃyogāt prasādaḥ parikīrtyate  BhN nāticūrṇapadairyuktā na ca vyarthābhidāyibhiḥ durbodhanaiśca na kṛtā samatvāt samatā matā  BhN anyonyasadṛśā yatra tathā hyanyonyabhūṣaṇāḥ alaṅkārā guṇāścaiva samāḥ syuḥ samatāṃ matāḥ  BhN abhiyuktairviśeṣastu yo rthasyehopalakṣyate tena cārthena sampannaḥ samādhiḥ parikīrtyate  BhN upamāsviha dṛṣṭānāmarthānāṃ yatnatastathā prāptānāṃ cātisaṃkṣepāt samādhirnirṇayo yataḥ  BhN bahuśo yacchrutaṃ vākyamuktaṃ vāpi punaḥ punaḥ nodvejayati yasmāddhi tanmādhuryamiti smṛtam  BhN samāsavadbhirvividhairvicitraiśca padairyutam sānusvārairudāraiśca tadojaḥ parikīrtyate  BhN avagīto pi hīno pi syādudāttāvabhāsakaḥ yatra śabdārthasampattistadojaḥ parikīrtitam  BhN sukhaprayojyairyacchabdairyuktaṃ suśliṣṭasandhibhiḥ sukumārārthasaṃyuktaṃ saukumāryaṃ taducyate  BhN suprasiddhābhidhānā tu lokakarmavyavasthitā yā kriyā kriyate kāvye sārthavyaktiḥ pratīyate  BhN yasyārthānupraveśena manasā parikalpyate anantaraṃ prayogastu sārthavyaktirudāhṛtā  BhN divyabhāvaparītaṃ yacchṛṅgārādbhutayojitam anekabhāvasaṃyuktamudāratvaṃ prakīrtitam  BhN anekārthaviśeṣairyat sūktaiḥ sauṣṭhavasaṃyutaiḥ upetamaticitrārthaiḥ udāttaṃ tacca kīrtyate  BhN yanmanaśśrotraviṣayamāhlādayati hīnduvat līlādyarthopapannāṃ vā tāṃ kāntiṃ kavayo viduḥ  BhN yo manaśśrotraviṣayaḥ prasādajanako bhavet śabdabandhaḥ prayogeṇa sa kānta iti bhaṇyate  BhN evamete hyalaṅkārā guṇā doṣāśca kīrtitāḥ prayogameṣāṃ ca punarvakṣyāmi rasasaṃśrayam  BhN laghvakṣaraprāyakṛtamupamārūpakāśrayam kāvyaṃ kāryaṃ tu nāṭyajñaiḥ vīraraudrādbhutāśrayam  BhN gurvakṣaraprāyakṛtaṃ bībhatse karuṇe tathā kadācidraudravīrābhyāṃ yadāgharṣaṇajaṃ bhavet  BhN rūpadīpakasaṃyuktamāryāvṛttasamāśrayam śṛṅgāre ca rase vīre kāvyaṃ syānnāṭakāśrayam  BhN uttarottarasaṃyuktaṃ vīre kāvyaṃ tu yadbhavet jagatyatijagatyāṃ vā saṃkṛtyāṃ vāpi tadbhavet  BhN tathaiva yuddhasampheṭā utkṛtyāṃ saṃprakīrtitau karuṇe śakvarī jñeyā tathaivātidhṛtirbhavet  BhN yadvīre kīrtitaṃ cchandaḥ tadraudre pi prayojayet śeṣāṇāmarthayogena cchandaḥ kāryaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN yacchandaḥ pūrvamuddiṣṭaṃ viṣamārdhasame samam udāramadhuraiḥ śabdaistatkāryaṃ tu rasānugam  BhN śabdānudāramadhurān pramadābhidheyān nāṭyāśrayeṣu kṛtiṣu prayayeta kartum tairbhūṣitā bahu vibhānti hi kāvyabandhāḥ padmākarā vikasitā iva rājahaṃsaiḥ  BhN trividhaṃ hyakṣaraṃ kāryaṃ kavibhirnāṭakāśrayam hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutañcaiva rasabhāvavibhāvakam  BhN ekamātraṃ bhaved hrasvaṃ dvimātraṃ dīrghamiṣyate plutaṃ caiva trimātraṃ syādakṣaraṃ svarayojanāt  BhN smṛte cāsūyite caiva tathā ca paridevite paṭhatāṃ brāhmaṇānāñca plutamakṣaramiṣyate  BhN akārastu smṛte kāryaṃ ūkāraścāpyasūyite paridevite tu hākāra Oṃkāro dhyayane tathā  BhN hrasvadīrghaplutānīha yathābhāvaṃ yathārasam kāvyayogeṣu sarveṣu hyakṣarāṇi prayojayet  BhN cekrīḍitaprabhṛtibhirvikṛtaistu śabdaiḥ yuktā na bhānti lalitā bharataprayogāḥ yajñakriyeva rurucarmadhuraiḥ kṛtāktaiḥ veśyā dvijairiva kamaṇḍaludaṇḍahastaiḥ  BhN mṛdulalitapadārthaṃ gūḍhaśabdārthahīnaṃ budhajanasukhabhogyaṃ yuktimannṛttayogyam bahurasakṛtamārgaṃ sandhisandhānayuktaṃ bhavati jagati yogyaṃ nāṭakaṃ prekṣakāṇām  BhN anubandhaḥbhūṣaṇākṣarasaṅghātau śobhodāharaṇe tathā hetusaṃśayadṛṣṭāntāḥ prāptābhiprāya eva ca  BhN nidarśanaṃ niruktaṃ ca siddhiścātha viśeṣaṇam guṇātipātātiśayau tulyatarkaḥ padoccayaḥ  BhN dṛṣṭaṃ caivopadiṣṭaṃ ca vicārastadviparyayaḥ bhraṃśaścānunayo mālā dākṣiṇyaṃ garhaṇaṃ tathā  BhN arthāpattiḥ prasiddhiśca pṛcchā sārūpyameva ca manorathaśca leśaśca kṣobho tha guṇakīrtanam  BhN jñeyānyanuktasiddhiśca priyaṃ vacanameva ca ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇānyeva kāvyabandheṣu nirdiśet  BhN alaṅkārairguṇaiścaiva bahubhiḥ samalaṃkṛtam bhūṣaṇairiva citrārthaistad bhūṣaṇamiti smṛtam  BhN yatrālpairakṣaraiḥ śliṣṭairvicitramupavarṇyate tamapyakṣarasaṅghātaṃ vidyāllakṣaṇasaṃjñitam  BhN siddhairarthaiḥ samaṃ kṛtvā hyasiddho rthaḥ prayujyate yatra śliṣṭā vicitrārthā sā śobhetyabhidhīyate  BhN yatra tulyārthayuktena vākyenābhipradarśanāt sādhyante nipuṇairarthāstadudāharaṇaṃ smṛtam  BhN yat prayojanasāmarthyāt vākyamiṣṭārthasādhakam samāsoktaṃ manogrāhi sa heturiti saṃjñitaḥ  BhN aparijñātatattvārthaṃ vākyaṃ yatra samāpyate anekatvādvicārāṇāṃ sa saṃśaya iti smṛtaḥ  BhN sarvalokamanogrāhi yastu pakṣārthasādhakaḥ hetornidarśanakṛtaḥ sa dṛṣṭānta iti smṛtaḥ  BhN dṛṣṭvaivāvayavān kāṃścid bhāvo yatrānumīyate prāptiṃ tāmapi jānīyāllakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam  BhN abhūtapūrvo yo pyarthaḥ sādṛśyātparikalpitaḥ lokasya hṛdayagrāhī so bhiprāya iti smṛtaḥ  BhN yatrārthānāṃ prasiddhānāṃ kriyate parikīrtanam parāpekṣādyudāsārthaṃ tannidarśanamucyate  BhN niravadyasya vākyasya pūrvoktārthaprasiddhaye yaducyate tu vacanaṃ niruktaṃ tadudāhṛtam  BhN bahūnāṃ ca pradhānānāṃ nāma yatrābhikīrtyate abhipretārthasiddhyarthaṃ sā siddhirabhidhīyate  BhN siddhān bahūn pradhānārthān uktvā yatra prayujyate viśeṣayuktaṃ vacanaṃ vijñeyaṃ tadviśeṣaṇam  BhN guṇābhidhānairvividhairviparītārthayojitaiḥ guṇātipāto madhurairniṣṭhurārthairbhavedatha  BhN bahūn guṇān kīrtayitvā sāmānyajanasambhavān viśeṣaḥ kīrtyate yastu jñeyaḥ so tiśayo budhaiḥ  BhN rūpakairupasābhirvā tulyārthaiḥ suprayojitaiḥ apratyakṣārthasaṃsparśastulyatarkaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN bahūnāṃ ca prayuktānāṃ padānāṃ bahubhiḥ padaiḥ uccayaḥ sadṛśārtho yaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ padoccayaḥ  BhN yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ yathārūpaṃ ca varṇyate yatpratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā dṛṣṭaṃ tadvarṇato pi vā  BhN parigṛhya tu śāstrārthaṃ yadvākyamabhidhīyate vidvanmanoharaṃ svantamupadiṣṭaṃ taducyate  BhN pūrvāśayasamānārthairapratyakṣārthasādhanaiḥ anekopādhisaṃyukto vicāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ  BhN vicārasyānyathābhāvastathā dṛṣṭopadiṣṭayoḥ sandehātkalpyate yastu sa vijñeyo viparyayaḥ  BhN vācyamarthaṃ parityajya dṛṣṭādibhiranekadhā anyasminneva patanādiha bhraṃśaḥ sa iṣyate  BhN ubhayoḥ prītijanano viruddhābhiniviṣṭayoḥ arthasya sādhakaścaiva vijñeyo nunayo budhaiḥ  BhN īpsitārthaprasiddhyarthaṃ kīrtyate yatra sūribhiḥ prayojanānyanekāni sā māletyabhisaṃjñitā  BhN hṛṣṭaiḥ prasannavadanairyatparasyānuvartanam kriyate vākyaceṣṭābhistaddākṣiṇyamiti smṛtam  BhN yatra saṃkīrtayan doṣaṃ guṇamarthena darśayet guṇātipātād doṣādvā garhaṇaṃ nāma tadbhavet  BhN arthāntarasya kathane yatrānyo rthaḥ pratīyate vākyamādhuryasampannā sārthāpattirudāhṛtā  BhN vākyaiḥ sātiśayairuktā vākyārthasya prasādhakaiḥ lokaprasiddhairbahubhiḥ prasiddhiriti kīrtitā  BhN yatrākārodbhavairvākyairātmānamathavā param pṛcchyate cābhidhatte rthaṃ sā pṛcchetyabhisaṃjñitā  BhN dṛṣṭaśrutānubhūtārthakathanādisamudbhavam sādṛśyaṃ kṣobhajananaṃ sārūpyamiti saṃjñitam  BhN hṛdayasthasya vākyasya gūḍhārthasya vibhāvakam anyāpadeśaiḥ kathanaṃ manoratha iti smṛtaḥ  BhN yadvākyaṃ vākyakuśalairupāyenābhidhīyate sadṛśārthābhiniṣpattyāḥ sa leśa iti kīrtitaḥ  BhN paradoṣairvicitrārthairyatrātmā parikīrtyate adṛṣṭo pyanyo pi vā kaścit sa tu kṣobha iti smṛtaḥ  BhN loke guṇātiriktānāṃ guṇānāṃ yatra nāmabhiḥ eko pi śabdyate tattu vijñeyaṃ guṇakīrtanam  BhN prastāvenaiva śeṣo rthaḥ kṛtsno yatra pratīyate vacanena vinānuktasiddhiḥ sā parikīrtitā  BhN yatprasannena manasā pūjyaṃ pūjayituṃ vacaḥ hṛṣṭaprakāśanārthaṃ tu sā priyoktirudāhṛtā  BhN etāni kāvyasya ca lakṣaṇāni ṣaṭtriṃśaduddeśanidarśanāni prabandhaśobhākaraṇāni tajjñaiḥ samyak prayojyāni rasāyanāni  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre vāgabhinaye kāvyalakṣaṇo nāma ṣoḍaśo dhyāyaḥatha aṣṭādaśo dhyāyaḥvarttayiṣyāmyahaṃ viprā daśarūpavikalpanam nāmataḥ karmataścaiva tathā caiva prayogataḥ  BhN nāṭakaṃ saprakaraṇamaṅko vyāyoga eva ca bhāṇaḥ samavakāraśca vīthī prahasanaṃ ḍimaḥ  BhN īhāmṛgaśca vijñeyā daśeme nāṭyalakṣaṇe eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇamahaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN sarveṣāmeva kāvyānāṃ mātṛkā vṛttayaḥ smṛtāḥ ābhyo vinisṛtaṃ hyetaddaśarūpaṃ prayogataḥ  BhN jātibhiḥ śrutibhiścaiva svarā grāmatvamāgatāḥ yathā tathā vṛttibhedaiḥ kāvyabandhā bhavanti hi  BhN grāmau pūrṇasvarau dvau tu yathā vai ṣaḍjamadhyamau sarvavṛttiviniṣpannau kāvyabandhau tathā tvimau  BhN jñeyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ caiva tathā nāṭakameva ca sarvavṛttiviniṣpannaṃ nānābandhasamāśrayam  BhN vīthī samavakāraśca tathehāmṛga eva ca utsṛṣṭikāṅko vyāyogo bhāṇaḥ prahasanaṃ ḍimaḥ  BhN kaiśikīvṛttihīnāni rūpāṇyetāni kārayet ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi kāvyabandhavikalpanam  BhN prakhyātavastuviṣayaṃ prakhyātodāttanāyakaṃ caiva rājarṣivaṃśyacaritaṃ tathaiva divyāśrayopetam  BhN nānāvibhūtibhiryutamṛddhivilāsādibhirguṇaiścaiva aṅkapraveśakāḍhyaṃ bhavati hi tannāṭakaṃ nāma  BhN nṛpatīnāṃ yaccaritaṃ nānārasabhāvaceṣṭitaṃ bahudhā sukhaduḥkhotpattikṛtaṃ bhavati hi tannāṭakaṃ nāma  BhN asyāvasthopetaṃ kāryaṃ prasamīkṣya binduvistārāt kartavyo ṅkaḥ so pi tu guṇānvitaṃ nāṭyatattvajñaiḥ  BhN aṅka iti rūḍhiśabdo bhāvaiśca rasaiśca rohayatyarthān nānāvidhānayukto yasmāttasmādbhavedaṅkaḥ  BhN aṅkasamāptiḥ kāryā kāvyacchedena bījasaṃhāraḥ vastuvyāpī binduḥ kāvyasamuttho tra nityaṃ syāt  BhN yatrārthasya samāptiryatra ca bījasya bhavati saṃhāraḥ kiñcidavalagnabinduḥ so ṅka iti sadāvagantavyaḥ  BhN ye nāyakā nigaditāsteṣāṃ pratyakṣacaritasaṃyogaḥ nānāvasthopetaḥ kāryastvaṅko viprakṛṣṭastu  BhN nāyakadevīgurujanapurohitāmātyasārthavāhānām naikarasāntaravihito hyaṅka iti sa veditavyastu  BhN pañcākṣarā daśaparā hyaṅkāḥ syurnāṭake prakaraṇe ca niṣkrāmaḥ sarveṣāṃ yasminnaṅkaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ  BhN krodhaprasādaśokāḥ śāpotsargo tha vidravodvāhau adbhutasambhavadarśanamaṅke pratyakṣajāni syuḥ  BhN ekadivasapravṛttaḥ kāryastvaṅko rthabījamadhikṛtya āvaśyakakāryāṇāmavirodhena prayogeṣu  BhN ekāṅkena kadācidbahūni kāryāṇi yojayeddhīmān āvaśyakāvirodhena tatra kāvyāni kāryāṇi  BhN raṅgaṃ tu ye praviṣṭāḥ sarveṣāṃ bhavati tatra niṣkrāmaḥ bījārthayuktiyuktaṃ kṛtvā kāvyaṃ yathārtharasam  BhN na bahūnīha kāryāṇi tvekāṅke viniyojayet āvaśyakānāṃ kāryāṇāṃ virodho hi tathā bhavet  BhN jñātvā divasāvasthāṃ kṣaṇayāmamuhūrtalakṣaṇopetām vibhajetsarvamaśeṣaṃ pṛthakpṛthakkāvyamaṅkeṣu  BhN divasāvasānakāryaṃ yadyaṅke nopapadyate sarvam aṅkacchedaṃ kṛtvā praveśakaistadvidhātavyam  BhN viprakṛṣṭaṃ tu yo deśaṃ gacchetkāryavaśānugaḥ aṅkacchede tha saṃkṣepānnirdiśettaṃ praveśakaiḥ  BhN sannihitanāyako ṅkaḥ kartavyo nāṭake prakaraṇe vā parijanakathānubandhaḥ praveśako nāma vijñeyaḥ  BhN prakaraṇanāṭakaviṣaye pañcādyā daśaparā bhavantyaṅkāḥ aṅkāntarasandhiṣu ca praveśakāsteṣu tāvantaḥ  BhN anayorantaravihitaḥ praveśako rthakriyāṃ samabhivīkṣya saṃkṣepārthaḥ sandhiṣvarthānāṃ saṃvidhātavyaḥ  BhN aṅkacchedaṃ kṛtvā māsakṛtaṃ varṣasañcitaṃ vāpi tatsarvaṃ kartavyaṃ varṣādūrdhvaṃ na tu kadācit  BhN yaḥ kaścitkāryavaśādgacchati puruṣaḥ prakṛṣṭamadhvānam tatrāpyaṅkacchedaḥ kartavyaḥ pūrvavattajñaiḥ  BhN aṅkāntarānusārī saṃkṣepārthamadhikṛtya bindūnām prakaraṇanāṭakaviṣaye praveśakaḥ saṃvidhātavyaḥ  BhN nottamamadhyamapuruṣairācarito nāpyudāttavacanakṛtaḥ prākṛtabhāṣācāraḥ prayogamāśritya kartavyaḥ  BhN kālotthānagatirasau vyākhyāsaṃrambhakāryaviṣayāṇām arthābhidhānayuktaḥ praveśakaḥ syādanekārthaḥ  BhN bahvāśrayamapi kāryaṃ praveśakaiḥ saṃkṣipecca sandhiṣu vā bahucūrṇapadairyuktaṃ janayati khedaṃ prayogasya  BhN yatrārthasya samāptirna bhavatyaṅke prayogabāhulyāt vṛttāntasvalpakathaiḥ praveśakaiḥ so bhidhātavyaḥ  BhN yuddhaṃ rājyabhraṃśo maraṇaṃ nagaroparodhanaṃ caiva pratyakṣāṇi tu nāṅke praveśakaiḥ saṃvidheyāni  BhN aṅke praveśake ca prakaraṇamāśritya nāṭake vāpi na vadhaḥ kartavyaḥ syādyo bhyudayī nāyakaḥ khyātaḥ  BhN apasaraṇameva kāryaṃ grahaṇaṃ vā sandhireva vā yojyaḥ kāvyaśleṣairbahubhiryathārasaṃ nāṭyatattvajñaiḥ  BhN na mahājanaparivāraṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭakaṃ prakaraṇaṃ vā ye tatra kāryapuruṣāścatvāraḥ pañca vā te syuḥ  BhN kāryaṃ gopucchāgraṃ kartavyaṃ kāvyabandhamāsādya ye codāttā bhāvāste sarve pṛṣṭhataḥ kāryāḥ  BhN sarveṣāṃ kāvyānāṃ nānārasabhāvayuktiyuktānām nirvahaṇe kartavyo nityaṃ hi raso dbhutastajjñaiḥ  BhN nāṭakalakṣaṇametanmayā samāsena kīrtitaṃ vidhivat prakaraṇamataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇayuktyā pravakṣyāmi  BhN yatra kavirātmaśaktyā vastu śarīraṃ ca nāyakaṃ caiva autpattikaṃ prakurute prakaraṇamiti tadbudhairjñeyam  BhN yadanārṣamathāhāryaṃ kāvyaṃ prakarotyabhūtaguṇayuktam utpannabījavastu prakaraṇamiti tadapi vijñeyam  BhN yannāṭake mayoktaṃ vastu śarīraṃ ca vṛttibhedāśca tatprakaraṇe pi yojyaṃ salakṣaṇaṃ sarvasandhiṣu tu  BhN vipravaṇikṣacivānāṃ purohitāmātyasārthavāhānām caritaṃ yannaikavidhaṃ jñeyaṃ tatprakaraṇaṃ nāma  BhN nodāttanāyakakṛtaṃ na divyacaritaṃ na rājasambhogam bāhyajanasaṃprayuktaṃ tajjñeyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ tajjñaiḥ  BhN dāsaviṭaśreṣṭhiyutaṃ veśastryupacārakāraṇopetam mandakulastrīcaritaṃ kāvyaṃ kāryaṃ prakaraṇe tu  BhN sacivaśreṣṭhibrāhmaṇapurohitāmātyasārthavāhānām gṛhavārtā yatra bhavenna tatra veśyāṅganā kāryā  BhN yadi veśayuvatiyuktaṃ na kulastrī saṅgamo pi syāt atha kulajanaprayuktaṃ na veśayuvatirbhavettatra  BhN yadi vā kāraṇayuktyā veśakulastrīkṛtopacāraḥ syāt avikṛtabhāṣācāraṃ tatra tu pāṭhyaṃ prayoktavyam  BhN madhyamapuruṣairnityaṃ yojyo viṣkambhako tra tattvajjñaiḥ saṃskṛtavacanānugataḥ saṃkṣepārthaḥ praveśakavat  BhN śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo vā dvividho viṣkambhako pi kartavyaḥ madhyamapātraḥ śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo nīcamadhyakṛtaḥ  BhN aṅkāntarālavihitaḥ praveśako rthakriyāṃ samabhivīkṣya saṃkṣepātsandhīnāmarthānāṃ caiva kartavyaḥ  BhN anayośca bandhayogādanyo bhedaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ kāryaḥ prakhyātastvitaro vā nāṭakayoge prakaraṇe vā  BhN prakaraṇanāṭakabhedādutpādyaṃ vastu nāyakaṃ nṛpatim antaḥpurasaṅgītakakanyāmadhikṛtya kartavyā  BhN strīprāyā caturaṅkā lalitābhinayātmikā suvihitāṅgī bahunṛttagītapāṭhyā ratisambhogātmikā caiva  BhN rājopacārayuktā prasādanakrodhadambhasaṃyuktā nāyakadevīdūtī saparijanā nāṭikā jñeyā  BhN antarbhāvagatā hyeṣā bhāvayorubhayoryataḥ ata eva daśaitāni rūpāṇītyuditāni vai  BhN prakaraṇanāṭakalakṣaṇamuktaṃ viprā mayā samāsena vakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ yuktyā samavakāram  BhN devāsurabījakṛtaḥ prakhyātodāttanāyakaścaiva tryaṅkastathā trikapaṭastrividravaḥ syāttriśṛṅgāraḥ  BhN dvādaśanāyakabahulo hyaṣṭādaśanāḍikāpramāṇaśca vakṣyāmyasyāṅkavidhiṃ yāvatyo nāḍikā yatra  BhN aṅkastu saprahasanaḥ savidravaḥ sakapaṭaḥ savīthīkaḥ dvādaśanāḍīvihitaḥ prathamaḥ kāryaḥ kriyopetaḥ  BhN kāryastathā dvitīyaḥ samāśrito nāḍikāścatasrastu vastusamāpanavihito dvināḍikaḥ syāttṛtīyastu  BhN nāḍīsaṃjñā jñeyā mānaṃ kālasya yanmuhūrtārdham tannāḍikāpramāṇaṃ yathoktamaṅkeṣu saṃyojyam  BhN yā nāḍiketi saṃjñā kālavibhāge kriyābhisaṃpannā kāryā ca sā prayatnādyathā krameṇaiva śāstroktā  BhN aṅko ṅkastvanyārthaḥ kartavyaḥ kāvyabandhamāsādya arthaṃ hi samavakāre hyapratisambandhamicchanti  BhN yuddhajalasambhavo vā vāyvagnigajendrasaṃbhramakṛto vā nagaroparodhajo vā vijñeyo vidravastrividhaḥ  BhN vastugatakramavihito devavaśādvā paraprayukto vā sukhaduḥkhotpattikṛtastrividhaḥ kapaṭo tra vijñeyaḥ  BhN trividhaścātra vidhijñaiḥ pṛthakpṛthakkāryavihitārthaḥ śṛṅgāraḥ kartavyo dharme cārthe ca kāme ca  BhN yasmin dharmaprāpakamātmahitaṃ bhavati sādhanaṃ bahudhā vrataniyamatapoyukto jñeyo sau dharmaśṛṅgāraḥ  BhN arthasyecchāyogādbahudhā caivārthato rthaśṛṅgāraḥ strīsaṃprayogaviṣayeṣvarthārthā vā ratiryatra  BhN kanyāvilobhanakṛtaṃ prāptau strīpuṃsayostu ramyaṃ vā nibhṛtaṃ sāvegaṃ vā yasya bhavetkāmaśṛṅgāraḥ  BhN uṣṇiggāyatryādīnyanyāni ca yāni bandhakuṭilāni vṛttāni samavakāre kavibhistāni prayojyāni  BhN evaṃ kāryastajjñairnānārasasaṃśrayaḥ samavakāraḥ vakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇamīhāmṛgasyāpi  BhN divyāpuruṣāśrayakṛto divyastrīkāraṇopagatayuddhaḥ suvihitavastunibaddho vipratyayakārakaścaiva  BhN uddhatapuruṣaprāyaḥ strīroṣagrathitakāvyabandhaśca saṃkṣobhavidravakṛtaḥ saṃpheṭakṛtastathā caiva  BhN strībhedanāpaharaṇāvamardanaprāptavastuśṛṅgāraḥ īhāmṛgastu kāryaḥ susamāhitakāvyabandhaśca  BhN yadvyāyoge kāryaṃ ye puruṣā vṛttayo rasāścaiva īhāmṛge pi te syuḥ kevalamamarastriyā yogaḥ  BhN yatra tu vadhepsitānāṃ vadho hyudagro bhaveddhi puruṣāṇām kiñcidvyājaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ śamayitavyam  BhN īhāmṛgasya lakṣaṇamuktaṃ viprāḥ samāsayogena ḍimalakṣaṇaṃ tu bhūyo lakṣaṇayuktyā pravakṣyāmi  BhN prakhyātavastuviṣayaḥ prakhyātodāttanāyakaścaiva ṣaḍrasalakṣaṇayuktaścaturaṅko vai ḍimaḥ kāryaḥ  BhN śṛṅgārahāsyavarjaṃ śeṣaiḥ sarvai rasaiḥ samāyuktaḥ dīptarasakāvyayonirnānābhāvopasampannaḥ  BhN nirghātolkāpātairuparāgeṇendusūryayoryuktaḥ yuddhaniyuddhādharṣaṇasaṃpheṭakṛtaśca kartavyaḥ  BhN māyendrajālabahulo bahupustotthānayogayuktaśca devabhujagendrarākṣasayakṣapiśācāvakīrṇaśca  BhN ṣoḍaśanāyakabahulaḥ sātvattyārabhaṭīvṛttisampannaḥ kāryo ḍimaḥ prayatnānnānāśrayabhāvasampannaḥ  BhN ḍimalakṣaṇamityuktaṃ mayā samāsena lakṣaṇānugatam vyāyogasya tu lakṣaṇamataḥ paraṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi  BhN vyāyogastu vidhijñaiḥ kāryaḥ prakhyātanāyakaśarīraḥ alpastrījanayuktastvekāhakṛtastathā caiva  BhN bahavaśca tatra puruṣā vyāyacchante yathā samavakāre na ca divyanāyakayuktaḥ kāryastvekāṅka evāyam  BhN na ca divyanāyakakṛtaḥ kāryo rājarṣināyakanibaddhaḥ yuddhaniyuddhāgharṣaṇasaṃgharṣakṛtaśca kartavyaḥ  BhN evaṃvidhastu kāryo vyāyogo dīptakāvyarasayoniḥ vakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇamutsṛṣṭāṅkasya  BhN prakhyātavastuviṣayastvaprakhyātaḥ kadācideva syāt divyapuruṣairviyuktaḥ śeṣairyukto bhavetpuṃbhiḥ  BhN karuṇarasaprāyakṛto nivṛttayuddhodyataprahāraśca strīparidevitabahulo nirveditabhāṣitaścaiva  BhN nānāvyākulaceṣṭaḥ sātvattyārabhaṭikaiśikīhīnaḥ kāryaḥ kāvyavidhijñaiḥ satataṃ hyutsṛṣṭikāṅkastu  BhN yaddivyanāyakakṛtaṃ kāvyaṃ saṃgrāmabandhavadhayuktam tadbhārate tu varṣe kartavyaṃ kāvyabandheṣu  BhN kasmādbhāratamiṣṭaṃ varṣeṣvanyeṣu devavihiteṣu hṛdyā sarvā bhūmiḥ śubhagandhā kāñcanī yasmāt  BhN upavanagamanakrīḍā vihāranārīratipramodāḥ syuḥ teṣu hi varṣeṣu sadā na tatra duḥkhaṃ na vā śokaḥ  BhN ye teṣāmadhivāsāḥ purāṇavādeṣu parvatāḥ proktāḥ sambhogasteṣu bhavetkarmārambho bhavedasmin  BhN prahasanamapi vijñeyaṃ dvividhaṃ śuddhaṃ tathā saṅkīrṇam aṅkasya lakṣaṇamidaṃ vyākhyātamaśeṣayogamātragatam  BhN prahasanamataḥ paraṃ salakṣaṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi vakṣyāmi tayoryuktyā pṛthagpṛthaglakṣaṇaviśeṣam  BhN bhagavattāpasaviprairanyairapi hāsyavādasambaddham kāpuruṣasaṃprayuktaṃ parihāsābhāṣaṇaprāyam  BhN avikṛtabhāṣācāraṃ viśeṣabhāvopapannacaritapadam niyatagativastuviṣayaṃ śuddhaṃ jñeyaṃ prahasanaṃ tu  BhN veśyāceṭanapuṃsakaviṭadhūrtā bandhakī ca yatra syuḥ anibhṛtaveṣaparicchadaceṣṭitakaraṇaistu saṃkīrṇam  BhN lokopacārayuktā yā vārtā yaśca dambhasaṃyogaḥ sa prahasane prayojyo dhūrtapravivādasampannaḥ  BhN vīthyaṅgaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ kartavyaṃ prahasanaṃ yathāyogyam bhāṇasyāpi tu lakṣaṇamataḥ paraṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi  BhN ātmānubhūtaśaṃsī parasaṃśrayavarṇanāviśeṣastu vividhāśrayo hi bhāṇo vijñeyastvekahāryaśca  BhN paravacanamātmasaṃsthaṃ prativacanairuttamottamagrathitaiḥ ākāśapuruṣakathitairaṅgavikārairabhinayaiścaiva  BhN dhūrtaviṭasaṃprayojyo nānāvasthāntarātmakaścaiva ekāṅko bahuceṣṭaḥ satataṃ kāryo budhairbhāṇaḥ  BhN bhāṇasyāpi hi nikhilaṃ lakṣaṇamuktaṃ tathāgamānugatam vīthyāḥ saṃprati nikhilaṃ kathayāmi yathākramaṃ viprāḥ  BhN sarvarasalakṣaṇāḍhyā yuktā hyaṅgaistrayodaśabhiḥ vīthī syādekāṅkā tathaikahāryā dvihāryā vā  BhN adhamottamamadhyābhiryuktā syātprakṛtibhistisṛbhiḥ uddhātyakāvalagitāvaspanditanālyasatpralāpāśca  BhN vākkelyatha prapañco mṛdavādhibale chalaṃ trigatam vyāhāro gaṇḍaśca trayodaśāṅgānyudāhṛtānyasyāḥ  BhN atha vīthī saṃproktā lakṣaṇameṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi padāni tvagatārthāni ye narāḥ punarādarāt  BhN yojayanti padairanyaistaduddhātyakamucyate yatrānyasmin samāveśya kāryamanyatprasādhyate  BhN taccāvalagitaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ākṣipte rthe tu kasmiṇścicchubhāśubhasamutthite  BhN kauśalāducyate nyo rthastadavaspanditaṃ bhavet hāsyenopagatārthaprahelikā nāliketi vijñeyā  BhN mūrkhajanasannikarṣe hitamapi yatra prabhāṣate vidvān na ca gṛhyate sya vacanaṃ vijñeyo satpralāpo sau  BhN ekadviprativacanā vākkelī syātprayoge smin yadasadbhūtaṃ vacanaṃ saṃstavayuktaṃ dvayoḥ parasparaṃ yattu  BhN ekasya cārthahetoḥ sa hāsyajananaḥ prapañcaḥ syāt yatkāraṇād guṇānāṃ doṣīkaraṇaṃ bhavedvivādakṛtam  BhN doṣaguṇīkaraṇaṃ vā tanmṛdavaṃ nāma vijñeyam paravacanamātmanaścottarottarasamudbhavaṃ dvayoryatra  BhN anyonyārthaviśeṣakamadhibalamiti tad budhairjñeyam anyārthameva vākyaṃ chalamabhisandhānahāsyaroṣakaram  BhN śrutisārūpyādyasmin bahavo rthā yuktibhirniyujyante yaddhāsyamahāsyaṃ vā tattrigataṃ nāma vijñeyam  BhN pratyakṣavṛttirukto vyāhāro hāsyaleśārthaḥ saṃrambhasaṃbhramayutaṃ vivādayuktaṃ tathāpavādakṛtam  BhN bahuvacanākṣepakṛtaṃ gaṇḍaṃ pravadanti tattvajñāḥ iti daśarūpavidhānaṃ sarvaṃ proktaṃ mayā hi lakṣaṇataḥ punarasya śarīragataṃ sandhividhau lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre daśarūpanirūpaṇaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo dhyāyaḥatha ekonaviṃśo dhyāyaḥitivṛttaṃ tu nāṭyasya śarīraṃ parikīrtitam pañcabhiḥ sandhibhistasya vibhāgaḥ samprakalpitaḥ  BhN itivṛttaṃ dvidhā caiva budhastu parikalpayet ādhikarikamekaṃ syāt prāsaṅgikamathāparam  BhN yatkāryaṃ hi phalaprāptyā sāmarthyātparikalpyate tadādhikārikaṃ jñeyamanyatprāsaṅgikaṃ viduḥ  BhN kāraṇātphalayogyasya vṛttaṃ syādādhikārikam tasyopakaraṇārthaṃ tu kīrtyate hyānuṣaṅgikam  BhN kaveḥ prayatnānnetṝṇāṃ yuktānāṃ viddhyupāśrayāt kalpyate hi phalaprāptiḥ samutkarṣātphalasya ca  BhN laukikī sukhaduḥkhākhyā yathāvasthā rasodbhavā daśadhā manmathāvasthā vyavasthāstrividhā matā  BhN saṃsāre phalayāge tu vyāpāraḥ kāraṇasya yaḥ tasyānupūrvyā vijñeyā pañcāvasthā prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN prārambhaśca prayatnaśca tathā prāpteśca saṃbhavaḥ niyatā ca phalaprāptiḥ phalayogaśca pañcamaḥ  BhN autsukyamātrabandhastu yadbījasya nibadhyate mahataḥ phalayogasya sa phalārambha iṣyate  BhN apaśyataḥ phalaprāptiṃ vyāpāro yaḥ phalaṃ prati paraṃ cautsukyagamanaṃ sa prayatnaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN īṣatprāptiryadā kācitphalasya parikalpate bhāvamātreṇa tu prāhurvidhijñāḥ prāptisambhavam  BhN niyatāṃ tu phalaprāptiṃ yadā bhāvena paśyati niyatāṃ tāṃ phalaprāptiṃ saguṇāṃ paricakṣate  BhN abhipretaṃ samagraṃ ca pratirūpaṃ kriyāphalam itivṛtte bhavedyasmin phalayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN sarvasyaiva hi kāryasya prārabdhasya phalārthibhiḥ etāstvanukrameṇaiva pañcāvasthā bhavanti hi  BhN āsāṃ svabhāvabhinnānāṃ parasparasamāgamāt vinyāsa ekabhāvena phalahetuḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN itivṛttaṃ samākhyātaṃ pratyagevādhikārikam tadārambhādi kartavyaṃ phalāntaṃ ca yathā bhavet  BhN pūrṇasandhi ca kartavyaṃ hīnasandhyapi vā punaḥ niyamāt pūrṇasandhi syāddhīnasandhyatha kāraṇāt  BhN ekalope caturthasya dvilope tricaturthayoḥ dvitīyatricaturthānāṃ trilope lopa iṣyate  BhN prāsaṅgike parārthatvānna hyeṣa niyamo bhavet yadvṛttaṃ sambhavettatra tadyojyamavirodhataḥ  BhN itivṛtte yathāvasthāḥ pañcārambhādikāḥ smṛtāḥ arthaprakṛtayaḥ pañca tathā bījādikā api  BhN bījaṃ binduḥ patākā ca prakarī kāryameva ca arthaprakṛtayaḥ pañca jñātvā yojyā yathāvidhi  BhN svalpamātraṃ samutsṛṣṭaṃ bahudhā yadvisarpati phalāvasānaṃ yaccaiva bījaṃ tatparikīrtitam  BhN prayojanānāṃ vicchede yadavicchedakāraṇam yāvatsamāptirbandhasya sa binduḥ parikīrtitaḥ  BhN yadvṛttaṃ tu parārthaṃ syāt pradhānasyopakārakampradhānavacca kalpyeta sā patāketi kīrtitā  BhN phalaṃ prakalpyate yasyāḥ parārthāyaiva kevalam anubandhavihīnatvāt prakarīti vinirdiśet  BhN yadādhikārikaṃ vastu samyak prājñaiḥ prayujyate tadartho yaḥ samārambhastatkāryaṃ parikīrtitam  BhN eteṣāṃ yasya yenārtho yataśca guṇa iṣyate tat pradhānaṃ tu kartavyaṃ guṇabhūtānyataḥ param  BhN eko neko pi vā sandhiḥ patākāyāṃ tu yo bhavet pradhānārthānuyāyitvādanusandhiḥ prakīrtyate  BhN āgarbhādāvimarśādvā patākā vinivartate kasmādyasmānnibandho syāḥ parārthaḥ parikīrtyate  BhN yatrārthe cintite nyasminstallinṅgo nyaḥ prayujyate āgantukena bhāvena patākāsthānakaṃ tu tat  BhN sahasaivārthasampattirguṇavatyupakārataḥ patākāsthānakamidaṃ prathamaṃ parikīrtitam  BhN vacaḥ sātiśayaṃ kliṣṭaṃ kāvyabandhasamāśrayam patākāsthānakamidaṃ dvitīayaṃ parikīrtitam  BhN arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yatra līnaṃ savinayaṃ bhavet śliṣṭapratyuttaropetaṃ tṛtīyamidamiṣyate  BhN dvyartho vacanavinyāsaḥ suśliṣṭaḥ kāvyayojitaḥ upanyāsasuyuktaśca taccaturthamudāhṛtam  BhN yatra sātiśayaṃ vākyamarthopakṣepaṇaṃ bhavet vināśidṛṣṭamante ca patākārdhaṃ tu tadbhavet   BhN catuṣpatākāparamaṃ nāṭake kāryayiṣyate pañcabhiḥ sandhibhiryuktaṃ tāṃśca vakṣyāmyataḥ param  BhN mukhaṃ pratimukhaṃ caiva garbho vimarśa eva ca tathā nirvahaṇaṃ ceti nāṭake pañca sandhayaḥ  BhN pañcabhiḥ sandhibhiryuktaṃ pradhānamanu kīrtyate śeṣāḥ pradhānasandhīnāmanugrāhyanusandhayaḥ  BhN yatra bījasamutpattirnānārtharasasambhavā kāvye śarīrānugatā tanmukhaṃ parikīrtitam  BhN bījasyodghāṭanaṃ yatra dṛṣṭanaṣṭamiva kvacit mukhanyastasya sarvatra tadvai pratimukhaṃ smṛtam  BhN udbhedastasya bījasya prāptiraprāptireva vā punaścānveṣaṇaṃ yatra sa garbha iti saṃjñitaḥ  BhN garbhanirbhinnabījārtho vilobhanakṛto thavā krodhavyasanajo vāpi sa vimarśa iti smṛtaḥ  BhN samānayanamarthānāṃ mukhādyānāṃ sabījinām nānābhāvottarāṇāṃ yadbhavennirvahaṇaṃ tu tat  BhN ete tu sandhayo jñeyā nāṭakasya prayoktṛbhiḥ tathā prakaraṇāsyāpi śeṣāṇāṃ ca nibodhata  BhN ḍimaḥ samavakāraśca catuḥsandhī prakīrtitau na tayoravamarśastu kartavyaḥ kavibhiḥ sadā  BhN vyāyogehāmṛgau cāpi sadā kāryau trisandhikau garbhāvamarśau na syātāṃ tayorvṛttiśca kaiśikī  BhN dvisandhi tu prahasanaṃ vīthyaṅko bhāṇa eva ca mukhanirvahane tatra kartavye kavibhiḥ sadā  BhN vīthī caiva hi bhāṇaśca tathā prahasanaṃ punaḥ kaiśikīvṛttihīnāni kāryāṇi kavibhiḥ sadā   BhN evaṃ hi sandhayaḥ kāryā daśarūpe prayoktṛbhiḥ punareṣāṃ tu sandhīnāmaṅgakalpaṃ nibodhadata  BhN sandhināṃ yāni vṛttāni pradeśeṣvanupūrvaśaḥ svasampadguṇayuktāni tānyaṅgānyupadhārayet  BhN iṣṭasyārthasya racanā vṛttāntasyānupakṣayaḥ rāgaprāptiḥ prayogasya guhyānāṃ caiva gūhanam  BhN āścaryavadabhikhyānaṃ prakāśyānāṃ prakāśanam aṅgānāṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ hyetad dṝṣṭaṃ śāstre prayojanam  BhN aṅgahīno naro yadvannaivārambhakṣamo bhavet aṅgahīnaṃ tathā kāvyaṃ na prayogakṣamaṃ bhavet  BhN udāttamapi tatkāvyaṃ syādaṅgaiḥ parivarjitam hīnatvāddhi prayogasya na satāṃ rañjayenmanaḥ  BhN kāvyaṃ yadapi hīnārthaṃ samyadaṅgaiḥ samanvitam dīptatvāttu prayogasya śobhāmeti na saṃśayaḥ  BhN tasmāt sandhipradeśeṣu yathāyogaṃ yathārasam kavināṅgāni kāryāṇi samyaktāni nibodhata  BhN upakṣepaḥ parikaraḥ parinyāso vilobhanam yuktiḥ prāptiḥ samādhānaṃ vidhānaṃ paribhāvanā  BhN udbhedaḥ karaṇaṃ bheda etānyaṅgāni vai mukhe tathā pratimukhe caiva śṛṇutāṅgāni nāmataḥ  BhN vilāsaḥ parisarpaśca vidhūtaṃ tāpanaṃ tathā narma narmadyutiścaiva tathā pragayaṇaṃ punaḥ  BhN nirodhaścaiva vijñeyaḥ paryupāsanameva ca puṣpaṃ vajramupanyāso varṇasaṃhāra eva ca  BhN etāni vai pratimukhe garbhe ṅgāni nibodhata abhūtāharaṇaṃ mārgo rūpodāharaṇe kramaḥ  BhN saṃgrahaścānumānaṃ ca prārthanākṣiptameva ca toṭakādhibale caiva hyudvego vidravastathā  BhN etānyaṅgāni vai garbhe hyavamarśe nibodhata apavādaśca saṃpheṭo vidravaḥ śaktireva ca  BhN vyavasāyaḥ prasaṅgaśca dyutiḥ khedo niṣedhanam virodhanamathādānaṃ chādanaṃ ca prarocanā  BhN vyavahāraśca yuktiśca vimarśāṅgānyamūni ca sandhirnirodho grathanaṃ nirṇayaḥ paribhāṣaṇam  BhN dyutiḥ prasāda ānandaḥ samayo hyupagūhanam bhāṣaṇaṃ pūrvavākyaṃ ca kāvyasaṃhāra eva ca  BhN praśastiriti saṃhāre jñeyānyaṅgāni nāmataḥ catuṣṣaṣṭhi budhairjñeyānyetānyaṅgāni sandhiṣu  BhN sampādanārthaṃ bījasya samyaksiddhikarāṇi ca kāryāṇyetāni kavibhirvibhajyārthāni nāṭake   BhN punareṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇāni yathākramam kāvyārthasya samutpattirupakṣepa iti smṛtaḥ  BhN yadutpannārthabāhulyaṃ jñeyaḥ parikarastu saḥ tanniṣpattiḥ parinyāso vijñeyaḥ kavibhiḥ sadā  BhN guṇanirvarṇanaṃ caiva vilobhanamiti smṛtam sampradhāraṇamarthānāṃ yuktirityabhidhīyate  BhN sukhārthasyābhigamanaṃ prāptirityabhisaṃjñitā bījārthasyopagamanaṃ samādhānamiti smṛtam  BhN sukhaduḥkhakṛto yo rthastadvidhānamiti smṛtam kutūhalottarāvego vijñeyā paribhāvanā  BhN bījārthasya praroho yaḥ sa udbheda iti smṛtaḥ prakṛtārthasamārambhaḥ karaṇaṃ nāma tadbhavet  BhN saṃghātabhedanārtho yaḥ sa bheda iti kīrtitaḥ etāni tu mukhāṅgāni vakṣye pratimukhe punaḥ  BhN samīhā ratibhogārthā vilāsa iti saṃjñitaḥ dṛṣṭanaṣṭānusaraṇaṃ parisarpa iti smṛtaḥ  BhN kṛtasyānunayasyādau vidhūtaṃ hyaparigrahaḥ apāyadarśanaṃ yattu tāpanaṃ nāma tadbhaveet  BhN krīḍārthaṃ vihitaṃ yattu hāsyaṃ narmeti tatsmṛtamdoṣapracchādanārthaṃ tu hāsyaṃ narmadyutiḥ smṛtā  BhN uttarottaravākyaṃ tu bhavetpragayaṇaṃ punaḥ yā tu vyasanasaṃprāptiḥ sa nirodhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN kruddhasyanunayo yastu bhavettatparyupāsanam viśeṣavacanaṃ yattu tatpuṣpamiti saṃjñitam  BhN pratyakṣarūkṣaṃ yadvākyaṃ vajraṃ tadabhidhīyate upapattikṛto yo rtha upanyāsaśca sa smṛtaḥ  BhN cāturvarṇyopagamanaṃ varṇasaṃhāra iṣyate kapaṭāpāśrayaṃ vākyamabhūtāharaṇaṃ viduḥ  BhN tattvārthavacanaṃ caiva mārga ityabhidhīyate citrārthasamavāye tu vitarko rūpamiṣyate yatsātiśayavadvākyaṃ tadudāharaṇaṃ smṛtam  BhN bhāvatattvopalabdhistu krama ityabhidhīyate sāmadānādisaṃpannaḥ saṃgrahaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  BhN rūpānurūpagamanamanumānamiti smṛtamratiharṣotsavānāṃ tu prārthanā prārthanā bhavet garbhasyodbhedanaṃ yatsākṣiptirityabhidhīyate  BhN saṃrambhavacanaṃ caiva toṭakaṃ tviti saṃjñitam kapaṭenātisaṃdhānaṃ bruvate dhibalaṃ budhāḥ  BhN bhayaṃ nṛpāridasyūtthamudvegaḥ parikīrtitaḥ śaṅkā bhayatrāsakṛto vidrayaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ  BhN doṣaprakhyāpanaṃ yattu so pavāda iti smṛtaḥ roṣagrathitavākyaṃ tu saṃpheṭaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  BhN guruvyatikramo yastu sa dravaḥ parikīrtitaḥ virodhipraśamo yaśca sa śaktiḥ parikīrtitā  BhN vyavasāyaśca vijñeyaḥ pratijñāhetusaṃbhavaḥ prasaṅgaścaiva vijñeyo gurūṇā parikīrtanam  BhN vākyamādharṣasaṃyuktaṃ dyutistajjñairudāhṛtā manaśceṣṭāviniṣpannaḥ śramaḥ kheda udāhṛtaḥ  BhN īpsitārthapratīghātaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ kāryātyayopagamanaṃ virodhanamiti smṛtam  BhN bījakāryopagamanamātānamiti saṃjñitam apamānakṛtaṃ vākyaṃ kāryārthaṃ cchādanaṃ bhavet  BhN prarocanā sa vijñeyā saṃhārārthapradarśinī pratyakṣavacanaṃ yattu sa vyāhāra iti smṛtaḥ  BhN savicchedaṃ vaco yatra sā yuktiriti saṃjñitā jñeyā vicalanā tajjñairavamānārthasaṃyuta  BhN etānyavamṛśe ṅgāni saṃhāre tu nibodhata mukhabījopagamanaṃ sandhirityabhidhīyate  BhN kāryasyānveṣaṇaṃ yuktyā nirodha iti kīrtitaḥ upakṣepastu kāryāṇāṃ grathanaṃ parikīrtitam  BhN anubhūtārthakathanaṃ nirṇayaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ parivādakṛtaṃ yasyāttadāhuḥ paribhāṣaṇam  BhN labdhasyārthasya śamanaṃ dyutimācakṣate punaḥ samāgamastathārthānāmānandaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  BhN duḥkhasyāpagamo yastu samayaḥ sa nigadyate śuśrūṣādyupasaṃpannaḥ prasādaḥ prītirucyate  BhN adbhutasya tu saṃprāptirūpagūhanamiṣyate sāmadānādi saṃpannaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam  BhN pūrvavākyaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ yathoktārthapradarśanam varapradānasaṃprāptiḥ kāvyasaṃhāra iṣyate  BhN nṛpadeśapraśāntiśca praśastirabhidhīyate yathāsandhi tu kartavyānyetānyaṅgāni nāṭake  BhN kavibhiḥ kāvyakuśalai rasabhāvamapekṣya tu saṃmiśrāṇi kadācittu dvitriyogena vā punaḥ  BhN jñātvā kāryamavasthāṃ ca kāryāṇyaṅgāni sandhiṣu eteṣāmeva cāṅgānāṃ saṃbaddhānyarthayuktitaḥ  BhN sandhyantarāṇi sandhīnāṃ viśeṣāstvekaviṃśatiḥ sāmabhedastathā daṇḍaḥ pradānaṃ vadha eva ca  BhN pratyutpannamatitvaṃ ca gotraskhalitameva ca sāhasaṃ ca bhayaṃ caiva hrīrmāyā krodha eva ca  BhN ojaḥ saṃvaraṇaṃ bhrāntistathā hetvapadhāraṇam dūto lekhastathā svapnaścitraṃ mada iti smṛtam  BhN viṣkambhacūlikā caiva tatha caiva praveśakaḥ aṅkāvatāro ṅkamukhamarthopakṣepapañcakam  BhN madhyamapuruṣaniyojyo nāṭakamukhasandhimātrasaṃcāraḥ viṣkambhakastu kāryaḥ purohitāmātyakañcukibhiḥ  BhN śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo vā dvividho viṣkaṃbhakastu vijñeyaḥ madhyamapātraiḥ śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo nīcamadhyakṛtaḥ  BhN antaryavanikāsaṃsthaiḥ sūtādibhiranekadhā arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yattu kriyate sā hi cūlikā  BhN aṅkāntarānusārī saṃkṣepārthamadhikṛtya bindūnām prakaraṇanāṭakaviṣaye praveśako nāma vijñeyaḥ  BhN aṅkānta eva cāṅko nipatati yasmin prayogamāsādya bījārthayuktiyukto jñeyo hyaṅkāvatāro sau  BhN viṣliṣṭamukhamaṅkasya striyā vā puruṣeṇa vā yadupakṣipyate pūrvaṃ tadaṅkamukhamucyate  BhN anyānyapi lāsyavidhāvaṅgāni tu nāṭakopayogīni asmādviniḥsṛtāni tu bhāṇa ivaiakaprayojyāni  BhN bhāṇākṛtivallāsyaṃ vijñeyaṃ tvekapātrahāryaṃ vā prakaraṇavadūhya kāryāsaṃstavayuktaṃ vividhabhāvam  BhN geyapadaṃ sthitapāṭhyamāsīnaṃ puṣpagaṇḍikā pracchedakaṃ trimūḍhaṃ ca saindhavākhyaṃ dvimūḍhakam  BhN uttamottamakaṃ caivamuktapratyuktameva ca lāsye daśavidhaṃ hyetadaṅganirdeśalakṣaṇam  BhN āsaneṣūpaviṣṭairyattantrībhāṇḍopabṛṃhitam gāyaneairgīyate śuṣkaṃ
