tadgeyapadamucyate  BhN yā nṛtyatyāsanā nārī geyaṃ priyaguṇānvitam sāṅgopāṅgavidhānena tadgeyapadamucyate  BhN prākṛtaṃ yadviyuktā tu paṭhedāttarasaṃ sthitā madanānalataptāṅgī sthitapāṭhyaṃ taducyate  BhN bahucārīsamāyuktaṃ pañcapāṇikalānugam cañcatpuṭena vā yuktaṃ sthitapāṭhyaṃ vidhīyate  BhN āsīnamāsyate yatra sarvātodyavivarjitam aprasāritagātraṃ ca cintāśokasamanvitam  BhN nṛttāni vividhāni syurgeyaṃ gāne ca saṃśritan ceṣṭābhiścāśrayaḥ puṃsā yatra sā puṣpagaṇḍikā  BhN yatra strī naraveṣeṇa lalitaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ paṭhet sakhīnāṃ tu vinodāya sā jñeyā puṣpagaṇḍikā  BhN nṛttaṃ tu vividhaṃ yatra gītaṃ cātodyasaṃyutam striyaḥ puṃvacca ceṣṭante sā jñeyā puṣpagaṇḍikā  BhN pracchedakaḥ sa vijñeyo yatra candrātapāhatāḥ striyaḥ priyeṣu sajjante hyapi vipriyakāriṣu  BhN aniṣṭhuraślakṣṇapadaṃ samavṛttairalaṅkṛtam nāṭyaṃ puruṣabhāvāḍhyaṃ trimūḍhakamiti smṛtam  BhN pātraṃ vibhraṣṭasaṃketaṃ suvyaktakaraṇānvitam prākṛtairvacanairyuktaṃ viduḥ saindhavakaṃ budhāḥ  BhN rūpavādyādisaṃyuktaṃ pāṭhyena ca vivarjitam nāṭyaṃ hi tattu vijñeyaṃ saindhavaṃ nāṭyakovidaiḥ  BhN mukhapratimukhopetaṃ caturaśrapadakramam śliṣṭabhāvarasopetaṃ vaicitryārthaṃ dvimūḍhake  BhN uttamottamakaṃ vidyādanekarasasaṃśrayam vicitraiḥ lokabandhaiśca helāhāvavicitritam  BhN kopaprasādajanitaṃ sādhikṣepapadāśrayam uktapratyuktamevaṃ syāccitragītārthayojitam  BhN yatra priyākṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā vinodayati mānasam madanānalataptāṅgī taccitrapadamucyate  BhN dṛṣṭvā svapne priyaṃ yatra madanānalatāpitā karotivividhān bhāvāṃstadvai bhāvikamucyate  BhN eteṣāṃ lāsyavidhau vijñeyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ prayogajñaiḥ tadihaiva tu yannauktaṃ prasaṅgavinivṛttahetostu  BhN pañcasandhi caturvṛtti catuḥṣaṣṭyaṅgasaṃyutam ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇopetaṃ guṇālaṅkārabhūṣitam  BhN mahārasaṃ mahābhogamudāttavacanānvitam mahāpuruṣasaṃcāraṃ sādhvācārajanapriyam  BhN suśliṣṭasandhisaṃyogaṃ suprayogaṃ sukhāśrayam mṛduśabdābhidhānaṃ ca kaviḥ kuryāttu nāṭakam  BhN avasthā yā tu lokasya sukhaduḥkhasamudbhavā nānāpuruṣasaṃcārā nāṭake sau vidhīyate  BhN na tajjñānaṃ na tacchilpaṃ na sā vidyā na sā kalā na tat karma na vā yogo nāṭye simnyanna dṛśyate  BhN yo yaṃ svabhāvo lokasya nānāvasthāntarātmakaḥ so ṅgādyabhinayairyukto nāṭyamityabhidhīyate  BhN devatānāmṛṣīnāṃ ca rājñāṃ cotkṛṣṭamedhasām pūrvavṛttānucaritaṃ nāṭakaṃ nāma tadbhavet  BhN yasmātsvabhāvaṃ saṃtyajya sāṅgopāṅgagatikramaiḥ prayujyate jñāyate ca tasmādvai nāṭakaṃ smṛtam  BhN sarvabhāvaiḥ sarvarasaiḥ sarvakarmapravṛttibhiḥ nānāvasthāntaropetaṃ nāṭakaṃ saṃvidhīyate  BhN anekaśilpajātāni naikakarmakriayāṇi ca tānyaśeṣāṇi rūpāṇi kartavyāni prayoktṛbhiḥ   BhN lokasvabhāvaṃ saṃprekṣya narāṇāṃ ca balābalam saṃbhogaṃ caiva yuktiṃ ca tataḥ kāryaṃ tu nāṭakam  BhN bhaviṣyati yuge prāyo bhaviṣyantyabudhā narāḥ ye cāpi hi bhaviṣyanti te yatnaśrutabuddhayaḥ  BhN karmaśilpāni śāstrāṇi vicakṣaṇabalāni ca sarvāṇyetāni naśyanti yadā lokaḥ praṇaśyati  BhN tadevaṃ lokabhāṣāṇāṃ prasamīkṣya balābalam mṛduśabdaṃ sukhārthaṃ ca kaviḥ kuryāttu nāṭakam  BhN caikrīḍitādyaiḥ śabdaistu kāvyabandhā bhavanti ye veśyā iva na te bhānti kamaṇḍaludharairdvijaiḥ  BhN daśarūpavidhānaṃ ca mayā proktaṃ dvijottamāḥ ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vṛttīnāmiha lakṣaṇam  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre sandhinirūpaṇaṃ nāmadhyāya ekonaviṃśaḥatha viṃśo dhyāyaḥsamutthānaṃ tu vṛttīnāṃ vyākhyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ yathā vastūdbhavaṃ caiva kāvyānāṃ ca vikalpanam  BhN ekārṇavaṃ jagat kṛtvā bhagavānacyuto yadā śete sma nāgaparyaṅke lokān saṃkṣipya māyayā  BhN atha vīryabalonmatāvasurau madhukaiaṭabhau tarjayāmāsaturdevaṃ tarasā yuddhakāṅkṣayā  BhN nijabāhū vimṛdanantau bhūtabhāvanamakṣayam jānubhirmuṣṭibhiścaiva yodhayāmāsatuḥ prabhum  BhN bahubhiḥ paruṣairvākyairanyonyasamabhidravam nānādhikṣepavacanaiḥ kampayantāvivodadhim  BhN tayornānāprakārāṇi vacāṃsi vadatostadā śrutvā tvabhihatamanā druhiṇo vākyamabravīt  BhN kimidaṃ bharatīvṛttirvāgbhireva pravartate uttarottarasaṃbaddhā nanvimau nidhanaṃ nayaḥ  BhN pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā provāca madhusūdanaḥ kāryahetormayā brahman bhāratīyaṃ vinirmitā  BhN vadatāṃ vākyabhūyiṣṭhā bhāratīyaṃ bhaviṣyati tasmādetau nihanmyadyetyuvāca vacanaṃ hariḥ  BhN śuddhairavikṛtairaṅgaiḥ sāṅgahāraistathā bhṛśam yodhayāmāsaturdaityau yuddhamārgaviśāradau  BhN bhūmisaṃyogasaṃsthānaiḥ padanyāsairharestadā atibhāro bhavad bhūmerbhāratī tatra nirmitā  BhN valgitaiḥ śārṅgadhanuṣastīvrairdīptatathairatha satvādhikairasaṃbhrāntaiḥ sāttvatī tatra nirmitā  BhN vicitrairaṅgahāraistu devo līlāsamanvitaiḥ babandha yacchikhāpāśaṃ kaiśikī tatra nirmitā  BhN saṃrambhāvegabahulairnānācārī samutthitaiḥ niyuddhakaraṇaiścitrairutpannārabhaṭī tataḥ  BhN yāṃ yāṃ devaḥ samācaṣṭe kriyāṃ vṛttiṣu saṃsthitām tāṃ tadarthānugairjapyeairdruhiṇaḥ pratyapūjayat  BhN yadā hatau tāvasurau hariṇā madhukaiṭabhau tato bravīt padmayonirnārāyaṇamarindamam  BhN aho vicitrairviṣamaiḥ sphuṭaiḥ salalitairapi aṅgahāraiḥ kṛtaṃ deva tvayā dānavanāśanam  BhN tasmādayaṃ hi lokasya niyuddhasamayakramaḥ sarvaśastravimokṣeṣu nyāyasaṃjño bhaviṣyati  BhN nyāyāśritairaṅgahārairnyāyāccaiva samutthitaiḥ yasmādyuddhāni vartante tasmānyāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BhN cārīṣu ca samutpanno nānācārīsamāśrayaḥ nyāyasaṃjñaḥ kṛto hyeṣa druhiṇena mahātmanā  BhN tato vedeṣu nikṣiptā druhiṇena mahātmanā punariṣvastrajāte ca nānācārīsamākule  BhN punarnāṭyaprayogeṣu nānābhāvasamnvitāḥ vṛttisaṃjñāḥ kṛtā hyetāḥ kāvyabandhasamāśrayāḥ  BhN caritairyasya devasya japyaṃ yadyādṛśaṃ kṛtam ṛṣibhistādṛśī vṛttiaḥ kṛtā pāṭhyādisaṃyutā  BhN nāṭyavedasamutpanā vāgaṅgābhinayātmikā mayā kāvyakriayāhetoḥ prakṣiptā druhiṇājñayā  BhN ṛgvedādbhāratī kṣiptā yajurvedācca sāttvatī kaiśikī sāmavedācca śeṣā cātharvaṇādapi  BhN yā vākpradhānā puruṣaprayojyā strīvarjitā saṃkṛtapāṭhyayuktā svanāmadheyairbharataiḥ prayuktā sā bhāratī nāma bhavettu vṛttiḥ  BhN bhedāstasyāstu vijñeyāścatvāro ṅgatvamāgatāḥ prarocanāmukhaṃ caiva vīthī prahasanaṃ tathā  BhN jayābhyudayinī caiva maṅgalyā vijayāvahā sarvapāpapraśamanī pūrvaraṅge prarocanā  BhN upakṣepeṇa kāvyasya hetuyuktisamāśrayā siddhenāmantraṇā yā tu vijñeyā sā prarocanā  BhN naṭī vidūṣako vāpi pāripārśvika eva vā sūtradhāreṇa sahitāḥ saṃlāpaṃ yattu kurvate  BhN citrairvākyaiḥ svakāryārotthairvītthyaṅgeranyathāpi vā āmukhaṃ tattu vijñeyaṃ budhaiḥ prastāvanāpi vā  BhN lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvamuktaṃ tu vītthyāḥ prahasanasya ca āmukhāṅgānyato vakṣye yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN uddhātyakaḥ kathoddhātaḥ prayogātiśayastathā pravṛttakāvalagite pañcāṅgānyāmukhasya tu  BhN uddhātyakāvalagitalakṣaṇaṃ kathitaṃ mayā śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ viprā vyākhyāsyāmyānupūrvaśaḥ  BhN sutradhārasya vākyaṃ vā yatra vākyārthameva vā gṛhītāṃ praviśetpātraṃ kathoddhātaḥ sa kīrtitaḥ  BhN prayoge tu prayogaṃ tu sūtradhāraḥ prayojayet tataśca praviśetpātraṃ prayogātiśayo hi saḥ  BhN kālapravṛttimāśritya varṇanā yā prayujyate tadāśrayācca pātrasya praveśastatpravṛttakam  BhN eṣāmanyatamaṃ śliṣṭaṃ yojayitvārthayuktibhiḥ tasmādaṅgadvayasyāpi sambhavo na nivāryate  BhN pātragranthairasaṃbādha prakuryādāmukhaṃ tataḥ evametadbudhairjñeyamāmukhaṃ vividhāśrayam  BhN lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvamuktaṃ tu vīthyāḥ prahasanasya ca ityaṣṭārdhavikalpā vṛttiriyaṃ bhāratī mayābhihitā sāttvatyāstu vidhānaṃ lakṣaṇayuktyā pravakṣyāmi  BhN yā sāttvateneha guṇena yuktā nyāyena vṛttena samanvitā ca harṣotkaṭā saṃhṛtaśokabhāvā sā sāttvatī nāma bhavettu vṛttiḥ  BhN vāgaṅgābhinayavatī sattvotthānavacanaprakaraṇeṣu sattvādhikārayuktā vijñeyā sāttvatī vṛttiḥ  BhN vīrādbhutaraudrarasā nirastaśṛṅgārakaruṇanirvedā uddhatapuruṣaprāyā parasparādharṣaṇakṛtā ca  BhN utthāpakaśca parivartakaśca sallāpakaśca saṃghātyaḥ catvāro syā bhedā vijñeyā nāṭyakovidaiaḥ  BhN ahamapyutthāsyāmi tvaṃ tāvaddarśayātmanaḥ śaktim iti saṃgharṣasamutthastajjñairutthāpako jñeyaḥ  BhN utthānasamārabdhānarthānutsṛjya yo rthayogavaśāt anyānarthān bhajate sa cāpi parivartako jñeyaḥ  BhN nirdiṣṭavastuviṣayaḥ prapañcabaddhastrihāsyasaṃyuktaḥ saṃgharṣaviśeṣakṛtastrividhaḥ parivartako jñeyaḥ  BhN sādharṣajo nirādharṣajo pi vā rāgavacasaṃyuktaḥ sādhikṣepālāpo jñeyaḥ sallāpakaḥ so pi  BhN dharmādharmasamutthaṃ yatra bhavedrāgadoṣasaṃyuktam sādhikṣepaṃ ca vaco jñeyaḥ saṃlāpako nāma  BhN mantrarthavākyaśaktyā daivavaśādātmadoṣayogādvā saṃghātabhedajananastajjñaiḥ saṃghātyako jñeyaḥ  BhN bahukapaṭasaṃśrayāṇāṃ paropaghātāśayaprayuktānām kūṭānāṃ saṃghāto vijñeyaḥ kūṭasaṃghātyaḥ   BhN ityaṣṭārdhavikalpā vṛttiriyaṃ sāttvatī mayābhihitā kaiśikyāstvatha lakṣaṇamataḥparaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi  BhN yā ślakṣṇanaipathyaviśeṣacitrā strīsaṃyutā yā bahunṛttagītā kāmopabhogaprabhavopacārā tāṃ kaiśikīṃ vṛttimudāharanti  BhN bahuvadyanṛttagītā śṛṅgārābhinayacitranaipathyā mālyālaṅkārayuktā praśastaveṣā ca kāntā ca  BhN citrapadavākyabandhairalaṅkṛtā hasitaruditaroṣādaiḥ strīpuruṣakāmayuktā vijñeyā kaiśikīvṛttiḥ  BhN narma ca narmasphuñjo narmasphoṭo tha narmagarbhaśca kaiśikyāścatvāro bhedā hyete samākhyātāḥ  BhN āsthāpitaśṛṅgāraṃ viśuddhakaraṇaṃ nivṛttavīrarasam hāsyapravacanabahulaṃ narma trividhaṃ vijānīyāt  BhN īrṣyākrodhaprāyaṃ sopālambhakaraṇānuviddhaṃ ca ātmopakṣepakṛtaṃ savipralambhaṃ smṛtaṃ narma  BhN navasaṅgamasambhogo ratisamudayaveṣavākyasaṃyuktaḥ jñeyo narmasphuñjo hyavasānabhayātmakaścaiva  BhN vividhānāṃ bhavānāṃ lavairlavairbhūṣito bahuviśeṣaiḥ asamagrākṣiptaraso narmasphoṭastu vijñeyaḥ  BhN vijñānarūpaśobhā dhanādibhirnāyako gaṇairyatra pracchanāṃ vyavaharte karyavaṣānnarmagarbho sau  BhN pūrvasthitau vipadyeta nāyako yatra cāparastiṣṭhet tamapīha narmagarbhaṃ vidyānnāṭyaprayogeṣu   BhN ityaṣṭārśavikalpā vṛttiriyaṃ kaiśikī mayābhihitā ata ūrdhvamuddhatarasāmarabhaṭiṃ sampravakṣyyami  BhN ārabhaṭaprāyaguṇā tathaiva bahukapaṭavañcanopetā dambhānṛtavacanavatī tvārabhaṭī nāma vijñeyā  BhN āvapātāplulaṅgitāni cchedyāni māyākṛtamindrajālam citrāṇī yuddhāni ca yatra nityaṃ tāṃ tādṛśīmārabhaṭīṃ vadanti  BhN śāḍguṇyasamārbdhā haṭhātisandhānavidravopetā lābhālābhārthakṛtā vijñeyā vṛttirārabhaṭī  BhN saṃkṣiptakāvapatau vastūtthāpanamathāpi saṃpheṭaḥ ete hyasyā bhedā lakṣaṇameṣaṃ pravakṣyāmi  BhN anvarthaśilpayukto bahupustotthānacitranepathyaḥ saṃkṣiptavastu viṣayo jñeyaḥ saṃkṣiptakao nāma  BhN bhayaharṣasamutthānaṃ vidravavinipātasambhramācaraṇam kṣiprapraveśanirgamamavapātamimaṃ vijānīyāt  BhN sarvarasasamāsakṛtaṃ savidravvvidravāśrayaṃ vvapi nāṭyaṃ vibhāvyate yattadvastūtthāpanaṃ jñeyam  BhN saṃrambhasaṃprayukto bahuyuddhakapaṭanirbhedaḥ śastrapraharabahulaḥ sampheṭo nāma vijñeyaḥ  BhN evametā budhairjñeyā vṛttayo nāṭyasaṃśrayā rasaprayogamāsāṃ ca kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata  BhN hāsyaśṛṅgarabahulā kaiśikī paricakṣitā sattvatī cāpi vijñeyā vīrādbhutaśamāśrayāḥ  BhN raudre bhayānake caiva vijñeyārabhaṭī budhaiḥ bībhatse karuṇe caiva bhāratī saṃprakīrtitā  BhN  na hyekarasajaṃ kavyaṃ kiñcidasti prayogataḥ bhāvo vāpi raso vāpi pravṛttirvṛttireva vā  BhN sarveṣāṃ samavetānāṃ yasya rūpaṃ bhavedbahu sa mantavyo rasa sthāyi śeṣāḥ sañcāriṇaḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN vṛtyanta eśo bhinayo mayokto vāgaṅgasattvaprabhavo yathāvad āhāryamevābhinayaṃ prayoge vakṣyāmi nepathyakṛtaṃ tu bhūyaḥ  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre vṛttivikalpanaṃ nāma viṃśo dhyāyaḥatha ekaviṃśo dhyāyaḥāhāryābhinayaṃ viprā vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ysmāt prayogaḥ sarvo yamāhāryābhinaye sthitaḥ  BhN nānāvasthā prakṛtaya pūrvaṃ naipathyasādhitāḥ aṅgādibhirabhivyaktimupagacchantyayatnataḥ  BhN āhāryābhinayo nāma jñeyo nepathyajo vidhiḥ tatra kāryaḥ prayatnastu nāṭyasya śubhamicchatā  BhN tasminyatnastu kartavyo naipathye siddhimicchatā nāṭyasyeha tvalaṅkāro naipathyaṃ yatprakīrtitam  BhN caturvidhaṃ tu nepathyaṃ pusto laṅkāra eva ca tathāṅkaracanā caiva jñeyaṃ sajjīvameva ca  BhN pustastu trividho jñeyo nānārūpapramāṇataḥ sandhimo vyājimaścaiva veṣṭimaśca prakīrtitaḥ  BhN kiliñjacarmavastrādyairyadrūpaṃ kriyate budhaiḥ sandhimo nāma vijñeyaḥ pusto nāṭakasaṃsśrayaḥ  BhN vyājimo nāma vijñeayo yantreṇa kriyate tu yaḥ veṣṭyate caiva yadrupaṃ veṣṭimaḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ  BhN śailayānavimānāni carmavarmadhvajā nagāḥ ye kriyante hi nāṭye tu sa pusta iti saṃjñitaḥ  BhN alaṅkārastu vijñeyo mālyābharaṇavāsasām nānāvidhaḥ samāyogo pyaṅgopāṅgavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN veṣṭimaṃ vitataṃ caiva saṃghātyaṃ granthimaṃ tathā prālambitaṃ tathā caiva mālyaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam  BhN caturvidhaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ nāṭye hyābharaṇaṃ budhaiḥ āvedhyaṃ bandhanīyaṃ ca kṣepyamāropyameva ca  BhN āvedhyaṃ kuṇḍalādīha yatsyācchravaṇabhūṣaṇam āropyaṃ hemasūtrādi hārāśca vividhāśrayāḥ  BhN śroṇīsūtrāṅgade muktābandhanīyāni sarvadā prakṣepya nūpuraṃ vidyādvastrābharaṇameva ca  BhN bhūṣaṇānāṃ vikalpaṃ hi puruṣastrīsamāśrayam nāvidhaṃ pravakṣyāmi deśajātisamudbhavam  BhN cūḍāmaṇiḥ samukuṭaḥ śiraso bhūṣaṇaṃ smṛtam kuṇḍalaṃ mocakaṃ kīlā karṇābharaṇamiṣyate  BhN muktāvalī harṣakaṃ ca sūtrakaṃ kaṇṭhabhūṣaṇam vetikāṅgulimudrā ca syādaṅgulivibhūṣaṇam  BhN hastalī valayaṃ caiva bāhunālīvibhūṣaṇam rucakaścūlikā kāryā maṇibandhavibhūṣaṇam  BhN keyūre aṅgade caiva kūrparoparibhūṣaṇe trisaraścaiva hāraśca tathā vakṣovibhūṣaṇam  BhN vyālambamauktiko hāro mālā caivāṅgabhūṣaṇam talakaṃ sūtrakaṃ caiva bhavetkaṭivibhūṣaṇam  BhN ayaṃ puruṣaniryogaḥ kāryastvābharaṇāśrayaḥ devānāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca punarvakṣyāmi yoṣitām  BhN śikhāpāśaṃ śikhāvyālaṃ piṇḍīpatraṃ tathaiva ca cūḍāmaṇirmakarikā muktājālagavākṣikam  BhN śiraso bhūṣaṇaṃ caiva vicitraṃ śīrṣajolakam kaṇḍakaṃ śikhipatraṃ ca veṇīpucchaḥ sadorakaḥ  BhN lalāṭatilakaṃ caiva nānāśilpaprayojitam bhrūgucchoparigucchaśca kusumānukṛtistathā  BhN karṇikā karṇavalayaṃ tathā syātpatrakarṇikā kuṇḍalaṃ karṇamudrā ca karṇotkīlakameva ca  BhN nānāratnavicitrāṇi dantapatrāṇi caiva hi karṇayorbhūṣaṇaṃ hyetatkarṇapūrastathaiva ca  BhN tilakāḥ patralekhāśca bhavedgaṇḍavibhūṣaṇam trivaṇī caiva vijñeyaṃ bhavedvakṣovibhūṣaṇam  BhN netrayorañjanaṃ jñeyamadharasya ca rañjanam dantānāṃ vividho rāgaścaturṇāṃ śuklatāpi vā  BhN rāgāntaravikalpo tha śobhanenādhikojvalaḥ mugdhānāṃ sundarīṇāṃ ca muktābhāsitaśobhanāḥ  BhN suraktā vāpi dantā syuḥḥ padmapallavarañjanāḥ aśmarāgoddyotitaḥ syādadharaḥ pallavaprabhaḥ  BhN vilāsaśca bhavettāsāṃ savibhrāntanirīkṣitam muktāvalī vyālapaṅktirmañjarī ratnamālikā  BhN ratnāvalī sūtrakaṃ ca jñeyaṃ kaṇṭhavibhūṣaṇam dvisarastrisaraścaiva catussarakameva ca  BhN tathā śṛṅkhalikā caiva bhavetkaṇṭhavibhūṣaṇam aṅgadaṃ valayaṃ caiva bāhumūlavibhūṣaṇam  BhN nānāśilpakṛtāścaiva hārā vakṣovibhūṣaṇam maṇijālāvanaddhaṃ ca bhavet stanavibhūṣaṇam  BhN kharjūrakaṃ socchitikaṃ bāhunālīvibhūṣaṇam kalāpī kaṭakaṃ śaṅkho hastapatraṃ sapūrakam  BhN mudrāṅgulīyakaṃ caiva hyaṅgulīnāṃ vibhūṣaṇam muktājālāḍhyatalakaṃ mekhalā kāñcikāpi vā  BhN raśanā ca kalāpaśca bhavecchroṇīvibhūṣaṇam ekayaṣṭirbhavetkāñcī mekhalā tvaṣṭayaṣṭikā  BhN dviraṣṭayaṣṭi raśanā kalāpaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ dvātriṃśacca catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tathā  BhN muktāhārā bhavantyete devapārthivayoṣitām nūpuraḥ kiṅkiṇīkāśca ghaṇṭikā ratnajālakam  BhN saghoṣe kaṭake caiva gulphoparivibhūṣāṇam jaṅghayoḥ pādapatraṃ syādaṅgulīṣvaṅgulīyakam  BhN aṅguṣṭhatilakāścaiva pādayośca vibhūṣaṇam tathālaktakarāgaśca nānābhaktiniveśitaḥ  BhN aśokapalāvacchāyaḥ syāt svābhāvika eva ca etadvibhūṣaṇaṃ nāryā ākeśādānakhādapi  BhN yathābhavarasāvasthaṃ vijñeyaṃ dvijasattamāḥ āgamaśca pramāṇaṃ ca rūpanirvarṇanaṃ tathā  BhN viśvakarmamatātkāryaṃ subuddhyāpi prayoktṛbhiḥ na hi śakyaṃ suvarṇena muktābhirmaṇibhistathā  BhN svādhīnamiti rucyaiva kartumaṅgasya bhūṣaṇam vibhāgato bhiprayuktamaṅgaśobhākaraṃ bhavet  BhN yathā sthānāntaragataṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ ratnasaṃyutam na tu nāṭyaprayogeṣu kartavyaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ guru  BhN khedaṃ janayate taddhi savyāyataviceṣṭanāt gurubhāvāvasannasya svedo mūrchā ca jāyate  BhN gurvābharaṇasanno hi ceṣṭāṃ na kurute punaḥ tasmāttanutvacakṛtaṃ sauvarṇaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ bhavet  BhN ratnavajjatubaddhaṃ vā na khedajananaṃ bhavet svecchayā bhūṣaṇavidhirdivyānāmupadiśyate  BhN yatnabhāvaviniṣpannaṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam veṣṭitaṃ vitataṃ caiva saṃghātyaṃ grathimaṃ tatha  BhN lambaśobhi tathā caiva mālyaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam ācchādanaṃ bahuvidhaṃ nānāpattanasaṃbhavam  BhN tajjñeyaṃ triprakāraṃ tu śuddhaṃ raktaṃ vicitritam divyānāṃ bhūṣaṇavidhirya eṣa parikīrtitaḥ  BhN mānuṣāṇāṃ tu kartavyo nānādeśasamāśrayaḥ bhūṣaṇaiścāpi veṣaiśca nānāvasthāsamāśrayaiḥ  BhN divyāṅganānāṃ kartavyā vibhaktiḥ svasvabhūmijā vidyādharīṇāṃ yakṣīṇāmapsaronāgayoṣitām  BhN ṛṣidaivatakanyānāṃ veṣairnānātvamiṣyate tathā ca siddhagandharvarākṣasāsurayoṣitām  BhN divyānāṃ naranārīṇāṃ tathaiva ca śikhaṇḍakam śikhāpuṭaśikhaṇḍaṃ tu muktābhūyiṣṭhabhūṣaṇam  BhN vidyādharīṇāṃ kartavyaḥ śuddho veṣaparicchadaḥ yakṣiṇyo psaraścaiva karyā ratnavibhūṣaṇāḥ  BhN samastānāṃ bhavedveṣo yakṣīṇā kevalaṃ śikhā divyanāmiva kartavyaṃ nāgastrīṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam  BhN muktāmaṇilatāprāyāḥ phaṇāstāsāṃ tu kevalāḥ kāryaṃ tu munikanyānāmekaveṇīdharaṃ śiraḥ  BhN na cāpi vibhūṣaṇavidhistāsāṃ veṣo vanocitaḥ muktāmarakataprāyaṃ maṇḍanaṃ siddhayoṣitām  BhN tāsāṃ tu caiva kartavyaṃ pītavastraparicchadam padmarāgamaṇiprāyaṃ gandharvīṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam  BhN vīṇāhastaśca kartavyaḥ kausumbhavasanastathā indranīlaistu kartavyaṃ rākṣasīṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam  BhN sitadaṃṣṭrā ca kartavyā kṛṣṇavastraparicchadam vaiḍūryamuktābharaṇāḥ kartavyā surayoṣitām  BhN śukapiñchanibhaiarvastraiḥ kāryastāsāṃ paricchadaḥ puṣyarāgaistu maṇibhiḥ kvacidvaiḍūryabhūṣitaiḥ  BhN divyavānaranārīṇāṃ kāryo nīlaparicchadaḥ evaṃ śṛṅgāriṇaḥ kāryā veṣā divyāṅganāśrayāḥ  BhN avasthāntamāsādya śuddhāḥ kāryāḥ punastathā mānuṣīṇāṃ tu kartavyā nānādeśasamudbhavāḥ  BhN veṣābharaṇasaṃyogān gadatastānnibodhata āvantyayuvatīnāṃ tu śirassālakakuntalam  BhN gauḍīyānāmalakaprāyaṃ saśikhāpāśaveṇikam ābhīrayuvatīnāṃ tu dviveṇīdhara eva tu  BhN śiraḥ parigamaḥ kāryo nīlaprāyamathāmbaram tathā pūrvotarastrīṇāṃ samunnaddhaśikhaṇḍakam  BhN ākeśācchādanaṃ tāsāṃ deśakarmaṇi kīrtitam tathaiva dakṣiṇastrīṇāṃ kāryamullekhyasaṃśrayam  BhN kumbhībandhakasaṃyuktaṃ tathāvartalalāṭikam gaṇikānāṃ tu kartavyamicchāvicchitti maṇḍanam  BhN deśajātividhānena śeṣāṇāmapi kārayet veṣaṃ tathā cābharaṇaṃ kṣurakarma paricchadam  BhN āgamaṃ cāpi naipathye nāṭyasyaivaṃ prayojayet adeśayukto veṣo hi na śobhāṃ janayiṣyati  BhN mekhalorasi baddhā tu hāsyaṃ samupapādayet tathā proṣitakāntāsu vyasanābhihatāsu ca  BhN veṣo vai malinaḥ kārya ekaveṇīdharaṃ śiraḥ vipralambhe tu nāryāstu śuddho veṣo bhavediha  BhN nātyābharaṇasaṃyukto na cāpi mṛjayānvitaḥ evaṃ strīṇāṃ bhavedveṣo deśāvasthāsamudbhavaḥ  BhN puruṣāṇāṃ punaścaiva veṣānvakṣyāmi tattvataḥ tatrāṅkaracanā pūrvaṃ kartavyā nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN tataḥ paraṃ prayoktavyā veṣā deśasamudbhavāḥ sito nīlaśca pītaśca caturtho rakta eva ca  BhN ete svabhāvajā varṇā yaiḥ kāryaṃ tvaṅgavartanam saṃyogajāḥ punaścānye upavarṇā bhavanti hi  BhN tānahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi yathākāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ sitanīlasamāyoge kāraṇḍava iti smṛtaḥ  BhN sitapītasāmāyogātpāṇḍuvarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ sitiaraktasamāyoge padmavarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN pītanīlasamāyogāddharito nāma jāyate nīlaraktasamāyogātkaṣāyo nāma jāyate  BhN raktapītasamāyogādgauravarṇa iti smṛtaḥ ete saṃyogajā varṇā hyupavarṇāstathāpare  BhN tricaturvarṇasaṃyuktā bahavaḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ balastho yo bhavedvarṇastasya bhāgo bhavettataḥ  BhN durbalasya ca bhāgau dvau nīlaṃ muktvā pradāpayet nīlasyaiko bhavedbhāgaścatvāro nye tu varṇake  BhN balavānsarvavarṇānāṃ nīla eva prakīrtitaḥ evaṃ varṇavidhiṃ jñātvā nānāsaṃyogasaṃśrayam  BhN tataḥ kuryādyathāyogamaṅgānāṃ vartanaṃ budhaḥ vartanacchādanaṃ rūpaṃ svaveṣaparivarjitam  BhN nāṭyadharmapravṛttaṃ tu jñeyaṃ tatprakṛtisthitam svavarṇamātmanaśchādyaṃ varṇakairveṣasaṃśrayaiḥ  BhN ākṛtistasya kartavyā yasya prakṛtirāsthitā yathā jantuḥ svabhāvaṃ svaṃ parityajyānyadaihikam  BhN tatsvabhāvaṃ hi bhajate dehāntaramupāśritaḥ veṣeṇa varṇakaiścaiva cchāditaḥ puruṣastathā  BhN parabhāvaṃ prakurute yasya veṣaṃ samāśritaḥ devadānavagandharvayakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ  BhN prāṇisaṃjñāḥ smṛtā hyete jīvabandhāśca ye pare strībhāvāḥ parvatāḥ nadyaḥ samudrā vāhanāni ca  BhN nānāśastrāṇyapi tathā vijñeyāḥ prāṇisaṃjñayā śailaprāsādayantrāṇi carmavarmadhvajāstathā  BhN nānāpraharaṇādyāśca te prāṇina iti smṛtāḥ athavā kāraṇopetā bhavantyete śarīriṇaḥ  BhN veṣabhāṣāśrayopetā nāṭyadharmamavekṣya tu varṇānāṃ tu vidhiṃ jñātvā vayaḥ prakṛtimeva ca  BhN kuryādaṅgasya racanāṃ deśajātivayaḥśritatām devā gaurāstu vijñeyā yakṣāścāpsarastathā  BhN rudrārkadruhiṇaskandāstapanīyaprabhāḥ smṛtāḥ somo bṛhaspatiḥ śukro varuṇastārakāgaṇāḥ  BhN samudrahimavadgaṅgāḥ śvetā hi syurbalastathā raktamaṅgārakaṃ vidyāt pītau budhahutāśanau  BhN nārāyaṇo naraścaiva śyāmo nāgaśca vāsukiḥ daityāśca dānavāścaiva rākṣasā guhyakā nagāḥ  BhN piśācā jalamākāśamasitāni tu varṇataḥ bhavanti ṣaṭsu dvīpeṣu puruṣaścaiva varṇataḥ  BhN kartavyā nāṭyayogena niṣṭaptakanakaprabhāḥ jāmbūdvīpasya varṣe tu nānāvarṇāśrayā narāḥ  BhN uttarāṃstu kurustyaktvā te cāpi kanakaprabhāḥ bhadrāśvapuruṣāḥ śvetāḥ kartavyā varṇatastathā  BhN ketumāle narā nīlā gaurāḥ śeṣeṣu kīrtitāḥ nānāvarṇāḥ smṛtā bhūtā gandharvā yakṣapannagāḥ  BhN vidyādharāstathā caiva pitarastu samā narāḥ punaśca bhārate varṣe tāṃstānvarṇānnibodhata  BhN rājānaḥ padmavarṇāstu gaurāḥ śyāmāstathaiva ca ye cāpi sukhino martyā gaurā kāryāstu vaiḥ budhaiḥ  BhN kukarmiṇo grahagrastāḥ vyādhitāstapasi sthitāḥ āyastakarmiṇaścaiva hyasitāśca kujātayaḥ  BhN ṛṣyayaścaiva kartavyā nityaṃ tu badaraprabhāḥ tapaḥsthitāśca ṛṣayo nityāmevāsitā budhaiḥ  BhN kāraṇavyapadeśena tathā cātmecchayā punaḥ varṇastatra prakartavyo deśajativaśānugaḥ  BhN deśaṃ karma ca jātiṃ ca pṛthivyuddeśasaṃśrayam vijñāya vartanā kāryā puruṣāṇāṃ prayogataḥ  BhN kirātabarbarāndhrāśca draviḍāḥ kāśikosalāḥ pulindā dākṣiṇātyāśca prāyeṇa tvasitāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN śakāśca yavanāścaiva pahlavā vāhlikāśca ye prāyeṇa gaurāḥ kartavyā uttarā ye śritā diśam  BhN pāñcālāḥ śaurasenāśca māhiṣāścauḍramāgadhāḥ aṅgā vaṅgāḥ kaliṅgāśca śyāmāḥ kāryāstu varṇataḥ  BhN brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścaiva gaurāḥ kāryāstathaiva hi vaiśyāḥ śūdrāstathā caiva śyāmāḥ kāryāstu varṇataḥ  BhN evaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ mukhāṅgopāṅgavartanām śmaśrukarma prayuñjīta deśakālavayo nugam  BhN śuddhaṃ vicitraṃ śyāmaṃ ca tathā romaśameva ca bhaveccaturvidhaṃ śmaśru nānāvasthāntarātmakam  BhN śuddhaṃ tu liṅgināṃ kāryaṃ tathāmātyapurodhasām madhyasthā ye ca puruṣā ye ca dīkṣāṃ samāśritāḥ  BhN divyā ye puruṣāḥ kecitsiddhavidyādharādayaḥ pārthivāśca kumārāśca ye ca rājopajīvinaḥ  BhN śṛṅgāriṇaśca ye martyā yauvanonmādinaśca ye teṣāṃ vicitraṃ kartavyaṃ śmaśru nāṭyaprayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN anistīrṇapratijñānāṃ duḥkhitānāṃ tapasvinām vyasanābhihatānāṃ ca śyāmaṃ śmaśru prayojayet  BhN ṛṣīṇāṃ tāpasānāṃ ca ye ca dīrghavratā narāḥ tathā ca cīrabaddhānāṃ romaśaṃ śmaśru kīrtitam  BhN evaṃ nānāprakāraṃ tu śmaśru kāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi veṣānnānāprayogajān  BhN śuddho vicitro malinastrividho veṣa ucyate teṣāṃ niyogaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN devābhigamane caiva maṅgale niyamasthite tithinakṣatrayoge ca vivāhakaraṇe tathā  BhN dharmapravṛttaṃ yatkarma striyo vā puruṣasya vā veṣasteṣāṃ bhavecchuddho ye ca prāyatnikā narāḥ  BhN devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām nṛpāṇāṃ karkaśānāṃ ca citro veṣa udāhṛtaḥ  BhN vṛddhānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca śreṣṭhyamātyapurodhasām vaṇijāṃ kāñcukīyānāṃ tathā caiva tapasvinām  BhN viprakṣetriyavaiśyānāṃ sthānīyā ye ca mānavāḥ śuddho vastravidhisteṣāṃ kartavyo nāṭakāśrayaḥ  BhN unmattānāṃ pramattānāmadhvagānāṃ tathaiva ca vyasanopahatānāṃ ca malino veṣa ucyate  BhN śuddharaktavicitrāṇi vāsāṃsyūrdhvāmbarāṇi ca yojayennāṭyatattvajño veṣayoḥ śuddhacitrayoḥ  BhN kuryādveṣe tu maline malinaṃ tu vicakṣaṇaḥ muninirgranthaśākyeṣu yatipāśupateṣu ca  BhN vratānugastu kartavyo veṣo lokasvabhāvataḥ cīravalkalacarmāṇi tāpasānāṃ tu yojayet  BhN parivāṇmuniṣkyānāṃ vāsaḥ kāṣāyamiṣyate nānācitrāṇi vāsāṃsi kuryātpāśupateṣvatha  BhN kujātayaśca ye proktāsteṣāṃ caiva yathārhataḥ antaḥpurapraveśe ca viniyuktā hi ye narāḥ  BhN kāṣāyakañcukapaṭāḥ kāryāste pi yathāvidhi avasthānatarataścaiva nṛṇāṃ veṣo bhavedatha  BhN veṣaḥ sāṃgrāmikaścaiva śūrāṇāṃ saṃprakīrtitaḥ vicitraśastrakavaco baddhatūṇo dhanurdharaḥ  BhN citro veṣastu kartavyo nṛpāṇāṃ nityameva ca kevalastu bhavecchuddho nakṣatrotpātamaṅgale  BhN evameṣa bhavedveṣo deśajātivayo nugaḥ uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ strīṇāṃ nṛṇāmathāpi ca  BhN evaṃ vastravidhiḥ kāryaḥ prayoge nāṭakāśraye nānāvasthāṃ samāsādya śubhāśubhakṛtastathā  BhN tathā pratiśiraścāpi kartavyaṃ nāṭakāśrayam divyānāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca deśajātivayaḥśritam  BhN pārśvāgatā mastakinastathā caiva kirīṭinaḥ trividho mukuṭo jñeyo divyapārthivasaṃśritaḥ  BhN devagandharvayakṣāṇāṃ pannagānāṃ sarakṣasām kartavyā naikavihiata mukuṭāḥ pārśvamaulayaḥ  BhN uttamā ye ca divyānāṃ te ca kāryāḥ kirīṭinaḥ madhyamā maulinaścaiva kaniṣṭhāḥ ṣirṣamaulinaḥ  BhN narādhipānāṃ kartavyā mastake mukuṭā budhaiḥ vidyādharāṇāṃ ca siddhānāṃ cāraṇānāṃ tathaiva ca  BhN granthimatkeśamukuṭāḥ kartavyāstu prayoktṛbhiḥ rākṣodānavadaityānāṃ piṅgakeśekṣaṇāni hi  BhN haricchśmaśrūṇi ca tathā mukuṭāsyāni kārayet uttamaścāpi ye tatra te kāryāḥ pārśvamaulinaḥ  BhN kasmāttu mukuṭāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ prayoge divypārthive keśānāṃ chedanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vedavāde yathāśruti  BhN bhadrīkṛtasya vā yajñe śirasaśchādanecchayā keśānāmapyadīrghatvātsmṛtaṃ mukuṭadhāraṇam  BhN senāpateḥ punaścāpi yuvarājasya caiva hi yojayedardhamukuṭaṃ mahāmātrāśca ye narāḥ  BhN amātyānāṃ kañcukināṃ tathā śreṣṭhipurodhasām veṣṭanābaddhapaṭṭāni pratiśīrṣāṇi kārayet  BhN piśāconmattabhūtānāṃ sādhakānāṃ tapasvinām anistīrṇapratijñānāṃ lambakeśaṃ bhavecchiraḥ  BhN śākyaśrotriyanirgranthaparivrāḍdīkṣiteṣu ca śiromuṇḍaṃ tu kartavyaṃ yajñadīkṣānviteṣu ca  BhN tathā vratānugaṃ caiva śeṣānāṃ liṅgināṃ śiraḥ muṇḍaṃ vā kuñcitaṃ vāpi lambakeśamathāpi vā  BhN dhūrtānāṃ caiva kartavyaṃ ye ca rātryupajīvinaḥ śṛṅgāracittāḥ puruṣāsteṣāṃ kuñcitamūrdhajāḥ  BhN bālānāmapi kartavyaṃ triśikhaṇḍavibhūṣitam jaṭāmakuṭabaddhaṃ ca munīnāṃ tu bhavecchiraḥ  BhN ceṭānāmapi kartavyaṃ triśikhaṃ muṇḍameva vā vidūṣakasya khalatiḥ syātkākapadameva vā  BhN śeeṣāṇāmarthayogena deśajātisamāśrayam śiraḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ kāryaṃ nānāvasthāntarāśrayam  BhN bhūṣaṇairvarṇakairvastrairmālyaiścaiva yathāvidhi evaṃ nānāprakāraistu buddhyā veṣānprakalpayet  BhN pūrvaṃ tu prakṛtiṃ sthāpya prayogaguṇasaṃbhavām strīṇāṃ vā puruṣāṇāṃ vāpyavasthāṃ prāpya tādṛśīm  BhN sarve bhāvāśca divyānāṃ kāryā mānuṣasaṃśrayāḥ teṣāṃ cānimiṣatvādi naiva kāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN iha bhāvarasāścaiva dṛṣṭibhiḥ saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ dṛṣṭyaiva sthāpito hyarthaḥ paścādaṅgairvibhāvyate  BhN evaṃ jñeeyāṅgaracanā nānāprakṛtisaṃbhavā sajīva iti yaḥ proktastasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN yaḥ prāṇināṃ praveśo vai sajīva iti saṃjñitaḥ catuṣpado tha dvipadastathā caivāpadaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN uragānapadān vidyād dvipadānkhagamānuṣān grāmyā āraṇyāḥ paśavo vijñeyāḥ syuścatuṣpadāḥ  BhN ye te tu yaddhasaṃpheṭairuparodhaistathaiva ca nānāpraharaṇopetāḥ prayojyā nāṭake budhaiḥ  BhN āyudhāni ca kāryāṇi puruṣāṇāṃ pramāṇataḥ tānyahaṃ vartayiṣyāmi yathāpustapramāṇataḥ  BhN bhiṇḍirdvādaśatālaḥ syāddaśa kunto bhavedatha aṣṭau śataghnī śūlaṃ ca tomaraḥ śaktireva vā  BhN aṣṭau tālā dhanurjñeyamāyāmo sya dvihastakaḥ śaro gadā ca vajrā ca catustālaṃ vidhīyate  BhN aṅgulāni tvasiḥ kāryaścatvāriṃśatpramāṇataḥ dvādaśāṅgulakaṃ cakraṃ tato rdhaṃ prāsa iṣyate  BhN prāsavatpaṭṭasaṃ vidyāddaṇḍaścaiva tu viṃśatiḥ viṃśatiḥ kaṇayaścaiva hyaṅgulāni pramāṇataḥ  BhN śoḍaṣāṅgulavistīrṇaṃ sabalaṃ saṃpraghaṇṭikam triṃśadaṅgulimānena kartavyaṃ kheṭakaṃ budhaiḥ  BhN jarjaro daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ ca tathaiva pratiśīrṣakam chatraṃ cāmaraṃ caiva dhvajo śṛṅgāra eva ca  BhN yatkiñcinmānuṣe loke dravyaṃ puṃsāṃ prayojakam yaccopakaraṇaṃ sarve nāṭye tatsaṃprakīrtitam  BhN yadyasya viṣayaprāptaṃ tenohyaṃ tasya lakṣaṇam jarjare daṇḍakāṣṭhe ca saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN māhendrā vai dhvajāJ proktā lakṣaṇairviśvakarmaṇā eṣānyatamaṃ kuryājjarjaraṃ dārukarmataḥ  BhN athavā vṛkṣayoniḥ syātpraroho vāpi jarjaraḥ veṇureva bhavecchreṣṭhastasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN śvetabhūmyāāṃ tu yo jātaḥ puṣyanakṣatrajastathā saṃgrāhyo vai bhavedveṇurjarjarārthe prayatnataḥ  BhN pramāṇamaṅgulānāṃ tu śatamaṣṭottaraṃ bhavet pañcaparvā caturgranthistālamātrastathaiva ca  BhN sthūlagranthirna kartavyo na śākhī na ca kīṭavān na kṛmikṣataparvā ca na hīnaścānyaveṇubhiḥ  BhN madhusarpissarṣapāktaṃ mālyadhūpapuraskṛtam upāsya vidhivadveṇuṃ gṛhṇiyājjarjaraṃ prati  BhN yo vidhiryaḥ kramaścaiva māhebdre tu dhvaje smṛtaḥ sa jarjarasya kartavyaḥ puṣyaveṇusamāśrayaḥ  BhN bhavedyo dīrghaparvā tu tanupatrastathaiva ca parvāgrataṇḍulaścaiva puṣyaveṇuḥ sa kīrtitaḥ  BhN vidhireṣa mayā prokto jarjarasya pramāṇataJḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi daṇḍakāṣṭhasya lakṣaṇam  BhN kapitthabilvavaṃśebhyo daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ bhavedatha vakraṃ caiva hi kartavyaṃ tribhāge lakṣaṇānvitam  BhN kīṭairnopahataṃ yacca vyādhinā na ca pīḍitam mandaśākhaṃ bhavedyacca daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ tu tadbhavet  BhN yastvebhirlakṣaṇairhīnaṃ daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ sajarjaram kārayetsa tvapacayaṃ mahāntaṃ prāpnuyāddhruvam  BhN atha śīrṣavibhāgārthaṃ ghaṭī kāryā prayatnataḥ svapramāṇavinirdiṣṭā dvātriṃśatyaṅgulāni vai  BhN bilvamadhyena kartavyā ghaṭī sirasamāśrayā svinnena bilvakalkena draveṇa ca samanvitā  BhN bhasmanā vā tuṣairvāpi kārayetpratiśīrṣakam saṃchādya tu tato vastrairbilvadugdhairghaṭāśrayaiḥ  BhN bilvakalkena cīraṃ tu digdhvā saṃyojayedghaṭīm na sthūlāṃ nānatāṃ tanvīṃ dīrghāṃ naiva ca kārayet  BhN tasyāmātapaśuṣkāyāṃ suśuṣkāyāmathāpi vā chedyaṃ budhāḥ prakurvanti vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā  BhN sutīkṣṇena tu śastreṇa ardhārdhaṃ pravibhajya ca svapramāṇavinirdiṣṭaṃ lalāṭakṛtakoṇakam  BhN ardhāṅgulaṃ lalāṭaṃ tu kāryaṃ chedyaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulam ardhārdhamaṅgulaṃ chedyaṃ kaṭayordvyaṅgulaṃ bhavet  BhN kaṭānte karṇanālasya chedyaṃ dvyadhikamaṅgulam tryaṅgulaṃ karṇavivaraṃ tathā syācchedyameva hi  BhN tataścaivāvaṭuḥ kāryā susamā dvādaśāṅgulā ghaṭyāṃ hyetatsadā cchedye vidhānaṃ vihitaṃ mayā  BhN tasyoparigatā kāryā mukuṭā bahuśilpajāḥ nānāratnapraticchannā bahurūpopaśobhitāḥ  BhN tathopakaraṇānīha nāṭyayogakṛtāni vai bahuprakārayuktāni kurvīta prakṛtiṃ prati  BhN yatkiñcidasmin loke tu carācarasamanvite vihitaṃ karma śilpaṃ vā tattūpakaraṇaṃ smṛtam  BhN yadyasya viṣayaṃ prāptaṃ tattadevābhigacchati nāstantaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ hi nāṭyopakaraṇāśraye  BhN yadyenotpāditaṃ karma śilpayogakriyāpi vā tasya tena kṛtā sṛṣṭiḥ pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tathā  BhN yā kāṣṭhayantrabhūyiṣṭhā kṛtā sṛṣṭirmahātmanā na sāsmākaṃ nāṭyayoge kasmātkhedāvahā hi sā  BhN yaddravyaṃ jīvaloke tu nānālakṣaṇalakṣitam tasyānukṛtisaṃsthānaṃ nāṭyoopakaraṇaṃ bhavet  BhN prāsādagṛhayānāni nānāpraharaṇāni ca na śakyaṃ tāni vai kartuṃ yathoktānīha lakṣaṇaiḥ  BhN lokadharmī bhavettvanyā nāṭyadharmī tathāparā svabhāvo lokadharmī tu vibhāvo nāṭyameva hi  BhN āyasaṃ na tu kartavyaṃ na ca sāramayaṃ tathā nāṭyopakaraṇaṃ tajjñairgurukhedakara bhavet  BhN kāṣṭhacarmasu vastrṣu jatuveṇudaleṣu ca nāṭyopakaraṇānīha laghukarmāṇi kārayet  BhN carmavarmadhvajāḥ śailāḥ prāsādā devatāgṛhāḥ hayavāraṇayānāni vimānāni gṛhāṇi ca  BhN pūrvaṃ veṇudalaiḥ kṛtvā kṛtīrbhāvasamāśrayāḥ tataḥ suraṅgairacchādya vastraiḥ sārūpyamānayet  BhN athavā yadi vastrāṇāmasānnidhyaṃ bhavediha tālīyairvā kiliñjairvā ślakṣṇairvastrakriyā bhavet  BhN tathā praharaṇāni syustṛṇaveṇudalādibhiḥ jantubhāṇḍakriyābhiśca nānārūpāṇi nāṭake  BhN pratipādaṃ pratiśiraḥ pratihastaṃ pratitvacam tṛṇaiḥ kiliñjairbhāṇḍairvā sārūpyāṇi tu kārayet  BhN yadyasya sadṛśaṃ rūpaṃ sārūpyaguṇasaṃbhavam mṛṇmayaṃ tattu kṛtsnaṃ tu nānārūpaṃ tu kārayet  BhN bhāṇḍavastramadhūcchiṣṭairlākṣayābhradalena ca nāgāste vividhāḥ kāryā hyatasīśaṇabilvajaiḥ  BhN nānākusumajātīśca phalāni vividhāni ca bhāṇḍavastramadhūcchiṣṭairlākṣayā vāpi kārayet  BhN bhāṇḍavastramadhūcchiṣṭaistāmrapatraistathaiva ca samyakca nīlīrāgeṇāpyabhrapatreṇa caiva hi  BhN rañjitenābhrapatreṇa maṇīścaiva prakārayet upāśrayamathāpyeṣaṃ śulbavaṅgena kārayet  BhN vividhā mukuṭā divā pūrvaṃ ye gaditā mayā te bhrapatrojvalāḥ kāryā maṇīvyālopaśobhitāḥ  BhN na śāstraprabhavaṃ karma teṣāṃ hi samudāhṛtam ācāryabuddhyā kartavyamūhāpohaprayojitam  BhN eṣa martyakriyāyogo bhaviṣyatkalpito mayā kasmādalpabalatvaṃ hi manuṣyeṣu bhaviṣyati  BhN martyānāmapi no śakyā vibhāvāḥ sarvakāñcanāḥ neṣṭāḥ suvarṇaratnaistu mukuṭā bhūṣaṇāni vā  BhN yuddhe niyuddhe nṛtte vā vṛṣṭivyāpārakarmaṇi gurubhāvāvasannasya svedo mūrchā ca jāyate  BhN svedamūrchāklamārtasya prayogastu vinaśyati prāṇātyayaḥ kadācicca bhavedvyāyataceṣṭayā  BhN tasmāttāmramayaiḥ patrairabhrakai rañjitairapi bheṇḍairapi madhūcchiṣṭaiḥ kāryāṇyābharaṇāni tu  BhN evaṃ lokopacāreṇa svabuddhivibhavena ca nāṭyopakaraṇānīha budhaḥ samyak prayojayet  BhN na bhedyaṃ naiva ca cchedyaṃ na prahartavyameva ca raṅge praharaṇaiḥ kāryaṃ saṃjñāmātraṃ tu kārayet  BhN athavā yogaśikṣābhirvidyāmāyākṛtena vā śastramokṣaḥ prakartavyo raṅgamadhye prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN evaṃ nānāprakāraistu āyudhābharaṇāni ca noktāni yāni ca mayā lokād grāhyāṇi tānyapi  BhN āhāryābhinayo hyeṣa mayā proktaḥ samāsataḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sāmānyābhinayaṃ prati  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre āhāryābhinayo nāmaikaviṃśo dhyāyaḥatha dvāviṃśo dhyāyaḥsāmānyābhinayo nāma jñeyo vāgaṅgasattvajaḥ tatra kāryaḥ prayatnastu nāṭyaṃ sattve pratiṣṭhitam  BhN sattvātirikto bhinayo jyeṣṭha ityabhidhīyate samasattvo bhavenmadhyaḥ satvahīno dhamaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN avyaktarūpaṃ sattvaṃ hi vijñeyaṃ bhāvasaṃśrayam yathāsthānarasopetaṃ romāñcāsrādibhirguṇaiḥ  BhN alaṅkārāstu nāṭyajñairjñeyā bhāvarasāśrayāḥ yauvane bhyadhikāḥ strīṇā vikārā vaktragātrajāḥ  BhN ādau trayo ṅgajasteṣāṃ daśa svābhāvikāḥ pare ayatnajāḥ punaḥ sapta rasabhāvopabṛṃhitāḥ  BhN dehātmakaṃ bhavetsattvaṃ sattvādbhāvaḥ samutthitaḥ bhāvātsamutthito hāvo hāvāddhelā samutthitā  BhN helā hāvaśca bhāvaśca parasparasamutthitāḥ sattvabhede bhavantyete śarīre prakṛtisthitāḥ  BhN vāgaṅgamukharāgaiśca sattvenābhinayena ca kaverantargataṃ bhāvaṃ bhāvayanbhāva ucyate  BhN bhāvasyātikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ vyatiriktaṃ svayoniṣu naikāvasthāntarakṛtaṃ bhāvaṃ tamiha nirdiśet  BhN tatrākṣibhrūvikārāḍhyaḥ śṛṅgārākārasūcakaḥ sagrīvārecako jñeyo hāvaḥ sthitasamutthitaḥ  BhN yo vai hāvaḥ sa evaiṣā śṛṅgārarasasaṃbhavā samākhyātā budhairhelā lalitābhinayātmikā  BhN līlā vilāso vicchittirvibhramaḥ kilikiñcitam moṭṭāyitaṃ kuṭṭimitaṃ bibboko lalitaṃ tathā  BhN vihṛtaṃ ceti vijñeyā daśa strīṇāṃ svabhāvajāḥ punareṣāṃ svarūpāṇi pravakṣyāmi pṛthakpṛthak  BhN vāgaṅgālaṅkāraiḥ śiṣṭaiḥ prītiprayojitairmadhuraiḥ iṣṭajanasyānukṛtirlīlā jñeyā prayogajñaiḥ  BhN sthānāsanagamanānāṃ hastabhrūnetrakarmaṇāṃ caiva utpadyate viśeṣo yaḥ śliṣṭaḥ sa tu vilāsaḥ syāt  BhN mālyācchādanabhūṣaṇa vilepanānāmanādaranyāsaḥ svalpo pi parāṃ śobhāṃ janayati yasmāttu vicchitiḥ  BhN vividhānāmarthānāṃ vāgaṅgāhāryasattvānām madarāgaharṣajanito vyatyāso vibhramo jñeyaḥ  BhN smitaruditahasitabhayaharṣagarvaduḥkhaśramābhilāṣāṇām saṅkarakaraṇaṃ harṣādasakṛt kilikiñcitaṃ jñeyam  BhN iṣṭajanasya kathāyāṃ līlāhelādidarśane vāpi tadbhāvabhāvanākṛtamuktaṃ moṭṭāyitaṃ nāma  BhN keśastanadharādigrahaṇādatiharṣasaṃbhramotpannam kuṭṭamitaṃ vijñeayaṃ sukhamapi duḥkhopacāreṇa  BhN iṣṭānāṃ bhāvānāṃ prāptāvabhimānagarvasaṃbhūtaḥ strīṇāmanādarakṛto bibboko nāma vijñeyaḥ  BhN hastapādāṅgavinyāso bhrūnetroṣṭhaprayojitaḥ saukumāryādbhavedyastu lalitaṃ tatprakīrtitam  BhN karacaraṇāṅganyāsaḥ sabhrūnetroṣṭhasaṃprayuktastu sukumāravidhānena strībhiuritīdaṃ smṛtaṃ lalitam  BhN vākyānāṃ prītiyuktānāṃ prāptānāṃ yadabhāṣaṇam vyājātsvabhāvato vāpi vihṛtaṃ nāma tadbhavet  BhN prāptānāmapi vacasāṃ kriyate yadabhāṣaṇaṃ hriyā strībhiḥ vyājātsvabhāvato vāpyetatsamudāhṛtaṃ vihṛtam  BhN śobhā kāntiśca dīptiśca tathā mādhuryameva ca dhairyaṃ prāgalbhyamaudāryamityete syurayatnajāḥ  BhN rūpayauvanalāvaṇyairupabhogopabṛṃhitaiḥ alaṅkaraṇamaṅgānāṃ śobheti parikīrtitā  BhN vijñeyā ca tathā kāntiḥ śobhaivāpūrṇamanmathā kāntirevātivistīrṇā dīptirityabhidhīyate  BhN sarvāvasthāviśeṣeṣu dīpteṣu laliteṣu ca anulbaṇatvaṃ ceṣṭāyā mādhuryamiti saṃjñitam  BhN cāpalenānupahatā sarvārtheṣvavikatthanā svābhāvikī cittavṛttirdhairyamityabhidhīyate  BhN prayoganissādhvasatā prāgalbhyaṃ samudāhṛtam audāryaṃ praśrayaḥ proktaḥ sarvāvasthānugo budhaiḥ  BhN sukumāre bhavantyete prayoge lalitātmike vilāsalalite hitvā dīpte pyete bhavanti hi  BhN śobhā vilāso mādhuryaṃ sthairyaṃ gāmbhīryameva ca lalitaudāryatejāṃsi sattvabhedāstu pauruṣāḥ  BhN dākṣyaṃ śauryamathotsāho nīcārtheṣu jugupsanam uttamaiśca guṇaiḥ spardhā yataḥ śobheti sā smṛtā  BhN dhīrasaṃcāriṇī dṛṣṭirgatirgovṛṣabhāñcitā smitapūrvamathālāpo vilāsa iti kīrtitaḥ  BhN abhyāsatkaraṇānāṃ tu śliṣṭatvaṃ yatra jāyate mahatsvapi vikāreṣu tanmādhuryamiti smṛtam  BhN dharrmārthakāmasaṃyuktācchubhāśubhasamutthitāt vyavasāyādacalanaṃ sthairyamityabhisaṃjñitam  BhN yasya prabhāvādākārā harṣakrodhabhayādiṣu bhāveṣu nopalakṣyante tadgāmbhīryamiti smṛtam  BhN abuddhipūrvakaṃ yattu nirvikārasvabhājam śṛṅgārākāraceṣṭatvaṃ lalitaṃ tadudāhṛtam  BhN dānamabhyupapattiśca tathā ca priyabhāṣaṇam svajane ca pare vāpi tadaudāryaṃ prakīrtitam  BhN adhikṣepāvamānādeḥ prayuktasya pareṇa yat prāṇatyaye pyasahanaṃ tattejaḥ samudāhṛtam  BhN sattvajo bhinayoḥ pūrvaṃ mayā proktao dvijottamāḥ śārīraṃ cāpyābhinayaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN ṣaḍātmakastu śārīro vākyaṃ sūcāṅkurastathā śākhā nāṭyāyitaṃ caiva nivṛttyaṅkura eva ca  BhN nānārasārthayuktairvṛttanibandhaiḥ kṛtaḥ sacūrṇapadaiḥ prākṛtasaṃskṛtapāṭho vākyābhinayo budhairjñeyaḥ  BhN vākyartho vākyaṃ vā sattvāṅgaiḥ sūcyate yadā pūrvam paścādvākyābhinayaḥ sūcetyabhisaṃjñitā sā tu  BhN hṛdayastho nirvacanairaṅgābhinayaḥ kṛto nipuṇasādhyaḥ sūcaivotpattikṛto vijñeyastvaṅkurābhinayaḥ  BhN yattu śiromukhajaṅghorupāṇipādairyathākramaṃ kriyate śākhādarśanamārgaḥ śākhābhinayaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ  BhN nāṭyāyitamupacārairyaḥ kriyate bhinayasūcayā nāṭye kālaprakarṣahetoḥ praveśakaiḥ saṃgamo yāvat  BhN sthāne dhruvāsvabhinayo yaḥ kriyate harṣaśokaroṣādyaiḥ bhāvarasasaṃprayuktairjñeyaṃ nāṭyāyitaṃ tadapi  BhN yatrānyoktaṃ vākyaṃ sūcābhinayena yojayedanyaḥ tatsaṃbandhārthakathaṃ bhavennivṛttyaṅkuraḥ so tha  BhN eteṣāṃ tu bhavenmārgo yathābhāvarasānvitaḥ kāvyavastuṣu nirdiṣṭo dvādaśābhinayātmakaḥ  BhN ālāpaśca pralāpaśca vilāpaḥ syāttathaiva ca anulāpo tha saṃlāpastvapalāpastathaiva ca  BhN sandeśāścātideśaśca nirdeśaḥ syāttathāparaḥ upadeśo padeśaśca vyapadeśaśca kīrtitaḥ  BhN ābhāṣaṇaṃ tu yadvākyamālāpo nāma sa smṛtaḥ anarthakaṃ vaco yattu pralāpaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ  BhN karuṇaprabhavo yastu vilāpaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ bahuśo bhihitaṃ vākyamanulāpa iti smṛtaḥ  BhN uktipratyuktisaṃyuktaḥ saṃlāpa iti kīrtitaḥ pūrvoktasyānyathāvādo hyapalāpa iti smṛtaḥ  BhN tadidaṃ vacanaṃ brūhītyeṣa sandeśa ucyate yattvayoktaṃ mayoktaṃ tatso tideśa iti smṛtaḥ  BhN sa eṣo haṃ bravīmīti nirdeśa iti kīrtitaḥ vyājāntareṇa kathanaṃ vyapadeśa ihocyate  BhN idaṃ kuru gṛhāṇeti hyupadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ anyārthakathanaṃ yat syāt so padeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN ete mārgāstu vijñeyāḥ sarvābhinayayojakāḥ saptaprakārameteṣāṃ punarvakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam  BhN pratyakṣaśca parokṣaśca tathā kālakṛtāstrayaḥ ātmasthaśca parasthaśca prakārāḥ sapta eva tu  BhN eṣā bravīmi nāhaṃ bho vadāmīti ca yadvacaḥ pratyakṣaśca parokṣaśca vartamānaśca tadbhavet  BhN ahaṃ karomi gacchāmi vadāmi vacanaṃ tava ātmastho vartamānaśca pratyakṣaścaiva sa smṛtaḥ  BhN kariṣyāmi gamiṣyāmi vadiṣyāmīti yadvacaḥ ātmasthaśca parokṣaśca bhaviṣyatkāla eva ca  BhN hatā jitā ca bhagnāśca mayā sarve dviṣadgaṇāḥ ātmasthaśca parokṣaśca vṛttakālaśca sa smṛtaḥ  BhN tvayā hata jitāśceti yo vadennāṭyakarmaṇi parokṣaśca parasthaśca vṛttakālastathaiva ca  BhN eṣa bravīmi kurute gacchatītyādi yadvacaḥ parastho vartamānaśca pratyakṣaścabhavettathā  BhN sa gacchati karotīti vacanaṃ yadutāhṛtam parasthaṃ vartamānaṃ ca parokṣaṃ caiva tadbhavet  BhN kariṣyanti gamiṣyanti vadiṣyantīti yadvacaḥ parasthameṣyatkālaṃ ca parokṣaṃ caiva tadbhavet  BhN hastamantarataḥ kṛtvā yadvadennāṭyakarmaṇi ātmasthaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ ca parokṣaṃ caiva tanmatam  BhN pareṣāmātmanaścaiva kālasya ca viśeṣaṇāt saptaprakārasyāsyaiva bhedā jñeyā anekadhā  BhN ete prayogā vijñeyā mārgābhinayayojitāḥ eteṣviha viniṣpanno vividho bhinayo bhavet  BhN śiro hastakaṭīvakṣojaṅghorukaraṇeṣu tu samaḥ karmavibhāgo yaḥ sāmānyābhinayastu saḥ  BhN lalitairhastasaṃcārastathā mṛdvaṅgaceṣṭitaiḥ abhineyastu nāṭyajñai rasabhāvasamanvitaiḥ  BhN anuddhatamasaṃbhrāntamanāviddhāṅgaceṣṭitam layatālakalāpātapramāṇaniyatātmakam  BhN suvibhaktapadālāpamaniṣṭhuramakāhalam yadīdṛśaṃ bhavennāṭyaṃ jñeyamābhyantaraṃ tu tat  BhN etadeva viparyastaṃ svacchandagaticeṣṭitam anibaddhagītavādyaṃ nāṭyaṃ bāhyamiti smṛtam  BhN lakṣaṇābhyantaratvāddhi tadābhyantaramiṣyate śāstrabāhyaṃ bhavedyattu tadbāhyamiti bhaṇyate  BhN anena lakṣyate yasmāt prayogaḥ karma caiva hi tasmāllakṣaṇametaddhi nāṭye smin saṃprayojitam  BhN anācāryoṣitā ye ca ye ca śāstrabahiṣkṛtāḥ bāhyaṃ prayuñjate te tu ajñātvācāryakīṃ kriyām  BhN śabdaṃ sparśaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca rasaṃ gandhaṃ tathaiva ca indriyānīndriyārthāṃśca bhāvairabhinayedbudhaḥ  BhN kṛtvā sācīkṛtāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ śiraḥ pārśvanataṃ tathā tarjanī karṇadeśe ca budhaḥ śabdaṃ vinirdiśet  BhN kiñcidākuñcite netre kṛtvā bhrūkṣepameva ca tathāṃsagaṇḍayoḥ sparśāt sparśamevaṃ vinirdiśet  BhN kṛtvā patākau mūrdhasthau kiṃcitpracalitānanaḥ nirvarṇayantyā dṛṣṭyā ca rūpaṃ tvabhinayed budhaḥ  BhN kiñcidākuñcite netre kṛtvotphullāṃ ca nāsikām ekocchvāsena ceṣṭau tu rasagandhau vinirdiśet  BhN pañcānāmindriyārthānāṃ bhāvā hyete nubhāvinaḥ śrotratvaṅnetrajihvānāṃ ghrāṇasya ca tathaiva hi  BhN indriyārthāḥ samanaso bhavanti hyanubhāvinaḥ na vetti hyamanāḥ kiṃcidviṣayaṃ pañcadhāgatam  BhN manasastrividho bhāvo vijñeyo bhinaye budhaiḥ iṣṭastathā hyaniṣṭaśca madhyasthaśca tathaiva hi  BhN prahlādanena gātrasya tathā pulakitena ca vadanasya vikāsena kuryādiṣṭanidarśanam  BhN iṣṭe śabde tathā rūpe sparśe gandhe tathā rase indriyairmanasā prāptaiḥ saumukhyaṃ saṃpradarśayet  BhN parāvṛttena śirasā netranāsāvikarṣaṇaiḥ cakṣuṣaścāpradānena hyaniṣṭamabhinirdiśet  BhN nātihṛṣṭena manasā na cātyarthajugupsayā madhyasthanaiva bhāvena madhyasthamabhinirdiśet  BhN tenedaṃ tasya vāpīdaṃ sa evaṃ prakaroti vā parokṣābhinayo yastu madhyastha iti sa smṛtaḥ  BhN ātmānubhāvī yo rthaḥ syādātmastha iti sa smṛtaḥ parārthavarṇanā yatra parasthaḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ  BhN prāyeṇa sarvabhāvānāṃ kāmānniṣpattiriṣyate sa cecchāguṇasampanno bahudhā parikalpitaḥ  BhN dharmakāmo rthakāmaśca mokṣakāmastathaiva ca strīpuṃsayostu yogo yaḥ sa tu kāma iti smṛtaḥ  BhN sarvasyaiva hi lokasya sukhaduḥkhanibarhaṇaḥ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dṛṣyate kāmaḥ sa sukhaṃ vyasaneṣvapi  BhN yaḥ strīpuruṣasaṃyogo ratisaṃbhogakārakaḥ sa śṛṅgāra iti jñeya upacārakṛtaḥ śubhaḥ  BhN bhūyiṣṭhameva loko yaṃ sukhamicchati sarvadā sukhasya hi striyo mūlaṃ nānā śīlāścā tāḥ punaḥ  BhN devadānavagandharvarakṣonāgapatatriṇām piśācayakṣavyālānāṃ naravānarahastinām  BhN mṛgamīnoṣṭramakarakharasūkaravājinām mahīṣājagavādīnāṃ tulyaśīlāḥ striyaḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN snigdhairaṅgairupāṅgaiśca sthirā mandanimeṣiṇi arogā dīptyupetā ca dānasattvārjavānvitā  BhN alpasvedā samaratā svalpabhuk suratapriyā gandhapuṣparatā hṛdyā devaśīlāṅganā smṛtā  BhN adharmaśāṭhyābhiratā sthirakrodhātiniṣṭhurā madyamāṃsapriayā nityaṃ kopanā cātimāninī  BhN capalā cātilubdhā ca paruṣā kalahapriyā īrṣyāśīlā calasnehā cāsuraṃ śīlamāśritā  BhN krīḍāparā cārunetrā nakhadantaiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ svaṅgī ca sthirabhāṣī ca mandāpatyā ratipriyā  BhN gīte vādye ca nṛtte ca ratā hṛṣṭā mṛjāvatī gandharvasattvā vijñeyā snigdhatvakkeśalocanā  BhN bṛhadvyāyatasarvāṅgī raktavistīrṇalocanā khararomā divāsvapnaniratātyuccabhāṣiṇī  BhN nakhadantakṣatakarī krodherṣyākalahapriyā niśāvihāraśīlā ca rākṣasaṃ śīlamāśritā  BhN tīkṣṇanāsāgradaśanā sutanustāmralocanā nīlotpalasavarṇā ca svapnaśīlātikopanā  BhN tiryaggatiścalārambhā bahuśvāsātimāninī gandhamālyāsavaratānāgasattvāṅganā smṛtā  BhN atyantavyāvṛtāsyā ca tīkṣṇaśīlā saritpriyā surāsavakṣīraratā bahvapatyā phalapriyā  BhN nityaṃ śvasanaśīlāca tathodyānavanapriyā capalā bahuvākchīghrā śākunaṃ sattvamāśritā  BhN ūnādhikāṅgulikarā rātrau niṣkuṭacāriṇi bālodvejanaśīlā ca piśunā kliṣṭabhāṣiṇi  BhN surate kutsitācārā romaśāṅgī mahāsvanā piśācasattvā vijñeyā madyamāṃsabalipriyā  BhN svapnaprasvedanāṅgī ca sthiraśayyāsanapriyā medhāvinī buddhimatī madyagandhāmiṣapriyā  BhN ciradṛṣṭeṣu harṣaṃ ca kṛtajñatvādupaiti sā adīrghaśāyinī caiva yakṣaśīlāṅganā smṛtā  BhN tulyamānāvamānā yā paruṣatvak kharasvarā śaṭhānṛtoddhatakathā vyālasattvā ca piṅgadṛk  BhN vibhaktāṅgī kṛtajñā ca gurudevadvijapriyā dharmakāmārthaniratā hyahaṅkāāravivarjitā suhṛtpriyā suśīlā ca mānuṣaṃ sattvamāśritā  BhN saṃhatālpatanurhṛṣṭā piṅgaromā chalapriyā pragalbhā capalā tīkṣṇā vṛkṣārāmavanapriyā  BhN svalpamapyupakāraṃ tu nityaṃ yā bahumanyate prasahyaratiśīlā ca vānaraṃ sattvamāśritā  BhN mahāhanulalāṭā ca śarīropacayānvitā piṅgākṣī romaśāṅgī ca gandhamālyāsavapriyā  BhN kopanā sthiracittā ca jalodyānavanapriyā madhurābhiratā caiva hastisattvā prakīrtitā  BhN svalpodarī bhagnanāsā tanujaṅghā vanapriyā calavīstīrṇanayanā capalā śīghragāminī  BhN divātrāsaparā nityaṃ gītavādyaratipriyā nivāsasthiracittā ca mṛgasattvā prakīrtitā  BhN dīrghapīnonnatoraskā calā nātinimeṣiṇī bahubhṛtyā bahusutā matsyasattvā jalapriyā  BhN lamboṣṭhī svedabahulā kiñcidvikaṭagāminī kṛśodarī puṣpaphalalavaṇāmlakaṭupriyā  BhN udbandhakaṭipārśvā ca kharaniṣṭhurabhāṣiṇī atyunnatakaṭīgrīvā uṣṭrasattvāṭavīpriyā  BhN sthūlaśīrṣāñcitagrīvā dāritāsyā mahasvanā jñeyā makarasattvā ca krūrā matsyaguṇairyutā  BhN sthūlajihvoṣṭhadaśanā rūkṣatvakkaṭubhāṣiṇī ratiyuddhakarī dhṛṣṭā nakhadantakṣatapriyā  BhN sapatnīdveṣiṇī dakṣā capalā śīghragāminī sarogā bahvapatyā ca kharasattvā prakīrtitā  BhN dīrghapṛṣṭhodaramukhī romaśālī balānvitā susaṃkṣiptalalāṭā ca kandamūlaphalapriyā  BhN kṛṣṇā daṃṣṭotkaṭamukhī hrasvodaraśiroruhā hīnācārā bahvapatyā saukaraṃ sattvamāśritā  BhN sthirā vibhaktapārśvorukaṭīpṛṣṭhaśirodharā subhagā dānaśīlā ca ṛjusthūlaśiroruhā  BhN kṛśā cañcalacittā ca snigdhavākchīghragāminī kāmakrodhaparā caiva hayasattvāṅganā smṛtā  BhN sthūlapṛṣṭhākṣidaśanā tanupārśvodarā sthirā hariromāñcitā raudrī lokadviṣṭā ratipriyā  BhN kiñcidunnatavaktrā ca jalakrīḍāvanapriyā bṛhallalāṭā suśroṇī māhiṣaṃ sattvamāśritā  BhN kṛśā tanubhujoraskā niṣṭabdhasthiralocanā saṃkṣiptapāṇipādā ca sūkṣmaromasamācitā  BhN bhayaśīlā jalodvignā bahvapatyā vanapriyā cañcalā śīghragamanā hyajasattvāṅganā smṛtā  BhN udbandhagātranayanā vijṛmbhaṇaparāyaṇā dīrghālpavadanā svalpapāṇipādavibhūṣitā  BhN uccaḥsvanā svalpanidrā krodhanā sukṛtapriyā hīnācārā kṛtajñā ca śvaśīlā parikīrtitā  BhN pṛthupīnoonnataśroṇī tanujaṅghā suhṛtpriyā saṃkṣiptapāṇipādā ca dṛḍhārambhā prajāhitā  BhN pitṛdevārcanaratā satyaśaucagurupriyā sthirā parikleśasahā gavāṃ sattvaṃ samāśritā  BhN nānāśīlāḥ striyo jñeyāḥ svaṃ svaṃ sattvaṃ samāśritāḥ vijñāya ca yathāsattvamupaseveta tāḥ punaḥ  BhN upacāro yathāsattvaṃ strīṇāmalpo pi harṣadaḥ mahānapyanyathāyukto naiva tuṣṭikaro bhavet  BhN yathā saṃprarthitāvāptyā ratiḥ samupajāyate strīpuṃsayośca ratyarthamupacāro vidhīyate  BhN dharmārthaṃ hi tapaścaryā sukhārthaṃ dharma iṣyate sukhasya mūlaṃ pramadāstāsu sambhoga iṣyate  BhN kāmopabhāgo dvividho nāṭyadharme bhidhīyate bāhyābhyantarataścaiva nārīpuruṣasaṃśrayaḥ  BhN ābhyantaraḥ pārthivānāṃ sa ca kāryastu nāṭake bāhyo veśyāgataścaiva sa ca prakaraṇe bhavet  BhN tatra rājopabhogaṃ tu vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ upacāravidhiṃ samyak kāmatantrasamutthitam  BhN trividhā prakṛtiḥ strīṇāṃ nānāsattvasamudbhavā bāhyā cābhyantarā caiva syādbāhyābhyantarāparā  BhN kulīnābhyantarā jñeyā bāhyā veśyāṅganā smṛtā kṛtaśaucā tu yā nārī sā bāhyābhyantarā smṛtā  BhN antaḥpuropacāre tu kulajā kanyakāpi vā na hi rājopacāre tu bāhyastrībhoga iṣyate  BhN ābhyantaro bhavedrājño bāhyo bāhyajanasya ca divyaveśāṅganānāṃ hi rājñāṃ bhavati saṅgamaḥ  BhN kulajākāmitaṃ yacca tajjñeyaṃ kanyakāsvapi yā cāpi veśyā sāpyatra yathaiva kulajā tathā  BhN iha kāmasamutpatīrnānābhāvasamudbhavā strīṇāṃ vā puruṣāṇāṃ vā uttamādhamamadhyamā  BhN śravaṇāddarśanādrūpādaṅgalīlāviceṣṭitaiḥ madhuraiśca samālāpaiḥ kāmaḥ samupajāyate  BhN rūpaguṇādisametaṃ kalādivijñānayauvanopetam dṛṣṭvā puruṣaviśeṣaṃ nārī madanāturā bhavati  BhN tataḥ kāmayamānānāṃ nṛṇāṃ strīṇāmathāpi ca kāmābhāveṅgitānīha tajjñaḥ samupalakṣayet  BhN lalitā calapakṣmā ca tathā ca mukulekṣaṇā srastottarapuṭā caiva kāmyā dṛṣṭirbhavediha  BhN valitāntā salālityasaṃmitairvyañjitairastathā dṛṣṭiḥ sā lalitā nāma strīṇāmardhāvalokane  BhN īṣtsaṃraktagaṇḍastu sasvedalavacitritaḥ praspandamānaromāñco mukharāgo bhavediha  BhN kāmyenāṅgavikāreṇa sakaṭākṣanirīkṣitaiḥ tathābharaṇasaṃsparśaiḥ karṇakaṇḍuyanairapi  BhN aṅguṣṭhāgravilikhanaiḥ stananābhipradarśanaiḥ nakhanistodanāccaiva keśasaṃyamanādapi  BhN veśyāmevaṃvidhairbhāvairlakṣayenmadanāturām kulajāyāstathā caiva pravakṣyāmīṅgitāni tu  BhN prahasantīva netrābhyāṃ pratataṃ ca nirīkṣate smayate sā nigūḍhaṃ ca vācaṃ cādhomukhī vadet  BhN smitottarā mandavākyā svedākāranigūhanī praspanditādharā caiva cakitā ca kulāṅganā  BhN evaṃvidhaiḥ kāmaliṅgairaprāptasuratotsavā daśasthānagataṃ kāmaṃ nānābhāvaiḥ pradarśayet  BhN prathame tvabhilāṣaḥ syād dvitīye cintanaṃ bhavet anusmṛtistṛtīye tu caturthe guṇakīrtanam  BhN udvegaḥ pañcame prokto vilāpaḥ ṣaṣṭha ucyate unmādaḥ saptame jñeyo bhavedvyādhistathāṣṭame  BhN navame jaḍatā caiva daśame maraṇaṃ bhavet strīpuṃsayoreṣa vidhirlakṣaṇaṃ ca nibodhata  BhN vyavasāyātsamārabdhaḥ saṃkalpecchāsamudbhavaḥ samāgamopāyakṛtaḥ so bhilāṣaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN niryāti viśati ca muhuḥ karoti cākārameva madanasya tiṣṭhati ca darśanapathe prathamasthāne sthitā kāme  BhN kenopāyena saṃprāptiḥ kathaṃ vāsau bhavenmama dūtīniveditairbhāvairiti cintāṃ nidarśayet  BhN ākekarārdhaviprekṣitāni valayaraśanāparāmarśaḥ nīvīnābhyāḥ saṃsparśanaṃ ca kāryaṃ dvitīye tu  BhN sumuhurmuhurniḥśvasitairmanorathavicintanaiḥ pradveṣāccānyakāryāṇāmanusmṛtirudāhṛtā  BhN naivāsane na śayane dhṛtimupalabhate svakarmaṇi vihastā taccintopagatatvāt tṛtīyameva prayuñjīta  BhN aṅgapratyaṅgalīlābhirvākceṣṭāhasitekṣitaiḥ nāstyanyaḥ sadṛśastenetyetat syād guṇakīrtanam  BhN guṇakīrtanollukasanairaśrusvedāpamārjanaiścāpi dūtyavirahavisrambhairabhinayayogaścaturthe tu  BhN āsane śayane cāpi na tuṣyati na tiṣṭhati nityamevotsukā ca syādudvegasthānamāśritā  BhN cintāniḥśvāsakhedena hṛddāhābhinayena ca kuryāttadevamatyantamudvegābhinayena ca  BhN iha sthita ihāsīna iha copagato mayā iti taistairvilapitairvilāpaṃ saṃprayojayet  BhN udvignātyarthamautsukyādadhṛtyā ca vilāpinī tatastataśca bhramati vilāpasthānamāśritā  BhN tatsaṃśritāṃ kathāṃ yuṅkte sarvāvasthāgatāpi hi puṃsaḥ pradveṣṭi cāpyanyānunmādaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ  BhN tiṣṭhatyanimiṣadṛṣṭirdīrghaṃ niḥśvasiti gacchati dhyānam roditi vihārakāle nāṭyamidaṃ syāttathonmāde  BhN sāmadānārthasaṃbhogaiḥ kāmyaiḥ saṃpreṣaṇairapi sarvairnirākṛtaiḥ paścād vyādhiḥ samupajāyate  BhN muhyati hṛdayaṃ kvāpi prayāti śirasaśca vedanā tīvrā na dhṛtiṃ cāpyupalabhate hyaṣṭamamevaṃ prayuñjīta  BhN pṛṣṭā na kiñcit prabrate na śṛṇoti na paśyati hākaṣṭavākyā tūṣṇīkā jaḍatāyāṃ gatasmṛtiḥ  BhN akāṇḍe dattahuṃkārā tathā praśithilāṅgikā śvāsagrastānanā caiva jaḍatābhinaye bhavet  BhN sarvaiḥ kṛtaiḥ pratīkārairyadī nāsti samāgamaḥ kāmāgninā pradīptāyā jāyate maraṇaṃ tataḥ  BhN evaṃ sthānāni kāryāṇi kāmatantraṃ samīkṣya tu aprāptau yāni kāmasya varjayitvā tu naidhanam  BhN vividhaiḥ puruṣo pyevaṃ vipralambhasamudbhavaiḥ bhāvairetāni kāmasya nānārūpāṇi yojayet  BhN evaṃ kāmayamānānāṃ strīṇā nṛṇāmathāpi vā sāmānyaguṇayogena yuñjītābhinayaṃ budhaḥ  BhN cintāniḥśvāsakhedena hṛddāhābhinayena ca tathānugamannāccāpi tathaivādhvanirīkṣaṇāt  BhN ākāśavīkṣaṇāccāpi tathā dīnaprabhāṣaṇāt sparśanānmoṭanāccāpi tathā sāpāśrayāśrayāt  BhN ebhirnānāśrayotpannairvipralambhasamudbhavaiḥ kāmasthānāni sarvāṇi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ samprayojayet  BhN srajo bhūṣaṇagandhāṃśca gṛhāṇyupavanāni ca kāmāgninā dahyamānaḥ śītalāni niṣevate  BhN pradahyamānaḥ kāmārto bahusthānasamarditaḥ preṣayetkāmato dūtīmātmāvasthāpradarśinīm  BhN sandeśaṃ caiva dūtyāstu pradadyānmadanāśrayam tasyeyaṃ samavastheti kathayedvinayena sā  BhN athāveditabhāvārtho ratyupāyaṃ vicintayet ayaṃ vidhirvidhānajñaiḥ kāryaḥ pracchannakāmite  BhN vidhiṃ rājopacārasya punarvakṣyāmi tattvataḥ abhyantaragataṃ samyak kāmatantrasamutthitam  BhN sukhaduḥkhakṛtān bhāvān nānāśīlasamutthitān yānyān prakurute rājā tānstān lokānuvartate  BhN na durlabhāḥ pārthivānāṃ stryarthamājñākṛtāḥ guṇāḥ dākṣiṇyāttu samudbhūtaḥ kāmo ratikaro bhavet  BhN bahumānena devīnāṃ vallabhānāṃ bhayena ca pracchannakāmitaṃ rājñā kāryaṃ parijanaṃ prati  BhN yadyapyasti narendrāṇāṃ kāmatantramanekadhā pracchannākāmitaṃ yattu tadvai ratikaraṃ bhavet  BhN yadvāmābhiniveśitvaṃ yataśca vinivāryate durlabhatvaṃ ca yannāryāḥ sā kāmasya parā ratiḥ  BhN rājñāmantaḥpurajane divāsambhoga iṣyate vāsoapacāro yaścaiaṣāṃ sa rātrau parikīrtitaḥ  BhN paripāṭyāṃ phalārthe vā nave prasava eva vā duḥkhe caiva pramode ca ṣaḍete vāsakāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN ucite vāsake strīnāmṛtukāle pi vā nṛpaiḥ preṣyāṇāmathaveṣṭānāṃ kāryaṃ caivopasarpaṇam  BhN tatra vāsakasajjā ca virahotkaṇṭhitāpi vā svādhīnabhartṛkā cāpi kalahāntaritāpi vā  BhN khaṇḍitā vipralabdhā vā tathā proṣitabhartṛkā tathābhisārikā caiva jñeyāstvaṣṭau tu nayikāḥ  BhN ucite vāsakae yā tu ratisaṃbhogalālasā maṇḍanaṃ kurute hṛṣṭā sā vai vāsakasajjikā  BhN anekakāryavyāsaṅgādyasyā nāgacchati priyaḥ tadanāgataduḥkhārtā virahotkaṇṭhitā tu sā  BhN suratātirasairbaddho yasyāḥ pārśve tu nāyakaḥ sāndrāmodaguṇaprāptā bhavet svādhīnabhartṛkā  BhN īrṣyākalahaniṣkrānto yasyā nāgacchati priyaḥ sāmarṣavaśasaṃprāptā kalahāntaritā bhavet  BhN vyāsaṅgāducite yasyā vāsake nāgataḥ priyaḥ tadanāgamaduḥkhārtā khaṇḍitā sā prakīrtitā  BhN yasyā dūtīṃ priyaḥ preṣya dattvā saṃketameva vā nāgataḥ kāraṇeneha vipralabdhā tu sā bhavet  BhN nānākāryāṇi sandhāya yasyā vai proṣitaḥ priyaḥ sārūḍhālakakeśāntā bhavet proṣitabhartṛkā  BhN hitvā lajjāṃ tu yā śliṣṭā madena madanena ca abhisārayate kāntaṃ sā bhavedabhisārikā  BhN āsvavasthāsu vijñeyā nāyikā nāṭakāśrayā etāsāṃ caiva vakṣyāmi kāmatantramanekadhā  BhN cintāniḥśvāsakhedena hṛddāhābhinayena ca sakhībhiḥ saha saṃlāpairātmāvasthāvalokanaiḥ  BhN glānidainyāśrupātaiśca roṣasyāgamanena ca nirbhūṣaṇamṛjātvena duḥkhena ruditena ca  BhN khaṇḍitā vipralabdhā vā kalahāntaritāpi vā tathā proṣitakāntā ca bhāvānetān prayojayet  BhN vicitrojjvalaveṣā tu pramododyotitānanā udīrṇaśobhā ca tathā kāryā svādhīnabhartṛkā  BhN veśyāyāḥ kulajāyāyāśca preṣyāyāśca prayoktṛbhiḥ ebhirbhāvaviśeṣaistu kartavyamabhisāraṇam  BhN samadā mṛduceṣṭā ca tathā parijanāvṛtā nānābharaṇacitrāṅgī gacchedveśyāṅganā śanaiḥ  BhN saṃlīnā sveṣu gātreṣu trastā vinamitānanā avakuṇṭhanasaṃvitā hacchettu kulajāṅganā  BhN madaskhalitasaṃlāpā vibhramotphullalocanā āviddhagatisaṃcārā gacchetpreṣyā samuddhatam  BhN gatvā sā cedyadā tatra paśyetsuptaṃ priyaṃ tadā anena tūpacāreṇa tasya kuryātprabodhanam  BhN alaṅkāreṇa kulajā veśyā gandhaistu śītalaiḥ preṣyā tu vastravyajanaiḥ kurvīta pratibodhanam  BhN kulāṅganānāmevāyaṃ noktaḥ kāmāśrayo vidhiḥ sarvāvasthānubhāvyaṃ hi yasmādbhavati nāṭakam  BhN navakāmapravṛttāyā kruddhāyā vā samāgame sāpadeśairupāyaistu vāsakaṃ saṃprayojayet  BhN nānālaṅkaravastrāṇi gandhamālyāni caiva hi priyayojitabhuktāni niṣeveta mudānvitaḥ  BhN na tathā bhavati manuṣyo madanavaśaḥ kāminīmalabhamānaḥ dviguṇopajātaharṣo bhavati yatha saṅgataḥ priyayā  BhN vilāsabhāveṅgitavākyalīlāmādhuryavistāraguṇopapannaḥ parasparapremanirīkṣitena samāgamaḥ kāmakṛtastu kāryaḥ  BhN tataḥ pravṛtte madane upacārasamudbhave vāsopacāraḥ kartavyo nāyakāgamanaṃ prati  BhN gandhamālye gṛhītvā tu cūrṇavāsastathaiva ca ādarśo līlayā gṛhyaśchandato vā punaḥ punaḥ  BhN vāsopacāre nātyarthaṃ bhūṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ bhavet raśanānūpuraprāyaṃ svanavacca praśasyate  BhN nāmbaragrahaṇaṃ raṅge na snānaṃ na vilepanam nāñjanaṃ nāṅgarāgaśca keśasaṃyamanaṃ tathā  BhN nāprāvṛttā naikavastrā na rāgamadharasya tu uttamā madhyamā vāpi kurvīta pramadā kvacit  BhN adhamānāṃ bhavedeṣa sarva eva vidhiḥ sadā kāraṇāntaramāsādya tasmādapi na kārayet  BhN preṣyādīnāṃ ca nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ vāpi nāṭake bhūṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ kāryaṃ puṣpagrahaṇameva ca  BhN gṛhītamaṇḍanā cāpi pratīkṣeta priyāgamam līlayā maṇḍitaṃ veṣaṃ kuryādyanna virudhyate  BhN vidhivadvāsakaṃ kuryānnāyikā nāyakāgame pratīkṣamāṇā ca tato nālikāśabdamādiśet  BhN śrutvā tu nālikāśabdaṃ nāyakāgamaviklavā viṣaṇṇā vepamānā ca gacchettoraṇameva ca  BhN toraṇaṃ vāmahastena kavāṭaṃ dakṣiṇena ca gṛhītvā toraṇāśliṣṭā saṃpratīkṣeta nāyakam  BhN śaṅkāṃ cintāṃ bhayaṃ caiva prakuryāttoraṇāśritā adṛṣṭvā ramaṇaṃ nārī viṣaṇṇā ca kṣaṇaṃ bhavet  BhN dīrghaṃ caiva viniḥśvasya nayanāmbu nipātayet sannaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ kṛtvā visṛjetadaṅgamāsane  BhN vyākṣepādvimṛśeccāpi nāyakāgamanaṃ prati taistairvicāraṇopāyaiḥ śubhāśubhasamutthitaiḥ  BhN gurukāryeṇa mitrairvā mantriṇā rājyacintayā anubaddhaḥ priyaṃ kiṃ nu vṛto vallabhayāpi vā  BhN utpātānnirdiśeccāpi śubhāśubhasamutthitān nimitairātmasaṃsthaistu sphuritaiḥ spandiataistathā  BhN śobhaneṣu tu kāryeṣu nimittaṃ vāmataḥ striyāḥ aniṣṭeṣvatha sarveṣu nimittaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bhavet  BhN savyaṃ netraṃ lalāṭaṃ ca bhrūnāsoṣṭhaṃ tathaiva ca urubāhustanaṃ caiva sphuredyadi samāgamaḥ  BhN eteṣamanyathābhāve durnimittaṃ vinirdiśet darśane durnimittasya mohaṃ gacchetkṣaṇaṃ tataḥ  BhN anāgame nāyakasya kāryo gaṇḍāśrayaḥ karaḥ bhūṣaṇe cāpyavajñānaṃ rodanaṃ ca samācaret  BhN atha cecchobhanaṃ tatsyānnimittaṃ nāyakāgame sūcyo nāyikayāsanno gandhāghrāṇena nāyakaḥ  BhN dṛṣṭvā cotthāya saṃhṛṣṭā pratyudgacchedyathāvidhi tataḥ kāntaṃ nirīkṣeta praharṣotphullalocanā  BhN sakhīskandhārpitakarā kṛtvā sthānakamāyatam darśayeta tataḥ kāntaṃ sacihnaṃ sarasavraṇam  BhN yadi syādaparāddhastu kṛtaistaistairupakramaiḥ upālambhakṛatairvākyairupālabhyastu nāyakaḥ  BhN mānāpamānasaṃmohairavahitthabhayakramaiḥ vacanasya samutpattiḥ strīṇāmīrṣyākṛtā bhavet  BhN visraṃbhasneharāgeṣu sandehe praṇaye tathā paritoṣe ca gharṣe ca dākṣiṇyākṣepavibhrame  BhN dharmārthakāmayogeṣu pracchannavacaneṣu ca hāsye kutūhale caiva saṃbhrame vyasane tathā  BhN strīpuṃsayoḥ krodhakṛte pṛthaṅmiśre tathāpi vā anābhāṣyo pi saṃbhāṣyaḥ priya ebhistu kāraṇaiḥ  BhN yatra sneho bhavettatra hīrṣyā madanasaṃbhavā catasro yonayastasyāḥ kīrtyamānā nibodhata  BhN vaimanasyaṃ vyalīkaṃ ca vipriyaṃ manyureva ca eteṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇāni yathākramam  BhN nidrākhedālasagatiṃ sacihnaṃ sarasavraṇam evavidhaṃ priyaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaimanasyaṃ bhavet striyāḥ  BhN nidrābhyasūyitāvekṣaṇena roṣaprakampamānāṅgyā sādhviti suṣṭhviti vacanaiḥ śobhata ityevamabhineyam  BhN bahudhā vāryamāṇo pi yastasminneva dṛśyate saṃgharṣamatsarāttatra vyalīkaṃ jāyate striyāḥ  BhN kṛtvorasi vāmakaraṃ dakṣiṇahastaṃ tathā vidhunvantyā caraṇaviniṣṭhambhena ca kāryo bhinayo vyalīke tu  BhN jīvantyā tvayi jīvāmi dāso haṃ tvaṃ ca me priyā uktvaivaṃ yo nyathā kuryādvipriyaṃ tatra jāyate  BhN dūtīlekhaprativacanabhedanaiḥ krodhahasitaruditaiśca vipriyakaraṇe bhinayaḥ saśiraḥkampaiśca kartavyaḥ  BhN pratipakṣasakāśāttu yaḥ saubhāgyavikatthanaḥ upasarpet sacinhnastu manyustatropajāyate  BhN valayaparivartanairatha suśithalamutkṣepeṇena raśanāyāḥ manyustvabhinetavyaḥ saśaṅkitaṃ bāṣpapūrṇākṣyā  BhN dṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ priyatamaṃ saśaṅkitaṃ sāparādhamatilajjam īrṣyāvacanasamutthaiḥ khedayitavyo hyupālambhaiḥ  BhN na ca niṣṭhuramabhibhāṣyo na cāpyatikrodhanastu parihāsaḥ bāṣponmiśrairvacanairātmopanyāsasaṃyuktaiḥ  BhN madhyāṅgulyaṅguṣṭhāgravicyavātpāṇinorasi kṛtena udvartitanetratayā pratatairabhivīkṣaṇaiścāpi  BhN kaṭihastavivartanayā vicchinnatayā tathāñjaleḥ karaṇāt mūrdhabhramaṇanihañcitanipātasaṃśleaṣṇāccāpi  BhN avahitthavīkṣaṇādvā aṅgulibhaṅgena tarjanailalitaiḥ ebhirbhāvaviśeṣairanunayaneṣvabhinayaḥ kāryaḥ  BhN śobhase sādhu dṛṣṭo si gaccha tvaṃ kiṃṃ vilambase mā māṃ sprākṣīḥ priyā yatra tatra yā te hṛdi sthitā  BhN gacchetyuktvā parāvṛtya vinivṛttāntareṇa tu kenacidvacanārthena praharṣaṃ yojayetpunaḥ  BhN rabhasagrahaṇāccāpi haste vastre ca mūrdhani kāryaṃ prasādanaṃ nāryā hyaparādhaṃ samīkṣya tu  BhN haste vastre tha keśānte nāryāpyatha gṛhītayā kāntamevopasarpantyā kartavyaṃ mokṣaṇaṃ śanaiḥ  BhN gṛhītāyātha keśānte haste vastre thavā punaḥ huṃ muñcetyupasarpantyā vācyaḥ sparśālasaṃ priyaḥ  BhN pādāgrasthitayā nāryā kiṃcitkuṭṭamitotkaṭam aśvakrāntena kartavyaṃ keśānāṃ mokṣaṇaṃ śanaiḥ  BhN amucyamāne keśānte saṃjātasvedaleśayā haṃ hu muñcāpasarpeti vācyaḥ sparśālasāṅgayā  BhN gaccheti roṣavākyena gatvā pratinivṛtya ca kenacidvacanārthena vācyaṃ yāsyasi neti ca  BhN vidhūnanena hastena huṃkāraṃ saṃprayojayet sa cāvadhūnane kāryaḥ śapathairvyāja eva ca  BhN akṣṇoḥ saṃvaraṇe kāryaṃ pṛṣṭhataścopagūhanam nāryāstvapahṛte vastre dīpacchādanameva ca  BhN tāvat khedayitavyastu yāvatpādagato bhavet tataścaraṇayoryāte kuryāddūtīnirīkṣaṇam  BhN utthāpyāliṅgayeccaiva nāyikā nāyakaṃ tataḥ ratibhogagatā hṛṣṭā śayanābhimukhī vrajet  BhN etadgītavidhānena sukumāreṇa yojayet yadā śṛṅgārasaṃyuktaṃ ratisambhogakāraṇam  BhN yadā cākāśapuruṣaparasthavacanāśrayam bhavetkāvyaṃ tadā hyeṣa kartavyo bhinayaḥ striyā  BhN yadantapurasambandhaṃ kāryaṃ bhavati nāṭake śṛṅgārarasasaṃyuktaṃ tatrāpyeṣa vidhirbhavet  BhN na kāryaṃ śayanaṃ raṅge nāṭyadharmaṃ vijānatā kenacidvacanārthena aṅkacchedo vidhīyate  BhN yadvā śayītārthavaśādekākī sahito pi vā cumbanāliṅganaṃ caiva tatha guhyaṃ ca yadbhavet  BhN dantacchedyaṃ nakhacchedyaṃ nīvīsraṃsanameva ca stanāntaravimardaṃ ca raṅgamadhye na kārayet  BhN bhojanaṃ salilakrīḍā tathā lajjākaraṃ ca yat evaṃvidhaṃ bhavedyadyattattadraṅge na kārayet  BhN pitāputrasnuṣāśvaśrūdṛśyaṃ yasmāttu nāṭakam tasmādetāni sarvāṇi varjanīyāni yatnataḥ  BhN vākyaiḥ sātiśayaiḥ śravyairmadhurairnātiniṣṭhuraiḥ hitopadeśasaṃyuktaistajjñaḥ kuryāttu nāṭakam  BhN evamantaḥpurakṛtaḥ kāryastvabhinayo budhaḥ samāgame tha nārīṇāṃ vācyāni madanāśraye  BhN priyeṣu vacanānīha yāni tāni nibodhata priayaḥ kānto vinītaśca nāthaḥ svāmyatha jīvitam  BhN nandanaścetyabhiprīte vacanāni bhavanti hi duḥśīlo tha durācāraḥ śaṭho vāmo vikatthanaḥ  BhN nirlajjo niṣṭhuraścaiava priyaḥ krodhe bhidhīyate yo vipriyaṃ na kurute na cāyuktaṃ prabhāṣate  BhN tathārjavasamācāraḥ sa priyastvabhidhīyate anyanārīsamudbhūtaṃ cihnaṃ yasya na dṛṣyate  BhN adhare vā śarīre vā sa kānta iti bhāṣyate saṃkruddhe pi hi yo nāryā nottaraṃ pratipadyate  BhN paruṣaṃ vā na vadati vinītaḥ sābhidhīyate hitaiṣī rakṣaṇe śakto na mānī na ca matsarī  BhN sarvakāryeṣvasaṃmūḍhaḥ sa nātha iti saṃjñitaḥ sāmadānārthasaṃbhogaistathā lālanapālanaiḥ  BhN nārīṃ niṣevate yastu sa svāmītyabhidhīyate nārīpsitairabhiprāyairnipuṇaṃ śayanakriyām  BhN karoti yastu saṃbhoge sa jīvitamiti smṛtaḥ kulīno dhṛtimāndakṣo dakṣiṇo vāgviśāradaḥ  BhN ślāghanīyaḥ sakhīmadhye nandanaḥ so bhidhīyate ete vacanavinyāsā ratiprītikarāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN tathā cāprītivākyāni gadato me nibodhata niṣṭhuraścāhiṣṇuśca māni dhṛṣṭo vikatthanaḥ  BhN anavasthitacittaśca duḥśīla iti sa smṛtaḥ tāḍanaṃ bandhanaṃ cāpi yo vimṛśya samācaret  BhN tathā paruṣavākyaśca durācāraḥ sa tanyate vācaiava madhuro yastu karmaṇa nopapādakaḥ  BhN yoṣitaḥ kiñcidapyarthaṃ sa śaṭhaḥ paribhāṣyate vāryate yatra yatrārthe tattadeva karoti yaḥ  BhN viparītaniveśī ca sa vāma iti saṃjñitaḥ sarasavraṇacihno yaḥ strīsaubhāgyavikatthanaḥ  BhN atimānī tathā stabdho vikatthana iti smṛtaḥ vāryamāṇo dṛḍhataraṃ yo nārīmupasarpati  BhN sacihnāḥ sāparādhaśca sa nirlajja iti smṛtaḥ yo parāddhastu sahasā nārīṃ sevitumicchati  BhN aprasādanabuddhiśca niṣṭhuraḥ so bhidhīyate ete vacanavinyāsāḥ priyāpriyavibhāṣitāḥ  BhN nartakīsaṃśritāḥ kāryā bahavo nye pi nāṭake eṣa gītavidhāne tu sukumāre vidhirbhavet  BhN śṛṅgārarasasaṃbhūto ratisaṃbhogakhedanaḥ yaccaivākāśapuruṣaṃ parasthavacanāśrayam  BhN śṛṅgāra evaṃ vācyaṃ syāttatrāpyeṣa kramo bhavet yadvā purusaṃbandhaṃ kāryaṃ bhavati nāṭake  BhN śṛṅgārarasasaṃyuktaṃ tatrāpyeṣa kramo bhavet evamantaḥpuragataḥ prayojyo bhinayo bhavet  BhN divyāṅganānāṃ tu vidhiṃ vyākhyāsyamyanupūrvaśaḥ nityamevojvalo veṣo nityaṃ pramuditaṃ manaḥ  BhN nityameva sukhaḥ kālo devānāṃ lalitāśrayaḥ na cairṣyā naiva ca krodho nāsūyā na prasādanam  BhN divyānāṃ dṛṣyate puṃsāṃ śṛṅgāre yoṣitāṃ tathā ye bhāvā mānuṣāṇāṃ syuryadaṅgaṃ yacca ceṣṭitam  BhN sarvaṃ tadeva kartavyaṃ divyairmānuṣasaṅgame yadā mānuṣasaṃbhogo divyānāṃ yoṣitāṃ bhavat  BhN tadā sarvāḥ prakartavyā ye bhāvā mānuṣāśrayāḥ śāpabhraṃśāttu divyānāṃ tathā cāpatyalipsayā  BhN kāryo mānuṣasaṃyogaḥ śṛṅgārarasasaṃśrayaḥ puṣpairbhūṣaṇajaiḥ śabdairadṛśyāpi pralobhayet  BhN punaḥ saṃdarśanaṃ dattvā kṣaṇādantaritā bhavet vastrābharaṇamālyādyairlekhasaṃpreṣaṇairapi  BhN īdṛśairupacāraistu samunmādyastu nāyakaḥ unmādanātsamudbhūtaḥ kāmo ratikaro bhavet  BhN svabhāvopagato yastu nāsāvatyarthabhāvikaḥ evaṃ rājopacāro hi kartavyo bhyantarāśrayaḥ  BhN bāhyamapyupacāraṃ tu pravakṣyāmyatha vaiśike iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre sāmānyābhinayo nāmādhyāyo dvāviṃśaḥatha trayoviṃśo dhyāyaḥviśeṣayetkalāḥ sarvā yasmāttasmāttu vaiśikaḥ veśopacāre sādhurvā vaiśikaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  BhN yo hi sarvakalopetaḥ sarvaśilpavicakṣaṇaḥ strīcittagrahaṇābhijño vaiśikaḥ sa bhavetpumān  BhN guṇastasya tu vijñeyāḥ svaśarīrasamutthitāḥ āhāryāḥ sahajāścaiva trayastriṃśatsamāsataḥ  BhN śāstravicchilpasaṃpanno rūpavān priyadarśanaḥvikrānto dhṛtimāṃścaiva vayoveṣakulānvitaḥ  BhN surabhirmadhurastyāgi sahiṣṇuravikatthanaḥaśaṅkitaḥ priyābhāṣī caturaḥ śubhadaḥ śuciḥ  BhN kāmopacārakuśalo dakṣiṇo deśakālavit adīnavākyaḥ smitavān vāgmī dakṣaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ  BhN strīlubdhāḥ saṃvibhāgī ca śraddhadhāno dṛḍhasmṛtiḥ gamyāsu cāpyavisrambhī mānī ceti hi vaiśikaḥ  BhN anuyuktaḥ śucirdakṣo dakṣiṇaḥ pratipattimān bhaveccitrābhidhāyī ca vayasyastasya tadguṇaḥ  BhN vijñānaguṇasaṃpanā kathinī liṅginī tathā prātiveśyā sakhī dāsī kumārī kāruśilpinī  BhN dhātrī pāṣaṇḍinī caiva tathā raṅgopajīvinī protsāhane thakuśalā madhurakathā dakṣiṇāthakālajñā  BhN laḍahā saṃvṛtamantrā dūtī tvebhirguṇaiḥ kāryā tayāpyutsāhanaṃ kāryaṃ nānādarśitakāraṇam  BhN yathoktakathanaṃ caiva tathā bhāvapradarśanam na jaḍaṃ rūpasampannaṃ nārthavantaṃ na cāturam  BhN dūtaṃ vāpyathavā dūtīṃ budhaḥ kuryātkadācana kulabhogadhanādhikyaiḥ kṛtvādhikavikatthanam  BhN dūtī nivedayetkāmamarthāṃścaivānuvarṇayet na cākāmapravṛttāyāḥ kṛddhāyā vāpi saṅgamaḥ  BhN nānupāyaḥ prakartavyo dūtyā hi puruṣāśrayaḥ utsave ratrisañcāra uddyāne mitraveśmani  BhN dhātrigṛheṣu sakhyā vā tathā caiva nimantraṇe vyādhitavyapadeśena śunyāgāraniveśane  BhN kāryaḥ samāgamo nṝṇāṃ strībhiḥ prathamasaṅgame evaṃ samāgamaṃ kṛtvā sopāyaṃ vidhipūrvakam  BhN anuraktā viraktā vā liṅgākāraistu lakṣayet svabhāvabhāvātiśayairnārī yā madanāśrayā  BhN karoti nibhṛtāṃ līlāṃ nityaṃ sā madanāturā sakhīmadhye guṇān brūte svadhanaṃ ca prayacchati  BhN pūjayatyasya mitrāṇi dveṣṭi śatrujanaṃ sadā gamāgame sakhīnāṃ yā hṛṣṭā bhavati cādhikam  BhN tuṣyatyasya kathābhistu sasnehaṃ ca nirīkṣate supte tu paścāt svapiti cumbitā praticumbati  BhN uttiṣṭhatyapi pūrvaṃ ca tathā kleśasahāpi ca utsave muditā yā ca vyasane yā ca duḥkhitā  BhN evaṃvidhairguṇairyuktā tvanuraktā tu sā smṛtā viraktāyāstu cinhāni cumbitā nābhicumbati  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre trayoviṃśaḥcaturviṃśo dhyāyaḥsamāsatastu prakṛtistrividhā parikīrtitā puruṣāṇāmatha strīṇāmuttamādhamamadhyamā  BhN jitendriya jñānavatī nānāśilpavicakṣaṇā dakṣiṇādhamahālakṣyā bhītānāṃ parisāntvanī  BhN nānāśāstrārthasaṃpannā gāmbhīryaudāryaśālinī sthairyatyāgaguṇopetā jñeyā prakṛtiruttamā  BhN lokopacāracaturā śilpaśāstraviśāradā vijñānamādhuryayutā madhyamā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā  BhN rūkṣavāco tha duḥśīlāḥ kusattvāḥ sthūlabuddhayaḥ krodhanāghātakāścaiva mitraghnāśchidramāninaḥ  BhN piśunāstūddhatairvākyairakṛtajñāstathālasāḥ mānyāmānyā viśeṣajñā strīlolāḥ kalahapriyāḥ  BhN sūcakāḥ pāpakarmāṇaḥ paradravyāpahāriṇaḥ ebhirdoṣaistusaṃpannā bhavantīhādhamā narāḥ  BhN evaṃ tu śīlato nṝṇāṃ prakṛtistrividhā smṛtā strīṇāṃ punaśca prakṛtiṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN mṛdubhābā cācapalā smitabhāṣiṇyaniṣṭhurā gurūṇāṃ vacane dakṣā salajjā vinayānvitā  BhN rūpābhijanamādhuryairguṇaiḥ svābhāvikeryutā gāmbhīryadhairyasampannā vijñeyā pramadottamā  BhN nātyutkṛṣṭairanikhilairebhirevānvitā guṇaiḥ alpadoṣānuviddhā ca madhyamā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā  BhN adhamā prakṛtiryā tu puruṣāṇāṃ prakīrtitā vijñeyā saiva nārīṇāmadhamānāṃ samāsataḥ  BhN napuṃsakastu vijñeyaḥ saṃkīrṇo dhama eva ca preṣyādirapi vijñeyā saṃkīrṇā prakṛtidvijāḥ  BhN śakāraśca viṭaścaiva ye cānyepyevamādayaḥ saṃkīrṇāste pi vijñeyā hyadhamā nāṭake budhaiḥ  BhN etā jñeyāḥ prakṛtayaḥ puruṣastrīnapuṃsakaiḥ āsāṃ tu saṃpravakṣyāmi vidhānaṃ śīlasaṃśrayam  BhN atra catvāra eva syurnāyakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ madhyamottamaprakṛtau nānālakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ  BhN dhīroddhatā dhīralalitā dhīrodāttāstathaiva ca dhīrapraśāntakāścaiva nāyakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  BhN devā dhīroddhatā jñeyāḥ syurdhīralalitā nṛpāḥ senāpatiramātyaśca dhīrodāttau prakīrtitau  BhN dhīrapraśāntā vijñeyā brāhmaṇā vāṇijastathā eteṣāṃ tu punarjñeyāścatvārastu vidūṣakaḥ  BhN liṃgī dvijo rājajīvī śiṣyaśceti yathākramam devakṣitibhṛtāmātyabrāhmaṇānāṃ prayojayet  BhN vipralaṃbhasuhṛdomī saṃkathālāpapeśalāḥ vyasanī prāpya duḥkhaṃ vā yujyate bhyudayena yaḥ  BhN tathā puruṣamāhustaṃ pradhānaṃ nāyakaṃ budhāḥ yatrānekasya bhavato vyasanābhyudayau punaḥ  BhN sapuṣṭau yatra tau syātāṃ na bhavettatra nāyakaḥ divyā ca nṛpapatnī ca kulastrī gaṇikā tathā  BhN etāstu nāyikā jñeya nānāprakṛtilakṣaṇāḥ dhīrā ca lalitā ca syādudāttā nibhṛtā tathā  BhN divyā rājāṅganāścaiva guṇairyuktā bhavanti hi udāttā nibhṛtā caiva bhavettu kulajāṅganā  BhN lalite cābhyudātte ca gaṇikāśilpakārike prakṛtīnāṃ tu sarvāsāmupacārād dvidhā smṛtāḥ  BhN bāhyaścābhyantaraścaiva tayorvakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam tatra rājopacāro yo bhavedābhyantaro hi saḥ  BhN tato vākyopacārastu yasya bāhyaḥ sa ucyate atha rājopacāre ca rājñāmantaḥpurāśritam  BhN strīvibhāgaṃ pravakṣyāmi vibhaktamupacārataḥ rājopacāraṃ vakṣyāmi hyantaḥpurasamāśrayam  BhN mahādevī tathā devyaḥ svāminyaḥ sthāpitā api bhoginyaḥ śilpakāriṇyo nāṭakīyāḥ sanartakāḥ  BhN anucārikāśca vijñeyāstathā ca paricārikāḥ tathā saṃcārikāścaiva tathā preṣaṇakārikāḥ  BhN mahattaryaḥ pratīhāryaḥ kumāryaḥ sthavirā api āyuktikāśca nṛpaterayamantaḥpuro janaḥ  BhN atra mūrdhābhiṣiktā yā kulaśīlasamanvitā guṇairyuktā vayassthā ca madhyasthā krodhanā tathā  BhN mukterṣyā nṛpaśīlajñā sukhaduḥkhasahā samā śāntisvastyayanairbhartussatataṃ maṅgalaiṣiṇī  BhN śāntā pativratā dhīrā antaḥpurahite ratā ebhirguṇaistu saṃyuktā mahadevītyudāhṛtā  BhN ebhireva guṇairyuktāstatsaṃskāravivarjitāḥ garvitāścātisaubhāgyāḥ patisaṃbhogatatparāḥ  BhN śucinityojvalākārāḥ patipakṣābhyasūyakāḥ vayorūpaguṇāḍhyā yāstā devya iti bhāṣitāḥ  BhN senāpateramātyānāṃ bhṛtyānāmathavā punaḥ bhaveyustanayā yāstu pratisammānavarjitāḥ  BhN śīlarūpaguṇairyāstu saṃpannā nṛpaterhitāḥ svaguṇairlabdhasammānā svāminya iti tāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN rūpayauvanaśālinyaḥ karkaśā vibhramānvitāḥ ratisaṃbhogakuśalāḥ pratipakṣābhyasūyakāḥ  BhN dakṣā bhartuśca cittajñā gandhamālyojvalāssadā nṛpateśchandavartinyo na hīrṣyāmānagarvitāḥ  BhN utthitāśca pramattāśca tyaktālasyā na niṣṭhurāḥ mānyāmānyaviśeṣajñāḥ sthāpitā iti tāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN kulaśīlalabdhapūjāmṛdavo nāticodbhaṭāḥ madhyasthā nibhṛtāḥ kṣāntā bhoginya iti tāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN nānākalāviśeṣajñā nānāśilpavicakṣaṇāḥ gandhapuṣpavibhāgajñā lekhyālekhyavikalpikāḥ  BhN śayanāsanabhāgajñāścaturā madhurāstathā dakṣāḥ saumyāḥ sphuṭāḥ śliṣṭhā nibhṛtāḥ śilpakārikāḥ  BhN grahamokṣalayajñā yā rasabhāvavikalpikāḥ caturānāṭyakuśalāścohāpohavicakṣaṇāḥ  BhN rūpayauvanasaṃpannā nāṭakīyāstu tāḥ smṛtāḥ helābhāvaviśeṣāḍhyā satvenābhinayena ca  BhN mādhuryena ca saṃpannā hyātodyakuśalā tathā aṅgapratyaṅgasaṃpannā catuṣṣaṣṭhikalānvitā  BhN caturāḥ praśnayopetāḥ strīdoṣaiśca vivarjitāḥ sadā pragalbhā ca tathā tyaktālasyā jitaśramā  BhN nānāśilpaprayogajñā nṛttagītavicakṣaṇā atha rūpaguṇaudāryadhairyasaubhāgyaśīlasaṃpannā  BhN peśalamadhurasnigdhānunādikalacitrakaṇṭhā ca samāgatāsu nārīṣu rūpayauvanakantibhiḥ  BhN na dṛśyate guṇairstulyā yasyāḥ sā nartakī smṛtā sarvāvasthopacāreṣu yā na muñcati parthivam  BhN vijñeyā dakṣiṇā dakṣā nāṭyajñairanucārikā śayyāpālī chatradhārī tathā vyajanadhāriṇī  BhN saṃvāhikā gandhayoktrī tathā caiva prasādhikā tathābharaṇayoktrī ca mālyasaṃyojikā tathā  BhN evaṃ vidhā bhaveyuryāḥ tā jñeyāḥ paricārikāḥ nānākakṣyā vicāriṇyaḥ tathoapavanasaṃcarāḥ  BhN devatāyatanakrīḍā prāsādaparicārikāḥ yāmakinyastathā caiva yāścaivaṃ lakṣaṇāḥ striyaḥ  BhN saṃcārikāstu vijñeyā nāṭyajñaiḥ samudāhṛtāḥ preṣaṇe kāmasaṃyukte guhyāguhyasamutthite  BhN nṛpairyāstu niyujyante tāḥ jñeyāḥ paricārikāḥ sarvāntaḥpurarakṣāsu stutisvastyayanena ca  BhN yā vṛddhimabhinandanti tā vijñeyā mahattarāḥ sandhivigrahasaṃbaddhanānācārasamutthitam  BhN nivedayanti yāḥ kāryaṃ pratihāryastu tāḥ smṛtāḥ aprāptarasasaṃbhogā na saṃbhrāntā na codbhaṭāḥ  BhN nibhṛtāśca salajjāśca kumāryo bālikāḥ smṛtāḥ purvarājanayajñā yāḥ purvarājābhipūjitāḥ  BhN purvarājānucaritāstā vṛddhā iti sujñitāḥ bhāṇḍāgāreṣvadhikṛtāścāyudhādhikṛtāstathā  BhN phalamūlauṣadhīnāṃ ca tathā caivānvavekṣakī gandhābharaṇavastrāṇāṃ mālyānāṃ caiva cintikā  BhN bahvāśraye tathā yuktā jñeyā hyāyuktikāstu tāḥ ityantaḥpuracāriṇyaḥ striyaḥ proktā samāsataḥ  BhN viśeṣaṇaviśeṣeṇa tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vai dvijāḥ anuraktāśca bhaktāśca nānāpārśvasamutthitāḥ  BhN yā niyuktā niyogeṣu kāryeṣu vividheṣu ca na codbhaṭā asaṃbhrāntā na lubdhā nāpi niṣṭhurāḥ  BhN dāntāḥ kṣāntāḥ prasannāśca jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ akāmā lobhaḍīnāśca strīdoṣaiśca vivarjitāḥ  BhN sā tvantaḥpurasaṃcāre yojyā pārthivaveśmani kārukāḥ kañcukīyāśca tathā varṣavarāḥ punaḥ  BhN aupasthāyikanirmuṇḍā strīṇā preṣaṇakarmaṇi rakṣaṇaṃ ca kumārīṇāṃ bālikānāṃ prayojayet  BhN antaḥpurādhikāreṣu rājacaryānuvarttinām sarvavṛttāntasaṃvāhāḥ patyāgāre niyojayet  BhN vinītāḥ svalpasattvā ye klībā vai strīsvabhāvikāḥ jātyā na doṣiṇaścaiva te vai varṣavarāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN brahmāṇāḥ kuśalā vṛddhāḥ kāmadoṣavivarjitāḥ prayojaneṣu devīnāṃ prayoktavyā nṛpaiḥ sadā  BhN etadaṣṭādaśavidhaṃ proktamantaḥpuraṃ mayā ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bāhyaṃ puruṣasaṃbhavam  BhN rājā senāpatiścaiva purodhā mantriṇastathā sacivāḥ prāḍvivākāśca kumārādhikṛtāstathā  BhN eke cānye ca bahavo mānyā jñeyā nṛpasya tu veśeṣameṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇena nibodhata  BhN balavān buddhisaṃpannaḥ satyavādī jitendriyaḥ dakṣaḥ pragalbho dhṛtimān vikrānto matimāñchuciḥ  BhN dīrghadarśī mahotsāhaḥ kṛtajñaḥ priyavāṅmṛduḥ lokapālavratadharaḥ karmamārgaviśāradaḥ  BhN utthitaścāpramattaśca vṛddhasevyarthaśāstravit parabhāveṅgitābhijñaḥ śūro rakṣāsamanvitaḥ  BhN ūhāpohavicārī ca nānāśilpaprayojakaḥ nītiśāstrārthakuśalastathā caivānurāgavān  BhN dharmajño vyasanī caiva guṇaireterbhavennṛpaḥ kulīnā buddhisaṃpannā nānāśāstravipaścitāḥ  BhN snigdhā parerahāryaśca na pramattāśca deśajāḥ alubdhāśca vinītāśca śucayo dhārmikāstathā  BhN purodho mantriṇastvebhirguṇairyuktā bhavanti hi buddhimānnītisaṃpannastyaktālasyaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ  BhN pararandhravidhijñaśca yātrākālaviśeṣavit arthaśāstrārthakuśalo hyanuraktaḥ kulodbhavaḥ  BhN deśavitkālaviccaiva kartavyaḥ kṣitipaiḥ sadā vyavahārārthatattvajñā buddhimanto bahuśrutāḥ  BhN madhyasthā dhārmikā dhīrāḥ kāryākāryavivekinaḥ kṣāntā dāntā jitakrodhā sarvatra samadarśinaḥ  BhN īdṛśaḥ prāḍvivākāstu sthāpyā dharmāsane dvijāḥ utthitāśca pramattāśca tyaktālasyā jitaśramāḥ  BhN snigdhā śāntā vinītāśca madhyasthā nipuṇāstathā nayajñā vinayajñāśca ūhāpohavicakṣaṇāḥ  BhN sarvaśātrārthasaṃpannāḥ kumārādhikṛtāstathā bṛhaspatimatādeṣāṃ guṇāṃścābhikāṃkṣayet  BhN vijñeyaṃ copahāryaṃ ca sabhyānāṃ ca vikalpanam ityeṣa vo mayā proktaḥ prāḍvivākanirṇayaḥ  BhN ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi citrābhinayanaṃ punaḥ iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāsre puṃstryupacāro nāmādhyāyaścaturviṃśaḥpañcaviṃśo dhyāyaḥaṅgābhinayasyaiva yo viśeṣaḥ kvacit kvacit anukta ucyate citraḥ citrābhinayassmṛtaḥ  BhN uttānau tu karau kṛtvā svastikau pārśvasaṃsthitau udvāhitena śirasā tathā cordhvanirīkṣaṇāt  BhN prabhātaṃ gaganaṃ rātriḥ pradoṣaṃ divasaṃ tathā ṛtūn ghanān vanāntāṃśca vistīrṇāṃśca jalāśayān  BhN diśo grahān sanakṣatrān kiñcit svasthaṃ ca yadbhavet tasya tvabhinayaḥ kāryo nānādṛṣṭisamanvitaḥ  BhN ebhireva karairbhūyastenaiva śirasā punaḥ adho nirīkṣaṇenātha bhūmisthān saṃpradarśayet  BhN sparśasya grahaṇenaiva tathollukasanena ca candrajyostnāṃ sukhaṃ vāyuṃ rasaṃ gandhaṃ ca nirdiśet  BhN vastrāvakuṇṭhanātsūryaṃ rajodhūmānilāṃstathā bhūmitāpamathoṣṇaṃ ca kuryācchāyābhilāṣataḥ  BhN ūrdhvākekaradṛṣṭistu madhyāhne sūryamādiśet udayāstagataṃ caiva vismayārthaiḥ pradarśayet  BhN yāni saumyārthayuktāni susvabhāvakṛtāni ca gātrasparśaissaromāñcaisteṣāmabhinayo bhavet  BhN yāni syustīkṣṇarūpāṇi tāni cābhinayetsudhīḥ asaṃsparśaistathodvegaistathā mukhavikuṇṭhanaiḥ  BhN gambhīrodātasaṃyuktānarthānabhinayedbudhaḥ sāṭopaiśca sagarvaiśca gātraiḥ sauṣṭhavasaṃyutaiḥ  BhN yajñopavītadeśasthamarālaṃ hāsamādiśet svastikau vicyutau hārasragdāmārthān nidarśayet  BhN bhramaṇena pradarśinyā dṛṣṭeḥ parigamena ca alapadmakapīḍāyāḥ sarvārthagrahaṇaṃ bhavet  BhN śravyaṃ śravaṇayogena dṛśyaṃ dṛṣṭivilokanaiḥ ātmasthaṃ parasaṃsthaṃ vā madhyasthaṃ vā vinirdiśet  BhN vidyudulkāghanaravāviṣphuliṃgārciṣastathā trastāṃgākṣinimeṣaiśca te bhineyāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN udveṣṭitakarāvṛttau karau kṛtvā nataṃ śiraḥ asaṃsparśe tathāniṣṭe jihmadṛṣṭena kārayet  BhN vāyumuṣṇaṃ tamastejo mukhapracchādanena ca reṇutoyapataṃgāṃśca bhramarāṃśca nivārayet  BhN kṛtvā svastikasaṃsthānau padmakośāvadhomukhau siaṃharkṣavānaravyāghraśvāpadāṃśca nirūpayet  BhN svastikau tripatākau tu gurūṇāṃ pādavandane khaṭakasvasthikau cāpi pratodagrahaṇe smṛtau  BhN ekaṃ dvi trīṇi catvāri pañca ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭadhā nava vā daśa vāpi syurgaṇanāṃgulibhirbhavet  BhN daśākhyāśca śatākhyāśca sahasrākhyāstathaiva ca patākābhyāṃ tu hastābhyāṃ prayojyāstāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN daśākhyagaṇanāyāstu parato yā bhavediha vākyārthenaiva sādhyāsau parokṣābhinayena ca  BhN chatradhvajapatākāśca nirdeśyā daṇḍadhāraṇāt nānāpraharaṇaṃ cātha nirdeśyaṃ dhāraṇāśrayam  BhN ekacitto hyadhodṛṣṭiḥ kiñcinnataśirāstathā savyahastaśca saṃdaṃśaḥ smṛte dhyāne vitarkite  BhN udvāhitaṃ śiraḥ kṛtvā haṃsapakṣau pradakṣiṇau apatyarūpaṇe kāryāvuchrayau ca prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN udvāhitaṃ śiraḥ kṛtvā haṃsavaktraṃ tathordhvagam prasādayacca yaṃ mānaṃ dīrghasatvaṃ ca nirdiśet  BhN arālaṃ ca śirasthāne samudvāhya tu vāmakam gate nirvṛtte dhvaste ca śrāntavākye ca yojayet  BhN sarvendriyasvasthatayā prasannavadanastathā vicitrabhūtalālokaiḥ śaradantu vinirdiśet  BhN gātrasaṃkocanāccāpi sūryāgnipaṭusevanāt hemantastvabhinetavyaḥ puruṣairmadhyamādhamaiḥ  BhN śirodantoṣṭhakampena gātrasaṃkocanena ca kūjitaiśca saśītkārairadhamaśśītamādiśet  BhN avasthāntaramāsādya kadācittūttamarairapi śītābhinayanaṃ kūryāddevādvyasanasaṃbhavam  BhN ṛtujānāṃ tu puṣpāṇāṃ gandhaghrāṇaistathaiva ca rūkṣasya vāyoḥ sparśācca śiśiraṃ rūpayedbudhaḥ  BhN pramodajananāraṃbhairupabhogaiḥ pṛthagvidhiḥ vasantastvabhinetavyo nānāpuṣpapradarśanāt  BhN sveda pramārjanaiścaiva bhūmitāpaiḥ savījanaiḥ uṣṇasya vāyoḥ sparśena grīṣmaṃ tvabhinayedbudhaḥ  BhN kadambanīpakuṭapaiḥ śādvalaiḥ sendragopakaiḥ meghavātaiḥ sukhasparśaiḥ prāvṛṭkālaṃ pradarśayet  BhN meghaughanādairgambhīrairdhārāprapatanaistadā vidyunnirghātaghoṣaiśca varṣārātraṃ samādiśet  BhN yadyasya cihnaṃ veṣo vā karma vā rūpameva vā nirdeśyaḥ sa ṛtustena iṣṭāniṣṭārthadarśanāt  BhN etānṛtūnarthavaśāddarśayeddhi rasānugān sukhinastu sukhopetān suḥkhārthān duḥkhasaṃyutān  BhN yo yena bhāvenāviṣṭaḥ sukhadenetareana vā sa tadāhitasaṃkāraḥ sarvaṃ paśyati tanmayam  BhN bhāvābhinayanaṃ kuryādvibhāvānāṃ nidarśanaiḥ tathaiva cānubhāvānāṃ bhāvasiddhiḥ pravartitā  BhN vibhāvenāhṛtaṃ kāryamanubhāvena nīyate ātmānubhavanaṃ bhāvo vibhāvaḥ paradarśanam  BhN gururmitraṃ sakhā snigdhaḥ saṃbandhī bandhureva vā āvedyate hi yaḥ prāptaḥ sa vibhāva iti smṛtaḥ  BhN yattvasya saṃbhramotthānairarghyapādyāsanādibhiḥ pūjanaṃ kriyate bhaktyā so nubhāvaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN evamanyeṣvapi jñeyo nānākāryapradarśanāt vibhāvo vāpi bhāvo vā vijñeyo rthavaśādbudhaiḥ  BhN yastvapi pratisaṃdeśo dūtasyeha pradīyate so nubhāva iti jñeyaḥ pratisandeśadarśitaḥ  BhN evaṃ bhāvo vibhāvo vāpyanubhāvaśca kīrtitaḥ puruṣairabhineyaḥ syātpramadābhirathāpi vā  BhN svabhāvābhinaye sthānaṃ puṃsāṃ kāryaṃ tu vaiṣṇavam āyataṃ vāvahitthaṃ vā strīṇāṃ kāryaṃ svabhāvataḥ  BhN prayojanavaśāccaiva śeṣāṇyapi bhavanti hi nānābhavābhinayanaiḥ prayogaiśca pṛthagvidhaiḥ  BhN dhairyalīlāṅgasaṃpannaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ viceṣṭitam mṛdulīlāṅgahāraiśca strīṇāṃ kāryaṃ tu ceṣṭitam  BhN karapādāṅgasañcārāsstrīṇāṃ tu lalitāḥ smṛtāḥ sudhīraścoddhataścaiva puruṣāṇāṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN yathā rasaṃ yathā bhāvaṃ strīṇāṃ bhāvapradarśanam narāṇāṃ pramadānāṃ ca bhāvābhinayanaṃ pṛthak  BhN bhāvānubhāvanaṃ yuktaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ āliṅganena gātrāṇāṃ sasmitena ca cakṣuṣā  BhN tathollukasānaccāpi harṣaṃ saṃdarśayennaraḥ kṣiprasanjātaromāñcāt bāṣpeṇāvṛtalocanā  BhN kurvīta nartakī harṣaṃ prītyā vākyaiśca sasmitaiḥ udvṛttaraktanetraśca sandaṣṭādhara eva ca  BhN niśvāsakaṃpitāṃgaśca krodhaṃ cābhinayennaraḥ netrābhyāṃ bāṣpapūrṇābhyāṃ cibukauṣṭhaprakaṃpanāt  BhN śirasaḥ kaṃpanāccaiva bhrukuṭīkaraṇena ca maunenāṅgulibhaṅgena mālyābharaṇavarjanāt  BhN āyatakasthānakakṣāyā īrṣyā krodhe bhavetstriyāḥ niśvāsocchvāsabahulairadhomukhavicintanaiḥ  BhN ākāśavacanāccāpi duḥkhaṃ puṃsāṃ tu yojayet ruditaiḥ śvasitaiścaiva śirobhihananena ca  BhN bhūmipātābhighātaiśca duḥkhaṃ strīṣu prayojayet ānandajaṃ cārtijaṃ vā īrṣyāsaṃbhūtameva vā  BhN yatpūrvamuktaṃ ruditaṃ tatstrīnīceṣu yojayet saṃbhramāvegaceṣṭābhiśśastrasaṃpātanena ca  BhN puruṣāṇāṃ bhayaṃ kāryaṃ dhairyāvegabalādibhiḥ calatārakanetratvādgātraiḥ sphuritakampitaiḥ  BhN santrastahṛdayatvācca pārśvābhyāmavalokanaiḥ
