bhartṛranveṣaṇāccaivamuccairākrandanādapi  BhN priyasyāliṃganāccaiva bhayaṃ kāryaṃ bhavetstriyāḥ madā ye bhihitāḥ pūrvaṃ te strīnīceṣu yojayet  BhN mṛdubhiḥ skhalitairnityamākāśasyāvalaṃbanāt netrāvaghūrṇanaiścaiva sālasyaiḥ kathitaistathā  BhN gātrāṇāṃ kaṃpanaiścaiva madaḥ kāryo bhavetstriyāḥ anena vidhinā kāryaḥ prayogāḥ kāraṇotthitāḥ  BhN pauruṣaḥ strīkṛto vāpi bhāvā hyabhinayaṃ prati sarve salalitā bhāvāsstrībhiḥ kāryāḥ prayatnataḥ  BhN dhairyamādhuryasaṃpannā bhāvāḥ kāryāstu pauruṣāḥ tripatākāṅgulībhyāṃ tu valitābhyāṃ prayojayet  BhN śukāśca sārikāścaiva sūkṣmā ye cāpi pakṣiṇaḥ śikhisārasahaṃsādyāḥ sthūlā ye pi svabhāvataḥ  BhN recakairaṅgahāraiśca teṣāmabhinayo bhavet kharoṣṭrāśvatarāsiṃhavyāghragomahiṣādaya  BhN gatipracarairaṅgaiśca te bhineyāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ bhūtāḥ piśācā yakṣāśca dānavāḥ saharākṣasaiḥ  BhN aṅgahārairavinirdeśyā nāmasaṃkīrtanādapi aṅgahārairvinirdeśyā apratyakṣā bhavanti ye  BhN pratyakṣāstvabhinetavyā bhayodvegaiḥ savismayaiḥ devāśca cihnaiśca praṇāmakaraṇairbhāvaiśca viceṣṭitaiḥ  BhN abhineyo hyarthavaśādapratyakṣāḥ prayogajñaiḥ savyotthitena hastena hyarālena śiraḥ spṛśet  BhN nare hyabhivādanaṃ hyetadapratyakṣe vidhīyate khaṭakāvardhamānena kapotākhyena vā punaḥ  BhN daivatāni gurūṃścaiva pramadāścābhivādayet divaukasaśca ye pūjyāḥ pratyakṣāśca bhavanti ye  BhN tān pramāṇaiḥ prabhāvaiśca gaṃbhīrārthaiśca yojayet mahājanaṃ sakhīvargaṃ viṭadhūrtajanaṃ tathā  BhN parimaṇḍalasaṃsthena hastenābhinayenannaraḥ parvatān prāṃśuyogena vṛkṣāṃścaiva samucchritān  BhN prasāritābhyāṃ bāhubhyāmutkṣiptābhyāṃ prayojayet samūhasāgaraṃ senā bahuvistīrṇameva ca  BhN patākābhyāṃ tu hastābhyāmutkṣiptābhyāṃ pradarśayet śauryaṃ dhairyaṃ ca garvaṃ ca darpamaudāryamucchrayam  BhN lalāṭadeśasthānena tvarālenābhidarśayet vakṣodeśādapāviddhau karau tu mṛgaśīrṣakau  BhN vistīrṇapradrutotkṣepau yojyau yasyādapāvṛtam adhomukhottānatalau hastau kiñcitprasāritau  BhN kṛtvā tvabhinayedvelāṃ biladvāraṃ gṛhaṃ guhān kāmaṃ śāpagrahagrastān jvaropahatacetasaḥ  BhN eteṣāṃ ceṣṭitaṃ kuryādaṅgādyaiḥ sadṛśairbudhaiḥ dolābhinayanaṃ kuryāddolāyāstu vilokanaiḥ  BhN saṃbhokṣeṇa ca gātrāṇāṃ rajvaśvāgrahaṇena ca yadā cāṅgavatī ḍolā pratyakṣā pustajā bhavet  BhN āsaneṣu praviṣṭānāṃ kartavyaṃ tatra ḍolanam ākāśavacanānīha vakṣyāmyātmagatāni ca  BhN apavāritakaṃ caiva janāntikamathāpi ca dūrasthābhāṣaṇaṃ yatsyādaśarīranivedanam  BhN parokṣāntaritaṃ vākyamākāśavacanaṃ tu tat tatrottarakṛtairvākyaiḥ saṃlāpaṃ saṃprayojayet  BhN nānākāraṇasaṃyuktaiḥ kāvyabhāvasamutthitaiḥ hṛdayasya vaco yattū tadātmagatamīṣyate  BhN savitarkaṃ ca tadyojyaṃ prāyaśo nāṭakādiṣu nigūḍhabhāvasaṃyuktamapavāritakaṃ smṛtam  BhN kāryavaśādaśravaṇaṃ pārśvagatairyajjanāntikaṃ tatsyāt hṛdayasthaṃ savikalpaṃ bhāvasthaṃ cātmagatameva  BhN iti gūḍhārthayuktāni vacanānīha nāṭake janāntikāni karṇe tu tāni yojyāni yoktṛbhiḥ  BhN pūrvavṛttaṃ tu yatkāryaṃ bhūyaḥ kathyaṃ tu kāraṇāt karṇapradeśe tadvācyaṃ māgāttatpunaruktatām  BhN avyabhicāreṇa paṭhedākāśajanāntikātmagatapāṭhyam pratyakṣaparokṣakṛtānāmātmasamutthān parakṛtāṃśca  BhN hastamantaritaṃ kṛtvā tripatākaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ janāntikaṃ prayoktavyamapavāritakaṃ tathā  BhN svapnāyitavākyārthaistvabhineyo na khalu hastasaṃcāraiḥ suptābhihitaireva tu vākyārthaiḥ so bhineyaḥ syāt  BhN mandasvarasañcārairvyaktāvyaktaṃ punaruktavacanārtham pūrvānusmaraṇakṛtaṃ kāryaṃ svapnāñcite pāṭhyam  BhN praśithilagurukaruṇākṣaraghaṇṭānusvaritavākyagadgadajaiḥ hikkāśvasopetāṃ kākuṃ kuryānmaraṇakāle  BhN hikkāśvāsopetāṃ mūrcchopagame maraṇavatkathayet atimatteṣvapi kāryaṃ tadvatsvapnāyite yathā pāṭhyam  BhN vṛddhānāṃ yojayetpāṭhyaṃ gadgadaskhalitākṣaram asamāptākṣaraṃ caiva bālānāṃ tu kalasvanam  BhN nānābhāvopagataṃ maraṇābhinaye bahukīrtitaṃ tu vikṣiptahastapādairnibhṛtaiḥ sannaistathā kāryam  BhN vyādhiplute ca maraṇaṃ niṣaṇṇagātraistu saṃprayoktavyam hikkāśvāsopetaṃ tathā parādhīnagātrasaṃcāram  BhN viṣapīte pi ca maraṇaṃ kāryaṃ vikṣiptagātrakaracaraṇam viṣavegasaṃprayuktaṃ visphuritāṃgakriyopetam  BhN pratheme vege kārśyaṃ tvabhineye vepathurdvitīye tu dāhastathā tṛtīye vilallikā syāccaturthe tu  BhN phenastu pañcamasthe tu grīvā ṣaṣṭhe tu bhajyate jaḍatā saptame tu syānmaraṇaṃ tvaṣṭame bhavet  BhN tatra prathamavege tu kṣāmavakrakapolatā kṛśatve bhinayaḥ kāryo vākyānāmalpabhāṣaṇam  BhN sarvāṅgavepathuṃ ca kaṇḍūyanaṃ tathāṅgānām vikṣiptahastagātraṃ dāhaṃ caivāpyabhinayettu  BhN udvṛttanimeṣatvādudgāracchardanaistathākṣepaiḥ avyaktākṣarakathanaiḥ vilallikāmabhinayedevam  BhN udgāravamanayogaiḥ śirasaśca vilolanairanekavidhaiḥ phenastvabhinetavyo niḥsaṃjñatayā nimeṣaiśca  BhN aṃsakapolasparśaḥ śiraso tha vināmanaṃ śiro pāṅgaḥ sarvendriayasaṃmohājjaḍatāmevaṃ tvabhinayettu  BhN saṃmīlitanetratvāt vyādhivivṛddhau bhujaṅgadaśanādvā evaṃ hi nāṭyadharme maraṇāni budhaiḥ prayojyāni  BhN saṃbhrameṣvatha roṣeṣu śokāveśakṛteṣu ca yāni vākyāni yujyante punaruktaṃ na teṣviha  BhN sādhvaho māṃ ca heheti kiṃ tvaṃ māmāvadeti ca evaṃvidhāni kāryāṇi dvitrisaṃkhyāni kārayet  BhN pratyaṅgahīnaṃ yatkāvyaṃ vikṛtaṃ ca prayujyate na lakṣaṇakṛtastatra kāryastvabhinayo budhaiḥ  BhN bhāvo yatrottamānāṃ tu na taṃ madhyeṣu yojayet yo bhāvaścaiva madhyānāṃ na te nīceṣu yojayet  BhN pṛthak pṛthagbhāvarasairātmaceṣṭāsamutthitaiḥ jyeṣṭhamadhyamanīceṣu nāṭyaṃ rāgaṃ hi gacchati  BhN ete bhinayaviśeṣāḥ kartavyāḥ sattvabhāvasaṃyuktāḥ anye tu laukikā ye tu te sarve lokavatkāryāḥ  BhN nānāvidhairyathā puṣpairmālāṃ grathnāti mālyakṛt aṃgopāṃgai rasairbhāvaistathā nāṭyaṃ prayojayet  BhN yā yasya līlā niyatā gatiśca raṅgapraviṣṭasya nidhānayuktaḥ tāmeva kuryādavimuktasattvo yāvannaraṅgātpratinirvṛtaḥ syāt  BhN evamete mayā proktā nāṭye cābhinayāḥ kramāt anye tu laukikā ye te lokādgrāhyāḥ sadā budhaiḥ  BhN loko vedastathādhyātmaṃ pramāṇaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam vedādhyātmapadārtheṣu prāyo nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  BhN vedādhyātmopapannaṃ tu śabdacchandassamanvitam lokasiddhaṃ bhavetsiddhaṃ nāṭyaṃ lokātmakaṃ tathā  BhN na ca śakyaṃ hi lokasya sthāvarasya carasya ca śāstreṇa nirṇayaṃ kartuṃ bhāvaceṣṭāvidhiṃ prati  BhN nānāśīlāḥ prakṛtayaḥ śīle nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhiatam tasmāllokapramāṇaṃ hi vijñeyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN etān vidhīṃścābhinayasya samyagvijñāya raṅge manujaḥ prayuṅkte sa nāṭyatattvābhinayaprayoktā saṃmānamagryaṃ labhate hi loke  BhN evamete hyabhinayā vāṅnepathyāṅgasaṃbhavāḥ prayogajñena kartavyā nāṭake siddhimicchatā  BhN ṣaḍviṃśo dhyāyaḥanurūpā virūpā ca tathā rūpānurūpiṇī triprakāreha pātrāṇāṃ prakṛtiśca vibhāvitā  BhN nānāvasthākriyopetā bhūmikā prakṛtistathā bhṛśamudyotayennāṭyaṃ svabhāvakaraṇāśrayam  BhN bahubāhūbahumukhāstathā ca vikṛtānanāḥ paśuśvāpadavaktrāśca kharoṣṭrāśca gajānanāḥ  BhN ete cānye ca bahavo nānārūpā bhavanti ye ācāryeṇa tu te kāryā mṛtkāṣṭhajatucarmabhiḥ  BhN svābhāvikena rūpena praviśedraṅgamaṇḍalam ātmarūpamavacchādya varṇakairbhūṣaṇairapi  BhN yādṛśaṃ yasya yadrūpaṃ prakṛtyā tatra tādṛśam vayoveṣānurūpeṇa prayojyaṃ nāṭyakarmaṇi  BhN yathā jīvatsvabhāvaṃ hi parityajyānyadehikam parabhāvaṃ prakurute parabhāvaṃ samāśritaḥ  BhN evaṃ budhaḥ paraṃbhāvaṃ so smīti manasā smaran yeṣāṃ vāgaṅgalīlābhiśceṣṭābhistu samācaret  BhN sukumāraprayogo yo rājñāmāmodasaṃbhavaḥ śṛṅgārarasamāsādya tannārīṣu prayojayet  BhN yuddhoddhatāviddhakṛtā saṃraṃbhārabhaṭāśca ye na te strībhiḥ prayoktavyāḥ yoktavyāḥ puruṣeṣu te  BhN anudbhaṭamasaṃbhrāntamanāviddhāṅgaceṣṭitam layatālakalāpātapramāṇaniyatākṣaram  BhN suvibhaktapadālāpamaniṣṭhuramakāhalam īdṛśaṃ yadbhavennāṭyaṃ nārībhiśca prayojayet  BhN evaṃ kāryaṃ prayogajñairbhūmikāviniveśanam striyo hi strīgato bhāvaḥ pauruṣaḥ puruṣasyaca  BhN yathā vayo yathāvasthamanurūpeti sā smṛtā puruṣaḥ strīkṛtaṃ bhāvaṃ rūpātprakurute tu yaḥ  BhN rūpānurūpā sā jñeyā prayoge prakṛtirbudhaḥ chandataḥ pauruṣīṃ bhūmiṃ strī kuryādanurūpataḥ  BhN na parasparaceṣṭāsu kāryau sthavirabāliśau pāṭhyaprayoge puruṣāḥ prayoktavyā hi saṃskṛte  BhN strīṇāṃ svabhāvamadhurāḥ kaṇṭhāḥ puṃsāṃ tu balavantaḥ yadyapi puruṣo vidyāt gītavidhānaṃ ca lakṣaṇopetam  BhN mādhuryaguṇavihīnaṃ śobhāṃ janayenna tadgītam yatra strīṇāṃ pāṭhyādguṇairnarāṇāṃ ca kaṇṭhamādhuryam  BhN prakṛtiviparyayajanitau vijñeyau tāvalaṅkārau prāyeṇa devapārthivasenāpatimukhyapuruṣabhavaneṣu  BhN strījanakṛtāḥ prayogā bhavanti puruṣasvabhāvena rambhorvaśīprabhṛtiṣu svarge nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  BhN tathaiva mānuṣe loke rājñāmantaḥpureṣviha upadeṣṭavyamācāryaiḥ prayatnenāṅganājane  BhN na svayaṃ bhūmikābhyāso budhaiḥ kāryastu nāṭake strīṣu yojyaḥ prayatnena prayogaḥ puruṣāśrayaḥ  BhN yasmātsvabhāvopagato vilāsaḥ strīṣu vidyate tasmātsvabhāvamadhuramaṅgaṃ sulabhasauṣṭhavam  BhN lalitaṃ sauṣṭhavaṃ yacca so laṅkāraḥ paro mataḥ prayogo dvividhaścaiva vijñeyo nāṭakāśrayaḥ  BhN sukumārastathāviddho nānābhāvarasāśrayaḥ nāṭakaṃ saprakaraṇaṃ bhāṇo vīthyaṅka eva ca  BhN jñeyāni sukumārāṇi mānuṣairāśritāni tu sukumāraprayogo yaṃ rājñāmāmodakārakaḥ  BhN śṛṅgārasamāsādya strīṇāṃ tattu prayojayet yuddhoddhatāviddhakṛtāsaṃraṃbhārabhaṭāśca ye  BhN na te strīṇāṃ prakartavyāḥ kartavyāḥ puruṣairhi te yathāviddhāṅgahāraṃ tu bhedyabhedyāhavātmakam  BhN māyendrajālabahulaṃ pustanaipathyadīpitam puruṣaprāyasaṃcāramalpastrīkamathoddhatam  BhN sātvatyārabhaṭīyuktaṃ nāṭyamāviddhasaṃjñitam ḍimaḥ samavakāraśca vyāyogehāmṛgau tathā  BhN etānyāviddhasaṃjñāni vijñeyāni prayoktṛbhiḥ eṣāṃ prayogaḥ kartavyo devadānavarākṣasaiḥ  BhN uddhatā ye ca puruṣāḥ śauryavīryasamanvitāḥ yogyaḥ sa ca prayatnaḥ kartavyaḥ satatapramādena  BhN na hi yogyayā vinā bhavati ca bhāvarasasauṣṭhavaṃ kiṃcit saṃgītaparikleśo nityaṃ pramadājanasya guṇa eva  BhN yanmadhurakarkaśatvaṃ labhate nāṭyaprayogeṇa pramadāḥ nāṭyavilāsairlabhate yat kusumairvicitralāvaṇyam kāmopacārakuśalā bhavanti ca kāmyā viśeṣeṇa  BhN gītaṃ vṛttaṃ tathā vādyaṃ prastāragamanakriyā śiṣyaniṣpādanaṃ caiva ṣaḍācāryaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN etāni pañca yo vetti sa ācāryaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ūhāpohau matiścaiva smṛtirmedhā tathaiva ca  BhN medhāsmṛtirguṇaślāghārāgaḥ saṃgharṣa eva ca utsāhaśca ṣaḍevaitān śiṣyasyāpi guṇān viduḥ  BhN evaṃ kāryaṃ prayogajñairnānābhūmivikalpanam ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhīnāmapi lakṣaṇam  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre vikṛtivikalpo nāma ṣaḍviṃśo dhyāyaḥatha saptaviṃśo dhyāyaḥsiddhīnāṃ tu pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam yasmātprayogaḥ sarvo yaṃ siddhyarthaṃṃ saṃpradarśitaḥ  BhN siddhistu dvividhā jñeyā vāṅmanoṅgasamudbhavā daivī ca mānuṣī caiva nānābhāvasamutthitā  BhN daśāṅgā mānuṣī siddhīrdaivī tu dvividhā smṛtā nānāsattvāśrayakṛtā vāṅnaipathyaśarīrajā  BhN smitāpahāsinī hāsā sādhvaho kaṣṭameva ca prabaddhanādā ca tathā siddhirjñeyātha vāṅmayī  BhN pulakaiśca saromāñcairabhyutthānaistathaiva ca celadānāṅgulikṣepaiḥ śārīrī siddhiriṣyate  BhN kiñcicchiṣṭo raso hāsyo nṛtyadbhiryatra yujyate smitena sa pratigrāhyaḥ prekṣakairnityameva ca  BhN kiñcidaspaṣṭahāsyaṃ yattathā vacanameva ca arthahāsyena tadgrāhyaṃ prekṣakairnityameva hi  BhN vidūṣakocchedakṛtaṃ bhavecchilpakṛtaṃ ca yat atihāsyena tadgrāhyaṃ prekṣakairnityameva tu  BhN ahokārastathā kāryo nṛṇāṃ prakṛtisaṃbhavaḥ yaddharmapadasaṃyuktaṃ yathātiśayasaṃbhavam  BhN tatra sādhviti yadvākyaṃ prayoktavyaṃ hi sādhakaiḥ vismayāviṣṭabhāveṣu praharṣārtheṣu caiva hi  BhN karuṇe pi prayoktavyaṃ kaṣṭaṃ śāstrakṛtena tu prabaddhanādā ca tathā vismayārtheṣu nityaśaḥ  BhN sādhikṣepeṣu vākyeṣu praspanditatanūruhaiḥ kutūhalottarāvedhairbahumānena sādhayet  BhN dīptapradeśaṃ yatkāryaṃ chedyabhedyāhavātmakam savidravamathotphullaṃ tathā yuddhaniyuddhajam  BhN prakampitāṃsaśīrṣañca sāśraṃ sotthānameva ca tatprekṣakaistu kuśalaissādhyamevaṃ vidhānataḥ  BhN evaṃ sādhayitavyaiṣā tajjñaiḥ siddhistu mānuṣī daivikīñca punaḥ siddhiṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tattvataḥ  BhN yā bhāvātiśayopetā sattvayuktā tathaiva ca sā prekṣakaistu kartavyā daivī siddhiḥ prayogataḥ  BhN na śabdo na yatra na kṣobho na cotpātanidarśanam saṃpūrṇatā ca raṃgasya daivī siddhistu sā smṛtā  BhN daivī ca mānuṣī caiva siddhireṣā mayoditā ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ghātāndaivasamutthitan  BhN daivātmaparasamutthā trividhā ghātā budhaistu vijñeyā autpātikaścaturthaḥ kadācidatha saṃbhavatyeṣu  BhN vātāgnivarṣakuñjarabhujaṅgamaṇḍapanipātāḥ kīṭavyālapipīlikapaśupraveśanāśca daivakakṛtā  BhN ghātanataḥ paramahaṃ parayuktān saṃpravakṣyāmi vaivarṇyaṃ cāceṣṭaṃ vibhramitatvaṃ smṛtipramohaśca  BhN anyavacanaṃ ca kāvyaṃ tathāṃgadoṣo vihastatvam ete tvātmasamutthā ghātā jñeyā prayogajñaiḥ  BhN mātsaryāddveṣādvā tatpakṣatvāttathārthabhedatvāt ete tu parasamutthā jñeyā ghātā budhairnityam  BhN atihasitaruditavisphoṭitānyathotkṛṣṭanālikāpātāḥ gomayaloṣṭapipīlikāvikṣepāścārisaṃbhūtāḥ  BhN autpatikāśca ghātā mattonmattapraveśaliṅgakṛtaḥ punarātmasamutthā ye ghātāṃstāṃstān pravakṣyāmi  BhN vailakṣaṇyamaceṣṭitavibhūmikatvaṃ smṛtipramoṣaśca anyavacanaṃ ca kāvyaṃ tathārtanādo vihastatvam  BhN atihasitaruditavisvarapipīlikākīṭapaśuvirāvāśca mukuṭābharaṇanipātā puṣkarajāḥ kāvyadoṣāśca  BhN atihasitaruditahasitāni siddhairbhāvasya dūṣakāṇi syuḥ kīṭapipīlikapātā siddhiṃ sarvātmanā ghnānta  BhN vivasvaramajātatālaṃ varṇasvarasaṃpadā ca parihīṇam ajñātasthānalayaṃ svaragatamevaṃvidhaṃ hanyāt  BhN mukuṭābharaṇanipātaḥ prabaddhanādaśca nāśano bhavati paśuviśasanaṃ tatha a syādbahuvacanaghnaṃ prayogeṣu  BhN viṣamaṃ mānavihīnaṃ vimārjanaṃ cākulaprahāraṃ ca avibhaktagrahamokṣaṃ puṣkaragatamīdṛśaṃ hanti  BhN punarukto hyasamāso vibhaktibhedo visandhayo pārthaḥ trailiṅgajaśca doṣaḥ pratyakṣaparokṣasaṃmohāḥ  BhN chandovṛttatyāgo gurulāghavasaṅkaro yaterbhedaḥ etāni yathā sthūlaṃ ghātasthānāni kāvyasya  BhN jñeyau tu kāvyajātau dvau ghātāvapratikriyau nityam prakṛtivyasanasamutthaḥ śeṣodakanālikatvam  BhN apratibhāgaṃ skhalanaṃ visvaramuccāraṇaṃ ca kāvyasya asthānabhūṣaṇatvaṃ patanaṃ mukuṭasya vibhraṃśaḥ  BhN vājisyandanakuñjarakharoṣṭraśibikāvimānayānānām ārohaṇāvataraṇeṣvanabhijñatvaṃ vihastvam  BhN praharaṇakavacānāmapyayathāgrahaṇaṃ vidhāraṇaṃ cāpi amukuṭabhūṣaṇayogaścirapraveśo thavā raṅge  BhN ebhiḥ sthānaviśeṣairghātā lakṣyāstu sūribhiḥ kuśalaiḥ yūpāgnicayanadarbhastragbhāṇḍaparigrahānmuktvā  BhN siddhyā miśro ghātassarvagataścaikadeśajo vāpi nāṭyakuśalaiḥ salekhyā siddhirvā syādvighāto vā  BhN nālekhyo bahudinajaḥ sarvagato vyaktalakṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ yastvaikadivasajātassa pratyavaro pi lekhyassyāt  BhN jarjaramokṣyasyānte siddhermokṣastu nālikāyāstu kartavyastviha satataṃ nāṭyajñaiḥ prāśnikairvidhinā  BhN dainye dīnatvamāyānti te nāṭye prekṣakāḥ smṛtāḥ ye tuṣṭau tuṣṭimāyānti śoke śokaṃ vrajanti ca  BhN yo nyasya mahe mūrdho nāṃdīślokaṃ paṭheddhi devasya svavaśena pūrvaraṅge siddherghātaḥ prayogasya  BhN yo deśabhāvarahitaṃ bhāṣākāvyaṃ prayojayedbuddhyā tasyāpyabhilekhyaḥ syādghāto deśaḥ prayogajñaiḥ  BhN kaḥ śakto nāṭyavidhau yathāvadupapādanaṃ prayogasya kartuṃ vyagramanā vā yathāvaduktaṃ parijñātam  BhN tasmādgambhīrārthāḥ śabdā ye lokavedasaṃsiddhāḥ sarvajanena grāhyā yojyā nāṭake vidhivat  BhN na ca kiñcidguṇahīnaṃ doṣaiḥ parivarjitaṃ na cākiñcit tasmānnāṭyaprakṛtau doṣā nāṭyārthato grāhyā  BhN na ca nādarastu kāryo naṭena vāgaṅgasattvanepathye rasabhāvayośca gīteṣvātodye lokayuktyāṃ ca  BhN evametattu vijñeyaṃ siddhīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ budhaiḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi prāśnikānāṃ tu lakṣaṇam  BhN cāritrābhijanopetāḥ śāntavṛttāḥ kṛtaśramāḥ yaśodharmaparāścaiva madhyasthavayasānvitāḥ  BhN ṣaḍaṅganāṭyakuśalāḥ prabuddhāḥ śucayaḥ samāḥ caturātodyakuśalāḥ vṛttajñāstattvadarśinaḥ  BhN deśabhāṣāvidhānajñāḥ kalāśilpaprayojakāḥ caturthābhinayopetā rasabhāvavikalpakāḥ  BhN śabdacchandovidhānajñā nānāśāstravicakṣaṇāḥ evaṃ vidhāstu kartavyāḥ prāśnikā daśarūpake  BhN avyagrairindriyaiḥ śuddha ūhāpohaviśāradaḥ tyaktadoṣonuarāgī ca sa nāṭye prekṣakaḥ smṛtaḥ  BhN na caivete guṇāḥ samyak sarvasmin prekṣake smṛtāḥ vijñeyasyāprameyatvātsaṃkīrṇānāṃ ca pārṣadi  BhN yadyasya śilpaṃ nepathyaṃ karmaceṣṭitameva vā tattathā tena kāryaṃ tu svakarmaviṣayaṃ prati  BhN nānāśīlāḥ prakṛtayaḥ śīle nāṭyaṃ vinirmitam uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ vṛddhabāliśayoṣitām  BhN tuṣyanti taruṇāḥ kāme vidagdhāḥ samayātvite artheṣvarthaparāścaiva mokṣe cātha virāgiṇaḥ  BhN śūrāstu vīraraudreṣu niyuddheṣvāhaveṣu ca dharmākhyāne purāṇeṣu vṛddhāstuṣyanti nityaśaḥ  BhN na śakyamadhamairjñātumuttamānāṃ viceṣṭitam tattvabhāveṣu sarveṣu tuṣyanti satataṃ budhāḥ  BhN bālā mūrkhāḥ striyaścaiva hāsyanaipathyayoḥ sadā yastuṣṭo tuṣṭimāyāti śoke śokamupaiti ca  BhN kruddhaḥ krodhe bhaye bhītaḥ sa śreṣṭhaḥ prekṣakaḥ smṛtaḥ evaṃ bhāvānukaraṇe yo yasmin praviśennaraḥ  BhN sa tatra prekṣako jñeyo guṇairebhiralaṅkṛtaḥ evaṃ hi prekṣakā jñeyāḥ prayoge daśarūpataḥ  BhN saṃgharṣe tu samutpanne prāśnikān saṃnibodhata yajñavinnartakaścaiva chandovicchabdavittathā  BhN astraviccitrakṛdveśyā gandharvo rajasevakaḥ yajñavidyajñayoge tu nartako bhinaye smṛtaḥ  BhN chandovidvṛttabandheṣu śabdavitpāṭhyavistare iṣvastravitsauṣṭhave tu nepathye caiva citrakṛt  BhN kāmopacāre veśyā ca gāndharvaḥ svarakarmaṇi sevakastūpacāre syādete vai prāśnikāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN ebhirdṛṣṭāntasaṃyuktairdoṣā vācyāstathā guṇāḥ aśāstrajñā vivādeṣu yathā prakṛtikarmataḥ  BhN athaite praśnikā jñeyāḥ kathitā ye mayānaghāḥ śāstrajñānādyadā tu syātsaṃgharṣaḥ śāstrasaṃśrayaḥ  BhN śāstraprāmāṇanirmāṇairvyavahāro bhavettadā bhartṛniyogādanyo nyavigrātspardhayāpi bharatānām  BhN arthapatākā hetossaṃgharṣo nāma saṃbhavati teṣāṃ kāryaṃ vyavahāradarśanaṃ pakṣapātaviraheṇa  BhN kṛtvā paṇaṃ patākāṃ vyavahāraḥ sa bhavitavyastu sarvairananyamatibhiḥ sukhopaviṣṭaiśca śuddhabhāvaiśca  BhN yairlekhakagamakasahāyāssaha siddhibhirghātāḥ nātyāsanairnadūrasaṃsthitaiḥ prekṣakaistu bhavitavyam  BhN teṣāmāsanayogo dvādaśahastasthitaḥ kāryaḥ yāni vihitāni pūrvaṃ siddhisthānāni tāni lakṣyāṇi  BhN ghātāśca lakṣaṇīyāḥ prayogato nāṭyayoge tu daivādghātasamutthāḥ parotthitā vā budhairnavairlekhyāḥ  BhN ghātā nāṭyasamutthā hyātmasamutthāstu lekhyāḥ syuḥ ghātā yasya tvalpāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ siddhayaśca bahulāḥ syuḥ  BhN viditaṃ kṛtvā rājñastasmai deyā patākā hi sidhyatiśayātpatākā samasiddhau pārthivājñayā deyā  BhN atha narapatiḥ samaḥ syādubhayorapi sā tadā deyā evaṃ vidhijñairyaṣṭavyo vyavahāraḥ samañjasām  BhN svasthacittasukhāsinaiḥ suviśiṣṭairguṇārthibhiḥ vimṛśya prekṣakairgrāhyaṃ sarvarāgaparāṅgamukhaiḥ  BhN sādhana dūṣaṇābhāsaḥ prayogasamayāśritaiḥ samatvamaṅgamādhuryaṃ pāṭhyaṃ prakṛtayo rasāḥ  BhN vādyaṃ gānaṃ sanepathyametajjñeyaṃ prayatnataḥ gītavāditratālena kalāntarakalāsu ca  BhN uadaṅgaṃ kriyate nāṭyaṃ samantāt samamucyate aṅgopāṅgasamāyuktaṃ gītatālalayānvitam  BhN gānavādyasamatvaṃ ca tadbudhaiḥ samamucyate sanirbhugnamuraḥ kṛtvā caturaśrakrutau karau  BhN grīvāñcitā tathā karyā tvaṅgamādhuryameva ca pūrvroktānīha śeṣāṇi yāni dravyāṇi sādhakaiḥ  BhN vadyādīnāṃ punarvuprā lakṣaṇaṃ sannibodhata vādyaprabhṛtayo gānaṃ vādyamāṇāni nirdiśet  BhN yāni sthānāni siddhīnāṃ taiḥ siddhiṃ tu prakāśayet harṣādaṅgasamudbhūtāṃ nānārasasamutthitām  BhN vārakālāstu vijñeyā nāṭyajñairvividhāśrayāḥ divasaiścaiva rātriśca tayorvārān nibodhata  BhN pūrvāhṇastvatha madhyāhnastvaparāhṇastathaiva ca divā samutthā vijñeyā nāṭyavārāḥ prayogataḥ  BhN prādoṣikārdharātriśca tathā prābhātiko paraḥ nāṭyavārā bhavantyete rātrāvityanupūrvaśaḥ  BhN eteṣāṃ atra yadyojyaṃ nāṭyakāryaṃ rasāśrayam tadahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi vārakālasamāśrayam  BhN yacchrotraramaṇīyaṃ syāddharmotthanakṛtaṃ ca yat pūrvāhṇe tatprayoktavyaṃ śuddhaṃ vā vikṛtaṃ tathā  BhN sattvotthānaguṇairyuktaṃ vādyabhūyiṣṭhameva ca puṣkalaṃ sattvayuktaṃ ca aparāhṇe prayojayet  BhN kaiśikīvṛttisaṃyuktaṃ śṛṅgārasasaṃśrayam nṛtyavāditragītāḍhyaṃ pradoṣe nāṭyamiṣyate  BhN yannarmahāsyabahulaṃ karuṇaprāyameva ca prabhātakāle tatkāryaṃ nāṭyaṃ nidrāvināśanam  BhN ardharātre niyuñjīta samadhyāhne tathaiva ca sandhyābhojanakāle ca nāṭyaṃ naiva prayojayet  BhN evaṃ kālaṃ ca deśaṃ ca samīkṣya ca balābalam nityaṃ nāṭyaṃ prayuñjīta yathābhāvaṃ yathārasam  BhN athava deśakālau ca na parīkṣyau prayoktṛbhiḥyathaivājñāpayedbhartā tadā yojyamasaṃśayam  BhN tathā samudiātāścaiva vijñeyā nāṭakāśritāḥ pātraṃ prayogamṛddhiśca vijñeyāstu trayo guṇāḥ  BhN buddhimatvaṃ surūpatvaṃ layatālajñatā tathā rasabhāvajñatā caiva vayassthatvaṃ kutūhalam  BhN grahaṇaṃ dhāraṇaṃ caiva gātrāvaikalyameva ca nijasādhvasatotsāha iti pātragato vidhiḥ  BhN suvādyatā sugānatvaṃ supāṭhyatvaṃ tathaiva ca śāstrakarmasamāyogaḥ prayoga iti saṃjñitaḥ  BhN śucibhūṣaṇatāyāṃ tu mālyābharaṇavāsasām vicitraracanā caiva samṛddhiriti saṃjñitā  BhN yadā samuditāḥ sarve ekībhūtā bhavanti hi alaṅkārāḥ sakutapā mantavyo nāṭakāśrayāḥ  BhN etaduktaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ siddhīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ mayā ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmyātodyānāṃ vikalpanam  BhN iti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre siddhivyañjako nāma saptaviṃśo dhyāyaḥatha aṣṭāviṃśo dhyāyaḥātodyavidhimidānīṃ vakṣyāmaḥtataṃ caivāvanaddhaṃ ca ghanaṃ suṣirameva ca caturvidhaṃ tu vijñeyamātodyaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam  BhN tataṃ tantrīkṛtaṃ jñeyamavanaddhaṃ tu pauṣkaram ghanaṃ tālastu vijñeyaḥ suṣiro vaṃśa ucyate  BhN prayogastrividho hyeṣāṃ vijñeyo nāṭakāśrayaḥ tataṃ caivāvanaddhaṃ ca tathā nāṭyakṛto paraḥ  BhN tataḥ kutapavinyāso gāyanaḥ saparigrahaḥ vaipañciko vaiṇikaśca vaṃśavādastathaiva ca  BhN mārdaṅgikaḥ pāṇavikastathā dārduriko budhaiḥ avanaddhavidhāveṣa kutapaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ  BhN uttamādhamamadhyābhistathā prakṛtibhiryutaḥ kutapo nāṭyayoge tu nānādeśasamāśrayaḥ  BhN evaṃ gānaṃ ca vādyaṃ ca nāṭyaṃ ca vividhāśrayam alātacakrapratimaṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN yattu tantrīkṛtaṃ proktaṃ nānātodyasamāśrayam gāndharvamiti tajjñeyaṃ svaratālapadātmakam  BhN atyarthamiṣṭaṃ devānāṃ tathā prītikaraṃ punaḥ gandharvāṇāṃ ca yasmāddhi tasmādgandharvamucyate  BhN asya yonirbhavedgānaṃ vīṇā vaṃśastathaiva ca eteṣāṃ caiva vakṣyāmi vidhiṃ svarasamutthitam  BhN gāndharvaṃ trividhaṃ vidyātsvaratālapadātmakam trividhasyāpi vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ karma caiva hi  BhN dvyadhiṣṭhānāḥ svarā vaiṇāḥ śārīrāśca prakīrtitāḥ eteṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi vidhānaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam  BhN svarā grāmau mūrcchanāśca tānāḥ sthānāni vṛttayaḥ śuṣkaṃ sādhāraṇe varṇā hyalaṅkārāśca dhātavaḥ  BhN śrutayo yatayaścaiva nityaṃ svaragatātmakāḥ dāravyāṃ samavāyastu vīṇāyāṃ samudāhṛtaḥ  BhN svarā grāmāvalaṅkārā varṇāḥ sthānāni jātayaḥ sādhāraṇe ca śarīryāṃ vīṇāyāmeṣa saṃgrahaḥ  BhN vyañjanāni svarā varṇāḥ sandhayo tha vibhaktayaḥ nāmākhyātopasargāśca nipātāstaddhitāḥ kṛtaḥ  BhN chandovidhiralaṅkārā jñeyaḥ padagato vidhiḥ nibaddhaṃ cānibaddhaṃ ca dvividhaṃ tatpadaṃ smṛtam  BhN dhruvastvāvāpaniṣkāmau vikṣepo tha praveśanam śamyā tālaḥ sannipātaḥ parivartaḥ savastukaḥ  BhN mātrā prakaraṇāṅgāni vivārī yatayo layāḥ gītayo vayavā mārgāḥ pādamārgāḥ sapāṇayaḥ  BhN ityekaviṃśatividhaṃ jñeyaṃ tālagataṃ budhaiḥ gāndharvasaṃgraho hyeṣa vistaraṃ tu nibodhata  BhN tatra svarāḥṣaḍjaśca ṛṣabhaścaiva gāndhāro madhyamastathā pañcamo dhaivataścaiva saptamo tha niṣādavān  BhN caturvidhatvameteṣāṃ vijñeyaṃ gānayoktṛbhiḥ vādī caivātha saṃvādī vivādī cānuvādyapi  BhN saṃvādo madhyamagrāme pañcamasyarṣabhasya ca ṣaḍjagrāme tu ṣaḍjasya saṃvādaḥ pañcamasya ca  BhN tisro dve ca catasraśca catasrastisra eva ca dve caivādya catasraśca ṣaḍjagrāme bhavedvidhiḥ  BhN catuḥśrutirbhavet ṣaḍja ṛṣabhastriśrutiḥ smṛtaḥ dviśrutiścaiva gāndhāro madhyamaśca catuḥśrutiḥ  BhN pañcamastadvadeva syāt triśrutirdhaivato mataḥ dviśrutiśca niṣādaḥ syāt ṣaḍjagrāme vidhirbhavet  BhN atha mūrcchanāḥ dvaigrāmikyaścaturdaśaādāvuttaramandrā syādrajanī cottarāyatā caturthī śuddhaṣaḍjā tu pañcamī matsarīkṛtā  BhN aśvakrāntā tathā ṣaṣṭhī saptamī cābhirudgatā ṣaḍjagrāmāśritā hyetā vijñeyāḥ saptamūrcchanāḥ  BhN ṣaḍje cottaramandrā syādṛṣabhe cābhirudgatā aśvakrāntā tu gāndhāre madhyame matsarīkṛtā  BhN pañcame śuddhaṣaḍjā syāddhaivate cottarāyatā niṣāde rajanī ca syādityetāḥ ṣaḍjamūrcchanāḥ  BhN atha madhyamagrāmesauvīrī hariṇāśvā ca syātkalopanatā tathā śuddhamadhyā tathā mārgī pauravī hṛṣyakā tathā madhyamagrāmajā hyetā vijñeyāḥ saptamūrcchanāḥ  BhN api cakramayuktāḥ svarāḥ sapta mūrcchanetyabhisaṃjñitāḥ ṣaṭpañcasvarakāstānāḥ ṣāḍavauḍuvitāśrayāḥ  BhN sādhāraṇakṛtāścaiva kākalīsamalaṅkṛtāḥ antarasvarasaṃyuktā mūrcchanā grāmayordvayoḥ  BhN yathāchāyāsu bhavati śītaṃ prasvedo bhavati cātapasthasya na ca nāgato vasanto na ca niḥśeṣaḥ śiśirakālaḥ  BhN bhavataścātraantarasvarasaṃyogo nityamārohisaṃśrayaḥ kāryo hyalpo viśeṣeṇa nāvarohī kadācana  BhN kriyamāṇo varohī syādalpo vā yadi vā bahuḥ jātirāgaṃ śrutiṃ caiva nayante tvantarasvarāḥ  BhN  itijātīridānīṃ vakṣyāmaḥsvarasādhāraṇagatāstisro jñeyāstu jātayaḥ madhyamā pañcamī caiva ṣaḍjamadhyā tathaiva ca  BhN āsāmaṃśāstu vijñeyāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ yathā svaṃ durbalatarā vyaktā sā pañcamī tathā  BhN jātayo ṣṭādaśetyevaṃ brahmaṇābhihitaṃ purā tāstvahaṃ vartayiṣyāmi grahāṃśādivibhāgataḥ  BhN ṣāḍjī caivārṣabhī caiva dhaivatyatha niṣādinī ṣaḍjodīcyavatī caiva tathā vai ṣaḍjakaiśikī  BhN ṣaḍjamadhyā tathā caiva ṣaḍjagrāmasamāśrayāḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi madhyamagrāmasaṃśritāḥ  BhN gāndhārī madhyamā caiva gāndhārodīcyavā tathā pañcamī raktagāndhārī tathā gāndhārapañcamī  BhN madhyamodīcyavā caiva nandayanti tathaiva ca karmāravī ca vijñeyā tathāndhrī kaiśikī matā  BhN svarasādhāraṇagatāstisro jñeyāstu jātayaḥ madhyamā ṣaḍjamadhyā ca pañcamī caiva sūribhiḥ  BhN āsāmaṃśāstu vijñeyāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ yathāsvaṃ durbalataraṃ vyatyāsāttvatra pañcamī  BhN śuddhā vikṛtāścaiva hi samavāyājjātayastu jāyante punarevāśuddhakṛtā bhavantyathaikādaśānyāstu  BhN tāsāṃ yannirvṛttāḥ svareṣvathāṃśeṣu jātiṣu ca jātiḥ tadvakṣyāmi yathāvatsaṃkṣepeṇa krameṇeha  BhN parasparaviniṣpannā jñeyā hyevaṃ tu jātayaḥ pṛthaglakṣaṇasaṃyuktā dvaigrāmikāḥ svarāśrayāḥ  BhN catasro jātayo nityaṃ jñeyāḥ saptasvarā budhaiḥ catasraḥ ṣaṭsvarā jñeyāḥ smṛtāḥ pañcasvarā daśa  BhN madhyamodīcyavā caiva tathā vai ṣaḍjakaiśikī kārmāravī ca saṃpūrṇā tathā gāndhārapañcamī  BhN ṣāḍjyāndhrī nandayantī ca gāndhārodīcyavā tathā catasraḥ ṣaṭsvarā hyetāḥ jñeyāḥ pañca svarā daśa  BhN naiṣādī cārṣabhī caiva dhaivatī ṣaḍjamadhyamā ṣaḍjodīcyavatī caiva pañca ṣaḍjāśritāḥ smṛtāḥ  BhN gāndhārī raktagāndhārī madhyamā pañcamī tathā kaiśikī caiva pañcaitā madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ  BhN yāstāḥ saptasvarā jñeyā yāścaitāḥ ṣaṭsvarāḥ smṛtāḥ kadācit ṣāḍavībhūtāḥ kadāciccauḍuve matāḥ  BhN ṣaḍjagrāme tu sampūrṇā vijñeyā ṣaḍjakaiśikī ṣaṭsvarā caiva vijñeyā ṣāḍjī gāndhārayogataḥ  BhN gāndhārapañcamī caiva madhyamodīcyavā tathā punaśca ṣaṭsvarā jñeyā gāndhārodīcyavā budhaiḥ  BhN āndhrī ca nandayantī ca madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ evametā budhairjñeyā dvaigrāmikyo pi jātayaḥ  BhN ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi tāsāmaṃśavikalpanam ṣaṭsvarāḥ saptame hyaṃśe neṣyante ṣaḍjamadhyamāḥ  BhN saṃvādyalopādgāndhāre tadvadeva hi neṣyate gāndhārīraktagāndhārīkaiśikīnāṃ tu pañcamaḥ  BhN ṣaḍjāyāṃ caiva gāndhāramaṃśakaṃ viddhi ṣāḍavam ṣāḍavaṃ dhaivate nāsti ṣaḍjodīcyāmathāṃśake  BhN saṃvādyalopātsaptaitāḥ ṣāṭsvaryeṇa vivarjitāḥ gāndhārīraktagāndhāryoḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ  BhN saptamaścaiva vijñeyo yeṣu nauḍuvitaṃ bhavet dvau ṣaḍjamadhyamāṃśo tu gāndhāro tha niṣādavān  BhN ṛṣabhaścaiva pañcamyāṃ kaiśikyāṃ caiva dhaivataḥ evaṃ tu dvādaśaiveha varjyāḥ pañca svarāḥ sadā  BhN tāstvanauḍuvitā nityaṃ kartavyā hi svarāśrayāḥ sarvasvarāṇāṃ nāśastu vihitastvatha jātiṣu  BhN na madhyamasya nāśastu kartavyo hi kadācana sarvasvarāṇāṃ pravaro hyanāśī madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ gāndharvakalpe vihitaḥ sāmasvapi ca madhyamaḥ  BhN daśakaṃ jātilakṣaṇamgrahāṃśau tāramandrau ca nyāso panyāsa eva ca alpatvaṃ ca bahutvaṃ ca ṣāḍavauḍuvite tathā  BhN atha grahāḥgrahāstu sarvajātīnāmaṃśavatparikīrtitāḥ yatpravṛttaṃ bhavedgeyamaṃśo grahavikalpitaḥ  BhN tatrāṃśo nāmayasmin bhavati rāgaśca yasmāccaiva pravartate mandraśca tāramandraśca yo tyarthaṃ copalabhyate  BhN grahāpanyāsavinyāsasaṃnyāsanyāsagocaraḥ anuvṛttaśca yasyeha soṃśaḥ syāddaśalakṣaṇaḥ  BhN pañcasvaraparā tāragatiryathāaṃśāttāragatiṃ vidyādācaturthasvarādiha ā pañcamātpañcamādvā nātaḥparamiheṣyate  BhN tridhā mandragatiḥ aṃśaparā nyāsaparā aparanyāsaparā ceti mandrastvaṃśaparo nāsti nyāsau tu dvau vyavasthitau gāndhāranyāsaliṅge tu dṛṣṭamārṣabhasevanam  BhN atha nyāsa ekaviṃśatisaṅkhyaḥ aṅgasamāptau nyāsaḥ tadvadapanyāso hyaṅgamadhye ṣaṭpañcāśatsaṅkhyaḥ yathānyāso ṅgasamāptau sa caikaviṃśatisaṅkhyastathā akṣarāṇi ṣaṭpañcāśatsaṃkhyo panyāso ṅgamadhye bhavet  BhN tatra prathamaṃ vidārīmadhye nyāsasvaraprayuktastu vivadanaśīlaṃ muktvā saṃnyāsaḥ so bhidhātavyaḥ kṛtvā padāvasāne vinyāsātkvāpi vinyāsaḥ  BhN tathāalpatve tha bahutve balavadabalatā viniścayādeva jātisvaraistu nityaṃ jātyalpatvaṃ dvividhametat  BhN sañcārāṃśe balasthānāmalpatve durbalāsu ca nyāsaścāntaramārgastu jātīnāṃ vyaktikārakaḥ  BhN pañcasvaramauḍuvitaṃ vijñeyaṃ daśavidhaṃ prayogajñaiḥ triṃśatprakāravihitaṃ pūrvoktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ cāsya  BhN ṣaṭsvarasya prayogo sti tathā pañcasvarasya ca catuḥsvaraprayogo pi hyavakṛṣṭadhruvāsviha  BhN dvaigrāmikīṇāṃ jātīnāṃ sarvāsāmapi nityaśaḥ aṃśāstriṣaṣṭirvijñeyāsteṣāṃ caivāṃśavad grahāḥ  BhN aṃśagrahamidānīṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatramadhyamodīcyavāyāstu nandayantyāstathaiva ca tathā gāndhārapañcamyāḥ pañcamoṃśo grahastathā  BhN dhaivatyāśca tathā hyaṃśau vijñeyau dhaivatarṣabhau pañcamyāśca tathā jñeyau grahāṃśau pañcamarṣabhau  BhN gāndhārodīcyavāyāstu grahāṃśau ṣaḍjamadhyamau ārṣabhyāśca grahā aṃśā dhaivatarṣabhasaptamāḥ  BhN gāndhāraśca niṣādaśca hyārṣabhaśca tathāparaḥ niṣādinyāstrayo hyete grahā aṃśāśca kīrtitāḥ  BhN ṣaḍjapañcamagāndhāraistribhireva prakīrtitāḥ aṃśairgrahaistathā caiva vijñeyā ṣaḍjakaiśikī  BhN ṣaḍjaśca madhyamaścaiva niṣādo dhaivatastathā ṣaḍjodīcyavatījātergrahā aṃśāśca kīrtitāḥ  BhN pañcamaścārṣabhaścaiva niṣādo dhaivatastathā kārmāravyā budhairaṃśā grahāśca parikīrtitāḥ  BhN gāndhāraścārṣabhaścaiva pañcamo tha niṣādavān catvaroṃśā bhavantyāndhryā grahāścaiva tathaiva hi  BhN ṣaḍjaścātharṣabhaścaiva madhyamaḥ pañcamastathā madhyamāyā grahā jñeyā aṃśāścaiva sadhaivatāḥ  BhN niṣādaṣaḍjagāndhāramadhyamāḥ pañcamastathā gāndhārīraktagāndhāryorgrahā aṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  BhN ṣaḍjī dhaivatagāndhāraṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamaiḥ grahairaṃśaiśca vijñeyā vikṛtā svarayogataḥ  BhN kaiśikyāścārṣabhaṃ hitvā grahāṃśāḥ ṣaṭ svarāḥ smṛtāḥ saptasvaragrahāṃśā tu vijñeyā ṣaḍjamadhyamā  BhN ete triṣaṣṭirvijñeyāḥ sarvāsvaṃśāstu jātiṣu aṃśavacca grahāstāsāṃ sarvāsāmeva nityaśaḥ  BhN sarvāsāmeva jātīnāṃ trijātistu gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ te ca sapta gaṇā jñeyā vardhamānasvarā budhaiḥ  BhN ekasvaro dvisvaraśca trisvaro tha catuḥsvaraḥ pañcasvaraścaturthā syādekadhā saptaṣaṭsvarau  BhN etaduktaṃ mayā tvāsāṃ grahāṃśaparikalpanam punaścaiva pravakṣyāmi nyāsāpanyāsayogataḥ  BhN pañcāṃśā tu bhavet ṣāḍjī niṣādarṣabhavarjitā apanyāso bhavedatra gāndhāraḥ pañcamastathā  BhN nyāsaścātra bhavet ṣaḍjo lopyaḥ saptama eva ca ṣaḍjagāndhārasañcāraḥ ṣaḍjadhaivatayostathā  BhN ṣāḍavaṃ saptamopetamalpau vai saptamarṣabhau gāndhārasya ca bāhulyaṃ tvatra kāryaṃ prayoktubhiḥ  BhN ārṣabhyāmṛṣabhastvaṃśo niṣādo dhaivatastathā eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsaścāpyṛṣabhaḥ smṛtaḥ ṣaṭpañcasvaratā cātra ṣaḍjapañcamayorvinā  BhN dhaivatyāṃ dhaivato nyāsastvaṃśāvṛṣabhadhaivato apanyāsā bhavantyatra dhaivatārṣabhamadhyamāḥ  BhN ṣaḍjapañcamahīnaṃ tu pāñcsvaryaṃ vidhīyate pañcamena vinā caiva ṣāḍavaṃ parikīrtitam  BhN ārohiṇau ca tau kāryau laṅghanīyau tathaiva ca niṣādaścarṣabhaścaiva gāndhāro balavāṃstathā  BhN niṣādinyāṃ niṣādoṃśo sagāndhārarṣabhastathā eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsaścaivātra saptamaḥ  BhN dhaivatyā iva kartavye ṣāḍavauḍuvite tathā tadvacca laṅghanīyau tu balavantau tathaiva ca  BhN aṃśāstu ṣaḍjakaiśikyāḥ ṣaḍjagāndhārapañcamāḥ apanyāsā bhavantyatra ṣaḍjapañcamasaptamāḥ  BhN gāndhāraśca bhavennyāso hainasvaryaṃ na cātra tu daurbalyaṃ cātra kartavyaṃ dhaivatasyārṣabhasya ca  BhN madhyamaṣaḍjaśca madhyamaścaiva niṣādo dhaivatastathā syuḥ ṣaḍjodīcyavāṃśāstu nyāsaścaiva tu madhyamaḥ  BhN apanyāso bhavatyasya dhaivataḥ ṣaḍja eva ca parasparāṃśagamanamiṣṭataśca vidhīyate  BhN ṣāṭsvaryamṛṣabhāpetaṃ kāryaṃ gāndharvavedibhiḥ pañcamārṣabhahīnaṃ tu pāñcasvaryaṃ tu tatra vai  BhN ṣaḍjaścāpyṛṣabhaścaiva gāndhāraśca balī bhavet gāndhārasya ca bāhulyaṃ mandrasthāne vidhīyate  BhN sarveṃśāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyāyāmapanyāsāstathaiva ca ṣaḍjaśca madhyamaścāpi nyāsau nāryau prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN gāndhārasaptamāpetaṃ pāñcasvaryaṃ vidhīyate ṣāḍavaṃ saptamāpetaṃ kāryaṃ cātra prayogataḥ  BhN sarvasvarāṇāṃ sañcāra iṣṭatastu vidhīyate ṣaḍjagrāmāśritā hyetā vijñeyāḥ sapta jātayaḥ  BhN ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ gāndhāryāḥ pañca evāṃśā dhaivatarṣabhavarjitāḥ  BhN ṣaḍjaśca pañcamaścaiva hyapanyāsau prakīrtitau gāndhāraśca bhavennyāsaḥ ṣāḍavaṃ carṣabhaṃ vinā  BhN dhaivatarṣabhayorhīnaṃ tathā cauḍuvitaṃ bhavet laṅghanīyau ca tau nityamārṣabhāddhaivataṃ vrajet vihitastviti gāndhāryāḥ svaranyāsāṃśagocaraḥ  BhN lakṣaṇaṃ raktagāndhāryā gāndhāryā eva yatsmṛtam dhaivato balavānatra daurbalyaṃ tasya lopataḥ  BhN gāndhāraṣaḍjayoścātra sañcāraścārṣabhādvinā apanyāsastathā caiva madhyamastu vidhīyate  BhN gāndhārodīcyavāṃśau tu vijñeyau ṣaḍjamadhyamau pāñcasvaryaṃ na caivātra ṣāṭsvaryamṛṣabhaṃ vinā  BhN kāryaścāntaramārgaśca nyāsopanyāsa eva ca ṣaḍjodīcyavatīvattu pāñcasvaryeṇa jātucit  BhN madhyamāyā bhavantyaṃśā vinā gāndhārasaptamau eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsaścaiva tu madhyamaḥ  BhN gāndhārasaptamāpetaṃ pāñcasvaryaṃ vidhīyate ṣāḍavaṃ cāpyagāndhāraṃ kartavyaṃ tu prayogataḥ  BhN ṣaḍjamadhyamayoścātra kāryaṃ bāhulyameva hi gāndhāralaṅghanaṃ cātra kāryaṃ nityaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN madhyamodīcyavā pūrṇā hyaṃśa ekastu pañcamaḥ śeṣo vidhistu kartavyo gāndhārodīcyavāṃ gataḥ  BhN dvāvaṃśāvatha pañcamyāmṛṣabhaḥ pañcamastathā saṛniṣādāvapanyāsau nyāsaścaiva tu pañcamaḥ  BhN madhyamāvattu kartavye ṣāḍavauḍuvite tathā daurbalyaṃ cātra kartavyaṃ ṣaḍjagāndhāramadhyamaiḥ  BhN kuryādapyatra sañcāraṃ pañcamasyārṣabhasya ca gāndhāragamanaṃ caiva kāryaṃ tvalpaśca saptamaḥ  BhN lpaṃ ca saptamātatha gāndhārapañcamyāḥ pañcamoṃśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ tāragatyā tu ṣaḍjo pi kadācinnātivartate  BhN ṛṣabhaḥ pañcamaścaiva hyapanyāsau prakīrtitau nyāsaścaiva tu gāndhāro sā ca pūrṇasvarā sadā pañcamyā yaśca gāndhāryāḥ sañcāraḥ sa vidhīyate  BhN pañcamaścārṣabhaścaiva gāndhāro tha niṣādavān catvāroṃśā bhavantyāndhryāmapanyāsāsta eva hi  BhN gāndhāraśca bhavennyāsaḥ ṣaḍjāpetaṃ tu ṣāḍavam gāndhārārṣabhayoścāpi sañcārastu parasparam  BhN saptamasya ca ṣaṣṭhasya nyāso gatyanupūrvaśaḥ ṣaḍjasya laṅghanaṃ cātra nāsti cauḍuvitaṃ sadā  BhN nandayantyāḥ kramān nyāsāpanyāsāṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ gāndhāro madhyamaścaiva pañcamaścaiva nityaśaḥ  BhN ṣaḍjo lopyaśca laṅghyaśca nāndhrīsañcaraṇaṃ bhavet laṅghanaṃ hyṛṣabhasyāpi tacca mandragataṃ smṛtam  BhN tāragatyā tu ṣaḍjastu kadācinnātivartate gāndhāro vā grahaḥ kāryastathā nyāsaśca nityaśaḥ  BhN kārmāravyāḥ smṛtā hyaṃśā ārṣabhaḥ pañcamastathā dhaivataśca niṣādaścāpyapanyāsāsta eva tu pañcamaśca bhavennyāso hainasvaryaṃ na cātra tu  BhN gāndhārasya viśeṣeṇa sarvato gamanaṃ bhavet  BhN kaiśikyāstu tathā hyaṃśāḥ sarve caivārṣabhaṃ vinā eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsau gāndhārasaptamau  BhN dhaivateṃśe niṣāde ca nyāsaḥ pañcama iṣyate apanyāsaḥ kadācittu ṛṣabho pi vidhīyate  BhN ārṣabhe ṣāḍavaṃ cātra dhaivatarṣabhavarjitam tathā cauḍuvitaṃ kuryād balinau cāntyapañcamau  BhN daurbalyamṛṣabhasyātra laṅghanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ aṃśavat kalpitaścānyaiḥ ṣāḍave tu vidhīyate ṣaḍjamadhyāvadatrāpi sañcārastu bhavediha  BhN evametā budhairjñeyā jātayo daśalakṣaṇāḥ yathā yasmin rase yāśca gadato me nibodhata  BhN iti jātivikalpādhyāyo ṣṭāviṃśaḥ samāptaḥatha ekonatriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥṣaḍjodīcyavatī caiva ṣaḍjamadhyā tathaiva ca madhyapañcamabāhulyāt kāryā śṛṅgārahāsyayoḥ  BhN ṣāḍjī tvathārṣabhī caiva svasvarāṃśaparigrahāt vīraraudrādbhuteṣvete prayojye gānayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN niṣāde ṃśe tu naiṣādī gāndhāre ṣaḍjakaiśikī karuṇe tu rase kāryā jātigānaviśāradaiḥ  BhN dhaivatī dhaivatāṃśe tu bībhatse sabhayānake dhruvāvidhāne kartavyā jātirgāne prayatnataḥ rasaṃ kāryamavasthāṃ ca jñātvā yojyā prayoktṛbhiḥ ṣaḍjagrāmāśritā hyetāḥ prayojyā jātayo budhaiḥ  BhN ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ gāndhārīraktagāndhāryau gāndhārāṃśopapattitaḥ karuṇe tu rase kārye niṣāde ṃśe tathaiva ca  BhN madhyamā pañcamī caiva nandayantī tathaiva ca gāndhārapañcamī caiva madhyamodīcyavā tathā madhyamapañcamabāhulyāt kāryāḥ śṛṅgārahāsyayoḥ  BhN kārmāravī tathā cāndhrī gāndhārodīcyavā tathā vīre raudre dbhute kāryāḥ ṣaḍjarṣabhāṃśayojitāḥ kaiśikī dhaivatāṃśe tu bībhatse sabhayānake  BhN ekaiva ṣaḍjamadhyā jñeyā sarvarasasaṃśrayā jātiḥ tasyāstvaṃśāḥ sarve svarāstu vihitāḥ prayogavidhau  BhN yo yadā balavān yasmin svaro jātisamāśrayāt tatpravṛttaṃ rase kāryaṃ gānaṃ geye prayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN madhyapañcamabhūyiṣṭhaṃ gānaṃ śṛṅgārahāsyayoḥ ṣaḍjarṣabhaprāyakṛtaṃ vīraraudrādbhuteṣu ca  BhN gāndhāraḥ saptamaścāyaṃ karuṇe gānamiṣyate tathā dhaivatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ bībhatse sabhayānake  BhN ekaiva ṣaḍjamadhyā vijñeyākhilarasāśrayā jātiḥ tasyāstvaṃśāḥ sarve svarāśca vihitāḥ prayogavidhau  BhN sarveṣvaṃśeṣu rasā niyamavidhānena saṃprayoktavyāḥ kākalyantaravihitā viśeṣayuktāstu balavantaḥ evametā budhairjñeyā jātayo nāṭyasaṃśrayāḥ  BhN pāṭhyaprayogavihitān svarāṃścāpi nibodhata hāsyaśṛṅgārayoḥ kāryau svarau madhyamapañcamau  BhN ṣaḍjarṣabhau ca kartavyau vīraraudrādbhuteṣvatha gāndhāraśca niṣādaśca kartavyau karuṇe rase  BhN dhaivataśca prayogajñairbībhatse sabhayānake ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi varṇālaṅkāralakṣaṇam  BhN ārohī cāvarohī ca sthāyisañcāriṇau tathā varṇāścatvāra evaite hyalaṅkārāstadāśrayāḥ  BhN ārohanti svarā yatrārohīti sa tu saṃjñitaḥ yatra caivāvarohanti so varohī prakīrtitaḥ  BhN sthirāḥ svarāḥ samā yatra sthāyī varṇaḥ sa ucyate sañcaranti svarā yatra sa sañcārīti kīrtitaḥ  BhN śārīrasvarasambhūtāstristhānaguṇagocarāḥ catvāro lakṣaṇopetā varṇāstatra prakīrtitāḥ  BhN evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ yadā varṇo nukarṣati tadā varṇasya niṣpattirjñeyā svarasamudbhavā  BhN ete varṇāstu vijñeyāścatvāro gītayojakāḥ etān samāśritān samyagalaṅkārān nibodhata  BhN prasannādiḥ prasannāntaḥ prasannādyanta eva ca prasannamadhyaśca tathā kramarecita eva ca prastāraśca prasādaśca saptaite sthāyivarṇagāḥ  BhN atha sañcārijān bhūyaḥ kīrtyamānānnibodhata mandrastathā prasannādiḥ preṅkhito bindureva ca sannivṛttaḥ pravṛttaśca recitaḥ kampitaḥ samaḥ  BhN kuharaścaiva veṇuśca rañcito hyavalokitaḥ āvartakaḥ parāvṛttaḥ sañcāriṇyaścaturdaśa  BhN niṣkarṣobhyucayaścaiva hasito bindureva ca preṅkholitastathākṣipto vistīrṇoddhaṭitastathā  BhN hrādamānaḥ sampradānaḥ sandhiḥ pracchādanastathā prasannādiḥ prasannānta ityārohe trayodaśa  BhN vidhūtaśca trivarṇaśca tathodvāhita eva ca udgītaśca tathā veṇirvijñeyā hyavarohiṇaḥ  BhN saptarūpagatā jñeyā alaṅkārā budhaistvime naite sarve dhruvāsviṣṭāḥ śrutivarṇaprakarṣaṇāt  BhN na hi varṇaprakarṣastu dhruvāṇāṃ siddhiriṣyate śyeno vāpyathavā bindurye cānyeti prakarṣiṇaḥ  BhN te dhruvāṇāṃ prayogeṣu na kāryāḥ svapramāṇataḥ taddhruvāṇāṃ prayoge tu kāryā hyārohiṇaḥ svarāḥ  BhN yasmādarthānurūpā hi dhruvā kāryārthadarśikā varṇānāṃ tu punaḥ kāryaṃ kṛśatvaṃ padasaṃśrayam  BhN ye tra prayoge gacchanti tāṃśca varṇān nibodhata prasannādiḥ prasannāntaḥ prasannādyanta eva ca  BhN prasannamadhyamaścaiva binduḥ kampitarecitau tāraścaiva hi mandraśca tathā tārataraḥ punaḥ preṅkholitastāramandro mandratāraḥ samastathā  BhN sannivṛttaḥ pravṛttaśca prasādo pāṅga eva ca ūrmiḥ preṅkho valokaśca ityete sarvavarṇagāḥ  BhN sthāyivarṇādṛte caiṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam kramaśo dīpito yaḥ syāt prasannādiḥ sa kathyate  BhN vyastoccārita evaiṣa prasannānto vidhīyate ādyantayoḥ prasannatvāt prasannādyanta iṣyate  BhN prasannamadhyo madhye tu prasannatvādudāhṛtaḥ sarvasāmyāt samo jñeyaḥ sthitastvekasvaro pi yaḥ  BhN ādimadhyalayo yatra sa cormiriti saṃjñitaḥ śrutayo ntyād dvitīyasya mṛdumadhyāyatāḥ svarāḥ  BhN āyatatvaṃ bhavennīce mṛdutvaṃ tu viparyaye sve svare madhyamatvaṃ ca mṛdumadhyamayostathā dīptāyate karuṇānāṃ śrutīnāmeṣa niścayaḥ  BhN bindurekakalo jñeyaḥ kampitaśca kalādvayam gatāgatapravṛtto yaḥ sa preṅkholita iṣyate  BhN yastu kaṇṭhe svaro dhaḥ syāt sa tu tāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ urogatastathā mandro mūrdhni tāratarastathā  BhN kramāgatastu yastāraḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ pañcama eva vā tāramandraprasannastu jñeyo mandragataḥ sa ca  BhN laṅghayitvā parān mandrāt parāṃ tāragatiṃ gataḥ mandratāraprasannastu vijñeyo hyavarohaṇāt  BhN prasannāntaḥ svaro yatra prasādaḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ apāṅgakistu vijñeyaḥ svarāṇāmatha sañcarāt  BhN recitaḥ śirasi jñeyaḥ kampitaṃ tu kalātrayam kaṇṭhe niruddhapavanaḥ kuharo nāma jāyate  BhN evamete tvalaṅkārā vijñeyā varṇasaṃśrayāḥ atha gītīḥ pravakṣyāmi chando kṣarasamanvitāḥ  BhN śaśinā rahiteva niśā vijaleva nadī latā vipuṣpeva avibhūṣiteva ca strī gītiralaṅkārahīnā syāt  BhN prathamā māgadhī jñeyā dvitīyā cārdhamāgadhī sambhāvitā tṛtīyā tu caturthī pṛthulā smṛtā  BhN trinivṛttapragītā yā gītiḥ sā māgadhī smṛtā ardhataḥ sannivṛttā ca vijñeyā hyardhamāgadhī  BhN sambhāvitā ca vijñeyā gurvakṣarasamanvitā pṛthulākhyā ca vijñeyā nityaṃ laghvakṣarānvitā  BhN etāstu gītayo jñeyā dhruvāyogaṃ vinaiva hi gāndharva eva yojyāstu nityaṃ gānaprayoktṛbhiḥ  BhN gītayo gaditāḥ samyag dhātūṃścaiva nibodhata vistāraḥ karaṇaśca syādāviddho vyañjanastathā catvāro dhātavo jñeyā vāditrakaraṇāśrayāḥ  BhN saṅghātajo tha samavāyajaśca vistārajo nubandhakṛtaḥ jñetaścatuṣprakāro dhāturvistārasaṃjñaśca  BhN vidhayastu smṛtāstasya pūrvaṃ vistāra eva ca saṅghātasamavāyau tu vijñeyau tau dviatrikau  BhN pūrvaścaturvidhastatra paścimo ṣṭavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ karaṇānāṃ viśeṣeṇa vijñeyau tau pṛthak pṛthak  BhN adhaścordhvaṃ ca vijñeyāvadharottarajau svarau saṅghātajo vidhistveṣa vijñeyo vādanaṃ prati  BhN dviruttaro dviradharastvadharādiścottarāvasānaśca jñeyastathottarādiḥ punarapyadharāvasānaśca  BhN samavāyajastathā syāt triruttarastriradharaśca vijñeyaḥ dviradharottarādharānto dviradharaścottaravirāmaśca  BhN uttaramukho dviradharo dviruttarāvasānaśca madhyottaro dviradharo dviruttaro pyadharamadhyaśca  BhN anubandhastu jñeyo vyāsasamāsācca niyatameṣāṃ hi evaṃ caturdaśavidho vistāro dhāturākhyātaḥ  BhN ribhitoccayanīribhito hrādastu tathānubandhaḥ syāt pañcavidho vijñeyo vīṇāvādye karaṇadhātuḥ  BhN trikapañcasaptanavakairyathākramaṃ saṃyuto bhavedvādye sarvairanubandhakṛtairgurvantaḥ syāt karaṇadhātuḥ  BhN kṣepaḥ pluto tipāto tikīrṇamanubandhasaṃjñitaścaiva āviddho viṣṭo yo dhāturvai pañcavidha eva  BhN dvitricatuṣkanavakaiḥ prahāraiḥ kramaśaḥ kṛtaiḥ āviddhadhāturvijñeyaḥ sānubandhavibhūṣitaḥ  BhN vyañjanadhātoḥ puṣpaṃ kalatalaniṣkoṭitaṃ tathoddhṛṣṭam repho nubandhasaṃjño nusvanitaṃ binduravamṛṣṭam  BhN kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhasaṃyuktaṃ puṣpamityabhisaṃjñitam aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ samaṃ tantryoḥ sparśanaṃ yat kalaṃ tu tat  BhN vāmena pīḍanaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇenāhatistale savyāṅguṣṭhaprahārastu niṣkoṭitamihocyate  BhN prahāro vāmatarjanyā uddhṛṣṭamiti saṃjñitam sarvāṅgulisamākṣepo repha ityabhisaṃjñitaḥ  BhN talasthāne dhastantrīṇāmanusvanitamucyate gurvakṣarakṛtā tantrī bindurityabhisaṃjñitaḥ  BhN kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhakābhyāṃ tu dakṣiṇābhyāmadhomukham tantrīṣu triprahāraṃ cāpyavamṛṣṭaṃ prakīrtitam  BhN vyāsasamāsādeṣāmanubandhaḥ sārvadhātuko jñeyaḥ iti daśavidhaḥ prayojyo vīṇāyāṃ vyañjano dhātuḥ  BhN ityete dhātavaḥ proktāścatvāro lakṣaṇānvitāḥ tisṛṇāmapi vṛttīnāṃ yeṣu vādyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  BhN tisrastu vṛttayaścitrādakṣiṇāvṛttisaṃjñitāḥ vādyagītobhayaguṇā nirdiṣṭāntā yathākramam  BhN tisro gītivṛttayaḥ prādhānyena grāhyāḥ citrā vṛttirdakṣiṇā ceti tāsāṃ tālagītilayayatimārgaprādhānyāni yathāsvaṃ vyañjakāni bhavanti tatra citrāyāṃ saṅkṣiptavādyatāladrutalayasamāyatynāgatagrahāṇāṃ prādhānyam tathāvṛttau gītavāditradvikalātālamadhyalayasrotogatāyatisamagrahamārgāṇāṃ prādhānyam dakṣiṇāyāṃ gīticatuṣkalatālavilambitalayagopucchāyatyatītagrahamārgāṇāṃ prādhānyam sarvāsāmeva vṛttīnāṃ lalitādyāstu jātayaḥ dhātubhiḥ saha saṃyuktā bhavanti guṇavattarāḥ  BhN eteṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ samavāyājjātayastu jāyante syādudāttalalitaribhitaghanasaṃjñāścatasrastu  BhN tatrodātā vistāradhātuviṣayā hyudāttatvāt lalitā vyañjanadhātorlalitatvādeva saṃprayoktavyā  BhN āviddhadhātuviṣayā ribhitā laghusañcayād vinirdiṣṭā karaṇaviṣayā ca ghanasaṃjñā gurulaghusañcayāttu syāt  BhN trividhaṃ gīte kāryaṃ vādyaṃ vīṇāsamudbhavaṃ tajjñaiḥ tattvaṃ hyanugatamoghaḥ sthānaikakaraṇasamāyuktāḥ  BhN layatālavarṇapadayatigītyakṣarabhāvakaṃ bhavet tattvam gītaṃ tu yadanugacchatyanugatamiti tadbhavedvādyam  BhN āviddhakaraṇabahulaṃ hyuparyuparipāṇikaṃ drutalayaṃ ca anapekṣitagītārthaṃ vādyaṃ tvoghe vidhātavyam  BhN evaṃ jñeyā vaiṇe vādyavidhāne tu dhātavastajjñaiḥ lakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ nirgītavidhānasamavāyam  BhN āśrāvaṇā tathārambho vaktrapāṇistathaiva ca saṅkhoṭanā tathā kāryaṃ punaśca parighaṭṭanā  BhN mārgāsāritametat syāllīlākṛtamathāpi ca āsāritāni ca tathā triprakārakṛtāni tu  BhN etāni tu bahirgītānyāhurvādyavido janāḥ satālāni hyatālāni cittavṛttau kṛtāni tu  BhN prayojanaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ pūrvaraṅgavidhiṃ prati eteṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ sanidarśanam  BhN āsrāvaṇā nāmavistāradhātuvihitaiḥ karaṇaiḥ pravibhāgaśo dvirabhyastaiḥ dviścāpi sannivṛttaiḥ karaṇopacayaiḥ krameṇa syāt  BhN guruṇī tvādāvekādaśakaṃ caturdaśaṃ sapañcadaśam sacaturviṃśakamevaṃ dviguṇīkṛtametadeva syāt  BhN laghunī guru caiva syādathāṣṭamaṃ guru bhavettathā ca punaḥ ṣaṭ ca laghūni tato ntye gurvādyāśrāvaṇāyāṃ tu  BhN triḥśamyoparipāṇau tālāvapyevameva caikikavān samapāṇau dve śamye tālāvapyevamevātha  BhN bhūyaḥ śamyātālāvavapāṇāvuttarasthā caiva cañcatpuṭastathā syādevaṃ hyāśrāvaṇātālaḥ  BhN atrodāharaṇam jhaṇṭuṃ jagati yavalitaka jambuka jhaṇṭuṃ titi ca laghu ca jhaṇṭum diṅgale gaṇapatipaśupatijambuka diṅgale varabhuja diginagi cā titi cādini nigicā paśupati nīticā athārambhaḥ dīrghāṇyādāvaṣṭau dvādaśa ca laghūni naidhanaṃ caiva catvāri gurūṇi tathā hrasvānyaṣṭau ca dīrghaṃ ca  BhN laghusaṃjñāni caturdhā nidhanaṃ dviguṇīkṛtāni dīrghe dve aṣṭau laghūni naidhanamityārambhe kṣaravidhānam  BhN atrodāharaṇam Jhaṇṭuṃ jhaṇṭuṃ jhaṇṭuṃ jhaṇṭuṃ jagati yavalitaka diginigicā diṅgle diṅgle titi jhajhalakucajhalajambuka titicā gaṇapati surapati paśupati cā asya tu vādyam kāryaṃ triparvarahitairudvahanairapyatha samavarohaiḥ talaribhitahrādayutaiḥ karaṇairvistārabhūyiṣṭhaiḥ  BhN apacayayuktairdvistristathā nivṛttairdvirabhyastaiḥ ārambho pyavataraṇastriparvayuktaiśca kartavyaḥ  BhN tālastrikalastvādau śamyaikakalā kalādvaye tālaḥ dvikalā ca punaḥ śamyā tālo dvikalaśca kartavyaḥ  BhN trikalaśca sannipātaḥ punaḥ pitāputrakaśca ṣaṭpūrvaḥ cañcatpuṭastathā syādārambhe tālayogastu  BhN asya tu vādyamkāryaṃ triparvarahitairudvahanairapyatha samavarohaiḥ talaribhitahrādayutaiḥ karaṇairvistābhūyiṣṭhaiḥ  BhN apacayayuktairdvistristathā nivṛttairdvirabhyastaiḥ ārambho pyavataraṇastriparvayuktaiśca kartavyaḥ  BhN atha vaktrapāṇiḥgurūṇi pañca hrasvāni ṣaḍguruśca caturguṇaḥ guruṇī dve laghu tvekaṃ catvāryatha gurūṇi hi  BhN catvāryatha laghūni syustrīṇi dīrghāṇi caiva hi laghūnyaṣṭau ca dīrghaṃ ca vaktrapāṇau bhavedvidhiḥ  BhN atrodāharaṇam diṅgale jhaṇṭuṃ jambuka jagati ya jhaṇṭuṃ diṅgale ghendṛṃ gheṭo ghāṭo bhaṭṭunakiṭi inaṃ duṅ ghadugadukiṭamaṭanam asya vādyam āviddhakaraṇayukto dvyaṅgaḥ syādekapravṛttau vā alpavyañjanadhāturvādyavidhirvaktrapāṇau tu  BhN dvikale madrake yattu śamyātālādipātam tatsarvaṃ vaktrapāṇau tu kāryamaṣṭakalānvitam  BhN tasyādhastāt punaḥ kāryaṃ pañcapāṇicatuṣṭayam vaktrapāṇerayaṃ tālo mukhapratimukhāśrayaḥ  BhN atha saṅkhoṭanāguruṇī laghūnyathāṣṭau dīrghaṃ dviguṇaṃ tathā ca kartavyam laghudīrghe laghu ca punaścaturguṇaṃ saṃprakartavyam  BhN punaraṣṭau hrasvāni syuriha tathā naidhanaṃ ca kartavyam saṅkhoṭanavastuvidhau hrasvaguruvidhiḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ  BhN saṅkhoṭanāyā udāharaṇaṃ prakalpya kṛtam diṅgale jagati ya valati katecāticātijha laghu cajhala paśupaticā asyā vādyavidhiḥ adhidaṇḍaṃ hastābhyāṃ vīṇāṃ vinigṛhya dakṣiṇāṅgulyā aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ ca tathā kāryaṃ saṅkhoṭanāvādyam  BhN saṅkhoṭayet svaraṃ vādinā tu saṃvādinā tathādhibalam samavāyibhiśca śeṣairanuvādibhiralpakaiścāṃśaiḥ  BhN vistāracitrakaraṇairdvistrirvinivartitairdvirabhyastaiḥ upacayayuktaiḥ kramaśo vadanti saṅkhoṭanāvādyam tālo syā gaditastajjñaiḥ śīrṣavat pañcapāṇinā  BhN atha parighaṭṭanādīrghāṇyādāvaṣṭau laghūni kuryāt punardviguṇitāni hrasvānyapi catvāri dviguṇāni syuḥ sadīrghāṇi  BhN ṣoḍaśa laghūni ca syuḥ saha nidhane caiva kāryāṇi eṣa parighaṭṭanāyāṃ gurulaghuvastukramaḥ proktaḥ  BhN etasyāmapyudāharaṇaṃ prakalpya kṛtam diṅgale diṅgale diṅgale diṅgale jagati ya valati ka titijhalakucajhaladiginigi gaṇapati cā calati ka gaṇapati paśupatisurapati cā vādyaṃ cāsyāstajjñaiḥ sodvahanaṃ hastalāghavāt kāryam vyañjanadhātusamutthaṃ nānākaraṇāśrayopetam  BhN sampiṣṭakavaccāsyāstālaḥ karaṇaistu dhātusaṃyuktaiḥ gurulaghuyogādevaṃ vihitaḥ kāryo budhairnityam  BhN mārgāsāritavādyaṃ vistārāviddhakaraṇasaṃyuktam sakalaiḥ satalaiḥ karaṇairatha gurulaghusañcayaścāyam  BhN catvāri gurūṇi syurlaghūni catvāri ca dviguṇitāni guruṇī laghūnyathāṣṭau guruṇī cetyetat tridhā yojyam  BhN athavācatvāri tu gurūṇi syurhrasvānyaṣṭau bhavanti hi guruṇī nava hrasvāni dīrghamantyamathāpi ca  BhN atrodāharaṇam diṅgale jhaṇṭuṃ jagati ya thalitaka jhaṇṭuṃ titi jhalakuca jhalatiticā bālāsāritavaccaiva tālo sya parikīrtitaḥ  BhN śravaṇamadhurāṇi līlākṛtānyabhisṛtaparisṛtāntarakṛtāni tānyapyarthavaśādiha kartavyāni prayogavidhau  BhN yathāsāritāni jyeṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni tālapramāṇanirdiṣṭāni tāni tālavidhāne vakṣyāmaḥ evametat svaragataṃ jñeyaṃ vīṇāśarīrajam vipañcīvādyayuktāni karaṇāni nibodhata  BhN rūpaṃ kṛtaṃ pratikṛtaṃ pratibhedo rūpaśeṣamoghaśca ṣaṣṭhī vai pratiśuṣkā tvevaṃ jñeyaṃ karaṇajātam  BhN vīṇāvādyadviguṇaṃ gurulāghavavādanaṃ bhavedrūpam rūpaṃ pratibhedakṛtaṃ pratikṛtamityucyate vādyam  BhN yugapatkṛte nyakaraṇaṃ pratibhedo dīrghalāghavakṛtaḥ syāt kṛtamekasyāṃ tantryāṃ pratiśuṣkā nāma vijñeyā  BhN vīṇāvādyavirāme pyaviratakaraṇaṃ tu rūpaśeṣaḥ syāt āviddhakaraṇayukto hyuparyuparipāṇikastvoghaḥ  BhN kāryaṃ dhruvāvidhāne prāyeṇa hi koṇavādanaṃ tajjñaiḥ sthānaprāptyarthaṃ cedyattatra bhavedayaṃ niyamaḥ  BhN taccaughatulyakaraṇaṃ vācyaṃ kāryaṃ vipañcyāstu saptatantrī bhaveccitrā vipañcī tu bhavennava koṇavādanā vipañcī syāccitrā cāṅgulivādanā  BhN tatavādyavidhānamidaṃ sarvaṃ proktaṃ samāsayogena vakṣyāmyataśca bhūyaḥ suṣirātodyaprayogaṃ tu  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre tatātodyavidhānaṃ nāma ekonatriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥtriṃśo dhyāyaḥatodyaṃ suṣiraṃ nāma jñeyaṃ vaṃśagataṃ budhaiḥ vaiṇa eva vidhistatra svaragrāmasamāśrayaḥ  BhN dvikatrikacatuṣkāstu jñeyā vaṃśagatāḥ svarāḥ kampyamānārthamuktāśca vyaktamuktāstathaiva ca  BhN tatropari yathā hyekaḥ svaro vaiṇasvarāntare prāpnotyanyatvameveha tathā vaṃśagato pi hi  BhN dvikastrikaścatuṣko vā śrutisaṅkhyo bhavet svaraḥ anīraṇāttu śeṣāṇāṃ svarāṇāmapi sambhavaḥ aṅgulīvādanakṛtaṃ tacca me sannibodhata  BhN vyaktamuktāṅgulistatra svaro jñeyaścatuḥśrutiḥ kampyamānāṅguliścaiva triśrutiḥ parikīrtitaḥ dviko rdhāṅgulimuktaḥ syāditi śrutyāśritāḥ svarāḥ  BhN ete syurmadhyamagrāme bhūyaḥ ṣaḍjāśritāḥ punaḥ vyaktamuktāṅgulikṛtāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ  BhN ṛṣabho dhaivataścāpi kampyamānāṅgulīkṛtau ardhamuktāṅguliścaiva gāndhāro tha niṣādavān  BhN svarasādhāraṇaścāpi kākalyantarasaṃjñayā niṣādagāndhārakṛtau ṣaḍjamadhyamayorapi  BhN viparyayā sannikarṣe śrutilakṣaṇasiddhitaḥ vaiṇakaṇṭhapraveśena siddhā ekāśritāḥ svarāḥ  BhN yaṃ yaṃ gātā svaraṃ gacchet taṃ taṃ vaṃśena vādayet śārīravaiṇavaṃśyānāmekībhāvaḥ praśasyate  BhN avicalitamavicchinnaṃ varṇālaṅkārasaṃyutaṃ vidhivat lalitaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ veṇorevaṃ smṛtaṃ vādyam  BhN evametat svaragataṃ vijñeyaṃgānayoktṛbhiḥ ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dhanātodyavikalpanam  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre suṣirātodyalakṣaṇaṃ nāmādhyāyastriṃśaḥatha trayastriṃśo dhyāyaḥguṇāt pravartate gānaṃ doṣaṃ caiva nirasyate tasmādyatnena vijñeyau guṇadoṣau samāsataḥ  BhN gātā pratyagravayāḥ snigdho madhurasvaropacitakaṇṭhaḥ layatālakalāpātapramāṇayogeṣu tattvajñaḥ  BhN rūpaguṇakāntiyuktā mādhuryopetasatvasampannāḥ peśalamadhurasnigdhānunādisamarakta gurukaṇṭhāḥ  BhN śubhasuvihitagamakavidhāyinyo kṣobhyās tālalayakuśalāḥ ātodyārpitakaraṇā vijñeyā gāyikāḥ śyāmāḥ  BhN prāyeṇa tu svabhāvāt strīṇāṃ gānaṃ nṛṇāṃ ca pāṭhyavidhiḥ strīṇāṃ svabhāvamadhuraḥ kaṇṭho nṛṇāṃ balitvaṃ ca  BhN yatra strīṇāṃ pāṭhyaṃ guṇairnarāṇāṃ ca gānamadhuratvam jñeyo laṅkāro sau na hi svabhāvo hyayaṃ teṣām  BhN suniviṣṭapāṇilayayatiyogajñausumadhuralaghuhastau gātṛguṇaiścopetāvavahitamanasau susaṅgītau  BhN sphuṭaracitacitrakaraṇau gītaśravaṇācalaupravīṇau ca citrādivādyakuśalauvīṇābhyāṃ vādakau bhavataḥ  BhN balavānavahitabuddhirgītalayajñastathāsusaṅgītaḥ śrāvakamadhurasnigdho dṛḍhapāṇirvaṃśavādako jñeyaḥ  BhN avicalitamavicchannaṃ varṇālaṅkārabodhakaṃmadhuram snigdhaṃ doṣavihīnaṃ veṇorevaṃ smṛtaṃ vādyam  BhN jñānavijñānakaraṇavacanaprayogasiddhiniṣpādanāni ṣaḍācāryaguṇā iti tatra jñānaṃ śāstrāvabodhaḥ yathā ca kriyāsampādanaṃ vijñānam kaṇṭhahastagauṇyaṃ karaṇam jitagranthatā vacanam deśādisampadārādhanaṃ prayogasiddhiḥ śiṣyasvabhāvamaviśeṣyopāttaya upadeśācchiṣyaniṣpādanamiti  BhN śrāvaṇo tha ghanaḥ snigdho madhurohyavadhānavān tristhānaśobhītyevaṃ tu ṣaṭ kaṇṭhasya guṇā matāḥ  BhN udāttaṃ śrūyate yasmāttasmācchrāvaṇa ucyate śrāvaṇaḥ susvaro yasmādacchinnaḥ sa ghano mataḥ  BhN arūkṣadhvanisaṃyuktaḥ snigdhastajjñaiḥ prakīrtitaḥ manaḥprahlādanakaraḥ sa vai madhura ucyate  BhN svare dhike ca hīne ca hyavirakto vidhānavān śiraḥkaṇṭheṣvabhihitaṃtristhānamadhurasvaraḥ tristhānaśobhītyevaṃ tu sa hi tajjñairudāhṛtaḥ  BhN kapilo hyavasthitaścaiva tathā sandaṣṭa eva ca kākī ca tumbakī caiva pañca doṣā bhavanti hi  BhN vaisvaryaṃ ca bhavedyatra tathā syād ghargharāyitam kapilaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ śleṣmakaṇṭhastathaiva ca  BhN ūnatādhikatā cāpi svarāṇāṃ yatra dṛśyate rūkṣadoṣahataścaiva jñeyaḥ sa tvavyavasthitaḥ  BhN daṇḍaprayogāt sandaṣṭastvācāryaiḥ parikīrtitaḥ yo na vistarati sthāne svaramuccāraṇāgatam  BhN nāsāgragrastaśabdastutumbakī so bhidhīyate  BhN anye tusamapraharaṇe caiva javinau viśadau tathā jitaśramau vikṛṣṭau ca madhurau svedavarjitau tathā bṛyannakhau caiva jñeyau hastasya vai guṇāḥ  BhN  itiete guṇāśca doṣāśca tattvataḥ kathito mayā ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi hyavanaddhavidhiṃ punaḥ  BhN pūrvaṃ yaduktaṃ prapitāmahena kuryāt ya evaṃ tu naraḥ prayoge sammānamagrayaṃ labhate sa loke  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre guṇadoṣavicāro nāmādhyāyastrayastriṃśaḥatha pañcatriṃśo dhyāyaḥvinyāsaṃ bhūmikānāṃ ca sampravakṣyāmi nāṭake yādṛśo yasya kartavyo vinyāso bhūmikāsvatha  BhN gativāgaṅgaceṣṭābhiḥ sattvaśīlasvabhāvataḥ parīkṣya pātraṃ tajjñastu yuñjyād bhūminiveśane  BhN tasminnanviṣya hi guṇavān kāryā pātrasamāśrayā na khedajananaṃ buddherācāryasya bhaviṣyati  BhN ācāryaḥ pātrajāṃścaiva guṇāñjñātvā svabhāvajān tataḥ kuryād yathāyogaṃ nṛṇāṃ bhūminiveśanam  BhN aṅgapratyaṅgasaṃyuktamahīnāṅgaṃ vayonvitam na sthūlaṃ na kṛśaṃ caiva na dīrghaṃ na ca mantharam  BhN śliṣṭāṅgaṃ dyutimantaṃ ca susvaraṃ priyadarśanam etairguṇaiśca saṃyuktaṃ devabhūmiṣu yojayet  BhN sthūlaṃ prāṃśuṃ bṛhaddehaṃ meghagambhīranisvanam raudrasvabhāvanetraṃ ca svabhāvabhrukuṭīmukham  BhN rakṣodānavadaityānāṃ bhūmikāsu prayojayet puruṣāṇāṃ prayogastu tathāṅgakriyayānvitaḥ  BhN sunetrasubhruvaḥ svaṅgāḥ sulalāṭāḥ sunāsikāḥ svoṣṭhāḥ sugaṇḍāḥ sumukhāḥ sukaṇṭhāḥ suśirodharāḥ  BhN svaṅgapratyaṅgasaṃyuktā na dīrghā na ca mantharāḥ na sthūlā na kṛśāścaiva svabhāvena vyavasthitāḥ  BhN suśīlā jñānavantaśca tathā ca priyadarśanāḥ kumārarājabhūmau tu saṃyojyāśca narottamāḥ  BhN aṅgairavikalairdhīraṃ sphuṭaṃ vasanakarmaṇi na dīrghaṃ naiva ca sthūlamūhāpohavicakṣaṇam  BhN adīnaṃ ca pragalbhaṃ ca pratyutpannaviniścayam senāpateramātyānāṃ bhūmikāsu prayojayet  BhN piṅgākṣaṃ ghoṇanāsaṃ ca netramuccamathāpi vā kañcukiśrotriyādīnāṃ bhūmikāsu niyojayet  BhN evamanyeṣvapi tathā nāṭyadharmavibhāgataḥ deśaveṣānurūpeṇa pātraṃ yojyaṃ svabhūmiṣu  BhN mantharaṃ vāmanaṃ kubjaṃ vikṛtaṃ vikṛtānanam viṣṭabdhanetraṃ kāṇākṣaṃ sthūlaṃ cipiṭanāsikam  BhN durjanaṃ dusvabhāvaṃ ca vikṛtācārameva ca dāsabhūmau prayuñjīta budho dāsāṅgasambhavam  BhN prakṛtyātikṛśaṃ kṣāmaṃ tapaḥśrānteṣu yojayet tathā ca puruṣaṃ sthūlamuparodheṣu yojayet  BhN yadi vā nedṛśāḥ santi prakṛtyā puruṣā dvijāḥ ācāryabuddhyā yojyāstu bhāvaceṣṭāsvabhāvataḥ  BhN yā yasya sadṛśī ceṣṭā hyuttamādhamamadhyamā sa tathācāryayogena niyamyā bhāvabhāvinī  BhN ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bharatānāṃ vikalpanam bharatāśrayāśca bharato vidūṣakaḥ saurikastathā nāndī nandī sasūtradhāro nāṭyaraso nāyakaścaiva  BhN mukuṭābharaṇavikalpau vijñeyo mālyavastuvividhaiśca kārakakuśīlavādyā vijñeyā nāmataścaiva  BhN dhuryavadeko yasmāduddhāro nekabhūmikāyuktaḥ bhāṇḍagrahopakaraṇaināṭyaṃ bharato bhavet tasmāt  BhN lokāhṛdāśrayakṛtā sarvaprakṛtipracārasaṃyuktā nānāśrayāṃ prakurute tathā ca nārī tu sarvatra  BhN pratyutpannapratibho narmakṛto narmagarbhanirbhedaḥ chedavidūṣitavacano vidūṣako nāma vijñeyaḥ  BhN tūryatistu naraḥ sarvātodyapravādane kuśalaḥ tūraparigrahayukto vijñeyastauriko nāma  BhN naṭanṛti dhātvartho yaṃ bhūtaṃ nāṭayati lokavṛttāntam rasabhāvasatvayuktaṃ yasmāt tasmānnaṭo bhavati  BhN stutyabhivādanakṛtairmadhurairvākyaiḥ sumaṅgalācāraiḥ sarva stauti hi lokaṃ yasmāt tasmādbhavedvādī  BhN bhāvebhyo bahudhāsmin rasā vadati nāṭyayogeṣu prākṛtasaṃskṛtapāṭhyo nandī nāmeti sa jñeyaḥ  BhN gītasya ca vādyasya ca pāṭhyasya ca naikabhāvavihitasya śiṣṭopadeśayogāt sūtrajñaḥ sūtradhārastu  BhN yasmāt yathopadiṣṭān rasāṃśca bhāvāṃśca satvasaṃyuktān bhūmivikalpairnayati ca nāṭyakaraḥ kīrtitastasmāt  BhN caturātodyavidhānaṃ sarvasya tu śāstrakhe davihitasya nāṭyasyāntaṃ gacchati tasmādvai nāyako bhihitaḥ  BhN nānāprakṛtisamutthaṃ karoti yaḥ śīrṣakaṃ mukuṭayoge vividhairveṣaviśeṣaiḥ sa ca kuṭakārastu vijñeyaḥ  BhN bhāṇḍakavādyajñā yā layatālajñā rasānuviddhā ca sarvāṅgasundarī vai kartavyā nāṭakīyā tu  BhN yastvābharaṇaṃ kuryād bahuvidhavihitaṃ sa cābharaṇaḥ yaścopakaraṇayogāt sa tena nāmnābhidhātavyaḥ  BhN yo vai mālyaṃ kurute paṅcavidhaṃ mālyākṛt sa vijñeyaḥ yaścāpi veṣayogaṃ kurute sa ca veṣakārī tu  BhN citrajñaścitrakaro vastrasya rañjānāttathā rajakaḥ jatvaśmalohakāṣṭhairdravyakaraiḥ kārukaścaiva  BhN nānātodyavidhāne prayogayuktaḥ pravādane kuśalaḥ atodye pyatikuśalo yasmāt sa kuśalavo jñeyaḥ  BhN yadyat samāśrayante śilpaṃ vā karma vā prayogaṃ vā tanaivopagataguṇā vijñeyā nāmataḥ puruṣāḥ  BhN evaṃ tu nāṭakavidhau jātirnaṭasaṃśrayā budhairjñeyā nāṭyopakaraṇayuktā nānāśilpaprasaktā ca  BhN ukto tra bhūmikānyāsaḥ prayoktāraśca yogataḥ ādiṣṭaṃ nāṭyaśāstraṃ ca munayaḥ kimihocyatām  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre bhūmikāvikalpādhyāyaḥ pañcatriṃśaḥatha ṣaṭtriṃśo dhyāyaḥathātreyo vasiṣṭhaśca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ aṅgirā gautamo gastyo manurāyustathātmavān  BhN viśvāmitraḥ sthūlaśirāḥ saṃvartaḥ pramatirdanuḥ uśanā bṛhaspatirvyāsaścyavanaḥ kāśyapo dhruvaḥ  BhN durvāsā jāmadagnyaśca mārkaṇḍeyo tha gālavaḥ bharadvājaśca raibhyaśca yavakrītastathaiva ca  BhN sthūlākṣaḥ śakalākṣaśca kāṇvo meghātithiḥ kratuḥ nāradaḥ parvataścaiva suvarmāthaikajo dvijaḥ  BhN nitamburbhuvanaḥ saumyaḥ śatānandaḥ kṛtavraṇaḥ jāmadagnyastathā rāmaḥ kacaścetyevamādayaḥ  BhN evaṃ te munayaḥ śrutvā sarvajñaṃ bharataṃ tataḥ punarūcuridaṃ vākyaṃ kutūhalapurogamam  BhN yastvayā gadito hyeṣa nāṭyavedaḥ purātanaḥ ekacittaiḥ sa cāsmābhiḥ samyak samupadhāritaḥ  BhN ekaśca saṃśayo smākaṃ taṃ no vyākhyātumarhasi ko vānyo nāṭyavedasya niścayaṃ vaktumarhati  BhN na vayaṃ parihāsena na virodhena na cerṣyayā pṛcchāmo bhagavan nāṭyamupadeśārthameva tu  BhN asmābhiśca tadā noktaṃ kathācchedo bhavediti idānīṃ tūpaśikṣārthaṃ nāṭyaguhyaṃ nidarśaya  BhN lokasya caritaṃ nāṭyamityavocastvamīdṛśam teṣāṃ tu lokaṃ guhyānāṃ niścayaṃ vaktumarhasi  BhN devasya kasya caritaṃ pūrvaraṅge dvijarṣabha kimarthaṃ bhujyate hyeṣa prayuktaḥ kiṃ karoti vā  BhN kasmāccaiva punaḥ śaucaṃ samyak carati sūtradṛk kathamurvītale nāṭyaṃ svargānnipatitaṃ vibho  BhN kathaṃ tavāyaṃ vaṃśaśca naṭasaṃjñaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ sarvameva yathātattvaṃ kathayasva mahāmune  BhN teṣaṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ pratyuvāca punarvākyaṃ guhyārthābhinayaṃ prati  BhN bravīmi vaḥ kathāṃ guhyāṃ yanmāṃ pṛcchan suvratāḥ pūrvaraṅgavidhānasya tāṃ ca me sannibodhata  BhN proktavānasmi yatpūrvaṃ śubhaṃ vighnanibarhaṇam tasyānubandhena mayā pūrvaraṅgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  BhN śastrāṇāṃ pratikārārthaṃ śarīrāvaraṇaṃ yathā kriyate hi tathā pāpaṃ hutenaiva praśāmyati  BhN evaṃ japyaiśca homaiśca devatābhyarcanena ca sarvātodyavidhānaiśca tathā gītasvanena ca  BhN stutyāśīrvacanaiḥ śāntaiḥ karmabhāvānukīrtanaiḥ mayā pāpāpaharaṇaiḥ kṛte vighnanibarhaṇe  BhN stutigītādisaṃsṛṣṭairdevairabhihito smyaham nitarāṃ parituṣṭāḥ smaḥ prayogeṇāmunā ca te  BhN devatāsuramānandya yasmāṃllokaśca nandati tasmādayaṃ prayogastu nāndīnāmā bhaviṣyati  BhN gītavādyānunādo hi yatra kākusvanaḥ śubhaḥ tasmin deśe vipāpmāno māṅgalyaṃ ca bhaviṣyati  BhN yāvattaṃ pūrayeddeśaṃ dhvanirnāṭyasamāśrayaḥ na sthāsyanti hi rakṣāṃsi taṃ deśaṃ na vināyakāḥ  BhN āvāhe ca vivāhe ca yajñe nṛpatimaṅgale nāndīśabdamupaśrutya hiṃsrā naśyanti caiva hi  BhN pāṭhyaṃ nāṭyaṃ tathā geyaṃ citravāditrameva ca vedamantrārthavacanaiḥ samaṃ hyetad bhaviṣyati  BhN śrutaṃ mayā devadevāt tattvataḥ śaṅkarāddhitam snānajapyasahasrebhyaḥ pavitraṃ gītavāditam  BhN yasminnātodyanāṭyasya gītapāṭhyadhvaniḥ śubhaḥ bhaviṣyatyaśubhaṃ deśe naiva tasmin kadācana  BhN evaṃ pūjādhikārārthaṃ pūrvaraṅgaḥ kṛto mayā nānāstutikṛtairvākyairdevatābhyarcanena ca  BhN yato bhivādanaṃ kliṣṭaṃ śiṣṭaṃ tadraṅgamaṇḍale tatastasya hi tacchaucaṃ vihitaṃ tu dvijottamāḥ  BhN śaucaṃ kṛtvā yato mantraṃ pūjanaṃ jarjarasya tu ucyate pūrvaraṅge smin tasmācchaucaṃ prakīrtitam  BhN yathāvatāritaṃ caiva nāṭyametanmahītale vaktavyaṃ sarvametaddhi na śakyaṃ hi nigūhitum  BhN mamaite tanayāḥ sarve nāṭyavedasamanvitāḥ sarvalokaṃ prahasanaiḥ bādhante nāṭyasaṃśrayaiḥ  BhN kasyacittvatha kālasya śilpakaṃ grāmyadharmakam ṛṣīṇāṃ vyaṅgyakaraṇaṃ kurvadbhirguṇasaṃśrayam  BhN aśrāvyaṃ taddurācāraṃ grāmyadharmapravartitam niṣṭhuraṃ cāprastutaṃ ca kāvyaṃ saṃsadi yojitam  BhN tacchrutvā munayaḥ sarve bhīmaroṣaprakampitāḥ ūcustān bharatān kruddhā nirdahanta ivāgnayaḥ  BhN mā tāvadbho dvijā yuktamidamasmadviḍambanam ko nāmāyaṃ paribhavaḥ kiñca nāsmāsu sammatam  BhN yasmājjñānamadonmattā na vetthāvinayāśritāḥ tasmādetaddhi bhavatāṃ kujñānaṃ nāśameṣyati  BhN ṛṣīṇāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca samavāyasamāgatāḥ nirāhutā vinā homaiḥ śūdrācārā bhaviṣyatha  BhN apāṅkteyāḥ kutsitāścāvamā eva bhaviṣyatha yaśca vo bhavitā vaṃśaḥ sarvāśauco bhaviṣyati  BhN ye ca vo vaṃśajāste pi bhaviṣyantyatha nartakāḥ paropasthānavantaśca śastrapaṇyopajīvinaḥ  BhN śāpaṃ dattaṃ tathā jñātvā sutebhyo me tadā surāḥ sarve vimanaso bhūtvā tānṛṣīn samupasthitāḥ  BhN yācamānaistataḥ proktaṃ devaiḥ śakrapurogamaiḥ idānīṃ duḥkhamutpannaṃ nāṭyametad vinaṅkṣati  BhN ṛṣibhiśca tataḥ proktaṃ na caitaddhi vinakṣyati śeṣamanyatra yad proktaṃ sarvametad bhaviṣyati  BhN etacchrutvā tu vacanaṃ munīnāmugratejasām viṣṇṇāste tataḥ sarve śrutvā māṃ samupasthitāḥ  BhN proktavantaśca māṃ putrāstvayāho nāśitā vayam anena nāṭyadoṣeṇa śūdrācārā hi yat kṛtāḥ  BhN mayāpi sāntvayitvoktā mā krodhaṃ vrajatānaghāḥ kṛtāntavihito smākaṃ nūnameṣa vidhiḥ sutāḥ  BhN munīnāṃ hi mṛṣā vākyaṃ bhaviṣyati kadācana nidhane ca mano mā bhūd yuṣmākamiti sāntvitāḥ  BhN jānīdhvaṃ tattathā nāṭyaṃ brahmaṇā saṃpravartitam śiṣyebhyaśca tadanyebhyaḥ prayacchāmaḥ prayogataḥ  BhN mā vai praṇaśyatāmetannāṭyaṃ duḥkhapravartitam mahāśrayaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ vedāṅgopāṅgasambhavam  BhN apsarobhya idaṃ caiva yathātattvaṃ yathāśrutam nāṭyaṃ dattvā tataḥ sarve prāyaścittaṃ cariṣyatha  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre nāṭyaśāpo nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo dhyāyaḥatha saptatriṃśo dhyāyaḥkasyacittvatha kālasya nahuṣo nāma pārthivaḥ prāptavān devarājyaṃ hi nayabuddhiparākramaḥ  BhN praśaśāsa tadā rājyaṃ devairvyuṣṭimavāpnuvan gāndharvaṃ caia nāṭyaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā cintāmupāgamat  BhN sa cintayitvā manasā kathameṣa gṛhe mama nāṭyaprayogo hi bhavediti sādara eva san  BhN kṛtāñjaliḥ prayogārthaṃ proktavāṃstu surān nṛpaḥ apsarobhiridaṃ sārdhaṃ nāṭyaṃ bhavatu me gṛhe  BhN pratyuktaśca tato devairbṛhaspatipurogamaiḥ divyāṅganānāṃ naiveha mānuṣaiḥ saha saṅgatiḥ  BhN hitaṃ pathyaṃ ca vaktavyo bhavān svargādhipo hi yat ācāryāstatra gacchantu gatvā kurvantu te priyam  BhN proktavāṃstu tato māṃ tu nṛpatiḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ idamicchāmi bhagavan nāṭyamurvyāṃ pratiṣṭhitam  BhN pūrvamācāryakaṃ caiva bhavatābhihitaṃ śrutam vyaktabhāvātvidaṃ labdhaṃ tvatsakāśād dvijottama  BhN pitāmahagṛhe smākaṃ tadantaḥpure jane pitāmahakriyāyukta murvaśyāṃ sampravartitam  BhN tasyāḥ praṇāśaśokena unmādoparate nṛpe vipanne ntaḥpurajane punarnāśamupāgatam  BhN prakāśametadicchāmo bhūyastat saṃprayojitam tithiyajñakriyāsvetad yathā syān maṅgalaiḥ śubhaiḥ  BhN tasmin mama gṛhe baddhaṃ nānāprakṛtisaṃśrayam strīṇāṃ lalitavinyāsairyato naḥ prathayiṣyati  BhN tathāstviti mayā prokto nahuṣaḥ pārthivastadā sutāścāhūya samproktā sāmapūrvaṃ suraiḥ saha  BhN ayaṃ hi nahuṣo rājā yācate naḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ gamyatāṃ sahitairbhūmiṃ prayoktuṃ nāṭyameva ca  BhN kariṣyamaśca śāpāntamasmin samyak prayojite brāhmaṇānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca bhaviṣyatha na kutsitāḥ  BhN tatra gatvā prayujyantāṃ prayogān vasudhātale na śakyaṃ cānyathā kartuṃ vacanaṃ pārthivasya hi  BhN asmākaṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ nahuṣasya mahātmanaḥ ātmopadeśasiddhaṃ hi nāṭyaṃ proktaṃ svayaṃbhuvā  BhN śeṣamuttaratantreṇa kohalastu kariṣyati prayogaḥ kārikāścaiva niruktāni tathaiva ca  BhN apsarobhiridaṃ sārdhaṃ krīḍanīyakahetukam adhiṣṭhitaṃ mayā svarge svātinā nāradena ca  BhN tataśca vasudhāṃ gatvā nahuṣasya gṛhe dvijāḥ strīṇāṃ prayogaṃ bahudhā baddhavanto yathākramam  BhN atropabhogataste tu mānuṣīṣu māmātmajāḥ baddhavanto dhikasnehaṃ tāsu tad dvijasattamāḥ  BhN putrānutpādya vadhvā ca prayogaṃ ca yathākramam brahmaṇā samanujñātāḥ prāptāḥ svargaṃ punaḥ sutāḥ  BhN evamurvītale nāṭyaṃ śiṣyaiḥ samavatāritam bharatānāṃ ca vaṃśo yaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca pravartitaḥ  BhN kohalādibhirevaṃ tu vatsaśāṇḍilyadhūrtitaiḥ matyadharmakriyāyuktaiḥ kaścitkālamavasthitaiḥ  BhN etacchātraṃ praṇītaṃ hi nārāṇāṃ buddhivardhanam trailokyasya kriyopetaṃ sarvaśāstranidarśanam maṅgalyaṃ lalitaṃ caiva brahmaṇo vadanodbhavam  BhN ya idaṃ śruṇuyān nityaṃ proktaṃ cedaṃ svayambhuvā kuryāt prayogaṃ yaścaivamathavādhītavān naraḥ  BhN yā gatirvedaviduṣāṃ yā gatiryajñakāriṇām yā gatirdānaśīlānāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ prāpnuyāddhi saḥ  BhN dānadharmeṣu sarveṣu kīrtyate tu mahat phalam prekṣaṇīyapradānaṃ hi sarvadāneṣu śasyate  BhN na tathā gandhamālyena devāstuṣyanti pūjitāḥ yathā nāṭyaprayogasthairnityaṃ tuṣyanti maṅgalaiḥ  BhN gāndharvaṃ ceha nāṭyaṃ ca yaḥ samyak paripālayet sa īśvaragaṇeśānāṃ labhate sadgatiṃ parām  BhN evaṃ nāṭyaprayoge bahuvidhivihitaṃ karmaśāstraṃ praṇītam noktaṃ yaccātra lokādanukṛtikaraṇāt saṃvibhāvyaṃ tu tajjñaiḥ kiṃ cānyat samprapūrṇā bhavatu vasumatī naṣṭadurbhikṣarogā śāntirgobrāhmaṇānāṃ bhavatu narapatiḥ pātu pṛthvīṃ samagrām  BhN iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre guhyatattvakathanādhyāyaḥ saptatriṃśaḥnāṭyaśāstram saṃpūrṇam
